

śrīmanmaharṣivedavyāsapraṇītaṃ
śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam

prathamo adhyāyaḥ
ārambhamaṅgalam
yadyogibhirbhavabhayārtivināśayogyam
āsādya vanditamatīva vivaktacittaiḥ ।
tadvaḥ punātu haripādasarojayugmam
avirbhavatkramavilaṅghitabhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ ।।
pāyāt sa vaḥ sakalakalmaṣabhedadakṣaḥ
kṣīrodakukṣiphaṇibhoganiviṣṭamūrtiḥ ।
śvāsāvadhūtasalilotkaṇikākarālaḥ
sindhuḥ pranṛtyamiva yasya karoti saṅgāt ।।
nārāyaṇaṃ samaskṛtya naraṃ caiva narottamam ।
devīṃ sarasvatīṃ vyāsaṃ tato jayamudīrayet ।।

tapaḥ svādhyāyanirataṃ mārkaṇḍeyaṃ mahāmunim ।
vyāsaśiṣyo mahātejā jaiminiḥ paryapṛcchata ।।
bhagavan bhāratākhyānaṃ vyāsenoktaṃ mahātmanā ।
pūrṇamastamalaiḥ śubhrairnānāśāstrasamuccayaiḥ ।।
jātiśuddhisamāyuktaṃ sādhuśabdopaśobhitam ।
pūrvapakṣoktisiddhāntapariniṣṭhāsamanvitam ।।
tridaśānāṃ yathā viṣṇurdvipadāṃ brāhmaṇo yathā ।
bhūṣaṇānāñca sarveṣāṃ yathā cūḍāmaṇirvaraḥ ।।
yathāyudhānāṃ kuliśamindriyāṇāṃ yathā manaḥ ।
tatheha sarvaśāstraṇāṃ mahābhāratamuttamam ।।
atrārthaścaiva dharmaśca kāmo mokṣaśca varṇyate ।
parasparānubandhāśca sānubandhāśca te pṛthak ।।
dharmaśāstramidaṃ śreṣṭhamarthaśāstramidaṃ param ।
kāmaśāstramidaṃ cāgryaṃ mokṣaśāstraṃ tathottamam ।।
caturāśramadharmāṇāmācārasthitisādhanam ।
proktametanmahābhāga vedavyāsena dhīmatā ।।
tathā tāta kṛtaṃ hyetad vyāsenodārakarmaṇā ।
yathā vyāptaṃ mahāśāstraṃ virodhairnābhibhūyate ।।
vyāsavākyajalaughena kutarkataruhāriṇā ।
vedaśailāvatīrṇena nīrajaskā mahī kṛtā ।।
kalaśabdamahāhaṃsaṃ mākhyānaparāmbujam ।
kathāvistīrṇasalilaṃ kārṣṇa vedamahāhradam ।।
tadidaṃ bhāratākhyānaṃ bahvirthaṃ śrutivistaram ।
tattvato jñātukāmo ahaṃ bhagavaṃstvāmupasthitaḥ ।।
kasmānmānuṣatāṃ prāpto nirguṇo api janārdanaḥ ।
vāsudevo jagatsūti-sthiti-saṃyamakāraṇam ।।
kasmācca pāṇḍuputtrāṇāmekā sā drupadātmajā ।
pañcānāṃ mahīṣī kṛṣṇā hyatra naḥ saṃśayo mahān ।।
bheṣajaṃ brahmahatyāyā baladevo mahābalaḥ ।

tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena kasmāccakre halāyudhaḥ ।।
kathañca draupadeyāste akṛtadārā mahārathāḥ ।
pāṇḍunāthā mahātmāno vadhamāpuranāthavat ।।
etatsarvaṃ vistaraśo mamākhyātumihārhasi ।
bhavanto mūḍhabuddhīnāmavabodhakarāḥ sadā ।।
iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā mārkaṇḍeyo māhamuniḥ ।
daśāṣṭadoṣarahito vaktuṃ samupacakrame ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

kriyākālo ayamasmākaṃ samaprāpto munisattama ।
vistare cāpi vaktavye naiṣa kālaḥ praśasyate ।।
ye tu vakṣyanti vakṣye adya tānahaṃ jaimine tava ।
tathā ca naṣṭasandehaṃ tvāṃ kariṣyanti pakṣiṇaḥ ।।
piṅgākṣaśca vibodhaśca suputtraḥ sumukhastathā ।

droṇaputrāḥ khagaśreṣṭhāstattvajñāḥ śāstracintakāḥ ।।
vedaśāstrārthavijñāne yeṣāmavyāhatā matiḥ ।
vindhyakandaramadhyasthāstānupāsya ca pṛccha ca ।।
evamuktastadā tena mārkaṇḍeyena dhīmatā ।
pratyuvācarṣiśārdūlo vismayotphullalocanaḥ ।।

jaiminiruvāca

atyadbhutamidaṃ brahman khagavāgiva mānuṣī ।
yat pakṣiṇaste vijñānamāpuratyantadurlabham ।।
tiryagyonyāṃ yadi bhavasteṣāṃ jñānaṃ kuto abhavat ।
kathañca droṇatanayāḥ procyante te patatriṇaḥ ।।
kaśca droṇaḥ pravikhyāto yasya putracatuṣṭayam ।
jātaṃ guṇavatāṃ teṣāṃ dharmajñānaṃ mahātmanām ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

śṛṇuṣvāvahito bhūtvā yadvṛttaṃ nandane purā ।
śakrasyāpyasarasāṃ caiva nāradasya ca saṅgame ।।
nārado nandane apaśyat puṃścalīgaṇamadhyagam ।
śakraṃ surādhirājānaṃ tanmukhāsaktalocanam ।।
sa tenarṣivariṣṭhena dṛṣṭamātraḥ śacīpatiḥ ।
samuttasthau svakaṃ cāsmai dadāvāsanamādarāt ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā balavṛtraghnamutthitaṃ tridaśāṅganāḥ ।
praṇemustāśca devarṣi vinayāvanatāḥ sthitāḥ ।।
tābhirabhyarcitaḥ so atha upaviṣṭe śatakratau ।
yathārhaṃ kṛtasambhāṣaḥ kathāścakre manoramāḥ ।।

śakra uvāca

tataḥ kathāntare śakrastamuvāca mahāmunim ।
dehyājñāṃ nṛtyatāmāsāṃ tava yābhimateti vai ।।
rambhā vā karkaśā vātha urvaśyatha tilottamā ।
ghṛtācī menakā vāpi yatra vā bhavato ruciḥ ।।
etacchrutvā dvijaśreṣṭho vaco śakrasya nāradaḥ ।
vicintyāpsarasaḥ prāha vinayāvanatāḥ sthitāḥ ।।
yuṣmākamiha sarvāsāṃ rūpaudāryaguṇādhikam ।
ātmānaṃ manyate yā tu sā nṛtyatu mamāgrataḥ ।।
guṇarūpavihīnāyāḥ siddhirnāṭyasya nāsti vai ।
cārvadhiṣṭhānavannṛtyaṃ nṛtyamanyadviḍambanam ।।
tadvākyasamakālaṃ ca ekaikāstā natāstataḥ ।
ahaṃ guṇādhikā na tvaṃ na tvaṃ cānyābravīdidam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tāsāṃ saṃbhramamālokya bhagavān pākaśāsanaḥ ।
pṛcchyatāṃ munirityāha vaktā yāṃ vo guṇādhikām ।।
śakracchandānuyātābhiḥ pṛṣṭastābhiḥ sanāradaḥ ।
provāca yat tadā vākyaṃ jaimine tannibodha me ।।
tapasyantaṃ nagendrasthaṃ yā vaḥ kṣobhayate balāt ।
durvāsasaṃ muniśreṣṭhaṃ tāṃ vo manye guṇādhikām ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sarvā vepatakandharāḥ ।
aśakyametadasmākamiti tāścakrire kathāḥ ।।
tatrāpsarā vapurnāma munikṣobhaṇagarvitā ।
pratyuvācādya yāsyāmi yatrāsau saṃsthito muniḥ ।।
adya taṃ dehayantāraṃ prayuktendriyavājinam ।
smaraśastragaladraśmiṃ kariṣyāmi kusārathim ।।
brahmā janārdano vāpi yadi vā nīlalohitaḥ ।
tamapyadya kariṣyāmi kāmabāṇakṣatāntaram ।।
ityuktvā prajagāmātha prāleyādriṃ vapustadā ।
munestapaḥ prabhāveṇa praśāntaśvāpadāśramam ।।
sa puṃskokilamādhuryā yatrāste sa mahāmuniḥ ।
krośamātraṃ sthitā tasmādagāyata varāpsarāḥ ।।
tadgītadhvanimākarṇya munirvismitamānasaḥ ।
jagāma tatra yatrāste sā bālā rucirānanā ।।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā cārusarvāṅgīṃ muniḥ saṃstabhya mānasam ।
kṣobhaṇāyāgatāṃ jñātvā kopāmarṣasanvitaḥ ।।
uvācedaṃ tato vākyaṃ maharṣistāṃ mahātapāḥ ।।
yasmādduḥ khārjitasyeha tapaso vidhnakāraṇāt ।
āgatāsi madonmatte mama duḥ khāya khecari ।।
tasmāt suparṇagotre tvaṃ matkrodhakaluṣīkṛtā ।
janma prāpsyasi duṣprajñe yāvadvarṣāṇi ṣoḍaśa ।।
nijarūpaṃ parityajya pakṣiṇīrūpadhāriṇī ।
catvāraste ca tanayā janiṣyante adhamāpsarāḥ ।।
aprāpya teṣu ca prītiṃ śastrapūtā punardivi ।
vāsamāpsyasi vaktavyaṃ nottaraṃ te kathañcana ।।
iti vacanamasahyaṃ kopasaṃraktadṛṣṭiś
calakalabalayāṃ tāṃ māninīṃ śrāvayitvā ।
taralatarataraṅgāṃ gāṃ parityajya vipraḥ
prathitaguṇagaṇaughāṃ saṃprayātāḥ khagaṅgām ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe vapuśāpo nāma prathamo adhyāyaḥ

dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ariṣṭanemiputro abhūd garuḍo nāma pakṣirāṭ ।
garuḍasyābhavat putraḥ sampātiriti viśrutaḥ ।।
tasyāpyāsīt sutaḥ śūraḥ supārśvo vāyuvikramaḥ ।
supārśvatanayaḥ kuntiḥ kuntiputraḥ pralolupaḥ ।।
tasyāpi tanayāvāstāṃ kaṅkaḥ kandhara eva ca ।।
kaṅkaḥ kailāsaśikhare vidyudrūpeti viśrutam ।
dadarśāmbujapatrākṣaṃ rākṣasaṃ dhanadānugam ।।
āpānāsaktamamalastragdāmāmbaradhāriṇam ।
bhāryāsahāyamāsīnaṃ śilāpaṭṭe amale śubhe ।।
taddṛṣṭamātraṃ kaṅkena rakṣaḥ krodhasamanvitam ।
provāca kasmādāyātastvamito hyaṇḍajādhama ।।
strīsannikarṣe tiṣṭhantaṃ kasmānmāmupasarpasi ।
naiṣa dharmaḥ subuddhīnāṃ mithoniṣpādyavastuṣu ।।

kaṅka uvāca

sādhāraṇo ayaṃ śailendro yathā tava tathā mama ।
anyeṣāṃ caiva jantūnāṃ mamatā bhavato atra kā ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

bruvāṇamitthaṃ khaḍgena kaṅkaṃ cincheda rākṣasaḥ ।
kṣaratkṣatajabībhatsaṃ visphurantamacetanam ।।
kaṅkaṃ vinihataṃ śrutvā kandharaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ ।
vidyudrūpavadhāyāśu manaścakre aṇḍajeśvaraḥ ।।
sa gatvā śailaśikharaṃ kaṅko yatra hataḥ sthitaḥ ।
tasya saṃkalanaṃ cakre bhrāturjyeṣṭhasya khecaraḥ ।
kopāmarṣavivṛtākṣo nāgendra iva niḥ śvasan ।।
jagāmātha sa yatrāste bhrātṛhā tasya rākṣasaḥ ।
pakṣavātena mahatā cālayan bhūdharān varān ।।
vegāt payodajālāni vikṣipan kṣatajekṣaṇaḥ ।
kṣaṇāt kṣayitaśatruḥ sa pakṣābhyāṃ krāntabhūdharaḥ ।।
pānāsaktamatiṃ tatra taṃ dadarśa niśācaram ।
ātāmravaktranayanaṃ hemaparyaṅkamāśritam ।।
stragdāmāpūritaśikhaṃ haricandanabhūṣitam ।
ketakīgarbhapatrābhairdantairghoratarānanam ।।
vāmorumāśritāṃ cāsya dadarśāyatalocanām ।
patnīṃ madanikāṃ nāma puṃskokilakalasvanām ।।
tato roṣaparītātmā kandharaḥ kandarasthitam ।
tamuvāca suduṣṭātmannehi yudhyasva vai mayā ।।
yasmājjeṣṭho mama bhrātā viśrabdho ghātatastvayā ।
tasmāttvāṃ madasaṃsaktaṃ nayiṣye yamasādanam ।।
viśvastaghātināṃ lokā ye ca strībālaghātinām ।
yāsyase nirayān sarvāṃstāṃstvamadya mayā hataḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityevaṃ patagendreṇa proktaṃ strīsannidhau tadā ।
rakṣaḥ krodhasamāviṣṭaṃ pratyabhāṣata pakṣiṇam ।।
yadi te nihato bhrātā pauruṣaṃ taddhi darśitam ।
tvāmapyadya haniṣye ahaṃ khaḍgenānena khecara ।।
tiṣṭha kṣaṇaṃ nātra jīvan patagādhama yāsyasi ।
ityuktvāñjanapuñjābhaṃ vimalaṃ khaḍgamādade ।।
tataḥ patagarājasya yakṣādhipabhaṭasya ca ।
babhūva yuddhamatulaṃ yathā garuḍa-śakrayoḥ ।।
tataḥ sa rākṣasaḥ krodhāt khaḍgamāvidhya vegavat ।
cikṣepa patagendrāya nirvāṇāṅgāravarcasam ।।
patagendraśca taṃ khaḍgaṅkiñcidutplutya bhūtalāt ।
vaktreṇa jagrāha tadā garuḍaḥ pannagaṃ yathā ।।
vaktrapādatalairbhaṅktvā cakre kṣobhamathātulam ।
tasmin bhagne tataḥ khaḍge bāhuyuddhamavartata ।।
tataḥ patagarājena vakṣasyākramya rākṣasaḥ ।
hasta-pāda-karairāśu śirasā ca viyojitaḥ ।।
tasmin vinihate sā strī khagaṃ śaraṇamabhyagāt ।
kiñcit saṃjātasaṃtrāsā prāha bhāryā bhavāmi te ।।
tāmādāya khagaśreṣṭhaḥ svakaṃ gṛhamagāt punaḥ ।
gatvā sa niṣkṛtiṃ bhrāturvidyudrupanipātanāt ।।
kandharasya ca sā veśma prāpyecchārūpadhāriṇī ।
menakātanayā subhrūḥ sauparṇaṃ rūpamādade ।।
tasyāṃ sa janayāmāsa tārkṣoṃ nāma sutāṃ tadā ।
muniśāpāgnivipluṣṭāṃ vapumapsarasāṃ varām ।
tasyā nāma tadā cakre tārkṣomiti vihaṅgamaḥ ।।
mandapālasutāścāsaṃścatvāro amitabuddhayaḥ ।
jaritāriprabhṛtayo droṇāntā dvijasattamāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ jaghanyo dharmātmā vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।
upayeme sa tāṃ tārkṣoṃ kandharānumate śubhām ।।
kasyacittvatha kālasya tārkṣo garbhamavāpa ha ।
saptapakṣāhite garbhe kurukṣetraṃ jagāma sā ।।
kuru-pāṇḍavayoryuddhe vartamāne sudāruṇe ।
bhāvitvāccaiva kāryasya raṇamadhye viveśa sā ।।
tatrāpaśyat tadā yuddhaṃ bhagadattakirīṭinoḥ ।
nirantaraṃ śarairāsīdākāśaṃ śalabhairiva ।।
pārthakodaṇḍanirmuktamāsannamativegavat ।
tasyā bhallamahiśyāmaṃ tvacaṃ ciccheda jāṭharīm ।।
bhinne koṣṭhe śasāṅkābhaṃ bhūmāvaṇḍacatuṣṭayam ।
āyuṣaḥ sāvaśeṣatvāt tūlarāśāvivāpatat ।।
tatpātasamakālaṃ ca supratīkādgajottamāt ।
papāta mahatī ghaṣṭā bāṇasaṃchinnabandhanā ।।
samaṃ samantāt prāptā tu nirbhinnadharaṇītalā ।
chādayantī khagāṇḍāni sthitāni piśitopari ।।
hate ca tasmin nṛpatau bhagadatte nareśvare ।
bahūnyahānyabhūdyuddhaṃ kurupāṇḍavasainyayoḥ ।।
vṛtte yuddhe dharmaputre gate śāntanavāntikam ।
bhīṣmasya gadato aśeṣān śrotuṃ dharmān mahātmanaḥ ।।
ghaṣṭāgatāni tiṣṭhanti yatrāṇḍāni dvijottama ।
ājagāma tamuddeśaṃ śamīko nāma saṃyamī ।।
sa tatra śabdamaśṛṇoccicīkucīti vāśatām ।
bālyādasphuṭavākyānāṃ vijñāne api pare sati ।।
atharṣiḥ śiṣyasahito ghaṣṭāmutpāṭya vismitaḥ ।
amātṛpitṛpakṣāṇi śiśukāni dadarśa ha ।।
tāni tatra tathā bhūmau śamīko bhagavān muniḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā sa vismayāviṣṭaḥ provācānugatān dvijān ।।
samyaguktaṃ dvijāgyreṇa śukreṇośanasā svayam ।
palāyanaparaṃ dṛṣṭvā daityasainyaṃ surārditam ।।
na gantavyaṃ nivartadhvaṃ kasmād vrajatha kātarāḥ ।
utsṛjya śauryayaśasī kva gatā na mariṣyatha ।।
naśyato yudhyato vāpi tāvadbhavati jīvitam ।
yāvaddhātāsṛjat pūrvaṃ na yāvanmanasepsitam ।।
eke mriyante svagṛhe palāyanto apare janāḥ ।
bhuñjanto annaṃ tathaivāpaḥ pibanto nidhanaṃ gatāḥ ।।
vilāsinastathaivānye kāmayānā nirāmayāḥ ।
avikṣatāṅgāḥ śastraiśca pretarājavaśaṅgatāḥ ।।
anye tapasyabhiratā nītāḥ pretanṛpānugaiḥ ।
yogābhyāse ratāścānye naiva prāpuramṛtyutām ।।
śambarāya purā kṣiptaṃ vajraṃ kuliśapāṇinā ।
hṛdaye abhihatastena tathāpi na mṛto asuraḥ ।।
tenaiva khalu vajreṇa tenainendreṇa dānavāḥ ।
prāpte kāle hatā daityāstatkṣaṇānnidhanaṃ gatāḥ ।।
viditvaivaṃ na santrāsaḥ kartavyo vinivartate ।
tato nivṛttāste daityāstyaktvā maraṇajaṃ bhayam ।।
iti śukravacaḥ satyaṃ kṛtamebhiḥ khagottamaiḥ ।
ye yuddhe api na samprāptāḥ pañcatvamatimānuṣe ।।
kvāṇāḍānāṃ patanaṃ viprāḥ kva ghaṇṭāpatanaṃ samam ।
kva ca māṃsa-vasā-raktairbhūmerāstaraṇakriyāḥ ।।
ke apyete sarvathā viprā naite sāmānyapakṣiṇaḥ ।
daivānukūlatā loke mahābhāgyapradarśinī ।।
evamuktvā sa tān vīkṣya punarvacanamabravīt ।
nivartatāśramaṃ yāta gṛhītvā pakṣibālakān ।।
mārjārākhubhayaṃ yatra naiṣāmaṇḍajajanmanām ।
śyenato nakulādvāpi sthāpyantāṃ tatra pakṣiṇaḥ ।।
dvijāḥ kiṃ vātiyatnena māryante karmabhiḥ svakaiḥ ।
rakṣyante cākhilā jīvā yathaite pakṣibālakāḥ ।।
tathāpi yatnaḥ kartavyo naraiḥ sarveṣu karmasu ।
kurvan puruṣakārantu vācyatāṃ yāti no satām ।।
iti munivaracoditāstataste
munitanayāḥ parigṛhya pakṣiṇastān ।
taruviṭapasamāśritālisaṅghaṃ
yayuratha tāpasaramyamāśramaṃ svam ।।
sa cāpi vanyaṃ manasābhikāmitaṃ
pragṛhya mūlaṃ kusumaṃ phalaṃ kuśān ।
cakāra cakrāyudha-rudra-vedhasāṃ
surendra-vaivasvataḥ jātavedasām ।।
apāmpatergoṣpativittarakṣiṇoḥ
samīraṇasyāpi tathā dvijottamāḥ ।
dhāturvidhātustvatha vaiśvadevikāḥ
śrutiprayuktā vivadhāstu satkriyāḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe caṭakotpattirnāma dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ

tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ahanyahani viprendra sa teṣāṃ munisattamaḥ ।
cakārāhārapayasā tathā guptyā ca poṣaṇam ।।
māsamātreṇa jagmuste bhānoḥ syandanavartmani ।
kautūhalavilolākṣairdṛṣṭā munikumārakaiḥ ।।
dṛṣṭvā mahīṃ sanagarāṃ sāmbhonidhisaridvarām ।
rathacakrapramāṇāṃ te punarāśramamāgatāḥ ।।
śramaklāntāntarātmāno mahātmāno viyonijāḥ ।
jñānañca prakaṭībhūtaṃ tatra teṣāṃ prabhāvataḥ ।।
ṛṣeḥ śiṣyānukampārthaṃ vadato dharmaniścayam ।
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ sarve caraṇāvabhyavādayan ।।
ūcuśca maraṇādghorānmokṣitāḥ smastvayā mune ।
āvāsa-bhakṣya-payasāṃ tvaṃ no dātā pitā guruḥ ।।
garbhasthānāṃ mṛtā mātā pitrā naivāpi pālitāḥ ।
tvayā no jīvitaṃ dattaṃ śiśavo yena rakṣitāḥ ।।
kṣitāvakṣatatejāstvaṃ kṛmīṇāmiva śuṣyatām ।
gajaghaṇṭāṃ samutpāṭya kṛtavān duḥ kharecanam ।।
kathaṃ vardheyurabalāḥ khasthān drakṣyāmyahaṃ kadā ।
kadā bhūmerdrumaṃ prāptān drakṣye vṛkṣāntaraṃ gatān ।।
kadā me sahajā kāntiḥ pāṃśunā nāśameṣyati ।
eṣāṃ pakṣānilotthena matsamīpavicāriṇām ।।
iti cintayatā tāta bhavatā pratipālitāḥ ।
te sāmprataṃ pravṛddhāḥ smaḥ prabuddhāḥ karavāma kim ।।
ityṛṣirvacanaṃ teṣāṃ śrutvā saṃskāravat sphuṭam ।
śiṣyaiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvaiḥ saha putreṇa śṛṅgiṇā ।।
kautūhalaparo bhūtvā romāñcapaṭasaṃvṛtaḥ ।
uvāca tattvato brūta pravṛtteḥ kāraṇaṃ giraḥ ।।
kasya śāpādiyaṃ prāptā bhavadbhirvikriyā parā ।
rūpasya vacasaścaiva tanme vaktumīhārhatha ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

vipulasvāniti khyātaḥ prāgāsīnmunisattamaḥ ।
tasya putradvayaṃ jajñe sukṛṣastumburustathā ।।
sukṛṣasya vayaṃ putrāścatvāraḥ saṃyatātmanaḥ ।
tasyarṣervinayācārabhaktinamrāḥ sadaiva hi ।।
tapaścaraṇasaktasya śāsyamānendriyasya ca ।
yathābhimatamasmābhistadā tasyopapāditam ।।
samitpuṣpādikaṃ sarvaṃ yaccaivābhyavahārikam ।
evaṃ tatrātha vasatāṃ tasyāsmākañca kānane ।।
ājagāma mahāvarṣmā bhagnapakṣo jarānvitaḥ ।
ātāmranetraḥ strastātmā pakṣī bhūtvā sureśvaraḥ ।।
satya-śauca-kṣamācāramatīvodāramānasam ।
jijñāsustamṛṣiśreṣṭhamasmacchāpabhavāya ca ।।

pakṣyuvāca
dvijendra māṃ kṣudhāviṣṭaṃ paritrātumihārhasi ।
bhakṣaṇārtho mahābhāga gatirbhava mamātulā ।।
vindhyasya śikhare tiṣṭhan patripatreritena vai ।
patito asmi mahābhāga śvasanenātiraṃhasā ।।
so ahaṃ mohasamāviṣṭo bhūmau saptāhamasmṛtiḥ ।
sthitastatrāṣṭamenāhnā cetanāṃ prāptavānaham ।।
prāptacetāḥ kṣudhāviṣṭo bhavantaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ ।
bhakṣyārtho vigatānando dūyamānena cetasā ।।
tat kuruṣvāmalamate mattrāṇāyācalāṃ matim ।
prayaccha bhakṣyaṃ viprarṣe prāṇayātrākṣamaṃ mama ।।
sa evamuktaḥ provāca tamindraṃ pakṣirūpiṇam ।
prāṇasandhāraṇārthāya dāsye bhakṣyaṃ tavepsitam ।।
ityuktvā punarapyenamapṛcchat sa dvijottamaḥ ।
āhāraḥ kastavārthāya upakalpyo bhavenmayā ।
sa cāha naramāṃsena tṛptirbhavati me parā ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

kaumāraṃ te vyatikrāntamatītaṃ yauvanañca te ।
vayasaḥ pariṇāmaste vartate nūnamaṇḍaja ।।
yasmin narāṇāṃ sarveṣāmaśeṣecchā nivartate ।
sa kasmād vṛddhabhāve api sunṛśaṃsātmako bhavān ।।
kva mānuṣasya piśitaṃ kva vayaścaramaṃ tava ।
sarvathā duṣṭabhāvānāṃ praśamo nopapadyate ।।
athavā kiṃ mayaitena proktenāsti prayojanam ।
pratiśrutya sadā deyamiti no bhāvitaṃ manaḥ ।।
ityuktvā taṃ sa viprendrastatheti kṛtaniścayaḥ ।
śīghramasmān samāhūya guṇato anupraśasya ca ।।
uvāca kṣubdhahṛdayo munirvākyaṃ suniṣṭhuram ।
vinayāvanatān sarvān bhaktiyuktān kṛtāñjalīn ।।
kṛtātmāno dvijaśreṣṭhā ṛṇairyuktā mayā saha ।
jātaṃ śreṣṭhamapatyaṃ vo yūyaṃ mama yathā dvijāḥ ।।
guruḥ pūjyo yadi mato bhavatāṃ paramaḥ pitā ।
tataḥ kuruta me vākyaṃ nirvyalīkena cetasā ।।
tadvākyasamakālañca proktamasmābhirādṛtaiḥ ।
yadvakṣyati bhavāṃstadvai kṛtamevāvadhāryatām ।।

ṛṣiruvāca
māmeṣa śaraṇaṃ prāpto vihagaḥ kṣuttṛṣānvitaḥ ।
yuṣmanmāṃsena yenāsya kṣaṇaṃ tṛptirbhaveta vai ।।
tṛṣṇākṣayañca raktena tathā śīghnaṃ vidhīyatām ।
tato vayaṃ pravyathitāḥ prakampodbhūtasādhvasāḥ ।
kaṣṭaṃ kaṣṭamiti procya naitat kurmeti cābruvan ।।
kathaṃ paraśarīrasya hetordehaṃ svakaṃ budhaḥ ।
vināśayed ghātayedvā yathā hyātmā tathā sutaḥ ।।
pitṛ-deva-manuṣyāṇāṃ yānyuktāni ṛṇāni vai ।
tānyapākurute putro na śarīrapradaḥ sutaḥ ।।
tasmānnaitat kariṣyāmo nī cīrṇaṃ yat purātanaiḥ ।
jīvan bhadrāṇyavāpnoti jīvan puṇyaṃ karoti ca ।।
mṛtasya dehanāśaśca dharmādyuparatistathā ।
ātmānaṃ sarvato rakṣyamāhurdharmavido janāḥ ।।
itthaṃ śrutvā vaco asmākaṃ muniḥ krodhādiva jvalan ।
provāca punarapyasmān nirdahanniva locanaiḥ ।।
pratijñātaṃ vaco mahyaṃ yasmānnaitat kariṣyatha ।
tasmānmacchāpanirdagdhāstiryagyonau prayāsyatha ।।
evamuktvā tadā so asmāstaṃ vihaṅgamathābravīt ।
antyeṣṭimātmanaḥ kṛtvā śāstrataścaurdhvadehikam ।।
bhakṣayasva suviśrabdhau māmatra dvijasattama ।
āhārīkṛtametat te mayā dehamihātmanaḥ ।।
etāvadeva viprasya brāhmaṇatvaṃ pracakṣyate ।
yāvat patagajātyagraya svasatyaparipālanam ।।
na yajñairdakṣiṇāvadbhistat puṇyaṃ prāpyate mahat ।
karmaṇānyena vā viprairyat satyaparipālanāt ।।
ityṛṣervacanaṃ śrutvā so antarvismayanirbharaḥ ।
pratyuvāca muniṃ śakraḥ pakṣirūpadharastadā ।।
yogamāsthāya viprendra tyajedaṃ svaṃ kalevaram ।
jīvajjantuṃ hi viprendra na bhakṣāmi kadācana ।।
tasmaitadvacanaṃ śrutvā yogayukto abhavanmuniḥ ।
taṃ tasya niścayaṃ jñātvā śakro apyāha svadehabhṛt ।।
bho bho viprendra budhyasva buddhyā bodhyaṃ budhātmaka ।
jijñāsārthaṃ mayāyaṃ te aparādhaḥ kṛto anagha ।।
tat kṣamasvāmalamate kā cecchā kriyatāṃ tava ।
pālanāt satyavākyasya prītirme paramā tvayi ।।
adyaprabhṛti te jñānamaindraṃ prādurbhaviṣyati ।
tapasyatha tathā dharme na te vighno bhaviṣyati ।।
ityuktvā tu gate śakre pitā kopasamanvitaḥ ।
praṇamya śirasāsmābhiridamukto mahāmuniḥ ।।
bibhyatāṃ maraṇāt tāta tvamasmākaṃ mahāmate ।
kṣantumarhasi dīnānāṃ jīvitapriyatā hi naḥ ।।
tvagasthimāṃsasaṅghāte pūyaśoṇitapūrite ।
kartavyā na ratiryatra tatrāsmākamiyaṃ ratiḥ ।।
śrūyatāṃ ca mahābhāga yathā loko vimuhyati ।
kāmakrodhādibhirdeṣairavaśaḥ prabalāribhiḥ ।।
prajñāprākārasaṃyuktamasthisthūṇaṃ paraṃ mahat ।
carmabhittimahārodhaṃ māṃsaśoṇitalepanam ।।
navadvāraṃ mahāyāmaṃ sarvataḥ snāyuveṣṭitam ।
nṛpaśca puruṣastatra cetanāvānavasthitaḥ ।।
mantriṇau tasya buddhiśca manaścaiva virodhinau ।
yatete vairanāśāya tāvubhāvitaretaram ।।
nṛpasya tasya catvāro nāśamicchanti vidviṣaḥ ।
kāmaḥ krodhastathā lobho mohaścānyastathā ripuḥ ।।
yadā tu sa nṛpastāni dvārāṇyāvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।
sadā susthabalaścaiva nirātaṅkaśca jāyate ।।
jātānurāgo bhavati śatrubhirnābhibhūyate ।।
yadā tu sarvadvārāṇi vivṛtāni sa muñcati ।
rāgo nāma tadā śatrurnetrādidvāramṛcchati ।।
sarvavyāpī mahāyāmaḥ pañcadvārapraveśanaḥ ।
tasyānumārgaṃ viśati tadvai ghoraṃ riputrayam ।।
praviśyātha sa vai tatra dvārairindriyasaṃjñakaiḥ ।
rāgaḥ śaṃśleṣamāyāti manasā ca sahetaraiḥ ।।
indriyāṇi manaścaiva vaśe kṛtvā durāsadaḥ ।
dvārāṇi ca vaśe kṛtvā prākāraṃ nāśayatyatha ।।
manastasyāśritaṃ dṛṣṭvā buddhirnaśyati tatkṣaṇāt ।
amātyarahitastatra pauravargojjhitastathā ।।
ripubhirlabdhavivaraḥ sa nṛpo nāśamṛcchati ।
evaṃ rāgastathā moho lobhaḥ krodhastathaiva ca ।।
pravartante durātmāno manuṣyasmṛtināśakāḥ ।
rāgāttu krodhaḥ prabhavati krodhāllobho abhijāyate ।।
lobhādbhavati saṃmohaḥ saṃmohāt smṛtivibhramaḥ ।
smṛtibhraṃśād buddhināśo buddhināśāt praṇaśyati ।।
evaṃ praṇaṣṭabuddhīnāṃ rāgalobhānuvartinām ।
jīvite ca salobhānāṃ prasādaṃ kuru sattama ।।
yo ayaṃ śāpo bhagavatā dattaḥ sa na bhavet tathā ।
na tāmasīṃ gatiṃ kaṣṭāṃ vrajema munisattama ।।
yanmayoktaṃ na tanmithyā bhaviṣyati kadācana ।
na me vāganṛtaṃ prāha yāvadadyeti putrakāḥ ।।
daivamatra paraṃ manye dhik pauruṣamanarthakam ।
akāryaṃ kārito yena balādahamacintitam ।।
yasmācca yuṣmābhirahaṃ praṇipatya prasāditaḥ ।
tasmāt tiryaktvamāpannāḥ paraṃ jñānamavāpsyatha ।।
jñānadarśitamārgāśca nirdhūtakleśakalmaṣāḥ ।
matprasādādasandigdhāḥ parāṃ siddhimavāpsyatha ।।
evaṃ śaptāḥ sma bhagavan pitrā daivavaśāt purā ।
tataḥ kālena mahatā yonyantaramupāgatāḥ ।।
jātāśca raṇamadhye vai bhavatā paripālitāḥ ।
vayamitthaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha khagatvaṃ samupāgatāḥ ।
nāstyasāviha saṃsāre yo na diṣṭena bādhyate ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā śamīko bhagavān muniḥ ।
pratyuvāca mahābhāgaḥ samīpasthāyino dvijān ।।
pūrvameva mayā proktaṃ bhavatāṃ sannidhāvidam ।
sāmānyapakṣiṇo naite ke apyete dvijasattamāḥ ।
ye yuddhe api na samprāptāḥ pañcatvamatimānuṣe ।।
tataḥ prītimatā tena te anujñātā mahātmanā ।
jagmuḥ śikhariṇāṃ śreṣṭaṃ vindhyaṃ drumalatāyutam ।।
yāvadadya sthitāstasminnacale dharmapakṣiṇaḥ ।
tapaḥ svādhyāyaniratāḥ samādhau kṛtaniścayāḥ ।।
iti munivaralabdhasatkriyāste
munitanayā vihagatvamabhyupetāḥ ।
girivaragahane atipuṇyatoye
yatamanaso nivasanti vindhyapṛṣṭhe ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe vindhyaprāptirnāma tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ

caturtho adhyāyaḥ

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evaṃ te droṇatanayāḥ pakṣiṇo jñānino abhavan ।
vasanti hyacale vindhye tānupāsva ca pṛccha ca ।।
ityṛṣervacanaṃ śrutvā mārkaṇḍeyasya jaiminiḥ ।
jagāma vindhyaśikharaṃ yatra te dharmapakṣiṇaḥ ।।
tannagāsannabhūtaśca śuśrāṭha paṭhatāṃ dhvanim ।
śrutvā ca vismayāviṣṭaścintayāmāsa jaiminiḥ ।।
sthānasauṣṭhavasampannaṃ jitaśvāsamaviśramam ।
vispaṣṭamapadoṣañca paṭhyate dvijasattamaiḥ ।।
viyonimapi samprāptānetān munikumārakān ।
citrametadahaṃ manye na jahāti sarasvatī ।।
bandhuvargastathā mitraṃ yacceṣṭamaparaṃ gṛhe ।
tyaktvā gacchati tatsarvaṃ na jahāti sarasvatī ।।
iti sañcintayanneva viveśa girikandaram ।
praviśya ca dadarśāsau śilāpaṭṭagātān dvijān ।।
paṭhatastān samālokya mukhadoṣavivarjitān ।
so atha śokena harṣeṇa sarvānevābhyabhāṣata ।।
svastyastu vo dvijaśreṣṭhā jaiminiṃ māṃ nibodhata ।
vyāsaśiṣyamanuprāptaṃ bhavatāṃ darśanotsukam ।।
manyurna khalu kartavyo yat pitrātīva manyunā ।
śaptāḥ khagatvamāpannāḥ sarvathā diṣṭameva tat ।।
sphītadravye kule kecijjātāḥ kila manasvinaḥ ।
dravyanāśe dvijendrāste śabareṇa susāntvitāḥ ।।
dattvā yācanti puruṣā hatvā vadhyanti cāpare ।
pātayitvā ca pātyante ta eva tapasaḥ kṣayāt ।।
etaddṛṣṭaṃ subahuśo viparītaṃ tathā mayā ।
bhāvābhāvasamucchedairajastraṃ vyākulaṃ jagat ।।
iti sañcintya manasā na śokaṃ kartumarhatha ।
jñānasya phalametāvacchokaharṣairadhṛṣyatā ।।
tataste jaiminiṃ sarve pādyārghyābhyāmapūjayan ।
anāmayañca papracchuḥ praṇipatya mahāmunim ।।
athocuḥ khagamāḥ sarve vyāsaśiṣyaṃ taponidhim ।
sukhopaviṣṭaṃ viśrāntaṃ pakṣānilahataklamam ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

adya naḥ saphalaṃ janma jīvitañca sujīvitam ।
yat paśyāmaḥ surairvandyaṃ tava pādāmbujadvayam ।।
pitṛkopāgnirudbhūto yo no deheṣu vartate ।
so adya śāntiṃ gato vipra yuṣmaddarśanavāriṇā ।।
kaccit te kuśalaṃ brahmannāśrame mṛgapakṣiṣu ।
vṛkṣeṣvatha latā-gulma-tvaksāra-tṛṇajātiṣu ।।
athavā naitaduktaṃ hi samyagasmābhirādṛtaiḥ ।
bhavatā saṅgamo yeṣāṃ teṣāmakuśalaṃ kutaḥ ।।
prasādañca kuruṣvātra brūhyāgamanakāraṇam ।
devānāmiva saṃsargo bhavato abhyudayo mahān ।
kenāsmadbhāgyaguruṇa ānīto dṛṣṭigocaram ।।

jaiminiruvāca

śrūyatāṃ dvijaśārdūlāḥ kāraṇaṃ yena kandaram ।
vindhyasyehāgato ramyaṃ revāvārikaṇokṣitam ।
sandehān bhārate śāstre tān praṣṭuṃ gatavānaham ।।
mārkaṇḍeyaṃ mahātmānaṃ pūrvaṃ bhṛgukulodvaham ।
tamahaṃ pṛṣṭavān prāpya sandehān bharataṃ prati ।।
sa ca pṛṣṭo mayā prāha santi vindhye mahācale ।
droṇaputrā mahātmānaste vakṣmantyarthavistaram ।।
tadvākyayoditaścemamāgato ahaṃ mahāgirim ।
tacchṛṇudhvamaśeṣeṇa śrutvā vyākhyātumarhatha ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

viṣaye sati vakṣyāmo nirviśaṅkaḥ śṛṇuṣva tat ।
kathaṃ tanna vadiṣyāmo yadasmadbuddhigocaram ।।
caturṣvapi hi vedeṣu dharmaśāstreṣu caiva hi ।
samasteṣu tathāṅgeṣu yaccānyadvedasaṃmitam ।।
eteṣu gocaro asmākaṃ buddherbrāhmaṇasattama ।
pratijñāntu samāroḍhuṃ tathāpi nahi śaknumaḥ ।।
tasmādvadasva viśrabdhaṃ sandigdhaṃ yadvi bhārate ।
vakṣyāmastava dharmajña na cenmoho bhaviṣyati ।।

jaiminiruvāca

sandigdhānīha vastūni bhārataṃ prati yāni me ।
śṛṇudhvamamalāstāni śrutvā vyākhyātumarhatha ।।
kasmānmānuṣatāṃ prāpto nirguṇo api janārdanaḥ ।
vāsudevo akhilādhāraḥ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।।
kasmācca pāṇḍuputrāṇāmekā sā drupadātmajā ।
pañcānāṃ mahiṣī kṛṣṇā sumāhanatra saṃśayaḥ ।।
bheṣajaṃ brahmahatyāyā baladevo mahābalaḥ ।
tīrthayātrāprasaṅgena kasmāccakre halāyudhaḥ ।।
kathaṃ ca draupadeyāste akṛtadārā mahārathāḥ ।
pāṇḍunāthā mahātmāno vadhamāpuranāthavat ।।
etat sarvaṃ kathyatāṃ me sandigdhaṃ bhārataṃ prati ।
kṛtārthohaṃ sukhaṃ yena gaccheyaṃ nijamāśramam ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

namaskṛtya sureśāya viṣṇave prabhaviṣṇave ।
puruṣāyāprameyāya śāśvatāyāvyayāya ca ।।
caturvyūhātmane tasmai triguṇāyāguṇāya ca ।
variṣṭhāya gariṣṭhāya vareṣyāyāmṛtāya ca ।।
yasmādaṇutaraṃ nāsti yasmānnāsti bṛhattaram ।
yena viśvamidaṃ vyāptamajena jagadādinā ।।
āvirbhāva-tirobhāva-dṛṣṭādṛṣṭa-vilakṣaṇam ।
vadanti yad sṛṣṭamidaṃ tathaivānte ca saṃhṛtam ।।
brahmaṇe cādidevāya namaskṛtya samādhinā ।
ṛksāmānyudgiran vaktrairyaḥ punāti jagattrayam ।।
praṇipatya tatheśānamekabāṇavinirjitaiḥ ।
yasyāsuragaṇairyajñā vilupyante na yajvinām ।।
pravakṣyāmo mataṃ kṛtsnaṃ vyāsasyādbhutakarmaṇaḥ ।
yena bhāratamuddiśya dharmādyāḥ prakaṭīkṛtāḥ ।।
āpo nārā iti proktā munibhistattvadarśibhiḥ ।
ayanaṃ tasya tāḥ pūrvaṃ tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
sa devo bhagavān sarvaṃ vyāpya nārāyaṇo vibhuḥ ।
caturdhā saṃsthito brahman saguṇo nirguṇastathā ।।
ekā mūrtiranirdeśyā śuklāṃ paśyanti tāṃ budhāḥ ।
jvālāmāloparuddhāṅgī niṣṭhā sā yogināṃ parā ।।
dūrasthā cāntikasthā ca vijñeyā sā guṇātigā ।
vāsudevābhidhānāsau nirmamatvena dṛśyate ।।
rūpavarṇādayastasyā na bhāvāḥ kalpanāmayāḥ ।
astyeva sā sadā śuddhā supratiṣṭhaikarūpiṇī ।।
dvitīyā pṛthivīṃ mūdrghnā śeṣākhyā dhārayatyadhaḥ ।
tāmasī sā samākhyātā tiryaktvaṃ samupāśritā ।।
tṛtīyā karma kurute prajāpālanatatparā ।
sattvodriktā tu sā jñeyā dharmasaṃsthānakāriṇī ।।
caturtho jalamadhyasthā śete pannagatalpagā ।
rajastasyā guṇaḥ sargaṃ sā karoti sadaiva hi ।।
yā tṛtīyā harermūrtiḥ prajāpālanatatparā ।
sā tu dharmavyavasthānaṃ karoti niyataṃ bhuvi ।।
proddhūtānasurān hanti dharmavicchittikāriṇaḥ ।
pāti devān sataścānyān dharmarakṣāparāyaṇān ।।
yadā yadā hi dharmasya glānirbhavati jaimine ।
abhyutthānamadharmasya tadātmānaṃ sṛjatyasau ।।
bhūtvā purā varāheṇa tuṇḍenāpo nirasya ca ।
ekayā daṃṣṭrayotkhātā nalinīva vasundharā ।।
kṛtvā nṛsiṃharūpañca hiraṇyakaśipurhataḥ ।
vipracittimukhāścānye dānavā vinipātitāḥ ।।
vāmanādīṃstathaivānyān na saṃkhyātumihotsahe ।
avatārāśca tasyeha māthuraḥ sāmprataṃ tvayam ।।
iti sā sāttvikī mūrtiravatārān karoti vai ।
pradyumneti ca sā khyātā rakṣākarmaṇyavasthitā ।।
devatve atha manuṣyatve tiryagyonau ca saṃsthitā ।
gṛhṇāti tatsvabhāvaṃ ca vāsudevecchayā sadā ।।
ityetat te samākhyātaṃ kṛtakṛtyo api yatprabhuḥ ।
mānuṣatvaṃ gato viṣṇuḥ śṛṇuṣvāsyottaraṃ punaḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe caturvyūhāvatāro nāma dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ

pañcamo adhyāyaḥ

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tvaṣṭṛputre hate pūrvaṃ brahmannindrasya tejasaḥ ।
brahmahatyābhibhūtasya parā hānirajāyata ।।
taddhamaṃ praviveśātha śākratejo apacārataḥ ।
nistejāścābhavacchakro dharme tejasi nirgate ।।
tataḥ putraṃ hataṃ śrutvā tvaṣṭā kruddhaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
avaluñcya jaṭāmekāmidaṃ vacanamabravīt ।।
adya paśyantu me vīryaṃ trayo lokāḥ sadevatāḥ ।
sa ca paśyatu durbuddhirbrahmahā pākaśāsanaḥ ।।
svakarmābhirato yena matsuto vinapātitaḥ ।
ityuktvā koparaktākṣo jaṭāmagnau juhāva tām ।।
tato vṛtraḥ samuttasthau jvālāmālī mahāsuraḥ ।
mahākāyo mahādaṃṣṭro bhinnāñjanacayaprabhaḥ ।।
indraśatrurameyātmā tvaṣṭṛtejopabṛṃhitaḥ ।
ahanyahani so avardhadiṣupātaṃ mahābalaḥ ।।
vadhāya cātmano dṛṣṭvā vṛtraṃ śakro mahāsuram ।
preṣayāmāsa saptarṣon sandhimicchan bhayāturaḥ ।।
sakhyañcakrustatastasya vṛtreṇa samayāṃstathā ।
ṛṣayaḥ prītamanasaḥ sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ ।।
samayasthitimullaṅghya yadā śakreṇa ghātitaḥ ।
vṛtro hatyābhibhūtasya tadā balamaśīryata ।।
tacchakradehavibhraṣṭaṃ balaṃ mārutamāviśat ।
sarvavyāpinamavyaktaṃ balasyaivādhidaivatam ।।
ahalyāñca yadā śakro gautamaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।
dharṣayāmāsa devendrastadā rūpamahīyata ।।
aṅgapratyaṅgalāvaṇyaṃ yadatīva manoram ।
vihāya duṣṭaṃ devendraṃ nāsatyāvagamat tataḥ ।।
dharmeṇa tejasā tyaktaṃ balahīnamarūpiṇam ।
jñātvā sureśaṃ daiteyāstajjaye cakrurudyamam ।।
rājñāmudriktavīryāṇāṃ devendraṃ vijigīṣavaḥ ।
kuleṣvatibalā daityā ajāyanta mahāmune ।।
kasyacittvatha kālasya dharaṇī bhārapīḍitā ।
jagāma meruśikharaṃ sado yatra divaukasām ।।
teṣāṃ sā kathayāmāsa bhūribhārāvapīḍitā ।
danujātmajadaityotthaṃ khedakāraṇamātmanaḥ ।।
ete bhavadbhirasurā nihatāḥ pṛthulaujasaḥ ।
te sarve mānuṣe loke jātā geheṣu bhūbhṛtām ।।
akṣauhiṇyo hi bahulāstadbhārārtā vrajāmyadhaḥ ।
tathā kurudhvaṃ tridaśā yathā śāntirbhavenmama ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tejobhāgaistato devā avaterurdivo mahīm ।
prajānāmupakārārthaṃ bhūbhāraharaṇāya ca ।।
yadindradehajaṃ tejastanmumoca svayaṃ vṛṣaḥ ।
kuntyā jāto mahātejāstato rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ।।
balaṃ mumoca pavanastato bhīmo vyajāyata ।
śakravīryārdhataścaiva jajñe pārtho dhanañjayaḥ ।।
utpannau yamajau mādrayāṃ śakrarūpau mahādyutī ।
pañcadhā bhagavānitthamavatīrṇaḥ śatakratuḥ ।।
tasyotpannā mahābhāgā patnī kṛṣṇā hutāśanāt ।।
śakrasyaikasya sā patnī kṛṣṇā nānyasya kasyacit ।
yogīśvarāḥ śarīrāṇi kurvanti bahulānyapi ।।
pañcānāmekapatnītvamityetat kathitaṃ tava ।
śrūyatāṃ baladevo api yathā yātaḥ sarasvatīm ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe indravikriyānāma pañcamo adhyāyaḥ

ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

rāmaḥ pārthe parāṃ prītiṃ jñātvā kṛṣṇasya lāṅgalī ।
cintayāmāsa bahudhā kiṃ kṛtaṃ sukṛtaṃ bhavet ।।
kṛṣṇena hi vinā nāhaṃ yāsye duryodhanāntikam ।
pāṇḍavān vā samāśritya kathaṃ duryodhanaṃ nṛpam ।।
jāmātaraṃ tathā śiṣyaṃ ghātayiṣye nareśvaram ।
tasmānna pārthaṃ yāsyāmi nāpi duryodhanaṃ nṛpam ।।
tīrtheṣvāplāvayiṣyāmi tāvadātmānamātmanā ।
kurūṇāṃ pāṇḍavānāṃ ca yāvadantāya kalpate ।।
ityāmantrya hṛṣīkeśaṃ pārtha-duryodhanāvapi ।
jagāma dvārakāṃ śauriḥ svasainyuparivāritaḥ ।।
gatvā dvāravatīṃ rāmo hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulām ।
śvo gantavyeṣu tīrtheṣu papau pānaṃ halāyudhaḥ ।।
pītapāno jagāmātha raivatodyānamṛddhimat ।
haste gṛhītvā samadāṃ revatīmapsaropamām ।।
strīkadambakamadhyastho yayau mattaḥ padā skhalan ।
dadarśaca vanaṃ vīro ramaṇīyamanuttamam ।।
sarvartuphalapuṣpāḍhyaṃ śākhāmṛgagaṇākulam ।
puṇyaṃ padmavanopetaṃ sapalvalamahāvanam ।।
sa śṛṇvan prītijananān bahūn madakalān śubhān ।
śrotraramyān sumadhurān śabdān khagamukheritān ।।
sarvartuphalabhārāḍhyān sarvartukusumojjvalān ।
apaśyat pādapāṃstatra vihagairanunāditān ।।
āmrānāmrātakān bhavyān nārikelān satindukān ।
āvilvakāṃstathā jīrān dāḍimān bījapūrakān ।।
panasān lakucān mocān nīpāṃścātimanoharān ।
pārāvatāṃśca kaṅkolān nalinānamlavetasān ।।
bhallātakānāmalakāṃstindukāṃśca mahāphalān ।
iṅgudān karamardāṃśca harītaka-vibhītakān ।।
etānanyāṃśca sa tarūn dadarśa yadunandanaḥ ।
tathaivāśoka-punnāga-ketakī-bakulānatha ।।
campakān saptaparṇāṃśca karṇikārān samālatīn ।
pārijātān kovidārān mandārān badarāṃstathā ।।
pāṭalān puṣpitān ramyān devadārudrumāṃstathā ।
sālāṃstālāṃstamālāṃśca kiṃśaukān vañjulān varān ।।
cakoraiḥ śātapatraiśca bhṛṅgarājaistathā śukaiḥ ।
kokilaiḥ kalaviṅkaiśca hārītairjovajīvakaiḥ ।।
priyaputraiścātakaiśca tathānyairvividhaiḥ khagaiḥ ।
śrotraramyaṃ sumadhuraṃ kūjadbhiścāpyadhiṣṭhitam ।।
sarāṃsi ca manojñāni prasannasalilāni ca ।
kumudaiḥ puṇḍarīkaiśca tathā nīlotpalaiḥ śubhaiḥ ।।
kahlāraiḥ kamalaiścāpi ācitāni samantataḥ ।
kādambaiścakravākaiśca tathaiva jalakukkuṭaiḥ ।।
kāraṇḍavaiḥ plavairhaṃsaiḥ kūrmairmadgubhireva ca ।
ebhiścānyaiśca kīrṇāni samantājjalacāribhiḥ ।।
krameṇetthaṃ vanaṃ śaurirvokṣamāṇo manoramam ।
jagāmānugataḥ strībhirlatāgṛhamanuttamam ।।
sa dadarśa dvijāṃstatra vedavedāṅgapāragān ।
kauśikān bhārgavāṃścaiva bhāradvājān sagautamān ।।
vividheṣu ca sambhūtān vaṃśeṣu dvijasattamān ।
kathāśravaṇabaddhotkānupaviṣṭān mahatsu ca ।।
kṛṣṇājinottarīyeṣu kuśeṣu ca vṛṣīṣu ca ।
sūtañca teṣāṃ madhyasthaṃ kathayānaṃ kathāḥ śubhāḥ ।।
paurāṇikīḥ surarṣoṇāmādyānāṃ caritāśrayāḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā rāmaṃ dvijāḥ sarve madhupānāruṇekṣaṇam ।।
matto ayamiti manvānāḥ samuttasthustvarānvitāḥ ।
pūjayanto haladharamṛte taṃ sūtavaṃśajam ।।
tataḥ krodhasamāviṣṭo halī sūtaṃ mahābalaḥ ।
nijaghāna vivṛttākṣaḥ kṣobhitāśeṣadānavaḥ ।।
adhyāsyāti padaṃ brāhmaṃ tasmin sūte nipātite ।
niṣkrāntāste dvijāḥ sarve vanāt kṛṣṇājināmbarāḥ ।।
avadhūtaṃ tathātmānaṃ manyamāno halāyudhaḥ ।
cintayāmāsa sumahanmayā pāpamidaṃ kṛtam ।।
brāhmaṃ sthānaṃ gato hyeṣa yad sūto vinipātitaḥ ।
tathā hīme dvijāḥ sarve māmavekṣya vinirgatāḥ ।।
śarīrasya ca me gandho lohasyevāsukhāvahaḥ ।
ātmānañcāvagacchāmi brahmaghnamiva kutsitam ।।
dhigamarṣaṃ tathā madyamatimānamabhīrutām ।
yairāviṣṭena sumahanmayā pāpamidaṃ kṛtam ।।
tatkṣayārthaṃ cariṣyāmi vrataṃ dvādaśavārṣikam ।
svakarmakhyāpanaṃ kurvaṃn prayaścittamanuttamam ।।
atha yeyaṃ samārabdhā tīrthayātrā mayādhunā ।
etāmeva prayāsyāmi pratilomāṃ sarasvatīm ।।
ato jagāma rāmo asau pratilomāṃ sarasvatīm ।
tataḥ paraṃ śṛṇuṣvemaṃ pāṇḍaveyakathāśrayam ।।

itiśrī mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe baladevabrahmahatyānāma ṣaṣṭhodhyāyaḥ

saptamo adhyāyaḥ

dharmapakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

hariścandreti rājarṣirāsīt tretāyuge purā ।
dharmātmā pṛthivīpālaḥ prollasatkīrtiruttamaḥ ।।
na durbhikṣaṃ na ca vyādhirnākālamaraṇaṃ nṛṇām ।
nādharmarucayaḥ paurāstasmin śāsati pārthive ।।
babhūvurna tathonmattā dhana-vīrya-tapomadaiḥ ।
nājāyanta striyaścaiva kāścidaprāptayauvanāḥ ।।
sa kadācinmahābāhuraraṇye anusaran mṛgam ।
śuśrāva śabdamasakṛt trāyasveti ca yoṣitām ।।
sa vihāya mṛgaṃ rājā mā bhaiṣīrityabhāṣata ।
mayi śāsati durmedhāḥ ko ayamanyāyavṛttimān ।।
tatkranditānusārī ca sarvārambhavighātakṛt ।
ekasminnantare raudro vighnarāṭ samacintayat ।।
viśvāmitro ayamatulaṃ tapa āsthāya vīryavān ।
prāgasiddhābhavādīnāṃ vidyāḥ sādhyati vratī ।।
sādhyamānāḥ kṣamāmaunacittasaṃyamināmunā ।
tā vai bhayārtāḥ krandanti kathaṃ kāryamidaṃ mayā ।।
tejasvī kauśikaśveṣṭho vayamasya sudurbalāḥ ।
krośantyetāstathā bhītā duṣpāraṃ pratibhāti me ।।
athavāyaṃ nṛpaḥ prāpto mā bhairiti vadan muhuḥ ।
imameva praviśyāśu sādhayiṣye yathepsitam ।।
iti saṃcintya raudreṇa vighnarājena vai tataḥ ।
tenāviṣṭo nṛpaḥ kopādidaṃ vacanamabravīt ।।
ko ayaṃ baghnāti vastrānte pāvakaṃ pāpakṛnnaraḥ ।
baloṣṇatejasā dīpte mayi patyāvupasthite ।।
so adya matkārmukākṣepa-vidīpitadigantaraiḥ ।
śarairvibhinnasarvāṅgo dīrghanidrāṃ pravekṣyati ।।
viśvāmitrastataḥ kruddhaḥ śrutvā tannṛpatervacaḥ ।
kruddhe carṣivare tasmin neśurvidyāḥ kṣaṇena tāḥ ।।
sa cāpi rājā taṃ dṛṣṭvā viśvāmitraṃ taponidhim ।
bhītaḥ prāvepatātyarthaṃ sahasāśvatthaparṇavat ।।
sa durātmanniti yadā munistiṣṭheti cābravīt ।
tataḥ sa rājā vinayāt praṇipatyābhyabhāṣata ।।
bhagavanneṣa dharmo me nāparādho mama prabho ।
na kroddhumarhasi mune nijadharmaratasya me ।।
dātavyaṃ rakṣitavyaṃ ca dharmajñena mahīkṣitā ।
cāpaṃ codyamya yoddhavyaṃ dharmaśāstrānusārataḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

dātavyaṃ kasya ke rakṣyāḥ kairyoddhavyaṃ ca te nṛpa ।
kṣiprametat samācakṣva yadyadharmabhayaṃ tava ।।

hariścandra uvāca

dātavyaṃ vipramukhyebhyo ye cānye kṛśavṛttayaḥ ।
rakṣyā bhītāḥ sadā yuddhaṃ kartavyaṃ paripanthibhiḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

yadi rājā bhavān samyagrājadharmamavekṣate ।
nirveṣṭukāmo vipro ahaṃ dīyatāmiṣṭadakṣiṇā ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

etadrājā vacaḥ śrutvā prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā ।
punarjātamivātmānaṃ mene prāha ca kauśikam ।।
ucyatāṃ bhagavan yatte dātavyamaviśaṅkitam ।
dattamityeva tadviddhi yadyapi syāt sudurlabham ।।
hiraṇyaṃ vā suvarṇaṃ vā putraḥ patnī kalevaram ।
prāṇā rājyaṃ puraṃ lakṣmīryadabhipretamātmanaḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

rājan pratigṛhīto ayaṃ yaste dattaḥ pratigrahaḥ ।
prayaccha prathamaṃ tāvad dakṣiṇāṃ rājasūyikīm ।।

rājovāca

brahmaṃstāmapi dāsyāmi dakṣiṇāṃ bhavato hyaham ।
vriyatāṃ dvijaśārdūla yastaveṣṭaḥ pratigrahaḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

sasāgarāṃ dharāmetāṃ sabhūbhṛdgrāmapattanām ।
rājyaṃ ca sakalaṃ vīra rathāśva-gajasaṅkulam ।।
koṣṭhāgāraṃ ca koṣaṃ ca yaccānyadvidyate tava ।
vinā bhāryāṃ ca putraṃ ca śarīraṃ ca tavānagha ।।
dharmaṃ ca sarvadharmajña yo yāntamanugacchati ।
bahunā vā kimuktena sarvametat pradīyatām ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

prahṛṣṭenaiva manasā so avikāramukho nṛpaḥ ।
tasyarṣervacanaṃ śrutvā tathetyāha kṛtāñjaliḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

sarvasvaṃ yadi me dattaṃ rājyamurvo balaṃ dhanam ।
prabhutvaṃ kasya rājarṣe rājyasthe tāpase mayi ।।

hariścandra uvāca

yasminnapi mayā kāle brāhman dattā vasundharā ।
tasminnapi bhavān svāmī kimutādya mahīpatiḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

yadi rājaṃstvayā dattā mama sarvā vasundharā ।
yatra me viṣaye svāmyaṃ tasmānniṣkrāntumarhasi ।।
śroṇīsūtrādisakalaṃ muktvā bhūṣaṇasaṃgraham ।
taruvalkalamābadhya saha patnyā sutena ca ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tatheti coktvā kṛtvā ca rājā gantuṃ pracakrame ।
svapatnyā śaivyayā sārdhaṃ bālakenātmajena ca ।।
vrajataḥ sa tato ruddhvā panthānaṃ prāha taṃ nṛpam ।
kva yāsyasītyadattvā me dakṣiṇāṃ rājasūyikīm ।।

hariścandra uvāca

bhagavan rājyametat te dattaṃ nihatakaṇṭakam ।
avaśiṣṭamidaṃ brahmannadya dehatrayaṃ mama ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

tathāpi khalu dātavyā tvayā me yajñadakṣiṇā ।
viśeṣato brāhmaṇānaṃ hantyadattaṃ pratiśrutam ।।
yāvat toṣo rājasūye brāhmaṇānāṃ tabhavennṛpa ।
tāvadeva tu dātavyā dakṣiṇā rājasūyikī ।।
pratiśrutya ca dātavyaṃ yoddhavyaṃ cātatāyibhiḥ ।
rakṣitavyāstathā cārtāstvayaiva prāk pratiśrutam ।।

hariścandra uvāca

bhagavan sāmprataṃ nāsti dāsye kālakrameṇa te ।
prasādaṃ kuru viprarṣe sadbhāvamanucintya ca ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

kimpramāṇo mayā kālaḥ pratīkṣyaste janādhipa ।
śīghramācakṣva śāpāgniranyathā tvāṃ pradhakṣyati ।।

haricandra uvāca

māsena tava viprarṣe pradāsye dakṣiṇādhanam ।
sāmprataṃ nāsti me vittamanujñāṃ dātumarhasi ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

gaccha gaccha nṛpaśreṣṭha svadharmamanupālaya ।
śivaśca te adhvā bhavatu mā santu paripanthinaḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

anujñātaśca gaccheti jagāma vasudhādhipaḥ ।
padbhyāmanucitā gantumanvagacchata taṃ priyā ।।
taṃ sabhāryaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭhaṃ niryāntaṃ sasutaṃ purāt ।
dṛṣṭvā pracukruśuḥ paurā rājñaścaivānuyāyinaḥ ।।
hānātha kiṃ jahāsyasmān nityārtiparipīḍitān ।
tvaṃ dharmatatparo rājan paurānugrahakṛt tathā ।।
nayāsmānapi rājarṣe yadi dharmamavekṣase ।
muhūrtaṃ tiṣṭha rājendra bhavato mukhapaṅkajam ।।
pibāmo netrabhramaraiḥ kadā drakṣyāmahe punaḥ ।
yasya prayātasya puro yānti pṛṣṭhe ca pārthivāḥ ।।
tasyānuyāti bhāryeyaṃ gṛhītvā bālakaṃ sutam ।
yasya bhṛtyāḥ prayātasya yāntayagre kuñjacarasthitāḥ ।।
sa eṣa padbhyāṃ rājendro hariścandro adya gacchati ।
hā rājan sukumāraṃ te subhru sutvacamunnasam ।।
pathi pāṃśuparikliṣṭaṃ mukhaṃ kīdṛgbhaviṣyati ।
tiṣṭha tiṣṭha nṛpaśreṣṭha svadharmamanupālaya ।।
ānṛśaṃsyaṃ paro dharmaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
kiṃ dāraiḥ kiṃ sutairnātha dhanairdhānyairathāpi vā ।।
sarvametat parityajya chāyābhūtā vayaṃ tava ।
hānātha hā mahārāja hā svāmin kiṃ jahāsi naḥ ।।
yatra tvaṃ tatra hi vayaṃ tat sukhaṃ yatra vai bhavān ।
nagaraṃ tadbhavān yatra sa svargo yatra no nṛpaḥ ।।
iti pauravacaḥ śrutvā rājā śokapariplutaḥ ।
atiṣṭhat sa tadā mārge teṣāmevānukampayā ।।
viśvāmitro api taṃ dṛṣṭvā pauravākyākulīkṛtam ।
roṣamarṣavivṛttākṣaḥ samāgamya vaco abravīt ।।
dhik tvāṃ duṣṭasamācāramanṛtaṃ jihmabhāṣaṇam ।
mama rājyaṃ ca datvā yaḥ punaḥ prākraṣṭumicchasi ।।
ityuktaḥ paruṣaṃ tena gacchāmīti savepathuḥ ।
bruvannevaṃ yayau śīghramākarṣan dayitāṃ kare ।।
karṣatastāṃ tato bhāryāṃ sukumārīṃ śramāturām ।
sahasā daṇḍakāṣṭhena tāḍayāmāsa kauśikaḥ ।।
tāṃ tathā tāḍitāṃ dṛṣṭvā hariścandro mahīpatiḥ ।
gacchāmītyāha duḥ khārto nānyat kiñcidudāharat ।।
atha viśve tadā devāḥ pañca prāhuḥ kṛpālavaḥ ।
viśvāmitraḥ supāpo ayaṃ lokān kān samavāpsyati ।।
yenāyāṃ yajvanāṃ śreṣṭhaḥ svarājyādavaropitaḥ ।
kasya vā śraddhayā pūtaṃ sutaṃ somaṃ mahādhvare ।
pītvā vayaṃ prayāsyāmo mudaṃ mantrapuraḥ saram ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

iti teṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā kauśiko atiruṣānvitaḥ ।
śaśāpa tān manuṣyatvaṃ sarve yūyamavāpsyatha ।।
prasāditaśca taiḥ prāha punareva mahāmuniḥ
mānuṣatve api bhavatāṃ bhavitrī naiva santatiḥ ।।
na dārasaṃgrahaścaiva bhavitā na ca matsaraḥ ।
kāmakrodhavinirmuktā bhaviṣyatha surāḥ punaḥ ।।
tato avateruraṃśaiḥ svairdevāste kuruveśmani ।
draupadīgarbhasambhūtāḥ pañca vai pāṇḍunandanāḥ ।।
etasmāt kāraṇāt pañca pāṇḍaveyā mahārathāḥ ।
na dārasaṃgrahaṃ prāptāḥ śāpāt tasya mahāmuneḥ ।।
etatte sarvamākhyātaṃ pāṇḍaveyakathāśrayam ।
praśnaṃ catuṣṭayaṃ gītaṃ kimanyacchrotumicchasi ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe draupadeyotpattirnāma saptamo adhyāyaḥ

aṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ

jaiminiruvāca

bhavadbhiridamākhyātaṃ yathāpraśnamanukramāt ।
mahat kautūhalaṃ me asti hariścandra kathāṃ prati ।।
aho mahātmanā tena prāptaṃ kṛcchramanuttamam ।
kaccit sukhamanuprāptaṃ tādṛgeva dvijottamāḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

viśvāmitravacaḥ śrutvā sa rājā prayayau śanaiḥ ।
śaivyayānugato duḥ khī bhāryayā balāputrayā ।।
sa gatvā vasudhāpālo divyāṃ vārāṇasīṃ purīm ।
naiṣā manuṣyabhogyeti śūlapāṇeḥ parigrahaḥ ।।
jagāma padbhyāṃ duḥ khārtaḥ saha patnyānukūlayā ।
purīpraveśe dadṛśe viśvāmitramupasthitam ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvā samanuprāptaṃ vinayāvanato abhavat ।
prāha caivāñjaliṃ kṛtvā hariścandro mahāmunim ।।
ime prāṇāḥ sutaścāyamiyaṃ patnī mune ! mama ।
yena te kṛtyamastyāśu tadgṛhāṇārghyamuttamam ।।
yadvānyat kāryamasmābhistadanujñātumarhasi ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

pūrṇaḥ sa māso rājarṣe dīyatāṃ mama dakṣiṇā ।
rājasūyanimittaṃ hi smaryate svavaco yadi ।।

hariścandra uvāca

brāhmannadyaiva sampūrṇo māso amlānatapodhana ।
tiṣṭhatyetad danārdhaṃ yattat pratīkṣasva māciram ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

evamastu mahārāja āgamiṣyāmyahaṃ punaḥ ।
śāpaṃ tava pradāsyāmi na cedadya pradāsyasi ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

ityuktvā prayayau vipro rājā cācintayat tadā ।
kathamasmai pradāsyāmi dakṣiṇā yā pratiśrutā ।।
kutaḥ puṣṭāni mitrāṇi kutor'thaḥ sāmprataṃ mama ।
pratigrahaḥ praduṣṭo me nāhaṃ yāyāmadhaḥ katham ।।
kimu prāṇān vimuñcāmi kāṃ diśaṃ yāmyakiñcanaḥ ।
yadi nāśaṃ gamiṣyāmi apradāya pratiśrutam ।।
brahmasvahṛtkṛmiḥ pāpo bhaviṣyāmyadhamādhamaḥ ।
athavā preṣyatāṃ yāsye varamevātmavikrayaḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

rājānaṃ vyākulaṃ dīnaṃ cintayānamadhomukham ।
pratyuvāca tadā patnī bāṣpagadgadayā girā ।।
tyaja cintāṃ mahārajā svasatyamanupālaya ।
śmaśānavad varjanīyo naraḥ satyabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।।
nātaḥ parataraṃ dharmaṃ vadanti puruṣasya tu ।
yādṛśaṃ puruṣavyāghra svasatyaparipālanam ।।
agnihotramadhītaṃ vā dānādyāścākhilāḥ kriyāḥ ।
bhajante tasya vaiphalyaṃ yasya vākyamakāraṇam ।।
satyamatyantamuditaṃ dharmaśāstreṣu dhīmatām ।
tāraṇāyānṛtaṃ tadvat pātanāyākṛtātmanām ।।
saptāśvamedhānāhṛtya rājasūyaṃ ca pārthivaḥ ।
kṛtirnāma cyutaḥ svargādasatyavacanāt sakṛt ।।
rājan jātamapatyaṃ me ityuktvā praruroda ha ।
bāṣpāmbuplutanetrāntāmuvācedaṃ mahīpatiḥ ।।

hariścandra uvāca

vimuñca bhadre santāpamayaṃ tiṣṭhati bālakaḥ ।
ucyatāṃ vaktukāmāsi yadvā tvaṃ gajagāmini ।।

patnyuvāca

rājan jātamapatyaṃ me satāṃ putraphalāḥ striyaḥ ।
sa māṃ pradāya vittena dehi viprāya dakṣiṇām ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

etadvākyamupaśrutya yayau mohaṃ mahīpatiḥ ।
pratilabhya ca saṃjñāṃ sa vilalāpātiduḥ khitaḥ ।।
mahadduḥ khamidaṃ bhadre yat tvamevaṃ bravīṣi mām ।
kiṃ tava smitasaṃlāpā mama pāpasya vismṛtāḥ ।।
hā hā kathaṃ tvayā śakyaṃ vaktumetat śucismite ।
durvācyametadvacanaṃ kartuṃ śaknomyahaṃ katham ।।
ityuktvā sa naraśreṣṭho dhigdhigityasakṛd bruvan ।
nipapāta mahīpṛṣṭhe mūrcchayābhipariplutaḥ ।।
śayānaṃ bhuvi taṃ dṛṣṭvā hariścandraṃ mahīpatim ।
uvācedaṃ sakaruṇaṃ rājapatnī suduḥ khitā ।।

patnyuvāca

hā mahārajā kasyedamapadhyānamupasthitam ।
yat tvaṃ nipatito bhūmau rāṅkavāstaraṇocitaḥ ।।
yena koṭyagragovittaṃ viprāṇāmapavarjitam ।
sa eṣa pṛthivīnātho bhūmau svapiti me patiḥ ।।
hā kaṣṭaṃ kiṃ tavānena kṛtaṃ deva ! mahīkṣitā ।
yadindropendratulyo ayaṃ nītaḥ prasvāpanīṃ daśām ।।
ityuktvā sāpi suśroṇī mūrcchitā nipapāta ha ।
bhartṛduḥ khamahābhāreṇāsahyena nipīḍitā ।।
tau tathā patitau bhūmāvanāthau pitarau śiśuḥ ।
dṛṣṭvātyantaṃ kṣudhāviṣṭaḥ prāha vākyaṃ suduḥ khitaḥ ।।
tāta tāta ! dadasvānnamambāmba ! bhojanaṃ dada ।
kṣunme balavatī jātā jihvāgraṃ śuṣyate tathā ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

etasminnantare prāpto viśvāmitro mahātapāḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā tu taṃ hariścandraṃ patitaṃ bhuvi mūrcchitam ।।
sa vāriṇā samabhyukṣya rājānamidamabravīt ।
uttiṣṭhotiṣṭha rājendra tāṃ dadasveṣṭadakṣiṇām ।।
ṛṇaṃ dhārayato duḥ khamahanyahani vardhante ।
āpyāyyamānaḥ sa tadā himaśītena vāriṇā ।।
avāpya cetanāṃ rājā viśvāmitramavekṣya ca ।
punarmohaṃ samāpede sa ca krodhaṃ yayau muniḥ ।।
sa samāśvāsya rājānaṃ vākyamāha dvijottamaḥ ।
dīyatāṃ dakṣiṇā sā me yadi dharmamavekṣase ।।
satyenārkaḥ pratapati satye tiṣṭhati medinī ।
satyaṃ coktaṃ paro dharmaḥ svargaḥ satye pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।।
aśvamedhasahasraṃ ca satyaṃ ca tulayā dhṛtam ।
aśvamedhasahasrāddhi satyameva viśiṣyate ।।
athavā kiṃ mamaitena sāmnā proktena kāraṇam ।
anārtye pāpasaṅkalpe krūre cānṛtavādini ।।
tvayi rājñi prabhavati sadbhāvaḥ śrūyatāmayam ।
adya me dakṣiṇāṃ rājan na dāsyati bhavān yadi ।।
astācalaṃ prayāter'ke śapsyāmi tvāṃ tato dhruvam ।
ityuktvā sa yayau vipro rājā cāsīdbhayāturaḥ ।।
kāndigbhūto adhamo niḥ svo nṛśaṃsadhaninārditaḥ ।
bhāryāsya bhūyaḥ prāhedaṃ kriyatāṃ vacanaṃ mama ।।
mā śāpānalanirdagdhaḥ pañcatvamupayāsyasi ।
sa tathā codyamānastu rājā patnyā punaḥ punaḥ ।।
prāha bhadre karomyeṣa vikrayaṃ tava nirghṛṇaḥ ।
nṛśaṃsairapi yad kartuṃ na śakyaṃ tat karomyaham ।
yadi me śakyate vāṇī vaktumīdṛk sudurvacaḥ ।
evamuktvā tato bhāryāṃ gatvā nāgaramāturaḥ ।
bāṣpāpihitakaṇṭhākṣastato vacanamabravīt ।।

rājovāca

bho bho nāgarikāḥ sarve śṛṇudhvaṃ vacanaṃ mama ।
kiṃ māṃ pṛcchatha kastvaṃ bho nṛśaṃso ahamamānuṣaḥ ।।
rākṣaso vātikaṭhinastataḥ pāpataro api vā ।
vikretuṃ dayitāṃ prāpto yo na prāṇāṃstyajāmyaham ।।
yadi vaḥ kasyacit kāryaṃ dāsyā prāṇeṣṭayā mama ।
sa brīvītu tvarāyukto yāvat sandhārayāmyaham ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

atha vṛddho dvijaḥ kaścidāgatyāha narādhipam ।
samarpayasva me dāsīmahaṃ kretā dhanapradaḥ ।।
asti me vittamastokaṃ sukumārī ca me priyā ।
gṛhakarma na śaknoti kartumasmāt prayaccha me ।।
karmaṇyatā-vayo-rūpa-śīlānāṃ tava yoṣitaḥ ।
anurūpamidaṃ vittaṃ gṛhāṇārpaya me abalām ।।
evamuktasya vipreṇa hariścandrasya bhūpateḥ ।
vyadīryata mano duḥ khānna cainaṃ kiñcidabravīt ।।
tataḥ sa vipro nṛpatervalkalānte dṛḍhaṃ dhanam ।
baddhvā keśeṣvathādāya nṛpapatnīmakarṣayat ।।
ruroda rohitāśvo api dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṭāṃ tu mātaram ।
hastena vastramākarṣan kākapakṣadharaḥ śiśuḥ ।।

rājapatnyuvāca

muñcārya muñca tāvanmāṃ yāvatpaśyāmyahaṃ śiśum ।
durlabhaṃ darśanaṃ tāta punarasya bhaviṣyati ।।
paśyaihi vatsa māmevaṃ mātaraṃ dāsyatāṃ gatām ।
māṃ mā sprārkṣo rājaputra ! aspṛśyāhaṃ tavādhunā ।।
tataḥ sa bālaḥ sahasā dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṭāṃ tu mātaram ।
samabhyadhāvadambeti rudan sāstrāvilekṣaṇaḥ ।।
tamāgataṃ dvijaḥ krodhādvālamabhyāhanat padā ।
vadaṃstathāpi so ambeti naivāmuñcata mātaram ।।

rājapatnyuvāca
prasādaṃ kuru meṃ nātha krīṇīṣvemaṃ ca bālakam ।
krītāpi nāhaṃ bhavato vinainaṃ kāryasādhikā ।।
itthaṃ mamālpabhāgyāyāḥ prasādasumukho bhava ।
māṃ saṃyojaya bālena vatseneva payasvinīm ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

gṛhyatāṃ vittametat te dīyatāṃ bālako mama ।
strīpuṃsordharmaśāstrajñaiḥ kṛtameva hi vetanam ।
śataṃ sahasraṃ lakṣaṃ ca koṭimūlyaṃ tathā paraiḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tathaiva tasya tadvittaṃ baddhvottarapaṭe tataḥ ।
pragṛhya bālakaṃ mātrā sahaikasthamabandhayat ।।
nīyamānau tu tau dṛṣṭvā bhāryā-putrau sa pārthivaḥ ।
vilalāpa suduḥ khārto niḥ śvasyoṣṇaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
yāṃ na vāyurna cādityo nendurna ca pṛthagjanaḥ ।
dṛṣṭavantaḥ purā patnīṃ seyaṃ dāsītvamāgatā ।।
sūryavaṃśaprasūto ayaṃ sukumārakarāṅguliḥ ।
samprāpto vikrayaṃ bālo dhiṅmāmastu sudurmatim ।।
hā priye ! hā śiśo ! natsa ! mamānāryasya durnayaiḥ ।
daivādhīnāṃ daśāṃ prāpto na mṛto asmi tathāpi dhik ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

evaṃ vilapato rājñaḥ sa vipro antaradhīyata ।
vṛkṣagehādibhistuṅgaistāvādāya tvarānvitaḥ ।।
viśvāmitrastataḥ prāpto nṛpaṃ vittamayācata ।
tasmai samarpayāmāsa hariścandro api taddhanam ।।
tadvittaṃ stokamālokya dāravikrayasambhavam ।
śokābhibhūtaṃ rājānaṃ kupitaḥ kauśiko abravīt ।।
kṣatrabandho ! mamemāṃ tvaṃ sadṛśīṃ yajñadakṣiṇām ।
manyase yadi tat kṣipraṃ paśya tvaṃ me balaṃ param ।।
tapaso atra sutaptasya brāhmaṇyasyāmalasya ca ।
matprabhāvasya cograsya śuddhasyādhyayanasya ca ।।
anyāṃ dāsyāmi bhagavan ! kālaḥ kaścitpratīkṣyatām ।
sāmprataṃ nāsti vikrītā patnī putraśca bālakaḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

caturbhāgaḥ sthito yo ayaṃ divasasya narādhipa ।
eṣa eva pratīkṣyo me vaktavyaṃ nottaraṃ tvayā ।।
pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tamevamuktvā rājendraṃ niṣṭhuraṃ nirghṛṇaṃ vacaḥ ।
tadādāya dhanaṃ tūrṇaṃ kupitaḥ kauśiko yayau ।।
viśvāmitre gate rājā bhayaśokābdhimadhyagaḥ ।
sarvākāraṃ viniścitya provācoccairadhomukhaḥ ।।
vittakrītena yo hyartho mayā preṣyeṇa mānavaḥ ।
sa bravītu tvarāyukto yāvat tapati bhāskaraḥ ।।
athājagāma tvarito dharmaścaṇḍālarūpadhṛk ।
durgandho vikṛto rūkṣaḥ śmaśrulo danturo ghṛṇī ।।
kṛṣṇo lambodaraḥ piṅgarūkṣākṣaḥ paruṣākṣaraḥ ।
gṛhītapakṣipuñjaśca śavamālyairalaṅkṛtaḥ ।।
kapālahasto dīrghāsyo bhairavo ativadan muhuḥ ।
śvagaṇābhivṛto ghoro yaṣṭihasto nirākṛtiḥ ।।

caṇḍāla uvāca

ahamartho tvayā śīghraṃ kathayasvātmavetanam ।
stokena bahunā vāpi yena vai labhyate bhavān ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

taṃ tādṛśamathālakṣya krūradṛṣṭiṃ suniṣṭhuram ।
vadantamatiduḥ śīlaṃ kastvamityāha pārthivaḥ ।।

caṇḍāla uvāca

caṇḍālo ahamihākhyātaḥ pravīreti purottame ।
vikhyāto vadhyavadhako mṛtakambalahārakaḥ ।।

hariścandra uvāca

nāhaṃ caṇḍāladāsatvamiccheyaṃ suvigarhitam ।
varaṃ sāpāgninā dagdho na caṇḍālavaśaṃ gataḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tasyaivaṃ vadataḥ prāpto viśvāmitrastaponidhiḥ ।
kopāmarṣavivṛtākṣaḥ prāha cedaṃ narādhaipam ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

caṇḍālo ayamanalpaṃ te dātuṃ vittamupasthitaḥ ।
kasmānna dīyate mahyamaśeṣā yajñadakṣiṇā ।।

hariścandra uvāca

bhagavan ! sūryavaṃśotthamātmānaṃ vedme kauśika ।
kathaṃ caṇḍāladāsatvaṃ gamiṣye vittakāmukaḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

yadi caṇḍālavittaṃ tvamātmavikrayajaṃ mama ।
na pradāsyasi kālena śāpsyāmi tvāmasaṃśayam ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

hariścandrastato rājā cintāvasthitajīvitaḥ ।
prasīdeti vadan pādāvṛṣerjagrāha vihvalaḥ ।।
dāso asmyārto asmi bhīto asmi tvadbhaktaśca viśeṣataḥ ।
kuru prasādaṃ viprarṣe kaṣṭaścaṇḍālasaṅkaraḥ ।।
bhaveyaṃ vittaśeṣeṇa sarvakarmakaro vaśaḥ ।
tavaiva muniśārdūla ! preṣyaścittānuvartakaḥ ।।

viśvāmitra uvāca

yadi preṣyo mama bhavān caṇḍālāya tato mayā ।
dāsabhāvamanuprāpto datto vittārbudena vai ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

ekamukte tadā tena śvapāko hṛṣṭamānasaḥ ।
viśvāmitrāya taddravyaṃ dattvā baddhvā nareśvaram ।।
daṇḍaprahārasambhrāntamatīva vyākulendriyam ।
iṣṭabandhuviyogārtamanayannijapattanam ।।
hariścandrastato rājā vasaṃścaṇḍālapattane ।
prātarmadhyāhnasamaye sāyañcaitadagāyata ।।
bālā dīnamukhī dṛṣṭvā bālaṃ dīnamukhaṃ puraḥ ।
māṃ smaratyasukhāviṣṭā mocayiṣyati nau nṛpaḥ ।।
upāttavitto viprāya dattvā vittamato adhikam ।
na sā māṃ mṛgaśāvākṣī vetti pāpataraṃ kṛtam ।।
rājyanāśaḥ suhṛttyāgo bharyātanayavikrayaḥ ।
prāptā caṇḍālatā ceyamaho duḥ khaparamparā ।।
evaṃ sa nivasan nityaṃ sasmāra dayitaṃ sutam ।
āryāñcātmasamāviṣṭāṃ hṛtasarvasva āturaḥ ।।
kasyacittvatha kālasya mṛtacelāpahārakaḥ ।
hariścandro abhavadrājā śmaśāne tadvaśānugaḥ ।।
caṇḍālenānuśiṣṭaśva mṛtacelāpahāriṇā ।
śavāgamanamanvicchanniha tiṣṭha divāniśam ।।
idaṃ rājñe api deyañca ṣaḍbhāgantu śavaṃ prati ।
trayastu mama bhāgāḥ syurdvo bhāgau tava vetanam ।।
iti pratisamādiṣṭo jagāma śavamandiram ।
diśantu dakṣiṇāṃ yatra vārāṇasyāṃ sthitaṃ tadā ।।
śmaśānaṃ ghorasaṃnādaṃ śivāśatasamākulam ।
śavamaulisamākīrṇaṃ durgandhaṃ bahudhūmakam ।।
piśāca-bhūta-vetāla-ḍākinī-yakṣasaṅkulam ।
gṛdhragomāyusaṅkīrṇaṃ śvavṛndaparivāritam ।।
asthisaṃghātasaṅkīrṇaṃ mahādurgandhasaṃkulam ।
nānāmṛtasuhṛnnāda-raudrakolāhalāyutam ।।
hā putra ! mitra ! hā bandho ! bhrātarvatsa ! priyādya me ।
hā pate ! bhagini ! mātarhā mātula ! pitāmaha ।।
mātāmaha ! pitaḥ ! kva gato asyehi bāndhava ।
ityevaṃ vadatāṃ yatra dhvaniḥ saṃśruyate mahān ।।
jvalanmāṃsa-vasā-medacchamacchamitasaṃkulam ।।
ardhadagdhāḥ śavāḥ śyāmā vikasaddantapaṅktayaḥ ।
hasantīvāgnimadhyasthāḥ kāyasyeyaṃ daśā tviti ।।
agneścaṭacaṭāśabdo vayasāmasthipaṅktiṣu ।
bāndhavākrāndaśabdaśca pukkaseṣu praharṣajaḥ ।।
gāyatāṃ bhūta-vetāla-piśācagaṇaḥ rakṣasām ।
śrūyate sumahān ghoraḥ kalpānta iva niḥ svanaḥ ।।
mahāmahiṣakārīṣa-gośakṛdrāśisaṅkulam ।
tadutthabhasmakūṭaiśca vṛtaṃ sāsthibhirunnataiḥ ।।
nānopahārastragdīpa-kākavikṣepakālikam ।
anekaśabdabahulaṃ śmaśānaṃ narakāyate ।।
savahnigarbhairaśivaiḥ śivārutair
nināditaṃ bhīṣaṇarāvagahvaram ।
bhayaṃ bhayasyāpyupasañjanairbhṛśaṃ
śmaśānamākrandavirāvadāruṇam ।।
sa rājā tatra samprāpto duḥ khitaḥ śocanodyataḥ ।
hā bhṛtyā mantriṇo viprāḥ tadrājyaṃ vidhe gatam ।।
hā śaivye putra hā bāla māṃ tyaktvā mandabhāgyakam ।
viśvāmitrasya doṣeṇa gatāḥ kutrāpi te mama ।।
ityevaṃ cintayaṃstatra caṇḍāloktaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
malino rūkṣasarvāṅgaḥ keśavān gandhavān dhvajī ।।
lakuṭī kālakalpaśca dhāvaṃścāpi tatastataḥ ।
asmin śava idaṃ mūlyaṃ prāptaṃ prāpsyāmi cāpyuta ।।
idaṃ mama idaṃ rājñe mukhyacaṇḍālake tvidam ।
iti dhāvan diśo rājā jīvan yonyantaraṃ gataḥ ।।
jīrṇakarpaṇṭasugranthi-kṛtakanthāparigrahaḥ
citābhasmarajolipta-mukhabāhūdarāṅighrakaḥ ।।
nānāmedo-vasā-majjā liptapāṇyaṅguliḥ śvasan ।
nānāśavodanakṛtā-hāratṛptiparāyaṇaḥ ।।
tadīyamālyasaṃśleṣakṛtamastakamaṇḍanaḥ ।
na rātrau na divā śete hā heti pravadan muhuḥ ।।
evaṃ dvādaśamāsāstu nītāḥ śatasamopamāḥ ।
sa kadācinnṛpaśreṣṭhaḥ śrānto bandhuviyogavān ।।
nidrābhibhūto rūkṣāṅgo niśceṣṭaḥ supta eva ca ।
tatrāpi śayanīye sa dṛṣṭavānadbhutaṃ hamat ।।
śmaśānābhyāsayogena daivasya balavattayā ।
anyadehena dattvā tu gurave gurudakṣiṇām ।।
tadā dvādaśa varṣāṇi duḥ khadānāttu niṣkṛtiḥ ।
ātmānaṃ sa dadarśātha pukkasīgarbhasambhavam ।।
tatrasthaścāpyasau rājā so acintayadidaṃ tadā ।
ito niṣkrāntamātro hi dānadharmaṃ karomyaham ।।
anantaraṃ sa jātastu tadā pukkasabālakaḥ ।
śmaśānamṛtasaṃskāra-karaṇeṣu sadodyataḥ ।।
prāpte tu saptame varṣe śmaśāne atha mṛto dvijaḥ ।
ānīto bandhubhirdṛṣṭastena tatrādhano guṇī ।।
mūlyārthinā tu tenāpi paribhūtāstu brāhmaṇāḥ ।
ūcuste brāhmaṇāstatra viśvāmitrasya ceṣṭitam ।।
pāpiṣṭhamaśubhaṃ karma kuru tvaṃ pāpakāraka ।
hariścandraḥ purā rājā viśvāmitreṇa pukkasaḥ ।।
kṛtaḥ puṇyavināśena brāhmaṇasvāpanāśanāt ।
yadā na kṣamate teṣāṃ taiḥ sa śapto ruṣā tadā ।।
gaccha tvaṃ narakaṃ ghoramadhunaiva narādhama ।
ityuktamātre vacane svapnasthaḥ sa nṛpastadā ।।
apaśyadyamadūtān vai pāśahastān bhayāvahān ।
taiḥ saṃgṛhītamātmānaṃ nīyamānaṃ tadā balāt ।।
paśyati sma bhṛśaṃ khinno hā mātaḥ pitaradya me ।
evaṃvādī sa narake tailadroṇyāṃ nipātitaḥ ।।
krakacaiḥ pāṭyamānastu kṣuradhārābhirapyadhaḥ ।
andhe tamasi duḥ khārtaḥ pūyaśoṇitabhojanaḥ ।।
saptavarṣaṃ mṛtātmānaṃ pukkasatve dadarśa ha ।
dinaṃ dinantu narake dahyate pacyate anyataḥ ।।
khidyate kṣobhyate anyatra māryate pāṭyate anyataḥ ।
kṣāryate dīpyate anyatra śītavātāhato anyataḥ ।।
evaṃ dinaṃ varṣaśata-pramāṇaṃ narake abhavat ।
tathā varṣaśataṃ tatra śrīvitaṃ narake bhaṭaiḥ ।।
tato nipātito bhūmau viṣṭhāśī śvā vyajāyata ।
vāntāśī śītadagdhaśca māsamātre mṛto api saḥ ।।
athāpaśyat kharaṃ dehaṃ hastinaṃ vānaraṃ paśum ।
chāgaṃ viḍālaṃ kaṅkañca gāmaviṃ pakṣiṇaṃ kṛmim ।।
matsyaṃ kūrmaṃ varāhañca śvāvidhaṃ kukkuṭaṃ śukam ।
śārikāṃ sthāvarāṃścaiva sarpamanyāṃśva dehinaḥ ।।
divase divase janma prāṇinaḥ prāṇinastadā ।
apaśyad duḥ khasantapto dinaṃ varṣaśataṃ tathā ।।
evaṃ varṣaśataṃ pūrṇaṃ gataṃ tatra kuyoniṣu ।
apaśyacca kadācit sa rājā tat svakulodbhavam ।।
tatra sthitasya tasyāpi rājyaṃ dyūtena hāritam ।
bhāryā hṛtā ca putraśca sa caikākī vanaṃ gataḥ ।।
tatrāpaśyata sa siṃhaṃ vai vyāditāsyaṃ bhayāvaham ।
bibhakṣayiṣumāyātaṃ śarabheṇa samanvitam ।।
punaśca bhakṣitaḥ so api bhāryāṃ śocitumudyataḥ ।
hā śaivye ! kva gatāsyadya māmihāpāsya duḥ khitam ।।
apaśyat punarevāpi bhāryāṃ svaṃ sahaputrakām ।
trāyasva tvaṃ hariścandra kiṃ dyūtena tava prabho ।।
putraste śocyatāṃ prāpto bharyaṃyā śaivyayā saha ।
sa nāpaśyat punarapi dhāvamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
athāpaśyat punarapi svargasthaḥ sa narādhipaḥ ।
nīyate muktakeśī sā dīnā vivasanā balāt ।।
hāhāvākyaṃ pramuñcantī trāyasvetyasakṛtsvanā ।
athāpaśyat punastatra dharmarājasya śāsanāt ।।
ākrāndantyantarīkṣasthā āgaccheha narādhipa ।
viśvāmitreṇa vijñapto yamo rājaṃstavārthataḥ ।।
ityuktvā sarpapāśaistu nīyate balavadvibhuḥ ।
śrāddhadevena kathitaṃ viśvāmitrasya ceṣṭitam ।।
tatrāpi tasya vikṛtirnādharmotthā vyavardhata ।
etāḥ sarvā daśāstasya yāḥ svapne sampradarśitāḥ ।।
sarvāstāstena sambhuktā yāvadvarṣāṇi dvādaśa ।
atīte dvādaśe varṣa nīyamāno bhaṭairbalāt ।।
yamaṃ so apaśyadākārāduvāca ca narādhipam ।
viśvāmitrasya kopo ayaṃ durnivāryo mahātmanaḥ ।।
putrasya te mṛtyumapi pradāsyati sa kauśikaḥ ।
gaccha tvaṃ mānuṣaṃ lokaṃ duḥ khaśeṣañca bhuṅkṣva vai ।
gatasya tatra rājendra śreyastava bhaviṣyati ।।
vyatīte dvādaśe varṣe duḥ khasyānte narādhipaḥ ।
antarīkṣācca patito yamadūtaiḥ praṇoditaḥ ।।
patito yamalokācca vibuddho bhayasambhramāt ।
aho kaṣṭamiti dhyātvā kṣate kṣārāvasevanam ।।
svapne duḥ khaṃ mahaddṛṣṭaṃ yasyānto nopalabhyate ।
svapne dṛṣṭaṃ mayā yattu kiṃ nu me dvādaśāḥ samāḥ ।।
gatetyapṛcchat tatrasthān pukkasāṃstu sa sambhramāt ।
netyucuḥ kecit tatrasthā evamevāpare abruvan ।।
śrutvā duḥ khī tadā rājā devān śaraṇamīyivān ।
svasti kurvantu me devāḥ śaivyāyā bālakasya ca ।।
namo dharmāya mahate namaḥ kṛṣṇāya vedhase ।
parāvarāya śuddhāya purāṇāyāvyayāya ca ।।
namo bṛhaspate tubhyaṃ namaste vāsavāya ca ।
evamuktvā sa rājā tu yuktaḥ pukkasakarmaṇi ।।
śavānāṃ mūlyakaraṇe punarnaṣṭasmṛtiryathā ।
malino jaṭilaḥ kṛṣṇo lakuṭī vihvalo nṛpaḥ ।।
naiva putro na bhāryā tu tasya vai smṛtigocare ।
naṣṭotsāho rājyanāśāt śmaśāne nivasaṃstadā ।।
athājagāma svasutaṃ mṛtamādāya lāpinī ।
bhāryā tasya narendrasya sarpadaṣṭaṃ hi bālakam ।।
hā vatsa ! hā putra ! śiśo ! ityevaṃ vadatī muhuḥ ।
kṛśā vivarṇā vimanāḥ pāṃśudhvastaśiroruhā ।।

rājapatnyuvāca

hā rājannadya bālaṃ tvaṃ paśya somaṃ mahītale ।
ramamāṇaṃ purā dṛṣṭaṃ duṣṭāhinā mṛtam ।।
tasyā vilāpaśabdaṃ tamākarṇya sa narādhipaḥ ।
jagāma tvarito atreti bhavitā mṛtakambalaḥ ।।
sa tāṃ rorudatīṃ bhāryāṃ nābhyajānāttu pārthivaḥ ।
cirapravāsasantaptāṃ punarjātāmivābalām ।।
sāpi taṃ cārukeśāntaṃ purā dṛṣṭvā jaṭālakam ।
nābhyajānānnṛpasutā śuṣkavṛkṣopamaṃ nṛpam ।।
so api kṛṣṇapaṭe bālaṃ dṛṣṭvāśīviṣapīḍitam ।
narendralakṣaṇopetaṃ cintāmāpa nareśvaraḥ ।।
aho kaṣṭaṃ narendrasya kasyāpyeṣa kule śiśuḥ ।
jāto nītaḥ kṛtāntena kāmapyāśāṃ durātmanā ।।
evaṃ dṛṣṭvā hi me bālaṃ māturutsaṅgaśāyinam ।
smṛtimabhyāgato bālo rohitāśvo abjalocanaḥ ।।
so apyetāmeva me vatso vayo avasthāmupāgataḥ ।
nīto yadi na ghoreṇa kṛtāntenātmano vaśam ।।

rājapatnyuvāca

hā vatsa ! kasya pāpasya apadhyānādidaṃ mahat ।
duḥ khamāpatitaṃ ghoraṃ yasyānto nopalabhyate ।।
hā nātha ! rājan ! bhavatā māmanāśvāsya duḥ khitām ।
kvāpi santiṣṭhatā sthāne viśrabdhaṃ sthīyate katham ।।
rājyanāśaḥ suhṛttyāgo bhāryātanayavikrayaḥ ।
hariścandrasya rājarṣeḥ kiṃ vidhe ! na kṛtaṃ tvayā ।।
iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā rājā svasthānataścyutaḥ ।
pratyabhijñāya dayitāṃ putrañca nidhanaṃ gatam ।।
kaṣṭaṃ śaivyeyameṣā hi sa bālo ayamitīrayan ।
ruroda duḥ khasantapto mūrcchāmabhijagāma ca ।।
sā ca taṃ pratyabhijñāya tāmavasthāmupāgatam ।
mūrcchitā nipapātārtā niśceṣṭā dharaṇītale ।।
cetaḥ samprāpya rājendro rājapatnī ca tai samam ।
vilepatuḥ susantaptau śokabhārāvapīḍitau ।।

rājovāca

hā vatsa ! sukumāraṃ te svakṣibhrūnāsikālakam ।
paśyato me mukhaṃ dīnaṃ hṛdayaṃ kiṃ na dīryate ।।
tāta ! tāteti madhuraṃ bruvāṇaṃ svayamāgatam ।
upaguhya vadiṣye kaṃ vatsa ! vatseti sauhṛdāt ।।
kasya jānupraṇītena piṅgena kṣitireṇunā ।
mamottarīyamutsaṅgaṃ tathāṅgaṃ malameṣyati ।।
aṅgapratyaṅgasambhūto manohṛdayanandanaḥ ।
mayā kupitrā hā vatsa ! vikrīto yena vastuvat ।।
hṛtvā rājyamaśeṣaṃ me sasādhanadhanaṃ mahat ।
daivāhinā nṛśaṃsena daṣṭo me tanayastataḥ ।।
ahaṃ daivāhidaṣṭasya putrasyānanapaṅkajam ।
nirīkṣannapi ghoreṇa viṣeṇāndhīkṛto adhunā ।।
ekamukttavā tamādāya bālakaṃ bāṣpagadgadaḥ ।
pariṣvajya ca niśceṣṭo mūrcchayā nipapāta ha ।।

rājapatnyuvāca

ayaṃ sa puruṣavyāghraḥ svareṇaivopalakṣyate ।
vidvajjanamanaścandro hariścandro na saṃśayaḥ ।।
tathāsya nāsikā tuṅgā agrato adhomukhaṃ gatā ।
dantāśca mukulaprakhyāḥ khyātakīrtermahātmanaḥ ।।
śmaśānamāgataḥ kasmādadyaiṣa sa nareśvaraḥ ।
apahāya putraśokaṃ sāpaśyat patitaṃ patim ।।
prakṛṣṭā vismitā dīnā bhartṛputrādhipīḍitā ।
vīkṣantī sā tato apaśyad bhartṛdaṇḍaṃ jugupsitam ।।
śvapākārhamato mohaṃ jagāmāyatalocanā ।
prāpya cetaśca śanakaiḥ sagadgadamabhāṣata ।।
dhik tvāṃ daivātikaruṇāṃ nirmaryādaṃ jugupsitam ।
yenāyamamaraprakhyo nīto rājā śvapākatām ।।
rājyanāśaṃ suhṛttyāgaṃ bhāryā-tanayavikrayam ।
prāpayitvāpi no kuktaścaṇḍālo ayaṃ kṛto nṛpaḥ ।।
hā rājan ! jātasantāpāmitthaṃ māṃ dharaṇītalāt ।
utthāpya nādya paryaṅkamāroheti kimucyate ।।
nādya paśyāmi te chatraṃ bhṛṅgāramathavā punaḥ ।
cāmaraṃ vyajanañcāpi ko ayaṃ vidhiviparyayaḥ ।।
yasyāgre vrajataḥ pūrvaṃ rājāno bhṛtyatāṃ gatāḥ ।
svottarīyairakurvanta nīrajaskaṃ mahītalam ।।
so ayaṃ kapālasaṃlagna-ghaṭīghaṭanirantare ।
mṛtanirmālyasūtrāntargūgkeśe sudāruṇe ।।
vasānisyandasaṃśuṣka-mahīpuṭakamaṇḍite ।
bhasmāṅgārārdhadagdhāsthi-majjāsaṅghaṭṭabhīṣaṇe ।।
gṛdhra-gomāyunādārtanaṣṭakṣudravihaṅgame ।
citādhūmātatirucā nīlīkṛtadigantare ।।
kuṇapāsvādanamudā samprahṛṣṭaniśācare ।
caratyamedhye rājendraḥ śmaśāne duḥ khapīḍitaḥ ।।
evamuktvā samāśliṣya kaṇṭhaṃ rājño nṛpātmajā ।
kaṣṭaśokaśatādhārā vilalāpārtayā girā ।।

rājapatnyuvāca

rājan ! svapno atha tathyaṃ vā yadetanmanyate bhavān ।
tat kathyatāṃ mahābhāga mano vai muhyate mama ।।
yadyetadevaṃ dharmajña nāsti dharme sahāyatā ।
tathaiva vipradevādipūjane pālane bhuvaḥ ।।
nāsti dharmaḥ kutaḥ satyamārjavaṃ cānṛśaṃsatā ।
yatra tvaṃ dharmaparamaḥ svarājyādavaropitaḥ ।।
iti tasyā vacaḥ śrutvā niśvasyoṣṇaṃ sagadgadam ।
kathayāmāsa tanvaṅgyā yathā prāptā śvapākatā ।।
ruditvā sāpi suciraṃ niśvasyoṣṇañca duḥ khitā ।
svaputramaraṇaṃ bhīruryathāvṛttaṃ nyavedayat ।।

rājovāca

priye ! na rocaye dīrghaṃ kālaṃ kleśamupāsitum ।
nātmāyattaśca tanvaṅgi paśya me mandabhāgyatām ।।
caṇḍālenānanujñātaḥ pravekṣye jvalanaṃ yadi ।
caṇḍāladāsatāṃ yāsye punarapyanyajanmani ।।
narake ca tapiṣyāmi koṭakaḥ kṛmibhojanaḥ ।
vaitaraṇyāṃ mahāpūya-vasāsṛk-snāyupicchile ।।
asipatravane prāpya chedaṃ prāpsyāmi dāruṇam ।
tāpaṃ prāpsyāmi vā prāpya mahārauravarauravau ।।
magnasya duḥ khajaladhau pāraḥ prāṇaviyojanam ।
eko api bālako yo ayamāsīdvaṃśakaraḥ sutaḥ ।।
mama daivāmbuvegena magnaḥ so api balīyasā ।
kathaṃ prāṇān vimuñcāmi parāyatto asmi durgataḥ ।।
athavā nārtinā kliṣṭo naraḥ pāpamavekṣate ।
tiryaktve nāsti tadduḥ śaṃ nāsipatravane tathā ।।
vaitaraṇyāṅkutastādṛg yādṛśaṃ putraviplave ।
so ahaṃ sutaśirīreṇa dīpyamāne hutāśane ।।
nipatiṣyāmi tanvaṅgi kṣantavyaṃ kukṛtaṃ mama ।
anujñātā ca gaccha tvaṃ vipraveśma suchismite ।।
mama vākyañca tanvaṅgi nibodhādṛtamānasā ।
yadi dattaṃ yadi hutaṃ guravo yadi toṣitāḥ ।।
paratra saṅgamo bhūyāt putreṇa saha ca tvayā ।
iha loke kutastvetad bhaviṣyati mameṅgitam ।।
tvayā saha mama śreyo gamanaṃ putramārgaṇe ।
yanmayā hasatā kiñcidrahasye vā śucismite ।।
aślīlamuktaṃ tat sarvaṃ kṣantavyaṃ mama yācataḥ ।
rājapatnīti garveṇa nāvajñeyaḥ sa te dvijaḥ ।
sarvayatnena te toṣyaḥ svāmidaivatavacchubhe ।।

rājapatnyuvāca

ahamapyatra rājarṣe dīpyamāne hutāśane ।
duḥ khabhārāsahādyaiva saha yāsyāmi vai tvayā ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tataḥ kṛtvā citāṃ rājā āropya tanayaṃ svakam ।
bhāryayā sahitaścāsau baddhāñjalipuṭastadā ।।
cintayan paramātmānamīśaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ harim ।
hṛtkoṭaraguhāsīnaṃ vāsudevaṃ sureśvaram ।
anādinidhanaṃ brahma kṛṣṇaṃ pītāmbaraṃ śubham ।।
tasya cintayamānasya sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ ।
dharmaṃ pramukhataḥ kṛtvā samājagmustvarānvitāḥ ।।
āgatya sarve procuste bho bho rājan ! śṛṇu prabho ।
ayaṃ pitāmahaḥ sākṣāddharmaśca bhagavān svayam ।।
sādhyāśca viśve maruto lokapālāḥ savāhanāḥ ।
nāgāḥ siddhāḥ sagandharvā rudrāścaiva tathāśvinau ।।
ete cānye ca bahavo viśvāmitrastathaiva ca ।
viśvatrayeṇa yo mitraṃ kartuṃ na śakitaḥ purā ।।
viśvāmitrastu te maitrīmiṣṭañcāhartumicchati ।
āruroha tataḥ prāpto dharmaḥ śakro atha gādhijaḥ ।।

dharmi uvāca

mā rājan ! sāhasaṃ kārṣordharmo ahaṃ tvāmupāgataḥ ।
titikṣā-dama-satyādyaiḥ svaguṇaiḥ paritoṣitaḥ ।।

indra uvāca

hariścandra māhabhāga ! prāptaḥ śakro asmite antikam ।
tvayā sabhāryaputreṇa jitā lokāḥ sanātanāḥ ।।
āroha tridivaṃ rājan ! bhāryāputrasamanvitaḥ ।
suduṣprāptaṃ narairanyairjitamātmīyakarmabhiḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tato amṛtamayaṃ varṣamapamṛtyuvināśanam ।
indraḥ prāsṛjadākāśāccitāsthānagataḥ prabhuḥ ।।
puṣpavarṣañca sumahaddevadundubhinisvanam ।
tatastato vartamāne samāje devasaṃkule ।।
samuttasthau tataḥ putro rājñastasya mahātmanaḥ ।
sukumāratanuḥ susthaḥ prasannendriyamānasaḥ ।।
tato rājā hariścandraḥ pariṣvajya sutaṃ kṣaṇāt ।
sabhāryaḥ sa śriyā yukto divyamālyāmbarānvitaḥ ।।
susthaḥ sampūrṇahṛdayo mudā paramayā yutaḥ ।
babhūva tatkṣaṇādindro bhūyaścainamabhāṣata ।।
sabhāryastvaṃ saputraśca prāpsyase sadgatiṃ parām ।
samāroha māhabhāga nijānāṃ karmaṇāṃ phalaiḥ ।।

hariścandra uvāca

devarājānanujñātaḥ svāminā śvapacena vai ।
agatvā niṣkṛtiṃ tasya nārokṣye ahaṃ surālayam ।।

dharma uvāca

tavainaṃ bhāvinaṃ kleśamavagamyātmamāyayā ।
ātmā śvapākatāṃ nīto darśitaṃ tacca cāpalam ।।

indra uvāca
prārthyate yat paraṃ sthānaṃ samastairmanujairbhuvi ।
tadāroha hariścandra sthānaṃ puṇyakṛtāṃ nṛṇām ।।

hariścandra uvāca

devārāja ! namastubhyaṃ vākyañcaitannibodha me ।
prasādasumukhaṃ yat tvāṃ bravīmi praśrayānvitaḥ ।।
macchokamagnamanasaḥ kośalānagare janāḥ ।
tiṣṭhanti tānapohyādya kathaṃ yāsyāmyahaṃ divam ।।
brahmahatyā gurorghāto govadhaḥ strīvadhastathā ।
tulyamebhirmahāpāpaṃ bhaktatyāge apyudāhṛtam ।।
bhajantaṃ bhaktamatyājyamaduṣṭaṃ tyajataḥ sukham ।
neha nāmutra paśyāmi tasmācchakra ! divaṃ vraja ।।
yadi te sahitāḥ svargaṃ mayā yānti sureśvara ।
tato ahamapi yāsyāmi narakaṃ vāpi taiḥ saha ।।

indra uvāca

bahūni puṇyapāpāni teṣāṃ bhinnāni vai pṛthak ।
kathaṃ saṅghātabhogyaṃ tvaṃ bhūyaḥ svargamavāpsyasi ।।

hariścandra uvāca

śakra bhuṅkte nṛpo rājyaṃ prabhāveṇa kuṭumbinām ।
yajate ca mahāyajñaiḥ karma paurtaṃ karoti ca ।।
tacca teṣāṃ prabhāveṇa mayā sarvamanuṣṭhitam ।
upakartṝn na santyakṣye tānahaṃ svargalipsayā ।।
tasmādyanmama deveśa kiñcidasti suceṣṭitam ।
dattamiṣṭamatho japtaṃ sāmānyaṃ taistadastu naḥ ।।
bahukālopabhogyaṃ hi phalaṃ yanmama karmaṇaḥ ।
tadastu dinamapyekaṃ taiḥ samaṃ tvatprasādataḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

evaṃ bhaviṣyatītyuktvā śakrastribhuvaneśvaraḥ ।
prasannacetā dharmaśca viśvāmitraśca gādhijaḥ ।।
vimānakoṭisambaddhaṃ svargalokānmahītalam ।
gatvāyodhyājanaṃ prāha divamāruhyatāmiti ।।
tadindrasya vacaḥ śrutvā prītyā tasya ca bhūpateḥ ।
ānīya rohitāścañca viśvāmitro mahātapāḥ ।।
ayodhyākhye pure ramye so abhyasiñcannṛpātmajam ।
devaiśca munibhiḥ siddhairabhiṣicya narādhipam ।।
rājñā saha tadā sarve hṛṣṭapuṣṭasuhṛjjanāḥ ।
saputrabhṛtyadārāste divamāruruhurjanāḥ ।।
pade pade vimānāt te vimānamagaman narāḥ ।
tadā sambhūtaharṣo asau hariścandraśca pārthivaḥ ।।
samprāpya bhūtimatulāṃ vimānaiḥ sa mahīpatiḥ ।
āsāñcakre purākāre vapraprākārasaṃvṛte ।।
tatastasyardhimālokya ślokaṃ tatrośanā jagau ।
daityācāryo mahābhāgaḥ sarvaśāstrārthatattvavit ।।

śukra uvāca

hariścandrasamo rājā na bhūto na bhaviṣyati ।
yaḥ śṛṇoti svaduḥ khārtaḥ sa sukhaṃ mahadāpnuyāt ।।
svargārthoprāpnuyāt svargaṃ putrārtho putramāpnuyāt ।
bhāryārtho prāpnuyādbhāryāṃ rājyārtho rājyamāpnuyāt ।।
aho titikṣāmāhātmyamaho dānaphalaṃ mahat ।
yadāgato hariścandraḥ purīñcendratvamāptavān ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

etat te sarvamākhyātaṃ hariścandraviceṣṭitam ।
ataḥ paraṃ kathāśeṣaḥ śrūyatāṃ munisattama ।।
vipāko rājasūyasya pṛthivīkṣayakāraṇam ।
tadvipākanimittañca yuddhamāḍibakaṃ mahat ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe hariścandropākhyānaṃ nāmāṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ

navamo adhyāyaḥ

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ
rājyacyute hariścandre gate ca tridaśālayam ।
niścakrāma mahātejā jalavāsāt purohitaḥ ।।
vaśiṣṭho dvādaśābdānte gaṅgāparyuṣito muniḥ ।
śuśrāva ca samastantu viśvāmitraviceṣcitam ।।
hariścandrasya nāśañca rājñaścodārakarmaṇaḥ ।
caṇḍālasamprayogañca bhāryātanayavikrayam ।।
sa śrutvā sumāhabhāgaḥ prītimānavanīpatau ।
cakāra kopaṃ tejasvī viśvāmitramṛṣiṃ prati ।।

vaśiṣṭha uvāca

mama putraśataṃ tena viśvāmitreṇa ghātitam ।
tatrāpi nābhavat krodhastādṛśo yādṛśo adya me ।।
śrutvā narādhipamimaṃ svarājyādavarīpitam ।
mahātmānaṃ mahābhāgaṃ devabrāhmaṇapūjakam ।।
yasmāt sa satyavāk śāntaḥ śatrāvapi vimatsaraḥ ।
anāgāścaiva dharmātmā apramatto madāśrayaḥ ।।
sapatnībhṛtyaputrastu prāpito antyāṃ daśāṃ nṛpaḥ ।
sa rājyāccyāvito anena bahuśaśca khilīkṛtaḥ ।।
tasmād durātmā brahmadviṭ prājñānāmavaropitaḥ ।
macchāpopahato mūḍhaḥ sa bakatvamavāpsyati ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

śrutvā śāpaṃ mahātejā viśvāmitro api kauśikaḥ ।
tvamapyāḍirbhavastevati pratiśāpamayacchata ।।
anyo anyaśāpāt tau prāptau tiryaktvaṃ paramadyutī ।
vaśiṣṭhaḥ sa mahātejā viśvāmitraśca kauśikaḥ ।।
anyajātisamāyogaṃ gatāvapyamitaujasau ।
yuyudhāte atisaṃrabdhau mahābalaparākramau ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasre dve pramāṇenāḍirucchritaḥ ।
yannavatyadhikaṃ brahman ! sahasratritayaṃ bakaḥ ।।
tau tu pakṣaprahārābhyāmanyonyasyoruvikramau ।
praharantau bhayaṃ tīvraṃ prajānāñcakratustadā ।।
vidhūya pakṣāṇi bako raktodvṛttākṣirāhanat ।
āḍiṃ so apyunnatagrīvo bakaṃ padbhyāmatāḍayat ।।
tayoḥ pakṣānilāpāstāḥ prapeturgirayo bhuvi ।
giriprapātābhihatā cakampe ca vasundharā ।।
kṣmā kampamānā jaladhīnudvṛttāmbūṃścakāra ca ।
nanāma caikapārśvena pātālagamanonmukhī ।।
kecidigarinipātena kecidambhodhivāriṇā ।
kecinmahīsañcalanāt prayayuḥ prāṇinaḥ kṣayam ।।
iti sarvaṃ paritrastaṃ hāhābhūtamacetanam ।
jagadāsīt susambhrāntaṃ paryastakṣitimaṇḍalam ।।
hā vatsa ! hā kānta ! śiśo ! prayāhyeṣo asmi saṃsthitaḥ ।
hā priye ! kānta ! śailo ayaṃ patatyāśu palāyatām ।।
ityākulīkṛte loke saṃtrāsavimukhe tadā ।
suraiḥ parivṛtaḥ sarvairājagāma pitāmahaḥ ।।
pratyuvāca ca viśveśāstāvubhāvatikopitau ।
yuddhaṃ vā viramatvetallokāḥ svāsthyaṃ vrajantu ca ।।
śṛṇvantāvapi tau vākyaṃ brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।
kopāmarṣasamāviṣṭo yuyudhāte na tasthatuḥ ।।
tataḥ pitāmaho devastaṃ dṛṣṭvā lokasaṃkṣayam ।
tayośca hitamanvicchan tiryagbhāvamapānudat ।।
tatastau pūrvadehasthau prāha devaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
vyudaste tāmase bhāve vaśiṣṭha-kauśikarṣabhau ।।
jahi vatsa vaśiṣṭha tvaṃ tvañca kauśika sattama ।
tāmasaṃ bhāvamāśritya īdṛgyuddhaṃ cikīrṣitam ।।
rājasūyavipāko ayaṃ hariścandrasya bhūpateḥ ।
yuvayorvigrahaścāyaṃ pṛthivīkṣayakārakaḥ ।।
na cāpi kauśikaśreṣṭhastasya rājño aparadhyate ।
svargaprāptikaro brahmannapakārapade sthitaḥ ।।
tapo vighnasya kartārau kāmakrodhavaśaṃ gatau ।
parityajata bhadraṃ vo brahma hi pracuraṃ balam ।।
evamuktau tatastena lajjitau tāvubhāvapi ।
kṣamayāmāsatuḥ prītyā pariṣvajya parasparam ।।
tataḥ surairvandyamāno brahmā lokaṃ nijaṃ yayau ।
vaśiṣṭho apyātmanaḥ sthānaṃ kauśiko api svāmāśrayam ।।
etadāḍibakaṃ yuddhaṃ hariścandrakathāṃ tathā ।
kathayiṣyanti ye martyāḥ samyak śroṣyanti caiva ye ।।
teṣāṃ pāpāpanodantu śrutaṃ hyeva kariṣyati ।
na caiva vighnakāryāṇi bhaviṣyanti kadācana ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe āḍi-bakayuddhavarṇanaṃ nāma navamo adhyāyaḥ

daśamo adhyāyaḥ

jaiminiruvāca

saṃśayaṃ dvijaśārdūlāḥ prabrūta mama pṛcchataḥ ।
āvirbhāva-tirobhāvau bhūtānāṃ yatra saṃsthitau ।।
kathaṃ sañjāyate jantuḥ kathaṃ vā savivardhate ।
kathaṃ vodaramadhyasthastiṣṭhatyaṅganipīḍitaḥ ।।
niṣkrāntimudarāt prāpya kathaṃ vā vṛddhimṛcchati ।
utkrāntikāle ca kathañcidbhāvena viyujyate ।।
kṛtsno mṛtastathāśnāti ubhe sukṛta-duṣkṛte ।
kathaṃ te ca tathā tasya phalaṃ sampādayantyuta ।।
kathaṃ na jīryate tatra piṇḍīkṛta ivāśaye ।
strīkoṣṭhe yatra jīryante bhuktāni sugurūṇyapi ।
bhakṣyāṇi yatra no janturjoryate kathamalpakaḥ ।।
etanme brūta sakalaṃ sandehoktivivarjitam ।
tadetat parama guhyaṃ yatra muhyanti jantavaḥ ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

praśnabhāro ayamatulastvayāsmāsu niveśitaḥ ।
durbhāvyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ bhāvābhāvasamāśritaḥ ।।
taṃ śṛṇuṣva mahābhāga yathā prāha pituḥ purā ।
putraḥ paramadharmātmā sumatirnāma nāmataḥ ।।
brāhmaṇo bhārgavaḥ kaścit sutamāha mahāmatiḥ ।
kṛtopanayanaṃ śāntaṃ sumatiṃ jaḍarūpiṇam ।।
vedānadhīṣva sumate ! yathānukramamāditaḥ ।
guruśuśrūṣaṇe vyagro bhaikṣānnakṛtabhojanaḥ ।।
tato gārhasthyamāsthāya ceṣṭvā yajñānanuttamān ।
iṣṭamutpādayāpatyamāśrayethā vanaṃ tataḥ ।।
vanasthaśca tato vatsa parivrāḍ niṣparigrahaḥ ।
evamāpsyasi tadbrahma yatra gatvā na śocasi ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

ityevamukto bahuśo jaḍatvānnāha kiñcana ।
pitāpi taṃ subahuśaḥ prāha prītyā punaḥ punaḥ ।।
iti pitrā sutasnehāt pralobhi madhurākṣaram ।
sa codyamāno bahuśaḥ prahasyedamathābravīt ।।
tātaitadbahuśo abhyastaṃ yat tvayādyopadiśyate ।
tathaivānyāni śāstrāṇi śilpāni vividhāni ca ।।
janmanāmayutaṃ sāgraṃ mama smṛtipathaṃ gatam ।
nirvedāḥ paritoṣāśca kṣayavṛddhyudaye gatāḥ ।।
śatrumitrakalatrāṇāṃ viyogāḥ saṅgamāstathā ।
mātaro vivadhā dṛṣṭāḥ pitaro vivadhāstathā ।।
anubhūtāni saukhyani duḥ khāni ca sahasraśaḥ ।
bāndhavā bahavaḥ prāptāḥ pitaraśca pṛthagvidhāḥ ।।
viṇmūtrapicchile strīṇāṃ tathā koṣṭhe mayoṣitam ।
pīḍāśca subhṛśaṃ prāptā rogāṇāñca sahasraśaḥ ।।
garbhaduḥ khānyanekāni bālatve yauvane tathā ।
vṛddhatāyāṃ tathāptāni tāni sarvāṇi saṃsmare ।।
brāhmaṇa-kṣatriya-viśāṃ śūdrāṇāñcāpi yoniṣu ।
punaśca puśukīṭānāṃ mṛgāṇāmatha pakṣiṇām ।।
tathaiva rājabhṛtyānāṃ rājñāñcāhavaśālinām ।
samutpanno asmi geheṣu tathaiva tava veśmani ।।
bhṛtyatāṃ dāsatāñcaiva gato asmi bahuśo nṛṇām ।
svāmitvamīśvaratvaṃ ca daridratvaṃ tathā gataḥ ।।
hataṃ mayā hataścānyairhataṃ me ghātitaṃ tathā ।
dattaṃ mamānyairanyebhyo mayā dattamanekaśāḥ ।।
pitṛ-mātṛ-suhṛd-bhrātṛ-kalatrādikṛtena ca ।
tuṣṭo asakṛt tathā dainyamaśrudhautānano gataḥ ।।
evaṃ saṃsāracakre asmin bhramatā tāta saṅkaṭe ।
jñānametanmayā prāptaṃ mokṣasamprāptikārakam ।।
vijñāte yatra sarvo ayamṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃjñitaḥ ।
kriyākalāpo viguṇo na samyak pratibhāti me ।।
tasmādutpannabodhasya vedaiḥ kiṃ me prayojanam ।
guruvijñānatṛptasya nirīhasya sadātmanaḥ ।।
ṣaṭ prakārakriyā-duḥkha-sukha-harṣa-rasaiśca yat ।
guṇaiśca varjitaṃ brahma tat prāpsyāmi paraṃ padam ।।
rasa-harṣa-bhayodvega-krodhāmarṣa-jarāturām ।
vijñātāṃ svamṛgagrāhisaṃghapāśaśatākulam ।।
tasmādyāsyāmyahaṃ tāta tyaktvemāṃ duḥ khasantatim ।
trayīdharmamadharmāḍhyaṃ kiṃ pāpaphalasannibham ।।
pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā harṣavismayagadgadam ।
pitā prāha mahābhāgaḥ svasutaṃ hṛṣṭamānasaḥ ।।

pitovāca

kimetadvadase vatsa kutaste jñānasambhavaḥ ।
kena te jaḍatā pūrvamidānīñca prabuddhatā ।।
kinnu śāpavikāro ayaṃ munidevakṛtastava ।
yatte jñānaṃ tirobhūtamāvirbhāvamupāgatam ।।

putra uvāca

śṛṇu tāta ! yathā vṛttaṃ mamedaṃ sukha-duḥkhadam ।
yaścāhamāsamanyasmin janmanyasmatparantu yat ।।
ahamāsaṃ purā vipro nyastātmā paramātmani ।
ātmavidyāvicāreṣu parāṃ niṣṭhāmupāgataḥ ।।
satataṃ yogayuktasya satatābhyāsasaṅgamāt ।
satsaṃyogāt svasvabhāvādvicāravidhiśodhanāt ।।
tasminnave parā prītirmamāsīd yuñjataḥ sadā ।
ācāryatāñca samprāptaḥ śiṣyasandehahṛttamaḥ ।।
tataḥ kālena mahatā aikāntikamupagataḥ ।
ajñānākṛṣṭasadbhāvo vipannaśca pramādataḥ ।।
utkrāntikālādārabhya smṛtilopo na me abhavat ।
yāvadabdaṃ gataṃ caiva janmanāṃ smṛtimāgatam ।।
pūrvābhyāsena tenaiva so ahaṃ tāta ! jitendriyaḥ ।
yatiṣyāmi tathā kartuṃ na bhaviṣye yathā punaḥ ।।
jñānadānaphalaṃ hyetadyajjātismaraṇaṃ mama ।
na hyetat prāpyate tāta trayīdharmāśritairnaraiḥ ।।
so ahaṃ pūrvāśramādeva niṣṭhādharmamupāśritaḥ ।
ekāntitvamupāgamya yatiṣyāmyātmamokṣaṇe ।।
tadbrūhi tvaṃ mahābhāga ! yat te saṃśayikaṃ hṛdi ।
etāvatāpi te prītimutpādyānṛṇyamāpnuyām ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

pitā prāha tataḥ putraṃ śraddadhat tasya tadvacaḥ ।
bhavatā yadvayaṃ pṛṣṭāḥ saṃsāragrahaṇāśrayam ।।

putra uvāca

śṛṇu tāta ! yathā tattvamanubhūtaṃ mayāsakṛt ।
saṃsāracakramajaraṃ sthitiryasya na vidyate ।।
so ahaṃ vadāmi te sarvaṃ tavaivānujñayā pitaḥ ।
utkrāntikālādārabhya yathā nānyo vadiṣyati ।।
ūṣmā prakupitaḥ kāye tīvravāyusamīritaḥ ।
bhinatti marmasthānāni dīpyamāno nirindhanaḥ ।।
udāno nāma pavanastataścordhvaṃ pravartate ।
bhuktānāmambubhakṣyāṇāmadhogatinirodhakṛt ।।
tato yenāmbudānāni kṛtānyannarasāstathā ।
dattāḥ sa tasya āhlādamāpadi pratipadyate ।।
annāni yena dattāni śraddhāpūtena cetasā ।
so api tṛptimavāpnoti vināpyannena vai tadā ।।
yenānṛtāni noktāni prītibhedaḥ kṛto na ca ।
āstikaḥ śraddadhānaśca sa sukhaṃ mṛtyumṛcchati ।।
devabrāhmaṇapūjāyāṃ ye ratā nānasūyavaḥ ।
śuklā vadānyā hrīmantaste narāḥ sukhamṛtyavaḥ ।।
yo na kāmānna saṃrambhānna dveṣāddharmamutsṛjet ।
yathoktakārī somyaśca sa sukhaṃ mṛtyumṛcchati ।।
avāridāyino dāhaṃ kṣudhāñcānannadāyinaḥ ।
prāpnuvanti narāḥ kāle tasmin mṛtyāvupasthite ।।
śītaṃ jayantīndhanadāstāpaṃ candanadāyinaḥ ।
prāṇaghnīṃ vedanāṃ kaṣṭāṃ ye cānudvegakāriṇaḥ ।।
mohājñānapradātāraḥ prāpnuvanti mahadbhayam ।
vedanābhirudagrābhiḥ prapīḍyante adhamā narāḥ ।।
kūṭasākṣī mṛṣāvādī yaścāsadanuśāsti vai ।
te mohamṛtyavaḥ sarve tathā vedavinindakāḥ ।।
vibhīṣaṇāḥ pūtigandhāḥ kūṭamudgarapāṇayaḥ ।
āgacchanti durātmāno yamasya puruṣāstadā ।।
prāpteṣu dṛkpathaṃ teṣu jāyate tasya vepathuḥ ।
krāndatyavirataṃ so atha bhrātṛ-mātṛsutānatha ।।
sāsya vāgasphuṭā tāta ekavarṇā vibhāvyate ।
dṛṣṭiśca bhrāmyate trāsācchvāsācchuṣyatyathānanam ।।
ūrdhvaśvāsānvitaḥ so atha dṛṣṭibhaṅgasamanvitaḥ ।
tataḥ sa vedanāviṣṭastaccharīraṃ vimuñcati ।।
vāyvagrasārī tadrūpaṃ dehamanyat prapadyate ।
tatkarmajaṃ yātanārthaṃ na mātṛ-pitṛsambhavam ।
tatpramāṇavayo avasthā-saṃsthānaiḥ prāgbhavaṃ yathā ।।
tato dūto yamasyāśu pāśairbadhnāti dāruṇaiḥ ।
daṇḍaprahārasambhrāntaṃ karṣate dakṣiṇāṃ diśam ।।
kuśa-kaṇṭaka-valamīka-śaṅku-pāṣāṇakarkaśe ।
tathā pradīptajvalane kvacicchṛbhraśatotkaṭe ।।
pradīptādityatapte ca dahyamāne tadaṃśubhiḥ ।
kṛṣyate yamadūtaiścāśivasannādabhīṣaṇaiḥ ।।
vikṛṣyamāṇastairghorairbhakṣyamāṇaḥ śivāśataiḥ ।
prayāti dāruṇe mārge pāpakarmā yamakṣayam ।।
chatropānatpradātāro ye ca vastrapradā narāḥ ।
ye yānti manujā mārgaṃ taṃ sukhena tathānnadāḥ ।।
evaṃ kleśānanubhavannavaśaḥ pāpapīḍitaḥ ।
nīyate dvādaśāhena dharmarājapuraṃ naraḥ ।।
kalevare dahyamāne mahāntaṃ dāhamṛcchati ।
tāḍyamāne tathaivārti chidyamāne ca dāruṇām ।।
klidyamāne cirataraṃ janturduḥkhamavāpnute ।
svena karmavipākena dehāntaragato api san ।।
tatra yadvāndhavāstoyaṃ prayacchanti tilaiḥ saha ।
yacca piṇḍaṃ prayacchanti nīyamānastadaśnute ।।
tailābhyaṅgo bāndhavānāmaṅgasaṃvāhanañca yat ।
tena cāpyāyyate janturyaccāśnanti sabāndhavāḥ ।।
bhūmau svapadbhirnātyantaṃ kleśamāpnoti bāndhavaiḥ ।
dānaṃ dadadbhiśca tathā janturāpyāyyate mṛtaḥ ।।
nīyamānaḥ svakaṃ gehaṃ dvādaśāhaṃ sa paśyati ।
upabhuṅkte tathā dattaṃ toyapiṇḍādikaṃ bhuvi ।।
dvādaśāhāt paraṃ ghoramāyasaṃ bhīṣaṇākṛtim ।
yāmyaṃ paśyatyatho jantuḥ kṛṣyamāṇaḥ puraṃ tataḥ ।।
gatamātro atiraktākṣaṃ bhinnāñjanacayaprabham ।
mṛtyukālāntakādīnāṃ madhye paśyati vai yamam ।।
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaṃ bhrakuṭīdāruṇākṛtim ।
virūpairbhoṣaṇairvaktrairvṛtaṃ vyādhiśataiḥ prabhum ।।
daṇḍāsaktaṃ mahābāhuṃ pāśahastaṃ subhairavam ।
tannirdiṣṭāṃ tato yāti gatiṃ jantuḥ śubhāśubhām ।।
raurave kūṭasākṣī tu yāti yaścānṛto naraḥ ।
tasya svarūpaṃ gadato rauravasya niśāmaya ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasre dve rauravo hi pramāṇataḥ ।
jānumātrapramāṇaśca tataḥ śvabhraḥ sudustaraḥ ।।
tatrāṅgāracayopetaṃ kṛtañca dharaṇīsamam ।
jājvalyamānastīvreṇa tāpitāṅgārabhūminā ।।
tanmadhye pāpakarmāṇaṃ vimuñcanti yamānugāḥ ।
sa dahyamānastīvreṇa vahninā tatra dhāvati ।।
pade pade ca pādo asya śīryate jīryate punaḥ ।
ahorātreṇoddharaṇaṃ pādanyāsaṃ ca gacchati ।।
evaṃ sahasramuttīrṇo yojanānāṃ vimucyate ।
tato anyaṃ pāpaśuddhyarthaṃ tādṛṅnirayamṛcchati ।।
tataḥ sarveṣu nistīrṇaḥ pāpī tiryakatvamaśnute ।
kṛmi-kīṭa-pataṅgeṣu śvāpade maśakādiṣu ।।
gatvā gajadrumādyeṣu goṣvaśveṣu tathaiva ca ।
anyāsu caiva pāpāsu duḥ khadāsu ca yoniṣu ।।
mānuṣaṃ prāpya kubjo vā kutsito vāmano api vā ।
caṇḍālapukkasādyāsu naro yoniṣu jāyate ।।
avaśiṣṭena pāpena puṇyena ca samanvitaḥ ।
tataścārohaṇīṃ jātiṃ śūdra-vaiśya-nṛpādikām ।।
vipradevendratāṃ cāpi kadācidavarohaṇīm ।
evantu pāpakarmāṇe narakeṣu patantyadhaḥ ।।
yathā puṇyakṛto yānti tanme nigatadaḥ śṛṇu ।
te yamena vinirdiṣṭāṃ yānti puṇyāṃ gatiṃ narāḥ ।।
pragītagandharvagaṇāḥ pravṛttāpsarasāṅgaṇāḥ ।
hāranūpuramādurya-śobhitānyuttamāni ca ।।
prayāntyāśu vimānāni nānādivyastragujjvalāḥ ।
tasmācca pracyutā rājñāmanyeṣāṃ ca mahātmanām ।।
jāyante ca kule tatra sadvṛttaparipālakāḥ ।
bhogān samprāpnuvantyugrāṃstato yāntyūrdhvamanyathā ।।
avarohaṇīṃ ca samprāpya pūrvavadyānti mānavāḥ ।
etat te sarvamākhyātaṃ yathā janturvipadyate ।
ataḥ śṛṇuṣva viprarṣe yathā garbhaṃ prapadyate ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe pitāputrasaṃvādo nāma daśamo adhyāyaḥ

ekādaśo adhyāyaḥ
putra uvāca

niṣekaṃ mānavaṃ strīṇāṃ bījaṃ prāptaṃ rajasyatha ।
vimuktamātro narakāt svargādvāpi prapadyate ।।
tenābhibhūtaṃ tat sthairyaṃ yāti bījadvayaṃ pitaḥ ।
kalalatvaṃ budbudatvaṃ tataḥ peṣitvameva ca ।।
peṣyāṃ yathāṇubījaṃ syādahkurastadvaducyate ।
aṅgānāṃ ca tathotpattiḥ pañcānāmanubhāgaśaḥ ।।
upāṅgānyaṅgulī-netra-nāsāsya-śravaṇāni ca ।
prarohaṃ yānti cāṅgebhyastadvat tebhyo nakhādikam ।।
tvaci romāṇi jāyante keśāścaiva tataḥ param ।
samaṃ samṛddhimāyāti tenaivodbhavakoṣakam ।।
nārikelaphalaṃ yadvat sakoṣaṃ vṛddhimṛcchati ।
tadvat prayātyasau vṛddhiṃ sakoṣo adhomukhaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
tale tu jānu-pārśvābhyāṃ karau nyasya sa vardhate ।
aṅguṣṭho copari nyastau jānvoragre tathāṅgulī ।।
jānupṛṣṭhe tathā netre jānumadhye ca nāsikā ।
sphicau pārṣṇidvayasthe ca bāhujaṅghe bahiḥ sthite ।।
evaṃ vṛddhiṃ kramādyāti jantuḥ strīgarbhasaṃsthitaḥ ।
anyasattvodare jantoryathā rūpaṃ tathā sthitiḥ ।।
kāṭhinyamagninā yāti bhuktapītena jīvati ।
puṇyāpuṇyāśrayamayī sthitirjantostathodare ।।
nāḍī cāpyāyanī nāma nābhyāṃ tasya nibadhyate ।
strīṇāṃ tathāntrasuṣire sā nibaddhopajāyate ।।
krāmanti bhuktapītāni strīṇāṃ garbhodare yathā ।
tairāpyāyitadeho asau janturvṛddhimupaiti vai ।।
smṛtīstasya prayāntyasya bahvyaḥ saṃsārabhūmayaḥ ।
