tato nirvedamāyāti pīḍyamāna itastataḥ ।।
punarnaivaṃ kariṣyāmi muktamātra ihodarāt ।
tathā tathā yatiṣyāmi garbhaṃ nāpsyāmyahaṃ yathā ।।
iti cintayate smṛtvā janmaduḥ khaśatāni vai ।
yāni pūrvānubhūtāni daivabhūtāni yāni vai ।।
tataḥ kālakramājjantuḥ parivartatyadhomukhaḥ ।
navame daśame vāpi māsi sajjayate yataḥ ।।
niṣkramyamāṇo vātena prājāpatyena pīḍyate ।
niṣkrāmyate ca vilapan hṛdi duḥ khanipīḍitaḥ ।।
niṣkrāntaścodarānmūrcchāmasahyāṃ pratipadyate ।
prāpnoti cetanāṃ cāsau vāyusparśasamanvitaḥ ।।
tatastaṃ vaiṣṇavī māyā samāskandati mohinī ।
tayā vimohitātmāsau jñānabhraṃśamavāpnute ।।
bhraṣṭajñāno bālabhāvaṃ tato jantuḥ prapadyate ।
tataḥ kaumārakāvasthāṃ yauvanaṃ vṛddhatāmapi ।।
punaśca maraṇaṃ tadvajjanma cāpnoti mānavaḥ ।
tataḥ saṃsāracakre asmin bhrāmyate ghaṭiyantravat ।।
kadācit svargamāpnoti kadācinnirayaṃ naraḥ ।
narakaṃ caiva svargaṃ ca kadācicca mṛto aśnute ।।
kadācidatraiva punarjātaḥ svaṃ karma so aśnute ।
kadācidbhuktakarmā ca mṛtaḥ svalpena gacchati ।।
kadācidalpaiśca tato jāyate atra śubhāśubhaiḥ ।
svarloke narake caiva bhuktaprāyo dvijottama ।।
narakeṣu mahadduḥ khametad yat svargavāsinaḥ ।
dṛśyante tāta modante pātyamānāśca nārakāḥ ।।
svarge api duḥ khamatulaṃ yadārohaṇakālataḥ ।
prabhṛtyahaṃ patiṣyāmītyetanmanasi vartate ।।
nārakāṃścaiva saṃprekṣya mahadduḥ khamavāpyate ।
etāṃ gatimahaṃ gantetyaharniśamanirvṛtaḥ ।।
garbhavāse mahadduḥ khaṃ jāyamānasya yonitaḥ ।
jātasya balābhāve ca vṛddhatve duḥ khameva ca ।।
kāmerṣyā-krodhasambandhaṃ yauvane cātiduḥ saham ।
duḥ khaprāyā vṛddhatā ca maraṇe duḥ khamuttamam ।।
kṛṣṇamāṇasya yāmyaiśca narakeṣu ca pātyataḥ ।
punaśca garbho janmātha maraṇaṃ narakastathā ।।
evaṃ saṃsāracakre asmin jantavo ghaṭiyantravat ।
bhrāmyante prākṛtairbandhairbaddhvā bādhyanti cāsakṛt ।।
nāsti tāta ! sukhaṃ kiñcidatra duḥ khaśatākule ।
tasmānmokṣāya yatatā kathaṃ sevyā mayā trayī ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhapitrāputrasaṃvādo' nāma ekādaśo adhyāyaḥ

dvādaśo adhyāyaḥ

pitovāca
sādhu vatsa ! tvayākhyātaṃ saṃsāragahanaṃ param ।
jñānapradānasambhūtaṃ samāśritya mahāphalam ।।
tatra te narakāḥ sarve yathā vai rauravastathā ।
varṇitāstān samācakṣva vistareṇa mahāmate ।।

putra uvāca

rauravaste samākhyātaḥ prathamaṃ narako mayā ।
mahārauravasaṃjñaṃ tu śṛṇuṣva narakaṃ pitaḥ ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi sapta pañca samantataḥ ।
tatra tāmramayī bhūmiradhastasya hutāśanaḥ ।।
tattāpataptā sarvāśā prodyadindusamaprabhā ।
vibhātyatimahāraudrā darśanasparśanādiṣu ।।
tasyāṃ baddhaḥ karābhyāñca padbhyāñcaiva yamānugaiḥ ।
mucyate pāpakṛnmadhye luṭhamānaḥ sa gacchati ।।
kākairvakairvṛkolūkairvṛścikairmaśakaistathā ।
bhakṣyamāṇastathā gṛdhrairdrutaṃ mārge vikṛṣyate ।।
dahyamānaḥ pitarmātarbhrātastāteti cākulaḥ ।
vadatyasakṛdudvigno na śāntimadhigacchati ।।
evaṃ tasmānnaraimarmokṣo hyatikrāntairavāpyate ।
varṣāyutāyutaiḥ pāpaṃ yaiḥ kṛtaṃ duṣṭabuddhibhiḥ ।।
tathānyastu tamo nāma so atiśītaḥ svabhāvataḥ ।
mahārauravavad dīrghastathā sa tamasā vṛtaḥ ।।
śītārtāstatra dhāvanto narāstamasi dāruṇe ।
parasparaṃ samāsādya parirabhyāśrayanti ca ।।
dantāsteṣāñca bhajyante śītārtiparikampitāḥ ।
kṣuttṛṣṇāprabalāstatra tathaivānye apyupadravāḥ ।।
himakhaṇḍavaho vāyurbhinattyasthīni dāruṇaḥ ।
majjāsṛggalitaṃ tasmādaśnuvanti kṣudhānvitāḥ ।।
lelihyamānā bhrāmyante parasparasamāgame ।
evaṃ tatrāpi sumahān kleśastamasi mānavaiḥ ।।
prāpyate brāhmaṇaśreṣṭha yāvadduṣkṛtasaṃkṣayaḥ ।
nikṛntana iti khyātastato anyo narakottamaḥ ।।
tasmin kulālacakrāṇi bhrāmyantyavirataṃ pitaḥ ।
teṣvāropya nikṛtyante kālasūtreṇa mānavāḥ ।।
yamānugāṅgulisthena āpādatalamastakam ।
na caiṣāṃ jīvitabhraṃśo jāyate dvijasattama ।।
chinnāni teṣāṃ śataśaḥ khaṇḍānyaikyaṃ vrajanti ca ।
evaṃ varṣasahasrāṇi chidyante pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।।
tāvad yāvadaśeṣaṃ vai tatpāpaṃ hi kṣayaṃ gatam ।
apratiṣṭhañca narakaṃ śṛṇuṣva gadato mama ।।
atrasthairnārakairduḥ khamasahyamanubhūyate ।
tānyeva yatra cakrāṇi ghaṭīyantrāṇi cānyataḥ ।।
duḥ khasya hetubhūtāni pāpakarmakṛtāṃ nṛṇām ।
cakreṣvāropitāḥ kecid bhrāmyante tatra mānavāḥ ।।
yāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi na teṣāṃ sthitirantarā ।
ghaṭīyantreṣu caivānyo baddhastoye yathā ghaṭī ।।
bhrāmyante mānavā raktamudigarantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
astrairmukhaviniṣkrāntaiḥ netrairaśruvilambibhiḥ ।।
duḥ khāni te prāpnuvanti yānyasahyāni jantubhiḥ ।
asipatravanaṃ nāma narakaṃ śṛṇu cāparam ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ yo jvaladagnyāstṛtāvaniḥ ।
taptāḥ sūryakaraiścaṇḍairyatrātīva sudāruṇaiḥ ।।
prapatanti sadā tatra prāṇino narakaukasaḥ ।
tanmadhye ca vanaṃ ramyaṃ snigdhapatraṃ vibhāvyate ।।
patrāṇi tatra khaṅgānāṃ phalāni dvijasattamam ।
śvānaśca tatra sabalāḥ svanantyayutaśobhitāḥ ।।
mahāvaktrā mahādaṃṣṭrā vyāghrā iva bhayānakāḥ ।
tatastadvanamālokya śiśiracchāyamagrataḥ ।।
prayānti prāṇinastatra tīvratṛṭparipīḍitāḥ ।
hā mātarhā tāta ! iti krāndanto atīva duḥ khitā ।।
dahyamānāṅghrayugalā dharaṇīsthena vahninā ।
teṣāṃ gatānāṃ tatrāsipatrapātī samīraṇaḥ ।।
pravāti tena pātyante teṣāṃ khaḍgānyathopari ।
tataḥ patanti te bhūmau jvalatpavakasañcaye ।।
lelihyamāne cānyatra vyāptāśeṣamahītale ।
sārameyāstataḥ śīghraṃ śātayanti śarīrataḥ ।।
teṣāmaṅgāni rudatāmanekānyatibhīṣaṇāḥ ।
asipatravanaṃ tāta ! mayaitat kīrtitaṃ tava ।।
ataḥ paraṃ bhīmataraṃ taptakumbhaṃ nibodha me ।
samantatastaptakumbhā vahnijvālāsamāvṛtāḥ ।।
jvaladagnicayodvṛttatailāyaścūrṇapūritāḥ ।
teṣu duṣkṛtakarmāṇo yāmyaiḥ kṣiptā hyadhomukhāḥ ।।
kvāthyante visphuṭadgātra-galanmajjajalāvilāḥ ।
sphuratkapālanetrāsthicchidyamānā vibhīṣaṇaiḥ ।।
gṛdhrairutpāṭya mucyante punasteṣveva vegitaiḥ ।
punaḥ simasimāyante tailenaikyaṃ vrajanti ca ।।
dravībhūtaiḥ śirogātra-snāyu-māṃsa-tvagasthibhiḥ ।
tato yāmyairnarairāśu darvyā ghaṭṭanaghaṭṭitāḥ ।।
kṛtāvarte mahātaile mathyante pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।
eṣa te vistareṇoktastaptakumbho mayā pitaḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe pitāḥ putrasaṃvāde mahārauravādinarakākhyānaṃ nāma dvādaśo adhyāyaḥ

trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ

putra uvāca

ahaṃ vaiśyakule jāto janmanyasmāttu saptame ।
samatīte gavāṃ rodhaṃ nipāne kṛtavān purā ।।
vipākāt karmaṇastasya narakaṃ bhṛśadāruṇam ।
samprāpto agniśikhāghoramayomukhakhagākulam ।।
yantrapīḍanagātrāsṛk-pravāhodbhūtakardamam ।
viśasyamānaduṣkarmi-tannipātaravākulam ।।
pātyamānasya me tatra sāgraṃ varṣaśataṃ gatam ।
mahātāpārtitaptasya tṛṣṇādāhānvitasya ca ।।
tatrāhlādakaraḥ sadyaḥ pavanaḥ sukhaśītalaḥ ।
karambha-bālukākumbha-madhyastho me samāgataḥ ।।
tatsamparkādaśeṣāṇāṃ nābhavadyātanā nṛṇām ।
mama cāpi yathā svarge svargiṇāṃ nirvṛtiḥ parā ।।
kimetaditi cāhlāda-vistārastimitekṣaṇaiḥ ।
dṛṣṭamasmābhirāsannaṃ nararatnamanattamam ।।
yāmyaśca puruṣo ghoro daṇḍahasto aśaniprabhaḥ ।
purato darśayan mārgamiti ehīti vagatha ।।
puruṣaḥ sa tadā dṛṣṭvā yātanāśatasaṃkulam ।
narakaṃ prāha taṃ yāmyaṃ kiṅkaraṃ kṛpayānvitaḥ ।।

puruṣa uvāca

bho yāmyapuruṣācakṣva kiṃ mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ।
yenedaṃ yātanābhīm prāpto asmi narakaṃ param ।।
vipaściditi vikhyāto janakānāmahaṃ kule ।
jāto videhaviṣaye samyaṅmanujapālakaḥ ।।
yajñairmayeṣṭaṃ bahubhirdharmataḥ pālitā mahī ।
notsṛṣṭaścaiva saṃgrāmo nātithirvimukho gataḥ ।।
pitṛ-devarṣi-bhṛtyāśca na cāpacaritā mayā ।
kṛtā spṛhā ca na mayā parastrīvibhavādiṣu ।।
parvakāleṣu pitarastithikāleṣu devatāḥ ।
puruṣaṃ svayamāyānti nipānamiva dhenavaḥ ।।
yataste vimukhā yānti niśvasya gṛhamedhinaḥ ।
tasmādiṣṭaśca pūrtaśca dhamau dvāvapi naśyataḥ ।।
pitṛniśvāsavidhvastaṃ saptajanmārjitaṃ śubham ।
trijanmaprabhavaṃ daivo niśvāso hantyasaṃśayam ।।
tasmād daive ca pitrye ca nityamevodyato abhavam ।
so ahaṃ kathamimaṃ prāpto naraṅka bhṛśadāruṇam ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe pitā-putrasaṃvādo nāma trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ

caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ

putra uvāca

iti pṛṣṭastadā tena śṛṇvatāṃ no mahātmanā ।
uvāca puruṣo yāmyo ghoro api prasṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।।

yamakiṅkara uvāca

mahārāja ! yathāttha tvaṃ tathaitannātra saṃśayaḥ ।
kintu svalpaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhavatā smārayāmi tat ।।
vaidarbho tava yā patnī pīvarī nāma nāmataḥ ।
ṛtumatyā ṛturvandhyastvayā tasyāḥ kṛtaḥ purā ।।
śuśobhanāyāṃ kaikeyyāmāsaktena tato bhavān ।
ṛtuvyatikramāt prāpto narakaṃ ghoramīdṛśam ।।
homakāle yathā vahnirājyapātamavekṣate ।
ṛtau prajāpatistadvad bījapātamavekṣate ।।
yastamullaṅghya dharmātmā kāmeṣvāsaktimān bhavet ।
sa tu pitryādṛṇāt pāpamavāpya narakaṃ patet ।।
etāvadeva te pāpaṃ nānyat kiñcana vidyate ।
tadehi gaccha puṇyānāmupabhogāya pārthiva ।।

rājovāca

yāsyāmi devānucara yatra tvaṃ māṃ nayiṣyasi ।
kiñcit pṛcchāmi tanme tvaṃ yathāvadvaktumarhasi ।।
vajratuṇḍāstvamī kākāḥ puṃsāṃ nayanahāriṇaḥ ।
punaḥ punaśca netrāṇi tadvadeṣāṃ bhavanti hi ।।
kiṃ karma kṛtavantaśca kathayaitajjugupsitam ।
harantyeṣāṃ tathā jihvāṃ jāyamānāṃ punarnavām ।।
parapatreṇa pāṭyante kasmādete atiduḥ khitāḥ ।
karambhavālukāsvete pacyante tailagocarāḥ ।।
ayomukhaiḥ khagaiścaite kṛṣyante kiṃvidhā vada ।
viśrliṣṭadehabandhārti-mahārāvavirāviṇaḥ ।।
ayaścañcunipātena sarvāṅgakṣataduḥ khitāḥ ।
kimete aniṣṭakartārastudyante aharniśaṃ narāḥ ।।
etāścānyāśca dṛśyante yātanāḥ pāpakarmiṇām ।
yena karmavipākeṇa tanmamāśeṣato vada ।।

yamakiṅkara uvāca

yanmāṃ pṛcchasi bhūpāla ! pāpakarmaphalodayam ।
tat te ahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi saṃkṣepeṇa yathātatham ।।
puṇyāpuṇye hi puruṣaḥ paryāyeṇa samaśnate ।
bhuñjataśca kṣayaṃ yāti pāpaṃ puṇyamathāpi vā ।।
na tu bhogādṛte puṇyaṃ kiñcidvā karma mānavam ।
pāpakaṃ vā punātyāśu kṣayo bhogāt prajāyate ।।
parityajati bhogācca puṇyāpuṇye nibodha me ।
durbhikṣādeva durbhikṣaṃ kleśāt kleśaṃ bhayādbhayam ।।
mṛtebhyaḥ pramṛtā yānti daridrāḥ pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।
gatiṃ nānāvidhāṃ yānti jantavaḥ karmabandhanāt ।।
utsavādutsavaṃ yānti svargāt svargaṃ sukhāt sukham ।
śraddhadhānāśca śāntāśca dhanadāḥ śubhakāriṇaḥ ।।
vyālakuñjaradurgāṇi sarpacaurabhayāni tu ।
hatāḥ pāpena gacchanti pāpinaḥ kimataḥ param ।।
anekaśatasāhastra-janmasaṃcayasañcitam ।
puṇyāpuṇyaṃ nṛṇāṃ tadvat sukhaduḥ khāṅkurodbhavam ।।
yathā bījaṃ hi bhūpāla ! payāṃsi samavekṣate ।
puṇyāpuṇye tathā kāladeśānyakarmakārakam ।।
svalpaṃ pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ puṃsā deśakālopapāditam ।
pādanyāsakṛtaṃ duḥ khaṃ kaṇṭakotthaṃ prayacchati ।।
tat prabhūtataraṃ sthūlaṃ śūlakīlakasambhavam ।
duḥ khaṃ yacchati tadvacca śirorogādi duḥ saham ।।
apathyāśanaśītoṣṇa-śramatāpādikārakam ।
tathānyo anyamapekṣante pāpāni phalasaṅgame ।।
evaṃ mahānti pāpāni dīrgharogādivikriyām ।
tadvacchastrāgnikṛcchrārti-bandhanādiphalāya vai ।।
svalpaṃ puṇyaṃ śubhaṃ gandhaṃ helayā samprayacchiti ।
sparśa vāpyathavā śabdaṃ rasaṃ rūpamathāpi vā ।।
cirād gurutaraṃ tadvanmahāntamapi kālajam ।
evañca sukhaduḥ khāni puṇyāpuṇyodbhavāni vai ।।
bhuñjāno anekasaṃsāra-sambhavānīha tiṣṭhati ।
jāti deśāvaruddhāni jñānājñānaphalāni ca ।।
tiṣṇanti tatra yuktāni liṅgamātreṇa cātmani ।
vapuṣā manasā vācā na kadācit kvacinnaraḥ ।।
akurvan pāpakaṃ karma puṇyaṃ vāpyavatiṣṭhate ।
yad yat prāpnoti puruṣo duḥ khaṃ sukhamathāpi vā ।।
prabhūtamathavā svalpaṃ vikriyākāri cetasaḥ ।
tāvatā tasya puṇyaṃ vā pāpaṃ vāpyatha cetarat ।।
upabhogāt kṣayaṃ yāti bhujyamānamivāśanam ।
evamete mahāpāpaṃ yātanābhiraharniśam ।।
kṣapayanti narā ghoraṃ narakāntarvivartinaḥ ।
tathaiva rājan ! puṇyāni svargaloke amaraiḥ saha ।।
gandharvasiddhāpsarasāṃ gītādyairupabhuñjate ।
devatve mānuṣatve ca tiryaktve ca śubhāśubham ।।
puṇyapāpodbhavaṃ bhuṅkte sukhaduḥ khopalakṣaṇam ।
yad tvaṃ pṛcchasi māṃ rājan ! yātanāḥ pāpakarmiṇām ।
kena keneti pāpena tat te vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ ।।
duṣṭena cakṣuṣā dṛṣṭāḥ paradārā narādhamaiḥ ।
mānasena ca duṣṭena paradravyañca saspṛhaiḥ ।।
vajratuṇḍāḥ khagāsteṣāṃ harantyete vilocane ।
punaḥ punaśca sambhūtirakṣṇoreṣāṃ bhavatyatha ।।
yāvato akṣinimeṣāṃstu pāpamebhirnṛbhiḥ kṛtam ।
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi netrātti prāpnuvantyuta ।।
asacchāstropadeśāstu yairdattā yaiśca mantritāḥ ।
samyagdṛṣṭervināśāya ripūṇāmapi mānavaiḥ ।।
yaiḥ śāstramanyathā proktaṃ yairasadvāgudāhṛtā ।
vedadevadvijātīnāṃ gurornindā ca yaiḥ kṛtā ।।
haranti teṣāṃ jihvāśca jāyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
tāvato vatsarānete vajratuṇḍāḥ sadāruṇāḥ ।।
mitrabhedaṃ tathā pitrā putrasya svajanasya ca ।
yājyopādhyāyayormātrā sutasya sahacāriṇaḥ ।।
bhāryāpatyośca ye kecid bhedaṃ cakrurnarādhamāḥ ।
ta hame paśya pāṭyante karapatreṇa pārthiva ।।
paropatāpakā ye ca ye cāhlādaniṣedhakāḥ ।
tālavṛntānilasthāna-candanośīrahāriṇaḥ ।।
prāṇāntikaṃ dadustāpamaduṣṭānāñca ye adhamāḥ ।
karambhavālukāsaṃsthāsta ime pāpabhāginaḥ ।।
bhuṅkte śrāddhantu yo anyasya naro anyena nimantritaḥ ।
daive vāpyathavā pitrye sa dvidhā kṛṣyate khagaiḥ ।।
marmāṇi yastu sādhūnāmasadvāgbhirnikṛntati ।
tamime tudamānāstu khagāstiṣṭhantyavāritā ।।
yaḥ karoti ca paiśunyamanyavāganyathāmatiḥ ।
pāṭyate hi dvidhā jihvā tasyetthaṃ niśitaiḥ kṣuraiḥ ।।
mātā-pitrorgurūṇāñca ye avajñāṃ cakruruddhatāḥ ।
ta ime pūyaviṇmūtra-garte majjantyadhomukhāḥ ।।
devatātithibhūteṣu bhṛtyeṣvabhyāgateṣu ca ।
abhuktavatsu ye aśnanti tadvat pitragnipakṣiṣu ।।
duṣṭāste pūyaniryāsa-bhujaḥ sūcīmukhāstu te ।
jāyante girivarṣmāṇaḥ paśyaite yādṛśā narāḥ ।।
ekapaṅktyā tu ye vipramathavetaravarṇajam ।
viṣamaṃ bojayantīha viḍbhujasta ime yathā ।।
ekasārthaprayātaṃ ye niḥ svamarthārthinaṃ naram ।
apāsya svānnamaśnanti ta ime śleṣmabhojinaḥ ।।
gobāhmaṇāgnayaḥ spṛṣṭā yairucchiṣṭairnareśvara ।
teṣāmete agnikumbheṣu lelihyantyāhitāḥ karāḥ ।।
sūryendutārakā dṛṣṭā yairucchiṣṭaistu kāmataḥ ।
teṣāṃ yāmyairnarairnetre nyasto vahniḥ samedhyate ।।
gāvo agnirjananī viprojyeṣṭhabhrātā pitā svasā ।
jāmayo guravo vṛddhā yaiḥ spṛṣṭāstu padā nṛbhiḥ ।।
baddhāṅghrayaste nigaḍailauhairagnipratāpitaiḥ ।
aṅgārarāśimadhyasthāstiṣṭhantyājānudāhinaḥ ।।
pāyasaṃ kṛśaraṃ chāgo devānnāni ca yāni vai ।
bhuktāni yairasaṃskṛtya teṣāṃ netrāṇi pāpinām ।।
nipātitānāṃ bhūpṛṣṭhe udvṛttākṣi nirīkṣatām ।
sandaṃśaiḥ paśya kṛṣyante narairyāmyairmukhāt tataḥ ।।
guru-deva-dvijātīnāṃ vedānāñca narādhamaiḥ ।
nindā niśāmitā yaiśca pāpānāmabhinandatām ।।
teṣāmayomayān kīlānagnivarṣān punaḥ punaḥ ।
karṇeṣu prerayantyete yāmyā vilapatāmapi ।।
yaiḥ prapā-devaviprauko-devālayasabhāḥ śubhāḥ ।
bhaṅktvā vidhvaṃsamānītāḥ krodhalobhānuvartibhiḥ ।।
teṣāmetaiḥ śitaiḥ śastrairmuhurvilapatāṃ tvacaḥ ।
pṛthak kurvanti vai yāmyāḥ śarīrādatidāruṇāḥ ।।
gobrāhmaṇārkamārgeṣu ye avamehanti mānavāḥ ।
teṣāmetāni kṛṣyante gudenāntrāṇi vāyasaiḥ ।।
dattvā kanyāṃ ca ekasmai dvitīyāya prayacchati ।
sa tvevaṃ naikadhācchinnaḥ kṣāranadyāṃ pravāhyate ।।
svapoṣaṇaparo yastu parityajati mānavaḥ ।
putra-bhṛtya-kalatrādi-bandhuvargamakiñcinam ।।
durbhikṣe sambhrame vāpi so apyevaṃ yamakiṅkaraiḥ ।
utkṛtya dattāni mukhe svamāṃsānyaśnute kṣudhā ।।
śaraṇāgatān yastyajati lobhād vṛttyupajīvinaḥ ।
so apyevaṃ yantrapīḍābhiḥ pīḍyate yamakiṅkaraiḥ ।।
sukṛtaṃ ye prayacchanti yāvajjanma kṛtaṃ narāḥ ।
te piṣyante śilāpeṣairyathaite pāpakarmiṇaḥ ।।
nyāsāpahāriṇo baddhāḥ sarvagātreṣu bandhanaiḥ ।
kṛmivṛścikakākolairbhujyante aharniśaṃ narāḥ ।।
kṣutkṣāmāstṛṭpatajjihvā-tālavo vedanāturāḥ ।
divāmaithuninaḥ pāpāḥ paradārabhujaśca ye ।।
tathaiva kaṇṭakairderghairāyasaiḥ paśya śālmalim ।
āropitā vibhinnāṅgāḥ prabhūtāsṛkstravāvilāḥ ।।
mūṣāyāmapi paśyaitān nāśyamānān yamānugaiḥ ।
puruṣaiḥ puruṣāvyāghra ! paradārāvamarṣiṇaḥ ।।
upādyāyamadhaḥ kṛtvā stabdho yo adhyayanaṃ naraḥ ।
gṛhṇāti śilpamathavā so apyevaṃ śirasā śilām ।।
bibhrat kleśamavāpnoti janamārge atipīḍitaḥ ।
kṣutkṣāmo aharniśaṃ bhārapīḍāvyathitamastakaḥ ।।
mūtra-śleṣma-pūrīṣāṇi yairutsṛṣṭāni vāriṇi ।
ta ime śleṣmaviṇmūtra-durgandhaṃ narakaṃ gatāḥ ।।
parasparañca māṃsāni bhakṣyanti kṣudhānvitāḥ ।
bhuktaṃ nātithyavidhinā pūrvamebhaiḥ parasparam ।।
apaviddhāstu yairvedā vahanayaścāhitāgnibhiḥ ।
ta ime śālaśṛṅgāgrāt pātyante adhaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
punarbhūpatayo jīrṇā yāvajjīvanti ye narāḥ ।
ime kṛmitvamāpannā bhakṣyante atra pipīlikaiḥ ।।
patitapratigrahādānādyajanānnityasevanāt ।
pāṣāṇamadhyakīṭatvaṃ naraḥ satatamaśnute ।।
paśyato bhṛtyavargasya mitrāṇāmatithestathā ।
eko miṣṭānnabhug bhuṅkte jvaladaṅgārasañcayam ।।
vṛkairbhayaṅkaraiḥ pṛṣṭhaṃ nityamasyopabhujyate ।
pṛṣṭhamāṃsaṃ nṛpaitena yato lokasya bhakṣitam ।।
andho atha badhiro mūko bhrāmyate ayaṃ kṣudhāturaḥ ।
akṛtajño adhamaḥ puṃsāmupakāreṣu vartatām ।।
ayaṃ kṛtaghro mitrāṇāmapakārī sudurmatiḥ ।
tatpakumbhe nipatati tato yāsyati peṣaṇam ।।
karambhavālukāṃ tasmāt tato yantrānapīḍanam ।
asipatravanaṃ tasmāt karapatreṇa pāṭanam ।।
kālasūtre tathā chedamanekāścaiva yātanāḥ ।
prāpya niṣkṛtimetasmānna vedmi kathameṣyati ।।
śrāddhasaṅgatino viprāḥ samutpatya parasparam ।
duṣṭā hi niḥ sṛtaṃ phenaṃ sarvāṅgebhyaḥ pibanti vai ।।
suvarṇasteyī vipraghraḥ surāpī gurutalpagaḥ ।
adhaścordhvañca dīptāgnau dahyamānāḥ samantataḥ ।।
tiṣṭhantyabdasahasrāṇi subahūni tataḥ punaḥ ।
jāyante mānavāḥ kuṣṭha-kṣayarogādicihnatāḥ ।।
mṛtāḥ punaśca narakaṃ punarjātāśca tādṛśam ।
vyādhimṛcchanti kalpāntaparimāṇaṃ narādhipa ।।
goghro nyūrataraṃ yāti narake atha trijanmani ।
tathopapātakānāñca sarveṣāmiti niścayaḥ ।।
narakapracyutā yāni yairyairvihitapātakaiḥ ।
prayānti yonijātāni tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe jaḍopākhyāne yamakiṅkarasaṃvādo nāma caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ

pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ

yamakiṅkara uvāca

patitāt pratigṛhyārthaṃ kharayoniṃ vrajed dvijaḥ ।
narakāt pratimuktastu kṛmiḥ patitayājakaḥ ।।
upādhyāyavyalīkantu kṛtvā śvā bhavati dvijaḥ ।
tajjāyāṃ manasāvāñchan taddravyañcāpyasaṃśayam ।।
gardabho jāyate jantuḥ pitroścāpyavamānakaḥ ।
mātāpitarāvākruśya śārikā samprajāyate ।।
bhrātuḥ patnyavamantā ca kapotatvaṃ prapadyate ।
tāmeva pīḍayitvā tu kacchapatvaṃ prapadyate ।।
bhartṛpiṇḍamupāśnan yastadiṣṭaṃ na niṣevate ।
so api mohasamāpanno jāyate vānaro mṛtaḥ ।।
nyāsāpahartā narakādvimukto jāyate kṛmiḥ ।
asūyakaśca narakānmukto bhavati rākṣasaḥ ।।
viśvāsahantā ca naro mīnayonau prajāyate ।
dhānyaṃ yavāṃstilān māṣān kulatthān sarṣapāṃścaṇān ।।
kalāyāna kalamān mudgān godhūmānatasīstathā ।
śasyānyanyāni vā hṛtvā mohājjanturacetanaḥ ।।
sañjāyate mahāvaktro mūṣiko babhrusannibhaḥ ।
paradārābhimarṣāttu vṛko ghoro abhijāyate ।।
śvā śṛgālo vako gṛdhro vyāḍaḥ kaṅkastathā kramāt ।
bhrātṛbhāryāñca durbuddhiryo dharṣayati pāpakṛt ।।
puṃskokilatvamāpnoti sa cāpi narakāccyutaḥ ।
sakhibhāryāṃ gurorbhāryāṃ rājabhāryāñca pāpakṛt ।।
pradharṣayitvā kāmātmā śūkaro jāyate naraḥ ।
yajña-dāna-vivāhānāṃ vighrakartā bhavet kṛmiḥ ।।
punardāt ca kanyāyāḥ kṛmirevopajāyate ।
devatā-pitṛ-viprāṇāmadatvā yo annamaśnute ।।
pramukto narakāt so api vāyasaḥ samprajāyate ।
jyeṣṭhaṃ pitṛsamaṃ vāpi bhrātaraṃ yo avamanyate ।।
narakāt so api vibhraṣṭaḥ krauñcayonau prajāyate ।
śūdraśca brāhmaṇariṃ gatvā kṛmiyonau prajāyate ।।
tasyāmapatyamutpādya kāṣṭhāntaḥ kīṭako bhavet ।
śūkaraḥ kṛmiko madguścaṇḍālaśca prajāyate ।।
akṛtajño adhamaḥ puṃsāṃ vimukto narakānnaraḥ ।
kṛtaghraḥ kṛmikaḥ kīṭaḥ pataṅgo vṛścikastathā ।।
matsyastu vāyasaḥ kūrmaḥ pukkaso jāyate tataḥ ।
aśastraṃ puruṣaṃ hatvā naraḥ sañjāyate kharaḥ ।।
kṛmiḥ strīvadhakartā ca bālahantā ca jāyate ।
bhojanaṃ corayitvā tu makṣikā jāyate naraḥ ।।
tatrāpyasti viśeṣo vai bhojanasya śṛṇuṣva tat ।
htvānnantu sa mārjāro jāyate narakāccyutaḥ ।।
tilapiṇyākasaṃmiśramannaṃ hṛtvā tu mūṣikaḥ ।
ghṛtaṃ hṛtvā ca nakulaḥ kāko madgurajāmiṣam ।।
matsyamāṃsāpahṛt kākaḥ śyeno mārgāmiṣāpahṛt ।
vīcīkākastvapahṛte lavaṇe dadhani kṛmiḥ ।।
corayitvā payaścāpi balākā samprajāyate ।
yastu corayate tailaṃ tailapāyī sa jāyate ।।
madhu hṛtvā naro daṃśaḥ pūpaṃ hṛtvā pipīlikaḥ ।
corayitvā tu niṣpāvān jāyate gṛhagolakaḥ ।।
āsavaṃ corayitvā tu tittiritvamavāpnuyāt ।
ayo hṛtvā tu pāpātmā vāyasaḥ samprajāyate ।।
hṛte kāṃsye ca hārītaḥ kapoto rupyabhājane ।
hṛtvā tu kāñcanaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ kṛmiyonau prajāyate ।।
patrorṇaṃ corayitvā tu krakaratvañca gacchati ।
koṣakāraśca kauṣeye hṛte vastre abhijāyate ।।
dukūle śārṅgakaḥ pāpo hṛte caivāṃśuke śukaḥ ।
tathaivājāvikaṃ hṛtvā vastraṃ kṣaumaṃ ca jāyate ।।
kārpāsike hṛte krauñco vālkahartā bakastathā ।
mayūro varṇakān hṛtvā śākapatraṃ ca jāyate ।।
jīvajjīvakatāṃ yāti raktavastrāpahṛnnaraḥ ।
chucchundariḥ śubhān gandhān vāso hṛtvā śaśo bhavet ।।
ṣaṇḍhaḥ phalāpaharaṇāt kāṣṭhasya ghuṇakīṭakaḥ ।
puṣpāpahṛd daridraśca paṅguryānāpahṛnnaraḥ ।।
śākahartā ca hārītastoyahartā ca cātakaḥ ।
bhūhartā narakān gatvā rauravādīn sudāruṇān ।।
tṛṇa-gulma-latā-valli-tvaksāratarutāṃ kramāt ।
prāpya kṣīṇālpapāpastu naro bhavati vai tataḥ ।।
kṛmiḥ kīṭaḥ pataṅgo atha pakṣī toya caro mṛgaḥ ।
gotvaṃ prāpya ca caṇḍāla-pukkasādi jugupsitam ।।
paṅgvandho vadhiraḥ kuṣṭhī yakṣmaṇā ca prapīḍitaḥ ।
mukharogākṣirogaiśca gudarogaiśca bādhyate ।।
apasmārī ca bhavati śūdratvaṃ ca sa gacchati ।
eṣa eva kramo dṛṣṭo gosuvarṇāpahāriṇām ।।
vidyāpahāriṇaścogrā niṣkrayabhraṃśino guroḥ ।
jāyāmanyasya puruṣaḥ pārakhyāṃ pratipādayan ।।
prāpnoti ṣaṇḍhatāṃ mūḍho yātanābhyaḥ paricyutaḥ ।
yaḥ karoti naro homamasamiddhe vibhāvasau ।।
so ajirṇavyādhiduḥ khārto mandāgniḥ saṃprajāyate ।
paranindā kṛtaghratvaṃ paramarmāvaghaṭṭanam ।।
naiṣṭhuryaṃ nirghṛṇatvañca paradāropasevanam ।
parasvaharaṇāśaucaṃ devatānāñca kutsanam ।।
nikṛtyā kañcanaṃ nṛṇāṃ kārpaṇyaṃ ca nṛṇāṃ vadhaḥ ।
yāni ca pratiṣiddhāni tatpravṛttiśca santatā ।।
upalakṣyāṇi jānīyānmuktānāṃ narakādanu ।
dayā bhūteṣu saṃvādaḥ paralokapratikriyā ।।
satyaṃ bhūtahitārthoktirvedaprāmāṇyadarśanam ।
guru-devarṣi-siddharṣipūjanaṃ sādhusaṅgamaḥ ।।
satkriyābhāyasanaṃ maitrīmiti budhyate paṇḍitaḥ ।
anyāni caiva saddharmaṅkriyābhūtāni yāni ca ।।
svargacyutānāṃ liṅgāni puruṣāṇāmapāpinām ।
etaduddeśato rājan bhavataḥ kathitaṃ mayā ।।
svakarmaphalabhoktṝṇāṃ puṇyānāṃ pāpināṃ tathā ।
tadehyanyatra gacchāmo dṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ tvayādhunā ।
tvayā dṛṣṭo hi narakastadehyanyatra gamyatām ।।

putra uvāca

tatastamagrataḥ kṛtvā sa rājā gantumudyataḥ ।
tataśca sarvairutkruṣṭaṃ yātanāsthāyibhirnṛbhiḥ ।।
prasādaṃ kuru bhūpeti tiṣṭha tāvanmuhūrtakam ।
tvadaṅgasaṅgī pavano mano hlādayate hi naḥ ।।
paritāpañca gātrebhyaḥ pīḍābādhāśca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।
apahanti naravyāghra yadāṃ kura mahīpate ।।
etacchrutvā vacasteṣāṃ taṃ yāmyapuruṣaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
papraccha kathameteṣāmāhlādo mayi tiṣṭhati ।।
kiṃ mayā karma tat puṇyaṃ martyaloke mahat kṛtam ।
āhlādadāyinī vyuṣṭiryeneyaṃ tadudīraya ।।

yamapuruṣa uvāca

pitṛdevātithipraiṣya-śiṣṭenānnena te tanuḥ ।
puṣṭimabhyāgatā yasmāt tadgataṃ ca mano yataḥ ।।
tatastvadgātrasaṃsargo pavano hlādadāyakaḥ ।
pāpakarmakṛto rājan yātanā na prabādhate ।।
aśvamedhādayo yajñāstvayeṣṭā vidhivadyataḥ ।
tatastvaddarśanādyāmyā yantraśastrāgnivāyasāḥ ।।
pīḍana-ccheda-dāhādi-mahāduḥ khasya hetavaḥ ।
mṛdutvamāgatā rājan tejasāpahatāstava ।।

rājovāca

na svarge brahmaloke vā tat sukhaṃ prāpyate naraiḥ ।
yadārtajantunirvāṇa-dānotthamiti me matiḥ ।।
yadi matsannidhāvetān yātanā na prabādhate ।
tato bhadramukhātrāhaṃ sthāsye sthāṇurivācalaḥ ।।

yamapuruṣa uvāca

ehi rājan pragacchāmo nijapuṇyasamarjitān ।
bhuṅkṣva bhogānapāsyeha yātanāḥ pāpakarmaṇām ।।

rājovāca

tasmānna tāvadyāsyāmi yāvadete suduḥ khitāḥ ।
matsannidhānāt sukhino bhavanti narakaukasaḥ ।।
dhik tasya jīvanaṃ puṃsaḥ śaraṇārthinamāturam ।
yo nārtamanugṛhṇāti vairipakṣamapi dhruvam ।।
yajña-dāna-tapāṃsīha paratra ca na bhūtaye ।
bhavanti tasya yasyārta-paritrāṇe na mānasam ।।
narasya yasya kaṭhinaṃ mano bālāturādiṣu ।
vṛddheṣu ca na taṃ manye mānuṣaṃ rākṣaso hi saḥ ।।
eteṣāṃ sannikarṣāt tu yadyagniparitāpajam ।
tathogragandhajaṃ vāpi duḥ khaṃ narakasambhavam ।।
kṣutpipāsābhavaṃ duḥ khaṃ yacca mūrcchāpradaṃ mahat ।
eteṣāṃ trāṇadānantu manye svargasukhāt param ।।
prāpsyantyārtā yadi sukhaṃ bahavo duḥ khite mayi ।
kinnu prāptaṃ mayā na syāt tasmāt tvaṃ vraja māciram ।।

yamapuruṣa uvāca

eṣa dharmaśca śakraśca tvāṃ netuṃ samupāgatau ।
avaśyamasmād gantavyaṃ tasmāt pārthiva ! gamyatām ।।

dharma uvāca

nayāmi tvāmahaṃ svargaṃ tvayā samyagupāsitaḥ ।
vimānametadāruhya mā vilambasva gamyatām ।।

rājovāca

narake mānavā dharma pīḍyante atra sahasraśaḥ ।
trāhīti cārtāḥ krandanti māmato na vrajāmyaham ।।

indra uvāca

karmaṇā narakaprāptireteṣāṃ pāpakarmiṇām ।
svargastvayāpi gantavyo nṛpa ! puṇyena karmaṇā ।।

rājovāca

yadi jānāsi dharma ! tvaṃ tvaṃ vā śakra ! śacīpate ।
mama yāvat pramāṇantu śubhaṃ tadvaktumarhathaḥ ।।

dharma uvāca

abbindavo yathāmbhodhau yathā vā divi tārakāḥ ।
yathā vā varṣatā dhārā gaḍgāyāṃ sikatā yathā ।।
asaṃkhyeyā mahārāja yathā bindvādayo hyapām ।
tathā tavāpi puṇyasya saṃkhyā naivopapadyate ।।
anukampāmimāmadya nārakeṣviha kurvataḥ ।
tadeva śatasāhastraṃ saṃkhyāmupagataṃ tava ।।
tad gaccha tvaṃ nṛpaśreṣṭha tadbhāktumamarālayam ।
ete api pāpaṃ narake kṣapayantu svakarmajam ।।

rājovāca

kathaṃ spṛhāṃ kariṣyanti matsamparkeṣu mānavāḥ ।
yadi satsannidhāveṣāmukatkarṣo nopajāyate ।।
tasmādyat sukṛtaṃ kiñcinmamāsti tridaśādhipa ।
tena mucyantu narakāt pāpino yātanāṃ gatāḥ ।।

indra uvāca

evamūrdhvataraṃ sthānaṃ tvayāvāptaṃ mahīpate ।
etāṃśca narakāt paśya vimuktān pāpakāriṇaḥ ।।

putra uvāca

tato apatat puṣpavṛṣṭistasyopari mahīpateḥ ।
vimānañcādhiropyainaṃ svarlokamanayaddhariḥ ।।
ahañcānye ca ye tatra yātanābhyaḥ paricyutāḥ ।
svakarmaphalanirdiṣṭaṃ tato jātyantaraṃ gatāḥ ।।
evamete samākhyātā narakā dvijasattama ।
yena yena ca pāpena yāṃ yāṃ yonimupaiti vai ।।
tat tat sarvaṃ samākhyātaṃ yathā dṛṣṭaṃ mayā purā ।
purānubhavajaṃ jñānamavāpyāvitathaṃ tava ।
ataḥ paraṃ mahābhāga kimanyat kathayāmi te ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe pitāputrasaṃvādo nāma pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ

ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ

pitāvāca

kathitaṃ me tvayā vatsa saṃsārasya vyavasthitam ।
svarūpamatiheyasya ghaṭīyantravadavyayam ।।
tadevametadakhilaṃ mayāvagatamīdṛśam ।
kiṃ mayā vada kartavyamevasmin vyavasthite ।।
putra uvāca

yadi madvacanaṃ tāta śraddadhāsyaviśaṅkitaḥ ।
tat parityajya gārhasthyaṃ vānaprasthaparo bhava ।।
tamanuṣṭhāya vidhivad vihāyāgniparigraham ।
ātmanyātmānamādhayā nirdvandvo niṣparigrahaḥ ।।
ekāntarāśī vaśyātmā bhava bhikṣuratandritaḥ ।
tatra yogāparo bhūtvā bāhyasparśavivarjitaḥ ।।
tataḥ prāpsyati taṃ yogaṃ duḥ śasaṃyogabheṣajam ।
muktihetumanaupamyamanākhyeyamasaṅginam ।
yatsaṃyogānna te yogo bhūyo bhūtairbhaviṣyati ।।

pitāvāca

vatsa yogaṃ mamācakṣva muktihetumataḥ param ।
yena bhūtaiḥ punarbhūto nedṛgaḥ khamavāpnuyām ।।
yatrāsaktiparasyātmā mama saṃsārabandhanaiḥ ।
naiti yogamayogo api taṃ yogamadhunā vada ।।
saṃsārādityatāpārti-vipluṣyaddehamānasam ।
brahmajñānāmbuśītena siñca māṃ vākyavāriṇā ।।
avidyākṛṣṇasarpeṇa daṣṭaṃ tadviṣapīḍitam ।
svavākyāmṛtapānena māṃ jīvaya punarmṛtam ।।
putra-dāra-gṛha-kṣetra-mamatvanigajaḍārditam ।
māṃ mocayeṣṭasadbhāva-vijñānodghāṭanaistvaran ।।

putra uvāca

śṛṇu tāta ! yathā yogo dattātreyeṇa dhīmatā ।
alarkāya purā proktaḥ samyak pṛṣṭena vistarāt ।।

pitovāca

dattātreyaḥ sutaḥ kasya kathaṃ vā yogamuktavān ।
kaścālarko mahābhāgo yo yaugaṃ paripṛṣṭavān ।।

putra uvāca

kauśiko brāhmaṇaḥ kaścit pratiṣṭhāne abhavat pure ।
so anyajanmakṛtaiḥ pāpaiḥ kuṣṭharogāturo abhavat ।।
taṃ tathā vyādhitaṃ bhāryā patiṃ devamivārccayat ।
pādābhyaṅgāṅgasaṃvāha-strānācchādanabhojanaiḥ ।।
śleṣma-mūtra-purīṣāsṛk-pravāhakṣālanena ca ।
rahaścaivopacāreṇa priyasambhāṣaṇena ca ।।
sa tayā pūjyamāno api sadātīva vinītayā ।
atīva tīvrakopatvānnirbhartsayati niṣṭhuraḥ ।।
tathāpi praṇatā bhāryā tamamanyata daivatam ।
taṃ tathāpyatibībhatsaṃ sarvaśreṣṭhamamanyata ।।
acaṅkramaṇaśolo api sa kadācid dvijottamaḥ ।
prāha bhāryāṃ nayasveti tvaṃ māṃ tasyā niveśanam ।।
yā sā veśyā mayā dṛṣṭā rājamārge gṛhoṣitā ।
tāṃ māṃ prāpaya dharmajñe ! saiva me hṛdi vartate ।।
dṛṣṭā sūryodaye bālā rātriśceyamupāgatā ।
darśanānantaraṃ sā me hṛdayānnāpasarpati ।।
yadi sā cārusarvāṅgī pīnaśroṇipayodharā ।
nopagūhati tanvaṅgī tanmāṃ drakṣyasi vai mṛtam ।।
vāmaḥ kāmo manuṣyāṇāṃ bahubhiḥ prārthyate ca sā ।
mamāśaktiśca gamane saṅkulaṃ pratibhāti me ।।
tat tadā vacanaṃ śrutvā bhartuḥ kāmāturasya sā ।
tatpatnī satkulotpannā mahābhāgā pativratā ।।
gāgṃ parikaraṃ baddhvā śulkamādāya cādhikam ।
skandhe bhartāramādāya jagāma mṛdugāminī ।।
niśi meghāstṛte vyomni caladvidyutpradarśite ।
rājamārge priyaṃ bhartuścikīrṣantī dvijāṅganā ।।
pathi śūle tathā protamacauraṃ yauraśaṅkayā ।
māṇḍavyamatiduḥ khārtamandhakāre atha sa dvijaḥ ।।
patnīskandhe samārūḍhaścālayāmāsa kauśikaḥ ।
pādāvamarṣaṇāt kruddho māṇḍavyastamuvāca ha ।।
yenāhamevamatyarthaṃ duḥ khitaścālitaḥ padā ।
daśāṃ kaṣṭāmanuprāptaḥ sa pāpātmā narādhamaḥ ।।
sūryodaye avaśaḥ prāṇairvimokṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।
bhāskarālokanādeva sa vināśamavāpsyati ।।
tasya bhāryātataḥ śrutvā taṃ śāpamatidāruṇam ।
provāca vyathitā sūryo naivodayamupaiṣyati ।।
tataḥ sūryodayābhāvādabhavat santatā niśā ।
bahūnyahaḥ pramāṇāni tato devā bhayaṃ yayuḥ ।।
niḥ svādhyāyavaṣaṭkāra-svadhāsvāhāvivarjitam ।
kathaṃ nu khalvidaṃ sarvaṃ na gacchet saṃkṣayaṃ jagat ।।
ahorātravyavasthāyā vinā māsartusaṃkṣayaḥ ।
tatsaṃkṣayānna tvayane jñāyete dakṣiṇottare ।।
vinā cāyanavijñānāt kālaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ kutaḥ ।
saṃvatsaraṃ vinā nānyat kālajñānaṃ pravartate ।।
pativratāyā vacasā nodgacchati divākaraḥ ।
sūryodayaṃ vinā naiva strānadānādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
nāgnerviharaṇañcaiva krātvabhāvaśca lakṣyate ।
naivāpyayanamasmākaṃ vinā homena jāyate ।।
vayamāpyāyitā martyairyajñabhāgairyathocitaiḥ ।
vṛṣṭyā tānanugṛhṇīmo martyān śasyādisiddhaye ।।
niṣpāditāsvoṣadhīṣu martyā yajñairyajanti naḥ ।
teṣāṃ vayaṃ prayacchāmaḥ kāmān yajñādipūjitāḥ ।।
adho hi varṣāma vayaṃ martyāścordhvapravarṣiṇaḥ ।
toyavarṣeṇa hi vayaṃ havirvarṣeṇa mānavāḥ ।।
ye nāsmākaṃ prayacchanti nityanaimittakīḥ kriyāḥ ।
kratubhāgaṃ durātmānaḥ svayañcāśnanti lolupāḥ ।।
vināśāya vayaṃ teṣāṃ toyasūryāgnimārutān ।
kṣitiñca sandūṣayāmaḥ pāpānāmapakāriṇām ।।
duṣṭatoyādibhogena teṣāṃ duṣkṛtakarmiṇām ।
upasargāḥ pravartante maraṇāya sudāruṇāḥ ।।
ye tvasmān prīṇayitvā tu bhuñjate śeṣamātmanā ।
teṣāṃ puṇyān vayaṃ yokān vidadhāma mahātmanām ।।
tannāsti sarvamevaitadvinaiṣāṃ vyuṣṭisaṃsthaitam ।
kathaṃ nu dinasargaḥ syādanyo anyamavadan surāḥ ।।
teṣāmeva sametānāṃ yajñavyucchittiśaṅkinām ।
devānāṃ vacanaṃ śrutvā prāha devaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
tejaḥ paraṃ tejasaiva tapasā ca tapastathā ।
praśāmyate amarāstasmācchṛṇudhvaṃ vacanaṃ mama ।।
pativratāyā māhātmyānnodgacchati divākaraḥ ।
tasya cānudayāddhānirmartyānāṃ bhavatāṃ tathā ।।
tasmāt pativratāmatreranubhūyāṃ tapasvinīm ।
prasādayata vai patnīṃ bhānorudayakāmyayā ।।

putra uvāca

taiḥ sā prasāditā gatvā proheṣṭaṃ vriyatāmiti ।
ayācanta dinaṃ devā bhavatviti yathā purā ।।
anasūyovāca

pativratāyā māhātmyaṃ na hīyeta kathantviti ।
saṃmānya tasmāt tāṃ sādhvīmahaḥ strakṣyāmyahaṃ surāḥ ।।
yathā punarahorātra-saṃsthānamupajāyate ।
yathā ca tasyāḥ svapatirna sādhvyā nāśameṣyati ।।

putra uvāca

evamuktvā surāṃstasyā gatvā sā mandiraṃ śubhā ।
uvāca kuśalaṃ pṛṣṭā dharmaṃ bhartustathātmanaḥ ।।

anasūyovāca

kaccinnandasi kalyāṇi svabharturmukhadarśanāt ।
kacciccākhiladevebhyo manyase abhyadhikaṃ patim ।।
bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇādeva mayā prāptaṃ mahat phalam ।
sarvakāmaphalāvāptyā pratyūhāḥ parivartitāḥ ।।
pañcarṇāni manuṣyeṇa sādhvi ! deyāni sarvadā ।
tathātmavarṇadharmeṇa kartavyo dhanasaṃcayaḥ ।।
prāptaścārthastataḥ pātre viniyojyo vidhānataḥ ।
satyārjava-tapo-dānairdayāyukto bhavet sadā ।।
kriyāśca śāstranirdiṣṭā rāgadveṣavivarjitāḥ ।
kartavyā anvahaṃ śraddhā-puraskāreṇa śaktitaḥ ।।
svajātivihitāneva lokānāpnoti mānavaḥ ।
kleśena mahatā sādhvi ! prājāpatyādikān kramāt ।।
striyastvevaṃ samastasya narairduḥ khārjitasya vai ।
puṇyasyārdhāpahāriṇyaḥ patiśuśrūṣayaiva hi ।।
nāsti strīṇāṃ pṛthagyajño na śrāddhaṃ nāpyupoṣitam ।
bhartṛśuśrūṣayaivaitān lokāniṣṭān vrajanti hi ।।
tasmāt sādhvi ! mahābhāge ! patiśuśrūṣaṇaṃ prati ।
tvayā matiḥ sadā kāryā yato bhartā parā gatiḥ ।।
yaddevebhyo yacca pitrāgatebhyaḥ
kuryādbhartābhyarccanaṃ satkriyātaḥ ।
tasyāpyardhaṃ kevalānanyacittā
nārī bhuṅkte bhartṛśuśrūṣayaiva ।।

putra uvāca

tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā pratipūjya tathādarāt ।
pratyuvācātripatnīṃ tāmanasūyāmidaṃ vacaḥ ।।
dhanyāsmyanugṛhītāsmi devaiścāpyavalokitā ।
yanme prakṛtikalyāṇi ! śraddhāṃ vardhayase punaḥ ।।
jānāmyetanna nārīṇāṃ kācit patisamā gatiḥ ।
tatprītiścopakārāya iha loke paratra ca ।।
patiprasādādiha ca pretya caiva yaśasvini ।
nārī sukhamavāpnoti nāryā bhartā hi devatā ।।
sā tvaṃ brūhi mahābhāge ! prāptāyā mama mandiram ।
āryāyā yanmayā kāryaṃ tathāryeṇāpi vā śubhe ।।

anasūyovāca

ete devāḥ sahendreṇa māmupāgamya duḥ khitāḥ ।
tvadvākhyāpāstasatkarmadinanaktanirūpaṇāḥ ।।
yācante aharniśāsaṃsthāṃ yathāvadavikhaṇḍitām ।
ahaṃ tadarthamāyātā śṛṇu caitadvaco mama ।।
dinābhāvāt samastānāmabhāvo yāgakarmaṇām ।
tadabhāvāt surāḥ puṣṭiṃ nopayānti tapasvini ।।
ahnaścaiva samucchedāducchedaḥ sarvakarmaṇām ।
taducchedādanāvṛṣṭyā jagaducchedameṣyati ।।
tat tvamicchasi cedetat jagaduddhartumāpadaḥ ।
prasīda sādhvi ! lokānāṃ pūrvavaddhartatāṃ raviḥ ।।

brāhmaṇyuvāca

māṇḍavyena mahābhāge ! śapto bhartā mameśvaraḥ ।
sūryodaye vināśaṃ tvaṃ prāpsyasītyatimanyunā ।।

anasūyovāca

yadi vā rocate bhadre ! tatastvadvacanādaham ।
karomi pūrvavaddehaṃ bhartārañca navaṃ tava ।।
mayā hi sarvathā strīṇāṃ māhātmyaṃ varavarṇini ।
pativratānāmārādhyamiti saṃmānayāmi te ।।

putra uvāca

tathetyukte tayā sūryamājuhāva tapasvinī ।
anasūyārghyamudyamya daśarātre tadā niśi ।।
tato vivasvān bhagavān phullapadmāruṇākṛtiḥ ।
śailarājānamudayamārurohorumaṇḍalaḥ ।।
samanantaramevāsyā bhartā prāṇairvyayujyata ।
papata ca mahīpṛṣṭhe patantaṃ jagṛhe ca sā ।।

anasūyovāca

na viṣādastvayā bhadre ! kartavyaḥ paśya me balam ।
patiśuśrūṣayāvāptaṃ tapasaḥ kiṃ cireṇa te ।।
yathā bhartṛsamaṃ nānyamapaśyaṃ puruṣaṃ kvacit ।
rūpataḥ śīlato buddhyā vāṅmādhurṃyyādibhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।
tena satyena vipro ayaṃ vyādhimuktaḥ punaryuvā ।
prāpnotu jīvitaṃ bhāryāsahāyaḥ śaradāṃ śatam ।।
yathā bhartṛsamaṃ nānyamahaṃ paśyāmi daivatam ।
tena satyena vipro ayaṃ punarjovatvanāmayaḥ ।।
karmaṇā manasā vācā bharturārādhanaṃ prati ।
yathā mamodyamo nityaṃ tathāyaṃ jīvatāṃ dvijaḥ ।।

putra uvāca

tato vipraḥ samuttasthau vyādhimuktaḥ punaryuvā ।
svabhābhirbhāsayan veśma vṛndāraka ivājaraḥ ।।
tato apatat puṣpavṛṣṭirdevavādyādinisvanaḥ ।
lebhire ca mudaṃ devā anasūyāmathābruvan ।।

devā ūcuḥ

varaṃ vṛṇīṣva kalyāṇi devakāryaṃ mahat kṛtam ।
tvayā yasmāt tato devā varadāste tapasvini ।।

anasūyovāca

yadi devāḥ prasannā me pitāmahapurogamāḥ ।
varadā varayogyā ca yadyahaṃ bhavatāṃ matā ।।
tadyāntu mama putratvaṃ brahma-viṣṇu-maheśvarāḥ ।
yogañca prāpnuyāṃ bhartṛsahitā kleśamuktaye ।।
evamastviti tāṃ devā brahma-viṣṇu-śivādayaḥ ।
proktvā jagmuryathānyāyamanumānya tapasvinīm ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe pitāputrasaṃvāde anasūyāvaraprāptirnāma ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ

saptadaśo adhyāyaḥ

putra uvāca

tataḥ kāle bahutithe dvitīyo brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।
svabhāryāṃ bhagavānatriranasūyāmapaśyata ।।
ṛtusnātāṃ sucārvaṅgīṃ lobhanīyottamākṛtim ।
sakāmo manasā bheje sa munistāmaninditām ।।
tasyābhidhyāyatastāntu vikāro yo anvajāyata ।
tamevovāha pavanastiraścordhvañca vegavān ।।
brahmarūpañca śuklābhaṃ patamānaṃ samantataḥ ।
somarūpaṃ rajopetaṃ diśastaṃ jagṛhurdaśa ।।
sa somo mānaso jajñe tasyāmatreḥ prajāpateḥ ।
putraḥ samastasattvānāmāyurādhāra eva ca ।।
tuṣṭena viṣṇunā jajñe dattātreyo mahātmanā ।
svaśarīrāt samutpādya sattvodrikto dvijāttamaḥ ।।
dattātreya iti khyātaḥ so anasūyāstanaṃ papau ।
viṣṇurevāvatīrṇo asau dvitīyo atreḥ suto abhavat ।।
saptāhāt pracyuto māturudarāt kupito yataḥ ।
haihayendramupāvṛttamaparādhyantamuddhatam ।।
dṛṣṭvātrau kupitaḥ sadyo dagdhukāmaḥ sa haihayam ।
garbhavāsamahāyāsa-duḥ khāmarṣasamanvitaḥ ।।
durvāsāstamasodrikto rudrāṃśaḥ samajāyata ।
iti putratrayaṃ tasyā jajñe brahmeśavaiṣṇavam ।।
somo brahmabhavadviṣṇurdattātreyo vyajāyata ।
durvāsāḥ śaṅkaro jajñe varadānāddivaukasām ।।
somaḥ svaraśmibhaiḥ śītairvorudhauṣadhimānavān ।
āpyāyayan sadā svarge vartate sa prajāpatiḥ ।।
dattātreyaḥ prajāṃ pāti duṣṭadaityanibarhaṇāt ।
śiṣṭānugrahakṛcceti jñeyaścāṃśaḥ sa vaiṣṇavaḥ ।।
nirdahatyavamantāraṃ durvāsā bhagavānajaḥ ।
raudraṃ samāśritya vapurdṛṅmanovāgbhiruddhataḥ ।।
somatvaṃ bhagavānatraiḥ punaścakre prajāpatiḥ ।
dattātreyo api viṣayān yogāstho bubhuje hariḥ ।।
durvāsāḥ pitaraṃ hitvā mātarañcottama vratam ।
unmattākhyaṃ samāśritya paribabhrāma medinīm ।।
muniputravṛto yogī dattātreyo apyasaṅgitām ।
abhīpsyamānaḥ sarasi nimamajja ciraṃ prabhuḥ ।।
tathāpi taṃ mahātmānamatīva priyadarśanam ।
tatyajurna kumārāste sarasastīramāśritāḥ ।।
divye varṣaśate pūrṇe yadā te na tyajanti tam ।
tatprītyā sarasastīraṃ sarve munikumārakāḥ ।।
tato divyāmbaradharāṃ cārupīnanitambinīm ।
nārīmādāya kalyāṇīmuttitāra jalānmuniḥ ।।
strīsannikarṣādyadyete parityakṣyanti māmiti ।
muniputrāstato asaṅgī sthāsyāmīti vicintayan ।।
tathāpi taṃ munisutā na tyajanti yadā munim ।
tataḥ saha tayā nāryā madyapānamathāpibat ।।
surāpānarataṃ te na sabhāryaṃ tatyajustataḥ ।
gītavādyādivanitā-bhogasaṃsargadūṣitam ।।
manyamānā mahātmānaṃ pītāsava-savikriyam ।
nāvāpa doṣaṃ yogīśo vāruṇīṃ sa pibannapi ।।
antāvasāyiveśmāntarmātariśvā vasanniva ।
surāṃ piban sapatnīkastapastepe sa yogavit ।
yogīśvāraścintyamāno yogibhirmuktikāṅkṣibhiḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍepurāṇe pitāputrasaṃvāde dattātreyotpattirnāma saptadaśo adhyāyaḥ

aṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ

putra uvāca
kasyacittvatha kālasya kṛtavīryātmajor'junaḥ ।
kṛtavīrye divaṃ yāte mantribhiḥ sapurohitaiḥ ।।
pauraiścātmābhiṣekārthaṃ samāhūto abravīdidam ।
nāhaṃ rājyaṃ kariṣyāmi mantriṇo narakottaram ।।
yadarthaṃ gṛhyate śulkaṃ tadaniṣpādayan vṛthā ।
paṇyānāṃ dvādaśaṃ bhāgaṃ bhūpālāya vaṇigjanaḥ ।।
dattvārtharakṣibhirmārge rakṣito yāti dasyutaḥ ।
gopāśca ghṛtatakrādeḥ ṣaḍbhāgañca kṛṣībalāḥ ।।
dattvānyadbhūbhuje dadyuryadi bhāgaṃ tato adhikam ।
paṇyādīnāmaśeṣāṇāṃ vaṇijo gṛhṇatastataḥ ।।
iṣṭāpūrtavināśāya tadrājñaścauradharmiṇaḥ ।
yadyanyaiḥ pālyate lokastadvṛttayantarasaṃśritaiḥ ।।
gṛhṇato baliṣaḍbhāgaṃ nṛpaternarako dhruvam ।
nirūpitamidaṃ rājñaḥ pūrvai rakṣaṇavetanam ।।
arakṣaṃścaurataścauryaṃ tadeno nṛpaterbhavet ।
tasmādyadi tapastaptvā prāpto yogitvamīpsitam ।।
bhuvaḥ pālanasāmarthya-yukta eko mahīpatiḥ ।
pṛthivyāṃ śastradhṛṅmānyastvahamevardhisaṃyutaḥ ।
tato bhaviṣye nātmānaṃ kariṣye pāpabhāginam ।।

putra uvāca

tasya tanniścayaṃ jñātvā mantrimadhyasthito abravīt ।
gargo nāma mahābuddhirmuniśreṣṭho vayo atigaḥ ।।
yadyevaṃ kartukāmastvaṃ rājyaṃ samyak praśāsitum ।
tato śṛṇuṣva me vākyaṃ kuruṣva ca nṛpātmaja ।।
dattātreyaṃ mahābhāgaṃ sahyadroṇīkṛtāśrayam ।
tamārādhaya bhūpāla ! pāti yo bhuvanatrayam ।।
yogayuktaṃ mahābhāgaṃ sarvatra samadarśinam ।
viṣṇoraṃśaṃ jagaddhāturavatīrṇaṃ mahītale ।।
yamārādhya sahasrākṣaḥ prāptavān padamātmanaḥ ।
hṛtaṃ durātmabhirdaityairjaghāna ca diteḥ sutān ।।

arjuna uvāca

kathamārādhito devairdattātreyaḥ pratāpavān ।
kathañcāpahṛtaṃ daityairindratvaṃ prāpa vāsavaḥ ।।

garga uvāca

devānāṃ dānavānāñca yuddhamāsīt sudāruṇam ।
daityānāmīśvaro jambho devānāñca śacīpatiḥ ।।

teṣāñca yudhyamānānāṃ divyaḥ saṃvatsaro gataḥ ।
tato devāḥ parābhūtā daityā vijayino abhavan ।।
vipracittimukhairdevā dānavaiste parājitāḥ ।
palāyanakṛtotsāhā nirutsāhā dviṣajjaye ।।
bṛhaspatimupāgamya daityasainyavadhepsavaḥ ।
amantrayanta sahitā bālakhilyaistatharṣibhiḥ ।।

bṛhaspatiruvāca

dattātreyaṃ mahātmānamatreḥ putraṃ tapodhanam ।
vikṛtācaraṇaṃ bhaktyā santoṣayitumarhatha ।।
sa vo daityavināśāya varado dāsyate varam ।
tato haniṣyatha surā sahitā daityadānavān ।।

garga uvāca

ityuktāste tadā jagmurdattātreyāśramaṃ surāḥ ।
dadṛśuśca mahātmānaṃ taṃ te lakṣmyā samanvitam ।।
udgīyamānaṃ gandharvaiḥ surāpānarataṃ munim ।
te tasya gatvā praṇatimavadan sādhyasādhanam ।।
cakruḥ stavañcopajahrurbhakṣyabhojyastragādikam ।
tiṣṭhantamanutiṣṭhanti yāntaṃ yānti divaukasaḥ ।।
ārādhayāmāsuradhaḥ sthitāstiṣṭhantamāsane ।
sa prāha praṇatān devān dattātreyaḥ kimiṣyate ।
matto bhavadbhiryeneyaṃ śuśrūṣā kriyate mama ।।

devā ūcuḥ

dānavairmuniśārdūla ! jambhādyairbhūrbhuvādikam ।
hṛtaṃ tailokyamākramya kratubhāgāśca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।।
tadvadhe kuru buddhiṃ tvaṃ paritrāṇāya no anagha ।
tvatprasādādabhīpsāmaḥ punaḥ prāptaṃ triviṣṭapam ।।

dattātreya uvāca

madyāsakto ahamucchiṣṭo na caivāhaṃ jitendriyaḥ ।

kathamicchatha matto api devāḥ śatruparābhavam ।।

devā ūcuḥ

anaghastvaṃ jagannātha na lepastava vidyate ।
vidyākṣālanaśuddhāntarniviṣṭajñānadīdhite ! ।।

dattātreya uvāca

satyametat surā vidyā mamāsti samadarśinaḥ ।
asyāstu yoṣitaḥ saṅgādahamucchiṣṭatāṃ gataḥ ।।
strīsambhogo hi doṣāya sātatyenopasevitaḥ ।
evamuktāstato devāḥ punarvacanamabruvan ।।

devā ūcuḥ

anagheyaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha jaganmātā na duṣyate ।
yathāṃśumālā sūryasya dvija-cāṇḍālasaṅginī ।।

garga uvāca

evamuktastato devairdattātreyo abravīdidam ।
prahasya tridaśān sarvān yadyetadbhavatāṃ matam ।।
tadāhūyāsurān sarvān yuddhāya surasattamāḥ ।
ihānayata maddṛṣṭigocaraṃ mā vilambataḥ ।।
maddṛṣṭipātahutabhuk-prakṣīṇabalatejasaḥ ।
yena nāśamaśeṣāste prayānti mama darśanāt ।।

garga uvāca

tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā devairdaityā mahābalāḥ ।
āhavāya samāhūtā jagmurdevagaṇān ruṣā ।।
te hanyamānā daiteyairdevā śīghraṃ bhayāturāḥ ।
dattātreyāśramaṃ jagmuḥ sametāḥ śaraṇārthinaḥ ।।
tameva viviśurdaityāḥ kālayanto divaukasaḥ ।
dadṛśuśca mahātmānaṃ dattātreyaṃ mahābalam ।।
vāmapārśvasthitāmiṣṭāmaśeṣajagatāṃ śubhām ।
bhāryāñcāsya sucārvaṅgīṃ lakṣmīmindunibhānanām ।।
nīlotpalābhanayanāṃ pīnaśroṇipayodharām ।
gadantīṃ madhurāṃ bhāṣāṃ sarvairyoṣidguṇairyutām ।।
te tāṃ dṛṣṭvāgrato daityāḥ sābhilāṣā manobhavam ।
na śesuruddhataṃ dhairyānmanasā voḍhumāturāḥ ।।
tyaktvā devān striyaṃ tāṃ tu hartukāmā hataujasaḥ ।
tena pāpena muhyantaḥ saṃśaktāste tato abruvan ।।
stroratnametat trailokye sāraṃ no yadi vai bhavet ।
kṛtakṛtyāstataḥ sarva iti no bhāvitaṃ manaḥ ।।
tasmāt sarve samutkṣipya śivikāyāṃ surārdanāḥ ।
āropya svamadhiṣṭhānaṃ nayāma iti niścitāḥ ।।

garga uvāca

sānurāgāstataste tu proktāścettthaṃ parasparam ।
tasya tāṃ yoṣitaṃ sādhvīṃ samutkṣipya smarārditāḥ ।।
śivikāyāṃ samāropya sahitā daityadānavāḥ ।
śiraḥ su śivikāṃ kṛtvā svasthānābhimukhaṃ yayuḥ ।।
dattātreyastato devān vihasyedamathābravīt ।
diṣṭyā vardhatha daityānāmeṣā lakṣmīḥ śirogatā ।
sapta sathānānyatikrāntā navamanyamupaiṣyati ।।

devā ūcuḥ

kathayasva jagannātha ! keṣu sthāneṣvasthitā ।
puruṣasya phalaṃ kiṃ vā prayacchatyatha naśyati ।।

dattātreya uvāca
nṛṇāṃ pade sthitā lakṣmīrnilayaṃ samprayacchati ।
sakthnyośca saṃsthitā vastraṃ tathā nānāvidhaṃ vasu ।।
kalātrañca guhyasaṃsthā kroḍasthāpatyadāyinī ।
manorathān pūrayati puruṣāṇāṃ hṛdi sthitā ।।
lakṣmīrlakṣmīvatāṃ śreṣṭhā kaṇṭhasthā kaṇṭhabhūṣaṇam ।
abhīṣṭabandhudāraiśca tathāśleṣaṃ pravāsibhiḥ ।।
sṛṣṭānuvākyalāvaṇyamājñāmavitathāṃ tathā ।
mukhasaṃsthā kavitvañca yacchatyudadhisambhavā ।।
śirogatā santyajati tato anyaṃ yāti cāśrayam ।
seyaṃ śirogatā caitān parityakṣyati sāmpratam ।।
pragṛhyāstrāṇi badhyantāṃ tasmādete surārayaḥ ।
na bhetavyaṃ bhṛśañcaite mayā nistejasaḥ kṛtāḥ ।
paradārāvamarṣācca dagdhapuṇyā hataujasaḥ ।।
tataste vividhairastrairvadhyamānāḥ surārayaḥ ।
mūdhni lakṣmyā samākrāntā vineśuriti naḥ śrutam ।।
lakṣmīścītpatya samprāptā dattātreyaṃ mahāmunim ।
stūyamānā suraiḥ sarvairdaityanāśānmudānvitaiḥ ।।
praṇipatya tato devā dattātreyaṃ manīṣiṇam ।
nākapṛṣṭhamanuprāptā yathāpūrvaṃ gatajvarāḥ ।।
tathā tvamapi rojendra ! yadīcchasi yathepsitam ।
prāptumaiśvaryamatulaṃ tūrṇamārādhayasva tām ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhagargavākyam' nāmāṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ

ekonaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

putra uvāca

ityṛṣervacanaṃ śrutvā kārtavīryo nareśvaraḥ ।
dattātreyāśramaṃ gattvā taṃ bhaktyā samapūjayat ।।
pādasaṃvāhanādyena madhvādyāharaṇena ca ।
strakcandanādigandhāmbu-phalādyanayanena ca ।।
tathānnasādhanaistasya ucchiṣṭāpohanena ca ।
parituṣṭo munirbhūtaṃ tamuvāca tathaiva saḥ ।।
yathaivoktāḥ purā devā madyabhogādikutsanam ।
strī ceyaṃ mama pārśvasthetyetadbhogācca kutsitam ।।
sadaivāhaṃ na māmevamuparoddhuṃ tvamarhasi ।
aśaktamupakārāya śaktamārādhayasva bhoḥ ।।

jaḍa uvāca
tenaivamukto muninā smṛtvā gargavacaśca tat ।
pratyuvāca praṇamyainaṃ sārtavīryārjunastadā ।।

arjuna uvāca

kiṃ māṃ mohayase deva ! svāṃ māyāṃ samupāśritaḥ ।
anaghastvaṃ tathaiveyaṃ devī sarvabhavāraṇiḥ ।।
ityuktaḥ prītimān devastatastaṃ pratyuvāca ha ।
kārtavīryaṃ mahābhāgaṃ vaśīkṛtamahītalam ।।
varaṃ vṛṇīṣva guhyaṃ me yat tvayā samudīritam ।
tena tuṣṭiḥ parā jātā tvayyadya mama pārthiva ।।
ye ca māṃ pūjayiṣyanti gandhamālyādibhirnarāḥ ।
māṃsamadyopahāraiśca miṣṭānnaiścājyasaṃyutaiḥ ।।
lakṣmīsametaṃ gītaiśca brāhmaṇānāṃ tathārccanaiḥ ।
vādyairmanoramairvoṇā-veṇu-śaṅkādibhistathā ।।
teṣāmahaṃ parāṃ tuṣṭiṃ putradāradhanādikam ।
pradāsyāmyavaghātañca haniṣyāmyavamanyatām ।।
sa tvaṃ varaya bhadraṃ te varaṃ yanmasepsitam ।
prasādasumukhaste ahaṃ guhyanāmaprakīrtanāt ।।

kārtavīrya uvāca

yadi deva prasannastvaṃ tat prayacchardhimuttamām ।
yayā prajāḥ pālaye ahaṃ na cādharmamavāpnuyām ।।
parānusaraṇe jñānamapratidvandvatāṃ raṇe ।
sahasramāptumicchāmi bāhūnāṃ laghutāguṇam ।।
asaṅgā gatayaḥ santu śailākāśāmbu-bhūmiṣu ।
pātāleṣu ca sarveṣu vadhaścāpyadhikānnarāt ।।
tathonmārgapravṛttasya cāstu sanmārgadeśakaḥ ।
santu me atithayaḥ ślāghyā vittadāne tathākṣaye ।।
anaṣṭadravyatā rāṣṭre mamānusmaraṇena ca ।
tvayi bhaktirmamaivāstu nityamavyabhicāriṇī ।।

dattātreya uvāca

yatra te kīrtitāḥ sarve tān varān samavāpsyasi ।
matprasādācca bhavitā cakravarto tvamīśvaraḥ ।।

jaḍa uvāca

praṇipatya tatastasmai dattātreyāya so arjunaḥ ।
ānāyya prakṛtīḥ samyagabhiṣekamagṛhṇata ।।
āghoṣayāmāsa tadā sthito rājye sa haihayaḥ ।
dattātreyāt parāmṛddhimavāpyātibalānvitaḥ ।।
adyaprabhṛti yaḥ śastraṃ māmṛte anyo grahīṣyati ।
hantavyaḥ sa mayā dasyuḥ parihaṃsārato api vā ।।
ityājñaptena tadrāṣṭre kaścidāyudhadhṛṅnaraḥ ।
tamṛte puruṣavyāghraṃ babhūvoruparākramaḥ ।।
sa eva grāmapālo abhūt paśupālaḥ sa eva ca ।
kṣetrapālaḥ sa evāsīd dvijātīnāñca rakṣitā ।।
tapasvināṃ pālayitā sārthapālastu so abhavat ।
dsyu-vyālāgri-śastrādi-bhayeṣvabdhau nimajjatām ।।
anyāsu caiva magrānāmāpatsu paravīrahā ।
sa eva saṃsmṛtaḥ sadyaḥ samuddhartābhavannṛṇām ।।
anaṣṭadravyatā cāsīt tasmin śāsati pārthive ।
teneṣṭaṃ bahubhiryajñaiḥ samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ ।।
tenaiva ca tapastaptaṃ saṃgrāmeṣvabhiceṣṭitam ।
tasyārdhimatimānañca dṛṣṭvā prāhāṅgirā muniḥ ।।
na nūnaṃ kārtavīryasya gatiṃ yāsyanti pārthivāḥ ।
yajñairdānaistapobhirvā saṃgrāme cāticeṣcitaiḥ ।।
dattātreyāddin yasmin sa prāpardhi nareśvaraḥ ।
tasmiṃstasmin dine yāgaṃ dattātreyasya so akarot ।।
tatraiva ca prajāḥ sarvāstasminnahani bhūpateḥ ।
tasyardhi paramāṃ dṛṣṭvā yāgaṃ cakruḥ samādhinā ।।
ityetat tasya māhātmyaṃ dattātreyasya dhīmataḥ ।
viṣṇoścarācaraguroranantasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
prādurbhāvāḥ purāṇeṣu kathyante śārḍgadhanvinaḥ ।
anantasyāprameyasya śaṅkha-cakra-gadābhṛtaḥ ।।
etasya paramaṃ rūpaṃ yaścintayati mānavaḥ ।
sa sukhī sa ca saṃsārāt samuttīrṇo acirādbhavet ।।
sadaiva vaiṣṇavānāñca bhaktyāhaṃ sulabho asmi bhoḥ ।
ityevaṃ yasya vai vācastaṃ kathaṃ nāśrayejjanaḥ ।।
adharmasya vināśāya dharmācārārthameva ca ।
anādinidhano devaḥ karoti sthiti-pālanam ।।
tathaiva janma cākhyātamalarkaṃ kathayāmi te ।
tathā ca yogaḥ kathito dattātreyeṇa tasya vai ।
pitṛbhaktasya rājarṣeralarkasya mahātmanaḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe dattātreyīye ūnaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

viṃśo adhyāyaḥ

jaḍa uvāca

prāgbabhūva mahāvīryaḥ śatrujinnāma pārthivaḥ ।
tutoṣa yasya yajñeṣu somāvāptyā purandaraḥ ।।
tasyātmajo mahāvīryo babhūvārividāraṇaḥ ।
buddhi-vikrama-lāvaṇyairguruśakrāśvibhiḥ samaḥ ।।
sa samānavayo-buddhi-sattva-vikrama-ceṣṭitaiḥ ।
nṛpaputro nṛpasutairnityamāste samāvṛtaḥ ।।
kadācicchāstrasambhāra-vivekakṛtaniścayaḥ ।
kadācit kāvyasaṃlāpa-gīta-nāṭakasambhavaiḥ ।।
tathaivākṣavinodaiśca śastrāstravinayeṣu ca ।
yogyāni yuddhanāgāśva-syandanābhyāsatatparaḥ ।।
reme narendraputro asau narendratanayaiḥ saha ।
yathaiva hi divā tadvadrātravapi mudā yutaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ tu krīḍatāṃ tatra dvija-bhūpa-viśāṃ sutāḥ ।
samānavayasaḥ prītyā rantumāyāntyanekaśaḥ ।।
kasyacittvatha kālasya nāgalokānmahītalam ।
kumārāvāgatau nāgau putrāvaśvatarasya tu ।।
brahmarūpapraticchannau taruṇau priyadarśanau ।
tau tairnṛpasutaiḥ sārdhaṃ tathaivānyairdvijanmabhiḥ ।।
vinodairvividhaistatra tasthatuḥ prītisaṃyutau ।
sarva ca te nṛpasutāste ca brahmaviśāṃ sutāḥ ।।
nāgarājātmajau tau ca strānasaṃvāhanādikam ।
vastragandhānusayuktāṃ cakrurbhāgabhujikriyām ।।
ahanyahanyanuprāpte tau ca nāgakumārakau ।
ājagmaturmudā yuktau prītyā sūnormahīpateḥ ।।
sa ca tābhyāṃ nṛpasutaḥ paraṃ nirvāṇamāptavān ।
vinodairvividhairhāsya-saṃlāpādibhireva ca ।।
vinā tābhyāṃ na bubhuje na sastrau na papau madhu ।
na rarāma na jagrāha śāstrāṇyātmaguṇardhaye ।।
rasātale ca tau rātriṃ vinā tena mahātmanā ।
niśvāsaparamau nītvā jagmatustaṃ dine dine ।।
martyaloke parā prītirbhavatoḥ kena putrakau ।
saheti papraccha pitā tāvubhau nāgadārakau ।।
dṛṣṭayoratra pātāle bahūni divasāni me ।
divā rajanyāmevobhau paśyāmi priyadarśanau ।।

jaḍa uvāca

iti pitrā svayaṃ pṛṣṭau praṇipatya kṛtāñjalī ।
pratyūcaturmahābhāgāvuragādhipateḥ sutau ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

putraḥ śatrujitastāta nāmnā khyāta ṛtadhvajaḥ ।
rūpavānārjavopetaḥ śūro mānī priyaṃvadaḥ ।।
anāpṛṣṭakatho vāggmī vidvān maitro guṇākaraḥ ।
mānyamānayitā dhīmān hrīmān vinayabhūṣaṇaḥ ।।
tasyopacārasamprīti-sambogāpahṛtaṃ manaḥ ।
nāgaloke bhuvarloke na ratiṃ vindate pitaḥ ।।
tadviyogena nastāta ! na pātālañca śītalam ।
paritāpāya tatsaṅgādāhlādāya ravirdivā ।।

pitovāca

putraḥ puṇyavato dhanyaḥ sa yasyaivaṃ bhavidvidhaiḥ ।
parokṣasyāpi guṇibhaiḥ kriyate guṇakīrtanam ।।
santi śāstravido aśīlāḥ santi mūrkhāḥ suśīlinaḥ ।
śāstraśīle samaṃ manye putrau dhanyatarantu tam ।।
tasya mitraguṇān mitrāṇyamitrāśca parākramam ।
kathayanti sadā satsu putravāṃstena vai pitā ।।
tasyopakāriṇaḥ kaccid bhavadbhyāmabhivāñchitam ।
kiñcinniṣpāditaṃ vatsau paritoṣāya cetasaḥ ।।
sa dhanyo jīvitaṃ tasya tasya janma sujanmanaḥ ।
yasyārthino na vimukhā mitrārtho na ca durbalaḥ ।।
madgṛhe yad suvarṇādi ratnaṃ vāhanamāsanam ।
yaccānyat prītaye tasya taddeyamaviśaṅkayā ।।
dhik tasya jīvitaṃ puṃso mitrāṇāmupakāriṇām ।
pratirūpamakurvan yo jīvāmītyavagacchati ।।
upakāraṃ suhṛdvarge yo apakārañca śatruṣu ।
nṛmegho varṣati prājñāstasyecchanti sadonnatim ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

kiṃ tasya kṛtakṛtyasya kartuṃ śakyeta kenacit ।
yasya sarvārthino gehe sarvakāmaiḥ sadārccitāḥ ।।
yāni ratnāni tadgehe pātāle tāni naḥ kutaḥ ।
vāhanāsanayānāni bhūṣaṇānyambarāṇi ca ।।
vijñānaṃ tatra yaccāsti tadanyatra na vidyate ।
prājñānāmapyasau tāta sarvasandehahṛttamaḥ ।।
ekaṃ tasyāsti kartavyamasādhyaṃ tacca nau matam ।
hiraṇyagarbha-govinda-śarvādīnīśvarādṛte ।।

pitovāca

pathāpi śrotumicchāmi tasya yad kāryamuttamam ।
asādhyamathavā sādhyaṃ kiṃ vāsādhyaṃ vipaścitām ।।
devatvamamareśatvaṃ tatpūjyatvañca mānavāḥ ।
prayānti vāñchitaṃ vānyad dṛḍhaṃ ye vyavasāyinaḥ ।।
nāvijñātaṃ na cāgamyaṃ nāprāpyaṃ divi ceha vā ।
udyatānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ yatacittendriyātmanām ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi vrajan yāti pitīlikaḥ ।
agacchan vainateyo api pādamekaṃ na gacchati ।।
kva bhūtalaṃ kva ca dhrauvyaṃ sthānaṃ yat prāptavān dhruvaḥ ।
uttānapādanṛpateḥ putraḥ san bhūmigocaraḥ ।।
tat kathyatāṃ mahābhāga kāryavān yena putrakau ।
sa bhūpālasutaḥ sādhuryenānṛṇyaṃ bhaveta vām ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

tenākhyātamidaṃ tāta pūrvavṛtaṃ mahātmanā ।
kaumārake yathā tasya vṛtaṃ sadvṛttaśālinaḥ ।।
tantu śatrujitaṃ tāta pūrvaṃ kaścididvajottamaḥ ।
gālavo abhyāgamaddhīmān gṛhītvā turagottamam ।।
pratyuvāca ca rājānaṃ samupetyāśramaṃ mama ।
ko api daityādhamo rājan vidhvaṃsayati pāpakṛt ।।
tattadrūpaṃ samāsthāya siṃhebha-vanacāriṇām ।
anyeṣāñcālpakāyānāmaharniśamakāraṇāt ।।
samādhidhyānayuktasya maunavrataratasya ca ।
tathā karoti vighrāni yathā calati me manaḥ ।।
dagdhaṃ kopāgninā sadyaḥ samarthastvaṃ vayaṃ na tu ।
duḥ khārjitasya tapaso vyayamicchāmi pārthiva ।।
ekadā tu mayā rājannatinirviṇṇacetasā ।
tat kleśitena niśvāso nirīkṣyāsuramujjhitaḥ ।।
tato ambaratalāt sadyaḥ patito ayaṃ turaṅgamaḥ ।
vāk cāśarīriṇī prāha naranātha śṛṇuṣva tām ।।
aśrāntaḥ sakalaṃ bhūmervalayaṃ turagottamaḥ ।
samarthaḥ krāntumarkeṇa tavāyaṃ pratipāditaḥ ।।
pātālāmbaratoyeṣu na cāsya vihatā gatiḥ ।
samastadikṣu vrajato na bhaṅgaḥ parvateṣvapi ।।
yato bhūvalayaṃ sarvamaśrānto ayaṃ cariṣyati ।
ataḥ kuvalayo nāmnā khyātiṃ loke prayāsyati ।।
kliśyatyaharniśaṃ pāpo yaśca tvāṃ dānavādhamaḥ ।
tamapyenaṃ samāruhya dvijaśreṣṭha haniṣyati ।।
śatrujinnāma bhūpālastasya putra ṛtadhvajaḥ ।
prāpyaitadaśvaratnañca khyātimetena yāsyati ।।
so ahaṃ tvāṃ samanuprāptastapaso vighrakāriṇam ।
taṃ nivāraya bhūpāla bhāgabhāṅnṛpatiryataḥ ।।
tadetaśvaratnaṃ te mayā bhūpa niveditam ।
putramājñāpaya tathā yathā dharmo na lupyate ।।
sa tasya vacanādrājā taṃ vai putramṛtadhvajam ।
tamaśvaratnamāropya kṛtakautukamaṅgalam ।।
apreṣayata dharmātmā gālavena samaṃ tadā ।
svamāśramapadaṃ so api tamādāya yayau muniḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe pitā-putrasaṃvādeṭhakuvalayāśvīyo' nāma viṃśo adhyāyaḥ

ekaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pitovāca

gālavena samaṃ gatvā nṛpaputreṇa tena yat ।
kṛtaṃ tat kathyatāṃ putrau vicitrā yuvayoḥ kathā ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

sa gālavāśrame ramye tiṣṭhan bhūpālanandanaḥ ।
sarvavighropaśamanaṃ cakāra brahmavādinām ।।
vīraṃ kuvalayāśvaṃ taṃ vasantaṃ gālavāśrame ।
madāvalepopahato nājānāddānavādhamaḥ ।।
tatastaṃ gālavaṃ vipraṃ sandhyopāsanatatparam ।
śaukaraṃ rūpamāsthāya pradharṣayitumāgatam ।।
muniśiṣyairathotkruṣṭe śīghramāruhya taṃ hayam ।
anvadhāvadvarāhaṃ taṃ nṛpaputraḥ śarāsanī ।।
ājaghāna ca bāṇena candrārdhākāravarcasā ।
ākṛṣya balavaccāpaṃ cārucitropaśobhitam ।।
nārācābhihataḥ śīghramātmatrāṇaparo mṛgaḥ ।
giripādapasambādhāṃ so anvakrāmanmahāṭavīm ।।
tamanvadhāvadvegena turago asau manojavaḥ ।
codito rājaputreṇa piturādeśakāriṇā ।।
atikramyātha vegena yojanāni sahasraśaḥ ।
dharaṇyāṃ vivṛte garte nipapāta laghukramaḥ ।।
tasyānantaramevāśu so apyaśvī nṛpateḥ sutaḥ ।
nipapāta mahāgarte timiraughasamāvṛte ।।
tato nādṛśyata mṛgaḥ sa tasmin rājasūnunā ।
prakāśañca sa pātālamapaśyat tatra nāpi nam ।।
tato apaśyat sa sauvarṇa-prāsādaśatasaṃkulam ।
purandarapuraprakhyaṃ puraṃ prākāraśobhitam ।।
tat praviśya sa nāpaśyat tatra kañcinnaraṃ pure ।
bhramatā ca tato dṛṣṭā tatra yoṣit tvarānvitā ।।
sā pṛṣṭā tena tanvaṅgī prasthitā kena kasya vā ।
novāca kiñcit prāsādamāruroha ca bhāminī ।।
so apyaśvamekato baddhvā tāmevānusasāra vai ।
vismayotphullanayano niḥ śaṅko nṛpateḥ sutaḥ ।।
tato apaśyat suvistīrṇe paryaṅke sarvakāñcane ।
niṣaṇṇāṃ kanyakāmekāṃ kāmayuktāṃ ratīmiva ।।
vispaṣṭendumukhīṃ subhrūṃ pīnaśroṇipayodharām ।
bimbādharoṣṭhīṃ nanvaṅgīṃ nīlotpalavilocanām ।।
raktatuṅganakhīṃ śyāmāṃ mṛdvīṃ tāmrakarāṅghrikām ।
karabhoruṃ sudaśanāṃ nīlasūkṣmasthirālakām ।।
tāṃ dṛṣṭvā cārusarvāṅgīmanaṅgāṅgalatāmiva ।
so amanyat pārthivasutastāṃ rasātaladevatām ।।
sā ca dṛṣṭvaiva taṃ bālā nīlakuñcitamūrdhajam ।
pīnoruskandhabāhuṃ tamamaṃsta madanaṃ śubhā ।।
uttasthau ca mahābhāgā cittakṣobhamavāpya sā ।
lajjāvismayadainyānāṃ sadyastanvī vaśaṃ gatā ।।
ko ayaṃ devo nu yakṣo vā gandharvo vorago api vā ।
vidyādharo vā samprāptaḥ kṛtapuṇyaratirnaraḥ ।।
evaṃ vicintya vahudhā niśvasya ca mahītale ।
upaviśya tato bheje sā mūrcchāṃ madirakṣaṇā ।।
so api kāmaśarāghātamavāpya nṛpateḥ sutaḥ ।
tāṃ samāśvāsayāmāsa na bhetavyamiti bruvan ।।
sā ca strī yā tadā dṛṣṭā pūrvaṃ tena mahātmanā ।
tālavṛntamupādāya paryavījayadākulā ।।
samāśvāsya tadā pṛṣṭā tena saṃmohakāraṇam ।
kiñcillajjānvitā bālā tasyāḥ sakhyurnyavedayat ।।
sā cāsmai kathayāmāsa nṛpaputrāya vistarāt ।
mohasya kāraṇaṃ sarvaṃ taddarśanasamudbhavam ।
yathā tayā samākhyātaṃ tadvṛttāntañca bhāminī ।।

stryuvāca

viśvāvasuriti khyāto divi gandharvarāṭ prabho ।
tasyeyamātmajā subhrūrnāmnarā khyātā madālasā ।।
vajraketoḥ sutaścogro dānavo arividāraṇaḥ ।
pātālaketurvikhyātaḥ pātālāntarasaṃśrayaḥ ।।
teneyamudyānagatā kṛtvā māyāṃ tamomayīm ।
apahṛtya mayāṃ hīnā bālā nītā durātmanā ।।
āgāminyāṃ trayodaśyāmudvakṣyati kilāsuraḥ ।
sa tu nārhati cārvaṅgīṃ śūdro vedaśrutīmiva ।।
atīte ca dine bālāmātmavyāpadanodyatām ।
surabhiḥ prāha nāyaṃ tvaṃ prāpsyate dānavādhamaḥ ।।
martyalokamanuprāptaṃ ya enaṃ chetsyate śaraiḥ ।
sate bhartā mahābhāge acireṇa bhaviṣyati ।।
ahaṃ cāsyāḥ sakhī nāmnarā kuṇḍaleti manasvinī ।
sutā vindhyavataḥ patnī vīrapuṣkaramālinaḥ ।।
hate bhartari śumbhena tīrthāt tīrthamanuvratā ।
carāmi divyayā gatyā paralokārthamudyatā ।।
pātālaketurduṣṭātmā vārāhaṃ vapurāsthitaḥ ।
kenāpi viddho bāṇena munīnāṃ trāṇakāraṇāt ।।
tañcāhaṃ tattvato anviṣya tvaritā samupāgatā ।
satyameva sa kenāpi tāḍito dānavādhamaḥ ।।
iyañca mūrcchāmagamat kāraṇaṃ yat śṛṇuṣva tat ।
tvayi prītimatī bālā darśanādeva mānada ।।
devaputropame cāru-vākyādiguṇaśālini ।
bharyā cānyasya vihitā yena viddhaḥ sa dānavaḥ ।।
etasmāt kāraṇānmohaṃ mahāntamiyamāgatā ।
yāvajjīvaṃ ca tanvaṅgī duḥ khamevopabhokṣyate ।।
tvayyasyā hṛdayaṃ rāgi bhartā cānyo bhaviṣyati ।
yāvajjīvamato duḥ khaṃ surabhyā nānyathā vacaḥ ।।
ahaṃ tvasyāḥ prabhī prītyā duḥ khitātra samāgatā ।
yato viśeṣo naivāsti svasakhī-nijadehayoḥ ।।
yadyeṣābhimataṃ vīraṃ patimāpnoti śobhanā ।
tatastapastvahaṃ kuryāṃ nirvyalīkena cetasā ।।
tvantu ko vā kimarthaṃ vā samprāpto atra mahāmate ।
devo daityo nu gandharvaḥ pannagaḥ kinnaro api vā ।।
na hyatra mānuṣagatirna cedṛṅmānuṣaṃ vapuḥ ।
tattvamākhyāhi kathitaṃ yathaivāvitathaṃ mayā ।।

kuvalayāśva uvāca

yanmāṃ pṛcchasi dharmajñe kastvaṃ kiṃ vā samāgataḥ ।
tacchṛṇuṣvāmalaprajñe kathayāmyāditastava ।।
rājñaḥ śatrujitaḥ putraḥ pitrā sampreṣitaḥ śubhe ।
munirakṣaṇamuddiśya gālavāśramamāgataḥ ।।
kurvato mama rakṣāñca munīnāṃ dharmacāriṇām ।
vighnārthamāgataḥ koṣa'pi śaukaraṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।।
mayā sa viddho bāṇena candrārdhākāravarccasā ।
apakrānto ativegena tamasmyanugato hayī ।।
papāta sahasā garte sakrīḍo aśvaśca māmakaḥ ।
so ahamaśvaṃ samārūḍhastamasyekaḥ paribhraman ।।
prakāśamāsāditavān dṛṣṭā ca bhavatī mayā ।
pṛṣṭayā ca na me kiñcidbhavatyā dattamuttaram ।।
tvāñcaivānupraviṣṭo ahamimaṃ prāsādamuttamam ।
ityetat kathitaṃ satyaṃ na devo ahaṃ na dānavaḥ ।।
na pannago na gandharvaḥ kinnaro vā śucismite ।
samastā pūjyapakṣo vai devādyā mama kuṇḍale ।
manuṣyo asmi viśaṅkā te na kartavyātra karhicit ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

tataḥ prahṛṣṭā sā kanyā sakhīvadanamuttamam ।
lajjājaḍaṃ vīkṣamāṇā kiñcinnovāca bhāminī ।।
sā sakhī punarapyenāṃ prahṛṣṭā pratyuvāca ha ।
yathāvat kathitaṃ tena surabhyā vacanānuge ।।

kuṇḍalovāca

vīra satyamasandigdhaṃ bhavatābhihitaṃ vacaḥ ।
nānyatra hṛdayantvasyā dṛṣṭvā sthairyaṃ prayāsyati ।।
candramevādhikā kāntiḥ samupaiti raviṃ prabhā ।
bhūtirdhanyaṃ dhṛtirdhoraṃ kṣāntirabhyeti cottamam ।।
tvayaiva viddho asandigdhaṃ sa pāpo dānavādhamaḥ ।
surabhiḥ sā gavāṃ mātā kathaṃ mithyā vadiṣyati ।।
taddhanyeyaṃ sabhāgyā ca tvatsambandhaṃ sametya vai ।
kuruṣva vīra yat kāryaṃ vidhinaiva samāhitam ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

paravānahamityāha rājaputraḥ satāṃ pituḥ ।
sā ca taṃ cintayāmāsa tumburuṃ tatkule gurum ।।
sa cāpi tatkṣaṇāt prāptaḥ pragṛhītasamitkuśaḥ ।
madālasāyāḥ samprītyā kuṇḍalāgauraveṇa ca ।।
prajvālya pāvakaṃ hutvā mantravit kṛtamaṅgalām ।
vaivāhikavidhiṃ kanyāṃ pratipādya yathāgatam ।।
jagāma tapase dhīmān svāśramapadaṃ tadā ।
sā cāha tāṃ sakhīṃ bālāṃ kṛtārthāsmi varānane ।।
saṃyuktāmamunā dṛṣṭvā tvāmahaṃ rūpaśālinīm ।
tamastapsye ahamatulaṃ nirvyalīkena cetasā ।।
tīrthāmbudhūtapāpā ca bhavitrī nedṛśī yathā ।
tañcāha rājaputraṃ sā praśrayāvanatā tadā ।
gantukāmā nijasakhī-snehaviklavabhāṣiṇī ।।

kuṇḍalovāca

puṃbhirapyamitaprajña nopadeśo bhavadvidhe ।
dātavyaḥ kimuta strībhirato nopadiśāmi te ।।
kintvasyāstanumadhyāyāḥ snehākṛṣṭena cetasā ।
tvayā viśrambhitā cāsmi smārayāmyarisūdana ।।
bhartavyā rakṣitavyā ca bhāryā hi patinā sadā ।
dharmārthakāmasaṃsiddhyai bhāryā bhartṛsahāyinī ।।
yadā bhāryā ca bhartā ca parasparavaśānugau ।
tadā dharmārthakāmānāṃ trayāṇāmapi saṅgatam ।।
kathaṃ bhāryāmṛte dharmamarthaṃ vā puruṣaḥ prabho ।
prāpnoti kāmamathavā tasyāṃ tritayamāhitam ।।
tathaiva bhartāramṛte bhāryā dharmādisādhane ।
na samarthā trivargo ayaṃ dāmpatyaṃ samupāśritaḥ ।।
devātā-pitṛ-bhṛtyānāmatithīnāñca pūjanam ।
na puṃbhiḥ śakyate kartumṛte bhāryāṃ nṛpātmaja ।।
prāpto api cārtho manujairānīto apī nijaṃ gṛham ।
kṣayameti vinā bhāryāṃ kubhāryāsaṃśraye api vā ।।
kāmastu tasya naivāsti pratyakṣeṇopalakṣyate ।
dampatyoḥ sahadharmeṇa trayīdharmamavāpnuyāt ।।
pitṝn putraistathaivānna-sādhanairatithīn naraḥ ।
pūjābhiramarāṃstadvat sādhvīṃ bhāryāṃ naro avati ।।
striyāścāpi vinā bhartrā dharmakāmārthasantatiḥ ।
naiva tasmāt trivargo ayaṃ dāmpatyamadhigacchati ।।
etanmayoktaṃ yuvayorgacchāmi ca yathepsitam ।
vardha tvamanayā sārdhaṃ dhana-putra-sukhāyuṣā ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

ityuktvā sā pariṣvajya svasakhīṃ taṃ namasya ca ।
jagāma divyayā gatyā yathābhipretamātmanaḥ ।।
so api śatrujitaḥ putrastāmāropya turaṅgamam ।
nirgantukāmaḥ pātālādvijñāto danusambhavaiḥ ।।
tatastaiḥ sahasotkruṣṭaṃ hriyate hriyate ati vai ।
kanyāratnaṃ yadānītaṃ divaḥ pātālaketunā ।।
tataḥ parigha-nistriṃśa-gadā-śūla-śarāyudham ।
dānavānāṃ balaṃ prāptaṃ saha pātālaketunā ।।
tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti jalpantaste tadā dānavottamāḥ ।
śaravarṣaistathā śūlairvavarṣurnṛpanandanam ।।
sa ca śatrujitaḥ putrastadastrāṇyativīryavān ।
ciccheda śarajālena prahasanniva līlayā ।।
kṣaṇena pātālatalamasikhaktyṛṣṭiśāyakaiḥ ।
chinnaiḥ sañchannamabhavadṛtadhvajaśarotkaraiḥ ।।
tato astraṃ tvāṣṭramādāya cikṣepa prati dānavān ।
tena te dānavāḥ sarve saha pātālaketunā ।।
jvālāmālātitīvreṇa sphuṭadasthicayāḥ kṛtāḥ ।
nirdagdhāḥ kāpilaṃ tejaḥ samāsādyeva sāgarāḥ ।।
tataḥ sa rājaputro aśvī nihatyāsurasattamān ।
strīratnena samaṃ tena samāgacchat pituḥ puram ।।
praṇipatya ca tat sarvaṃ sa tu pitre nyavedayat ।
pātālagamanañcaiva kuṇḍalāyāśca darśanam ।।
tadvanmadālasāprāptiṃ dānavaiścāpi saṅgaram ।
vadhañca teṣāmastreṇa punarāgamanaṃ tathā ।।
iti śrutvā pitā tasya caritaṃ cārucetasaḥ ।
prītimānabhavaccedaṃ pariṣvajyāha cātmajam ।।
satpātreṇa tvayā putra tārito ahaṃ mahātmanā ।
bhayebhyo munayastrātā yena saddharmacāriṇaḥ ।।
matpūrvaiḥ khyātimānītaṃ mayā vistāritaṃ punaḥ ।
parākramavatā vīra tvayā tadvahulīkṛtam ।।
yadupāttaṃ yaśaḥ pitrā dhanaṃ vīryamathāpi vā ।
tanna hāpayate yastu sa naro madhyamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
tadvīryādadhikaṃ yastu punaranyat svaśaktitaḥ ।
niṣpādayati taṃ prājñāḥ pravadanti narottamam ।।
yaḥ pitā samupāttāni dhanavīryayaśāṃsi vai ।
nyūnatāṃ nayati prājñāstamāhuḥ puruṣādhamam ।।
tanmayā brāhmaṇatrāṇaṃ kṛtamāsīdyathā tvayā ।
pātālagamanaṃ yacca yaccāsuravināśanam ।।
etadapyadhikaṃ vatsa tena tvaṃ puruṣottamaḥ ।
taddhanyo asmya bāla tvamahameva guṇādhikam ।।
tvāṃ putramīdṛśaṃ prāpya ślāghyaḥ puṇyavatāmapi ।
na sa putrakṛtāṃ prītiṃ manye prāpnoti mānavaḥ ।।
putreṇa nātiśayito yaḥ prajñādānavikramaiḥ ।
dhigjanma tasya yaḥ pitrā loke vijñāyate naraḥ ।।
yaḥ putrāt khyātimabhyeti tasya janma sujanmanaḥ ।
ātmanā jñāyate dhanyo madhyaḥ pitṛpitāmahaiḥ ।।
mātṛpakṣeṇa mātrā ca khyātimeti narādhamaḥ ।
tat putra dhanavīryaistvaṃ vivardhasva sukhena ca ।।
ghandharvatanayā ceyaṃ mā tvayā vai viyujyatām ।
iti pitrā bahuvidhaṃ priyamuktaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
pariṣvajya svamāvāsaṃ sabhāryaḥ sa visarjitaḥ ।
sa tayā bhāryāyā sārdhaṃ reme tatra pituḥ pure ।।
anyeṣu ca tathodyāna-vana-parvatasānuṣu ।
śvaśrū-śvasurayoḥ pādau praṇipatya ca sā śubhā ।
prātaḥ prātastatastena saha reme sumadhyamā ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe kuvalayāśvīye madālasāpariṇayanaṃ nāmaikaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

putrāvūcatuḥ

tataḥ kāle vahutithe gate rājā punaḥ sutam ।
prāha gacchāśu viprāṇāṃ trāṇāya cara medinīm ।।
aśvamenaṃ samāruhya prātaḥ prātardine dine ।
abādhā dvijamukhyānāmanveṣṭavyā sadaiva hi ।।
durvṛttāḥ santi śataśo dānavāḥ pāpayonayaḥ ।
tebhyo na syādyathā bādhā munīnāṃ tvaṃ tathā kuru ।।
sa yathoktastataḥ pitrā tathā cakre nṛpātmajaḥ ।
parikramya mahīṃ sarvāṃ vavande caraṇau pituḥ ।।
ahanyahanyanuprāpte pūrvāhne nṛpanandanaḥ ।
tataśca śeṣaṃ divasaṃ tayā reme sumadhyayā ।।
ekadā tu cāran so atha dadarśa yamunātaṭe ।
pātālaketoranujaṃ tālaketuṃ kṛtāśramam ।।
māyāvī dānavaḥ so atha munirūpaṃ samāsthitaḥ ।
sa prāha rājaputraṃ taṃ pūrvavairamanusmaran ।।
rājaputra brīvīmi tvāṃ tat kuruṣva yadīcchasi ।
na ca te prārthanābhaṅgaḥ kāryaḥ satyapratiśrava ।।
yakṣye yajñena dharmāya kartavyāśca tatheṣṭayaḥ ।
citayastatra kartavyā nāsti me dakṣaiṇā yataḥ ।।
ataḥ prayaccha me vīra hiraṇyārthaṃ svabhūṣaṇam ।
yadetat kaṇṭhalagnaṃ te rakṣa cemaṃ māśramam ।।
yāvadantarjale devaṃ varuṇaṃ yādasāṃ patim ।
vaidikairvāruṇairmantraiḥ prajānāṃ puṣṭihetukaiḥ ।।
abhiṣṭūya tvarāyuktaḥ samabhyemīti vādinam ।
taṃ praṇamya tataḥ prādāt sa tasmai kaṇṭhabhūṣaṇam ।।
prāha yainaṃ bhavān yātu nirvyalīkena cetasā ।
sthāsyāmi tāvadatraiva tavāśramasamīpataḥ ।।
tavādeśānmahābhāga yāvadāgamanaṃ tava ।
na te atra kaścidābādhāṃ kariṣyati mayi sthite ।
viśrabdhaścātvaran brahman kuruṣva tvaṃ manogatam ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

ekamuktastatastena sa mamajja nadījale ।
rarakṣa so api tasyaiva māyāvihitamāśramam ।।
gatvā jalāśayāt tasmāt tālaketuśca tatparam ।
madālasāyāḥ pratyakṣamanyeṣāñcaitaduktavān ।।

tālaketuruvāca

vīraḥ kuvalayāśvo asau mamāśramasamīpataḥ ।
kenāpi duṣṭadaityena kurvan rakṣāṃ tapasvinām ।।
yudhyamāno yathāśakti nighnan brahmadviṣo yudhi ।
māyāmāśritya pāpena bhinnaḥ śūlena vakṣasī ।।
mriyamāṇena tenedaṃ dattaṃ me kaṇṭhabhūṣaṇam ।
prāpitaścāgnisaṃyogaṃ sa vane śūdratāpasaiḥ ।।
kṛtārtahreṣāśabdo vai trastaḥ sāśruvilocanaḥ ।
nītaḥ so aśvaśca tenaiva dānavena durātmanā ।।
etanmayā nṛśaṃsena dṛṣṭaṃ duṣkṛtakāriṇā ।
yadatrānantaraṃ kṛtyaṃ kriyatāṃ tadakālikam ।।
hṛdayāśvāsanañcaitad gṛhyatāṃ kaṇṭhabhūṣaṇam ।
nāsmākaṃ hi suvarṇena kṛtyamasti tapasvinām ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

ityuktvotsṛjya datbhūmau sa jagāma yathāgatam ।
nipapāta janaḥ so atha śokārto mūrcchayā'turaḥ ।।
tatkṣaṇāt cetanāṃ prāpya sarvāstā nṛpayoṣitaḥ ।
rājapatnyaśca rājā ca vilepuratiduḥ khitāḥ ।।
madālasā tu d dṛṣṭvā tadīyaṃ kaṇṭhabhūṣaṇam ।
tatyājāśu priyān prāṇān śrutvā ca nihanta patim ।।
tatastathā mahākrandaḥ paurāṇāṃ bhavaneṣvabhūt ।
yathaiva tasya nṛpateḥ svagehe samavartata ।।
rājā ca tāṃ mṛtāṃ dṛṣṭvā vinā bhartrā madālasām ।
pratyuvāca janaṃ sarvaṃ vimṛśya susthamānasaḥ ।।
na roditavyaṃ paśyāmi bhavatāmātmanastathā ।
sarveṣāmeva saṃcintya sambandhānāmanityatām ।।
kinnu śocāmi tanayaṃ kinnu śocāmyahaṃ snuṣām ।
vimṛśya kṛtakṛtyatvāmnamye aśocyāvubhāvapi ।।
macchru śrupurmadvacanāddvijarakṣaṇatatparaḥ ।
prāpto me yaḥ suto mṛtyuṃ kathaṃ śocyaḥ sa dhīmatām ।।
avaśyaṃ yāti yaddehaṃ taddvijānāṃ kṛte yadi ।
mama putreṇa saṃtyaktaṃ nanvabhyudayakāri tat ।।
iyañca satkulotpannā bhartaryevamanuvratāṃ ।
kathannu śocyā nārīṇāṃ bharturanyanna daivatam ।।
asmākaṃ bāndhavānāñca tathānyeṣāṃ dayāvatām ।
śocyā hyeṣā bhavedevaṃ yadi bhartrā viyoginī ।।
yā tu bharturvadhaṃ śrutvā tatkṣaṇādeva bhāminī ।
bhartāramanuyāteyaṃ na śocyāto vipaścitām ।।
tāḥ śocyā yā viyoginyo na śocyā yā mṛtāḥ saha ।
bhartrā viyogastvanayā nānubhūtaḥ kṛtajñayā ।।
dātāraṃ sarvasaukhyānāmiha cāmutra cobhayoḥ ।
lokayoḥ kā hi bhartāraṃ nārī manyeta mānuṣam ।।
nāsau śocyo na caiveyaṃ nāhaṃ tajjananī na ca ।
tyajatā brāhmaṇārthāya prāṇān sarve sma tāritāḥ ।।
viprāṇaṃ mama dharmasya gataḥ sa hi mahāmatiḥ ।
ānṛṇyamardhabhuktasya tyāgād dehasya me sutaḥ ।।
mātuḥ satītvaṃ madvaṃśavaimalyaṃ śauryamātmanaḥ ।
saṃgrāme saṃtyajan prāṇān nātyajad dvijarakṣaṇam ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

tataḥ kuvalayāśvasya mātā bharturanantaram ।
śrutvā putravadhaṃ tādṛk prāha dṛṣṭvā tu taṃ patim ।।

mātovāca
na me mātrā na me svastrā prāptā prītirnṛpedṛśī ।
śrutvā muniparitrāṇe hataṃ putraṃ yathā mayā ।।
śocatāṃ bāndhavānāṃ ye niḥ śvasanto atiduḥ khitāḥ ।
mriyante vyādhinā kliṣṭāsteṣāṃ mātā vṛthāprajā ।।
saṃgrāme yudhyamānā ye abhītā godvijarakṣaṇe ।
kṣuṇṇāḥ śastrairvipadyante ta eva bhuvi mānavāḥ ।।
arthināṃ mitravargasya vidviṣāñca parāṅmukhaḥ ।
yo na yāti pitā tena putrī mātā ca vīrasūḥ ।।
garbhakleśaḥ striyo manye sāphalyaṃ bhajate tadā ।
yadārivijayī vā syāt saṃgrāme vā hataḥ sutaḥ ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

tataḥ sa rājā saṃskāraṃ putrapatnīmalambhayat ।
nirgamya ca bahiḥ snāto dadau putrāya codakam ।।
tālaketuśca nirgamya tathaiva yamunājalāt ।
rājaputramuvācedaṃ praṇayānmadhuraṃ vacaḥ ।।
gaccha bhūpālaputra ! tvaṃ kṛtārtho ahaṃ kṛtastvayā ।
kāryaṃ cirābhilaṣitaṃ tvayyatrāvicale sthite ।।
vāruṇaṃ yajñakāryañca jaleśasya mahātmanaḥ ।
tanmayā sādhitaṃ sarvaṃ yanmamāsīdabhīpsitam ।।
praṇipatya sa taṃ prāyādrājaputraḥ puraṃ pituḥ ।
samāruhya tamevāśvaṃ suparṇānilavikramam ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe kuvalayāśvīye madālasāviyogo nāma dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

trayoviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

putrāvūcatuḥ

sa rājaputraḥ saṃprāpya vegādātmapuraṃ tataḥ ।
pitrorvavandiṣuḥ pādau didṛkṣuśca madālasām ।।
dadarśa janamudvignamaprahṛṣṭamukhaṃ puraḥ ।
punaśca vismitākāraṃ prahṛṣṭavadanaṃ tataḥ ।।
anyamutphullanayanaṃ diṣṭyā diṣṭyetivādinam ।
pariṣvajantamanyonyamatikautūhalānvitam ।।
ciraṃ jīvorukalyāṇa ! hatāste paripanthinaḥ ।
pitroḥ prahlādaya manastathāsmākamakaṇṭakam ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

ityevaṃ vādibhiḥ pauraiḥ puraḥ pṛṣṭhe ca saṃvṛtaḥ ।
tatkṣaṇaprabhavānandaḥ praviveśa piturgṛham ।।
pitā ca taṃ pariṣvajya mātā cānye ca bāndhavāḥ ।
ciraṃ jīveti kalyāṇīrdadustasmai tadāśiṣaḥ ।।
praṇipatya tataḥ so atha kimetaditi vismitaḥ ।
papraccha pitaraṃ tāta ! so asmai samyak taduktavān ।।
sa bhāryāṃ tāṃ mṛtāṃ śrutvā hṛdayeṣṭāṃ madālasām ।
pitarau ca puro dṛṣṭvā lajjāśokābdhimadhyagaḥ ।।
cintayāmāsa sā bālā māṃ śrutvā nidhanaṃ gatam ।
tatyāja jīvitaṃ sādhvī dhiṅmāṃ niṣṭhuramānasam ।।
nṛśaṃso ahamanāryo ahaṃ vinā tāṃ mṛgalocanām ।
matkṛte nidhanaṃ prāptāṃ yajjīvāmyatinirghṛṇaḥ ।।
punaḥ sa cintayāmāsa parisaṃstabhya mānasam ।
mohodgamamapāsyāśu niḥ śvasyocchavasya cātaraḥ ।।
mṛteti sā mannamittaṃ tyajāmi yadi jīvitam ।
kiṃ mayopakṛtaṃ tasyāḥ ślāghyametattu yoṣitām ।।
yadi rodimi vā dīno hā priyeti ! vadanmuhuḥ ।
tathāpyaślāghyametanno vayaṃ hi puruṣāḥ kila ।।
atha śokajaḍo dīno strajā hīno malānvitaḥ ।

vipakṣasya bhaviṣyāmi tataḥ paribhavāspadam ।।
mayāriśātanaṃ kāryaṃ rājñaḥ śuśruṣaṇaṃ pituḥ ।
jīvitaṃ tasya cāyattaṃ santyājyaṃ tatkathaṃ mayā ।।
kintvatra manye kartavyastyāgo bhāgasya yoṣitaḥ ।
sa cāpi nopakārāya tanvaṅgyāḥ kintu sarvathā ।।
mayā nṛśaṃsyaṃ kartavyaṃ nopakāryapakāri ca ।
yā madarthe atyajat prāṇāṃstadarthe alpamidaṃ mama ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

iti kṛtvā matiṃ so atha niṣpādyodakadānikam ।
kriyāścānantaraṃ kṛtvā pratyuvāca ṛtadhvajaḥ ।।

ṛtadhvaja uvāca

yadi sā mama tanvaṅgī na syādbhāryā madālasā ।
asmin janmani nānyā me bhavitrī sahacāriṇī ।।
tāmṛte mṛgaśāvākṣīṃ gandharvatanayāmaham ।
na bhokṣye yoṣitaṃ kāñciditi satyaṃ mayoditam ।।
saddharmacāriṇīṃ patnīṃ tāṃ muktvā gajagāminīm,।
kāñcinnāṅgīkariṣyāmītyetat satyaṃ mayoditam ।।

putrāvūcatuḥ

parityajya ca strībhogān tāta ! sarvaṃstayā vinā ।
krīḍannāste samaṃ tulyairvayasyaiḥ śīlasampadā ।।
etattasya paraṃ kāryaṃ tāta ! tat kena śakyate ।
kartumatyarthaduṣprāpyamīśvaraiḥ kimutetaraiḥ ।।

jaḍa uvāca

iti vākyaṃ tayoḥ śrutvā vimarśamagamatpitā ।
vimṛśya cāha tau putrau nāgarāṭ prahasanniva ।।

nāgarāḍaśvatara uvāca

yadyaśakyamiti jñātvā na kariṣyanti mānavāḥ ।
karmaṇyudyamamudyogahānyā hānistataḥ param ।।
ārabheta naraḥ karma svapauruṣamahāpayan ।
niṣpattiḥ karmaṇo daive pauruṣe ca vyavasathitā ।।
tasmādahaṃ tathā yatnaṃ kariṣye putrakāvitaḥ ।
tapaścaryāṃ samāsthāya yathaitat sādhyate acirāt ।।

jaḍa uvāca

evamuktvā sa nāgendraḥ plakṣāvataraṇaṃ gireḥ ।
tīrthaṃ himavato gatvā tapastepe suduścaram ।।
tuṣṭāva gīrbhiśca tatastatra devīṃ sarasvatīm ।
tanmanā niyatāhāro bhūtvā triṣavaṇāplutaḥ ।।

aśvatara uvāca

jagaddhātrīmahaṃ devīmārirādhayiṣuḥ śubhām ।
stoṣye praṇamya śirasā brahmayoniṃ sarasvatīm ।।
sadasaddevi ! say kiñcinmokṣavaccārthavat padam ।
tatsarvaṃ tvayyasaṃyogaṃ yogavaddevi ! saṃsthitam ।।
tvamakṣaraṃ paraṃ devi ! yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
akṣaraṃ paramaṃ devi ! saṃsthitaṃ paramāṇuvat ।।
akṣaraṃ paramaṃ brahma viśvañcaitat kṣarātmakam ।
dāruṇyavasthito vahnirbhaumāśca paramāṇavaḥ ।।
tathā tvayi sthitaṃ brahma jagaccedamaśeṣataḥ ।
oṅkārākṣarasaṃsthānaṃ yattu devi ! sthirāsthiram ।।
tatra mātrātrayaṃ sarvamasti yaddevi nāsti ca ।
trayo lokāstrayo vedāstraividyaṃ pāvakatrayam ।।
trīṇi jyotīṃṣi varṇāśca trayo dharmāgamāstathā ।
trayo guṇāstrayaḥ śabdastrayo vedāstathāśramāḥ ।।
trayaḥ kālāstathāvasthāḥ pitaro aharniśādayaḥ ।
etanmātrātrayaṃ devi ! tava rūpaṃ sarasvati ।।
vibhinnadarśināmādyā brahmaṇo hi sanātanāḥ ।

somasaṃsthā haviḥ saṃsthāḥ pākasaṃsthāśca sapta yāḥ ।।
tāstvaduccāraṇāddevi ! kriyante brahmavādibhiḥ ।
anirdeśyaṃ tathā cānyadardhamātrānvitaṃ param ।।
avikāryakṣayaṃ divyaṃ pariṇāmavivarjitam ।
tavaitatparamaṃ rūpaṃ yanna śakyaṃ mayoditum ।।
na cāsye na ca tajjihvā tāmroṣṭhādibhirucyate ।
indro api vasavo brahmā candrākau jyotireva ca ।।
viśvāvāsaṃ viśvarūpaṃ viśveśaṃ parameśvaram ।
sāṃkhyavedāntavādoktaṃ bahuśākhāsthirīkṛtam ।।
anādimadhyanidhanaṃ sadasanna sadeva yat ।
ekantvanekaṃ nāpyekaṃ bhavabhedasamāśraitam ।।
anākhyaṃ ṣaḍguṇākhyañca vargākhyaṃ triguṇāśrayam ।
nānāśaktimatāmekaṃ śaktivaibhavikaṃ param ।।
sukhāsukhaṃ mahāsaukhyarūpaṃ tvayi vibhāvyate ।

evaṃ devi ! tvayā vyāptaṃ sakalaṃ niṣkalañca yat ।
advaitāvasthitaṃ brahma yacca dvaite vyavasthitam ।।
yer'thā nityā ye vinaśyanti cānye
ye vā sthūlā ye ca sūkṣmātisūkṣmāḥ ।
ye vā bhūmau ye antarīkṣe anyato vā
teṣāṃ teṣāṃ tvatta evopalabdhiḥ ।।
yaccāmūrtaṃ yacca mūrtaṃ samastaṃ
yadvā bhūteṣvekamekañca kiñcit ।
yaddivyasti kṣmātale khe anyato vā
tvatsambaddhaṃ tvatsvarairvyañjanaiśca ।।

jaḍa uvāca

evaṃ stutā tadā devī viṣṇorjihvā sarasvatī ।
pratyuvāca mahātmānaṃ nāgamaśvataraṃ tataḥ ।।

sarasvatyuvāca

varaṃ te kambalabhrātaḥ prayacchāmyuragādhipa ! ।
taducyatāṃ pradāsyāmi yatte manasi vartate ।।

aśvatara uvāca

sahāyaṃ dehi devi ! tvaṃ pūrvaṃ kambalameva me ।
samastasvarasambandhamubhayoḥ saṃprayaccha ca ।।

sarasvatyuvāca

sapta svarā grāmarāgāḥ sapta pannagasattama ! ।
kītakāni ca saptaiva tāvatīścāpi mūrcchanāḥ ।।
tālāścaikonapañcāśattathā grāmatrayañca yat ।
etatsarvaṃ bhavān gātā kambalaśca tathānagha ! ।।
jñāsyase matprasādena bhujagendrāparaṃ tathā ।
caturvidhaṃ padaṃ tālaṃ triḥ prakāraṃ layatrayam ।।
yaditrayaṃ tathā'todyaṃ mayā dattaṃ caturvidham ।
etadbhavān matprasādāt pannagendrāparañca yat ।।
asyāntargatamāyattaṃ svaravyañjanasaṃmitam ।
tadaśeṣaṃ mayā dattaṃ bhavataḥ kambalasya ca ।।
tathā nānyasya bhūrloke pātāle cāpi pannaga ।
praṇetārau bhavantau ca sarvasyāsya bhaviṣyataḥ ।
pātāle devaloke ca bhūrloke caiva pannagau ।।

jaḍa uvāca

ityuktvā sā tadā devī sarvajihvā sarasvatī ।
jagāmādarśanaṃ sadyo nāgasya kamalekṣaṇā ।।
tayośca tadyathāvṛttaṃ bhrātroḥ sarvamajāyata ।
vijñānamubhayoragryaṃ padatālasvarādikam ।।
tataḥ kailāsaśailendra-śikharasthitamīśvaram ।
gītakaiḥ sptabhirnāgau tantrīlayasamanvitau ।।
ārirādhayiṣū devamanaṅgāṅgaharaṃ haram ।
pracakratuḥ paraṃ yatnamubhau saṃhatavākkalau ।।
prātarniśāyāṃ madhyāhne sandhyayoścāpi tatparau ।
tayoḥ kālena mahatā stūyamāno vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।।
tutoṣa gītakaistau ca prāheśo gṛhyatāṃ varaḥ ।
tataḥ praṇamyāśvataraḥ kambalena samaṃ tadā ।।
vyajñāpayanmahādevaṃ śitikaṇṭhamumāpatim ।
yadi nau bhagavān prīto devadevastrilocanaḥ ।।
tato yathābhilaṣitaṃ varamenaṃ prayaccha nau ।
mṛtā kuvalayāśvasya patnī deva ! madālasā ।।
tenaiva vayasā sadyo duhitṛtvaṃ prayātu me ।
jātismarā yathā pūrvaṃ tadvatkāntisamanvitā ।
yoginī yogamātā ca madgehe jāyatāṃ bhava ।।

mahādeva uvāca

yathoktaṃ pannagaśreṣṭha ! sarvemetadbhaviṣyati ।
matprasādādasandigdhaṃ śruṇu cedaṃ bhujaṅgama ।।
śrāddhe tu samanuprāpte madhyamaṃ piṇḍamātmanā ।
bhakṣayethāḥ phaṇiśreṣṭha ! śuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ ।।
bhakṣite tu tatastasmin bhavato madhyamāt phaṇāt ।
samutpatsyati kalyāṇī tathārūpā yathāmṛtā ।।
kāmañcemamabhidhyāya kuru tvaṃ pitṛtarpaṇam ।
tatkṣaṇādeva sā subhrūḥ śvasato madhyamāt phaṇāt ।।
samutpatsyati kalyāṇī tathārūpā yathāmṛtā ।
etacchrutvā tatastau tu praṇipatya maheśvaram ।।
rasātalaṃ punaḥ prāptau paritoṣasamanvitau ।

tathā ca kṛtavān śrāddhaṃ sa nāgaḥ kambalānujaḥ ।।
piṇḍañca madhyamaṃ tadvadyathāvadupabhuktavān ।
tañcāpi dhyāyaḥ kāmaṃ tataḥ sā tanumadhyamā ।।
jajñe niśvasataḥ sadyastadrūpā madhyamāt phaṇāt ।
na cāpi kathayāmāsa kaṃsyacit sa bhujaṅgamaḥ ।।
antargṛhe tāṃ sudatīṃ strībhirguptāmadhārayat ।
tau cānudinamāgamya putrau nāgapateḥ sukham ।।
ṛtadhvajena sahitau cikrīḍāte amarāviva ।
ekadā tu sutau prāha nāgarājau mudānvitaḥ ।।
yanmayā pūrvamuktantu kriyate kiṃ na tattathā ।
sa rājaputro yuvayorupakārī mamāntikam ।।
kasmānnānīyate vatsāvupakārāya mānadaḥ ।
evamuktau tatastena pitrā snehavatā tu tau ।।
gatvā tasya puraṃ sakhyū remāte tena dhīmatā ।
tataḥ kuvalayāśvaṃ tau kṛtvā kiñcitkathāntaram ।।
abrūtāṃ praṇayopetaṃ svagehagamanaṃ prati ।
tāvāha nṛpaputro asau nanvidaṃ bhavatorgṛham ।।
dhanavāhanavastrādi yanmadīyaṃ tadeva vām ।
yattu vāṃ vāñchitaṃ dātuṃ dhanaṃ ratnamathāpi vā ।।
taddoyatāṃ dvijasutau yadi vāṃ praṇayo mayi ।
etāvatāhaṃ daivena vañcito asmi durātmanā ।।
yadbhavadbhyāṃ mamatvaṃ no madīye kriyate gṛhe ।
yadi vāṃ matpriyaṃ kāryamanugrāhyo asmi vāṃ yadi ।।
taddhane mama gehe ca mamatvamanukalpyatām ।

yuvayoryanmadīyaṃ tanmāmakaṃ yuvayoḥ svakam ।।
etat satyaṃ vijānītaṃ yuvāṃ prāṇā bahiścarāḥ ।
punarnaivaṃ vibhinnārthaṃ vaktavyaṃ dvijasattamau ।।
matprasādaparau prītyā śāpitau hṛdayena me ।
tataḥ snehārdravadanau tāvubhau nāganandanau ।।
ūcaturnṛpateḥ putraṃ kiñcit praṇayakopitau ।
ṛtadhvaja ! na sandeho yathaivāha bhavānidam ।।
tathaiva cāsmanmanasi nātra cintyamato anyathā ।
kintvāvayoḥ svayaṃ pitrā proktametanmahātmanā ।।
draṣṭuṃ kuvalayāśvaṃ tamicchāmīti punaḥ punaḥ ।
tataḥ kuvalayāśvo asau samutthāya varāsanāt ।
yathāha tāteti vadan praṇāmamakarodbhuvi ।।

kuvalayāśva uvāca

dhanyo ahamatipuṇyo ahaṃ ko anyo asti sadṛśo mayā ।
yattāto māmabhidraṣṭuṃ karoti pravaṇaṃ manaḥ ।।
taduttiṣṭhata gacchāmastātājñāṃ kṣaṇamapyaham ।
nātikrāntumihecchāmi padebhyāṃ tasya śapāmyaham ।।

jaḍa uvāca

evamuktvā yayau so atha saha tābhyāṃ nṛpātmajaḥ ।
prāptaśca gomatīṃ puṇyāṃ nirgamya nagarādvahiḥ ।।
tanmadhyena yayuste ve nāgendranṛpanandanāḥ ।
mene ca rājaputro asau pāre tasyāstayorgṛham ।।
tataścākṛṣya pātālaṃ tābhyāṃ nīto nṛpātmajaḥ ।
pātāle dadṛśe cobhau sa pannagakumārakau ।।
phaṇāmaṇikṛtodyotau vyaktasvastikalakṣaṇau ।
vilokya tau surūpāṅgau vismayotphullalocanaḥ ।।
vihasya cābravīt premṇā sādhu bho dvijasattamau ।
kathayāmāsatustau ca pitaraṃ pannageśvaram ।।
śāntamaśvataraṃ nāma mānanīyaṃ divaukasām ।
ramaṇīyaṃ tato apasyat pātālaṃ sa nṛpātmajaḥ ।।
kumāraistaruṇairvṛddhairuragairupaśobhitam ।
tathaiva nāgakanyābhiḥ krīḍantībhiritastataḥ ।।
cārukuṇḍalahārābhistārābhirgaganaṃ yathā ।
gītaśabdaistathānyatra vīṇāveṇusvanānugaiḥ ।।
mṛdaṅgapaṇavātodyaṃ hāriveśmaśatākulam ।
vīkṣamāṇaḥ sa pātālaṃ yayau śatrujitaḥ sutaḥ ।।
saha tābhyāmabhīṣṭābhyāṃ pannagābhyāmarindamaḥ ।
tataḥ praviśya te sarve nāgarājaniveśanam ।।
dadṛśuste mahātmānamuragādhipatiṃ sthitam ।
divyamālyāmbaradharaṃ maṇikuṇḍalabhūṣaṇam ।।

svacchamuktāphalalatāhārihāropaśobhitam ।
keyūriṇaṃ mahābhāgamāsane sarvakāñcane ।।
maṇividrumavaidūrya-jālāntaritarūpake ।
sa tābhyāṃ darśitastasya tāto asmākamasāviti ।।
vīraḥ kuvalayāśvo ayaṃ pitre cāsau niveditaḥ ।
tato nanāma caraṇau nāgendrasya ṛtadhvajaḥ ।।
tamutthāpya balādgāḍhaṃ nāgendraḥ parīṣasvaje ।
mūrdhni cainamupāghrāya ciraṃ jīvetyuvāca saḥ ।।
nihatāmitravargaśca pitroḥ suśrūṣaṇaṃ kuru ।
vatsa ! dhanyasya kathyante parokṣasyāpi te guṇāḥ ।।

bhavato mama putrābhyāmasāmānyā niveditāḥ ।
tvamevānena vardhethā manovākkāyaceṣṭitaiḥ ।।
jīvitaṃ guṇinaḥ ślāghyaṃ jīvanneva mṛto aguṇaḥ ।
guṇavān nirvṛtiṃ pitroḥ śatruṇāṃ hṛdayajvaram ।।
karotyātmahitaṃ kurvan viśvāsañca mahājane ।
devatāḥ pitaro viprā mitrārthivikalādayaḥ ।।
bāndhavāśca tathecchanti jīvitaṃ guṇinaściram ।
parivādanivṛttānāṃ durgateṣu dayāvatām ।
guṇināṃ saphalaṃ janma saṃśritānāṃ vipadgataiḥ ।।

jaḍa uvāca

evamuktvā sa taṃ vīraṃ putrāvidamathābravīt ।
pūjāṃ kuvalayāśvasya kartukāmo bhujaṅgamaḥ ।।

snānādikakramaṃ kṛtvā sarvameva yathākramam ।
madhupānādisambhogamāhārañca yathepsitam ।।
tataḥ kuvalayāśvena hṛdayotsavabhūtayā ।
kathayā svalpakaṃ kālaṃ sthāsyāmo hṛṣṭacetasaḥ ।।
anumena ca tanmauno vacaḥ śatrujitaḥ sutaḥ ।
tathā cakāra nṛpatiḥ pannagānāmudāradhīḥ ।।
sametya tairātmajabhūpanandanair
mahoragāṇāmadhipaḥ sa satyavāk ।
mudānvito annāni madhūni cātmavān
yathopayogaṃ bubhuje sa bhogabhuk ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe madālasopākhyāne kuvalayāśvapātālagamanaṃ nāma trayoviṃso adhyāyaḥ

caturviśo adhyāyaḥ

jaḍa uvāca

kṛtāhāraṃ mahātmanāmadhipaṃ pavanāśinām ।
upāsāñcakrire putrau bhūpālatanayastathā ।।
kathābhiranurūpābhiḥ sa mahātmā bhujaṅgamaḥ ।
prītiṃ sañjanayāmāsa putrasakhyuruvāca ca ।।
tava bhadra ! sukhaṃ brūhi gehamabhyāgatasya yat ।
kartavyamutsṛjāśaṅkāṃ pitarīva suto mayi ।।
rajataṃ vā suvarṇaṃ vā vastraṃ vāhanamāsanam ।
yadvābhimatamatyarthaṃ durlabhaṃ tadvṛṇuṣva mām ।।

kuvalayāśva uvāca

tava prasādādbhagavan ! suvarṇādi gṛhe mama ।
piturasti mamādyāpina kiñcit kāryamīdṛśam ।।
tāte varṣasahasrāṇi śāsatīmāṃ vasundharām ।
tathaiva tvayi pātālaṃ na me yāñconmukaṃ manaḥ ।।
te svargyāśca supuṇyāśca yeṣāṃ pitari jīvati ।
tṛṇakoṭisamaṃ vittaṃ tāruṇyādvittakoṭiṣu ।।
mitrāṇi tulyaśiṣṭāni tadvaddehamanāmayam ।
janitā dhriyate vittaṃ yauvanaṃ kinnu nāsti me ।।
asatyarthe nṛṇāṃ yāñcāpravaṇaṃ jāyate manaḥ ।
satyaśeṣe kathaṃ yāñcāṃ mama jihvā kariṣyati ।।
yairna cintyaṃ dhanaṃ kiñcinmama gehe asti nāsti vā ।
pitṛbāhutarucchāyāṃ saṃśritāḥ sukhino hi te ।।
ye tu bālyāt prabhṛtyeva vinā pitrā kuṭumbinaḥ ।
te sukhāsvādavibhraṃśānmanye dhātraiva vañcitāḥ ।।
tadvayaṃ tvatprasādena dhanaratnādisañcayān ।
pitṛmuktān prayacchāmaḥ kāmato nityamarthinām ।।
tat sarvamiha saṃprāptaṃ yadaṅghriyugalaṃ tava ।
maccūḍāmaṇinā spṛṣṭaṃ yaccāṅgasparśamāptavān ।।

jaḍa uvāca
ityevaṃ prasṛtaṃ vākyamuktaḥ pannagasattamaḥ ।
prāha rājasutaṃ prītyā putrayorupakāriṇam ।।

nāga uvāca

yadi ratnasuvarṇādi matto avāptuṃ na te manaḥ ।
yadanyanmanasaḥ prītyai tadbrūhi tvaṃ dadāmyaham ।।

kuvalayāśva uvāca

bhagavaṃstvatprasādena prārthitasya gṛhe mama ।
sarvamasti viśeṣeṇa samprāptaṃ tava darśanāt ।।
kṛtakṛtyo asmi caitena saphalaṃ jīvitañca me ।
yadaṅgasaṃśleṣamitastava devasya mānuṣaḥ ।।
mamottamāṅge tvatpādarajasā yadihāspadam ।
kṛtaṃ tenaiva na prāptaṃ kiṃ mayā pannageśvara ।।
yadi tvavaśyaṃ dātavyo varo mama yathepsitaḥ ।
tatpuṇyakarmasaṃskāro hṛdayānmā vyapaitu me ।।
