prākāśyaṃ manaso nītāste mātrā nāsya pārthiva ।।
yathaikamarthe yātānāmekasminnavasīdati ।
duḥ khaṃ bhavati sādhūnāṃ tatāsmākaṃ mahīpate ।।
gārhasthyamohamāpanne sīdatyasminnareśvara ।
sambandhinyasya dehasya bibhrati bhrātṛkalpanām ।।
tato mayā viniścitya duḥ khādvairāgyabhāvanā ।
bhaviṣyatītyasya bhavānityudyogāya saṃśritaḥ ।।
tadasya duḥ khādvairāgyaṃ saṃbodhādavanīpate ।
samudbhūtaṃ kṛtaṃ kāryaṃ bhadraṃ te astu vrajāmyaham ।।
uṣṭvā madālasāgarbhe pītvā satsāstathā stanam ।
nānyanārīsutairyātaṃ vartma yātviti pārthiva ।।
vicārya tanmayā sarvaṃ yuṣmatsaṃśrayapūrvakam ।
kṛtaṃ taccāpi niṣpannaṃ prayāsye siddhaye punaḥ ।।
upekṣyate sīdamānaḥ svajano bāndhavaḥ suhṛt ।
yairnarendra ! na tān manye sendriyā vikalā hi te ।।
suhṛdi svajane bandhau samarthe yo avasīdati ।
dharmārthakāmamokṣebhyo vācyāste tatra na tvasau ।।
etat tvatsaṅgamād bhūpa ! mayā kāryaṃ mahat kṛtam ।
svasti te astu gamiṣyāmi jñānabhāgbhava sattama ।।

kāśirāja uvāca

upakārastvayā sādhoralarkasya kṛto mahān ।
mamopakārāya kathaṃ na karoṣi svamānasam ।।
phaladāyī satāṃ sadibhaḥ saṅgamo nāphalo yataḥ ।
tasmāttavatsaṃśrayādyuktā mayā prāptā samunnatiḥ ।।

subāhuruvāca

dharmārthakāmamokṣākhyaṃ puruṣārthacatuṣṭayam ।
tatra dharmārthakāmāste sakalā hīyate aparaḥ ।।
tatte saṃkṣepato vakṣye tadihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu ।
śrutvā ca samyagālocya yatethāḥ śreyase nṛpa ।।
mametipratyayo bhūpa ! na kāryo ahamiti tvayā ।
samyagālocya dharmo hi dharmābhāve nirāśrayaḥ ।।
kasyāhamiti saṃjñeyamityālocya tvayātmanā ।
bāhyantargatamālocyamālocyāpararātriṣu ।।
avyaktādiviśeṣantamavikāramacetanam ।
vyaktāvyaktaṃ tvayā jñeyaṃ jñātā kaścāhamityuta ।।
etasminneva vijñāne vijñātamakhilaṃ tvayā ।
anātmanyātmavijñānamakhe khamiti mūḍhatā ।।
so ahaṃ sarvagato bhūpa ! lokasaṃvyavahārataḥ ।
mayedamucyate sarvaṃ tvayā pṛṣṭo vrajāmyaham ।।
evamuktvā yayau dhīmān ! subāhuḥ kāśibhūmipam ।
kāśirājo api saṃpūjya so alarkaṃ svapuraṃ yayau ।।
alarko api sutaṃ jyeṣṭhamabhiṣicya narādhipam ।
vanaṃ jagāma santyaktasarvasaṅgaḥ svasiddhaye ।।
tataḥ kālena mahātā nirdvandvo niṣparigrahaḥ ।
prāpya yogardhimatulāṃ paraṃ nirvāṇamāptavān ।।
paśyan jagadidaṃ sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।
pāśairguṇamayairbaddhaṃ badhyamānañca nityaśaḥ ।।
putrādibhrātṛputrādi-svapārakyādibhāvitaiḥ ।
ākṛṣyamāṇaṃ karaṇairduḥkhārtaṃ bhinnadarśanam ।।
ajñānapaṅkagarbhasthamanuddhāraṃ mahāmatiḥ ।
ātmānañca samuttīrṇaṃ gāthāmetāmagāyata ।।
aho kaṣṭaṃ yadasmābhaiḥ pūrvaṃ rājyamanuṣṭhitam ।
iti paścānmayā jñātaṃ yogānnāsti paraṃ sukham ।।

jaḍa uvāca

tātainaṃ tvaṃ samātiṣṭha muktaye yogamuttamam ।
prāpsyase yena tad brahma yatra gatvā na śocasi ।।
tato ahamapi yāsyāmi kiṃ yajñaiḥ kiṃ japena me ।
kṛtakṛtyasya karaṇaṃ brahmabhāvāya kalpate ।।
tvatto anujñāmavāpyāhaṃ nirdvandvo niṣparigrahaḥ ।
prayatiṣye tathā muktau yathā yāsyāmi nirvṛtim ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

evamuktvā sa pitaraṃ prāpyānujñāṃ tataśca saḥ ।
brahman ! jagāma medhāvī parityaktaparigrahaḥ ।।
so api tasya pitā tadvat krameṇa sumahāmatiḥ ।
vānaprasthaṃ samāsthāya caturthāśramamabhyagāt ।।
tatrātmajaṃ samāsādya hitvā bandhaṃ guṇādikam ।
prāpa siddhiṃ parāṃ prājñastatkālopāttasaṃmatiḥ ।।
etatte kathitaṃ brahman ! yatpṛṣṭā bhavatā vayam ।
suvistaraṃ yathāvacca kimanyacchrotumicchasi ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe pitāputrasaṃvāde jaḍopākhyānaṃ nāma catuścatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

pañcacatvāriṃbho adhyāyaḥ

jaiminiruvāca

samyagetanmamākhyātaṃ bhavadibhardvijasattamāḥ ।
pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca dvividhaṃ karma vaidikam ।।
aho pitṛprasādena bhavatāṃ jñānamīdṛśam ।
yena tiryaktvamapyetat prāpya mohastiraskṛtaḥ ।।
dhanyā bhavantaḥ saṃsiddhyai prāgavasthāsthitaṃ yataḥ ।
bhavatāṃ viṣayodbhūtairna mohaiścālyate manaḥ ।।
diṣṭyā bhagavatā tena mārkaṇḍeyena dhīmatā ।
bhavanto vai samākhyātāḥ sarvasandehahṛttamāḥ ।।
saṃsāre asmin manuṣyāṇāṃ bhramatāmatisaṅkaṭe ।
bhavadvidhaiḥ samaṃ saṅgo jāyate nātapasvinām ।।
yadyahaṃ saṅgamāsādya bhavadibharjñānadṛṣṭibhiḥ ।
na syāṃ kṛtārthastannūnaṃ na me anyatra kṛtārthatā ।।
pravṛte ca nivṛtte ca bhavatāṃ jñānakarmaṇi ।
matimastamalāṃ manye yathā nānyasya kasyacit ।।
yadi tvanugrahavatī mayī buddhirdvijottamāḥ ।
bhavatāṃ tatsamākhyātumarhatedamaśeṣataḥ ।।
kathametatsamudbhūtaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।
kathañca pralayaṅkāle punaryāsyati sattamāḥ ।।
kathañca vaṃśāḥ devarṣi-pitṛbhūtādisambhavāḥ ।
manvantarāṇi ca kathaṃ vaṃśānucaritañca yat ।।
yāvatyaḥ sṛṣṭayaścaiva yāvantaḥ pralayāstathā ।
yathā kalpavibhāgaśca yā ca manvantarasthitiḥ ।।
yathā ca kṣitisaṃsthānaṃ yat pramāṇañca vai bhuvaḥ ।
yathāsthiti samudrādri-nimnagāḥ kānanāni ca ।।
bhūrlokādisvarlokānāṃ gaṇaḥ pātālasaṃśrayaḥ ।
gatistathārkasomādi-graharkṣajyotiṣāmapi ।।
śrotumicchāmyahaṃ sarvametadāhūtasaṃplavam ।
upasaṃhṛte ca yaccheṣaṃ jagatyasmin bhaviṣyati ।।

pakṣiṇa ūcuḥ

praśnabhāro ayamatulo yastvayā munisattama ।
pṛṣṭastaṃ te pravakṣyāmastat śṛṇuṣveha jaimine ।।
mārkaṇḍeyena kathitaṃ purā krauṣṭukaye yathā ।
dvijaputrāya śāntāya vratastrātāya dhīmate ।।
mārkaṇḍeyaṃ mahātmānamupāsīnaṃ dvijottamaiḥ ।
krauṣṭukiḥ paripapraccha yadetat pṛṣṭavān prabho ।।
tasya cākathayat prītyā yanmunirbhṛgunandanaḥ ।
tatte prakathayiṣyāmaḥ śṛṇu tvaṃ dvijasattama ।।
praṇipatya jagannāthaṃ padmayoniṃ pitāmaham ।
jagadyoniṃ sthitaṃ sṛṣṭau sthitau viṣṇusvarūpiṇam ।
pralaye cāntakartāraṃ raudraṃ rudrasvarūpiṇam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

utpannamātrasya purā brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।
purāṇametadvedāśca mukhebhyo anuviniḥ sṛtāḥ ।।
purāṇasaṃhitāścakrurbahulāḥ paramarṣayaḥ ।
vedānāṃ pravibhāgaśca kṛtastaistu sahasraśaḥ ।।
dharmajñānañca vairāgyamaiśvaryañca mahātmanaḥ ।
tasyopadeśena vinā na hi siddhaṃ catuṣṭayam ।।
vedān saptarṣayastasmājjagṛhustasya mānasāḥ ।
purāṇaṃ jagṛhuścādyā munayastasya mānasāḥ ।।
bhṛgoḥ sakāśāccyavanastenoktañca dvijanmanām ।
ṛṣibhiścāpi dakṣāya proktametanmahātmabhiḥ ।।
dakṣeṇa cāpi kathitamidamāsīttadā mama ।
tattubhyaṃ kathayāmyadya kalikalmaṣanāśanam ।।
sarvametanmahābhaga ! śrūyatāṃ me samādhinā ।
yathāśrutaṃ mayā pūrvaṃ dakṣasya gadato mune ।।
praṇipatya jagadyonimajamavyayamāśrayam ।
carācarasya jagatodhātāraṃ paramaṃ padam ।।
brahmāṇamādipuruṣamutpatti-sthiti-saṃyame ।
yatkāraṇamanaupamyaṃ yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।
tasmai hiraṇyagarbhāya lokatantrāya dhīmate ।
praṇamya samyagvakṣyāmi bhūtavargamanuttamam ।।
mahadādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ savairupyaṃ salakṣaṇam ।
pramāṇaiḥ pañcabhirgamyaṃ strotobhiḥ ṣaḍbhiranvitam ।।
puruṣādhiṣṭhitaṃ nityamanityamiva ca sthitam ।
tacchrūyatāṃ mahābhāga ! parameṇa samādhinā ।।
pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattadavyaktākhyaṃ maharṣayaḥ ।
yadāhuḥ prakṛtiṃ sūkṣmāṃ nityāṃ sadasadātmikām ।।
dhruvamakṣayyamajaramameyaṃ nānyasaṃśrayam ।
gandharūparasairhenaṃ śabdasparśavivarjitam ।।
anādyantaṃ jagadyoni triguṇaprabhavāpyayam ।
asāmpratamavijñeyaṃ brahmāgre samavartata ।।
pralayasyānu tenedaṃ vyāptamāsīdaśeṣataḥ ।
guṇasāmyāttatastasmāt kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitānmune ।।
guṇabhāvāt sṛjyamānāt sargakāle tataḥ punaḥ ।
pradhānaṃ tattvamudbhūtaṃ mahāntaṃ tat samāvṛṇot ।।
yathā bījaṃ tvacā tadvadavyaktenāvṛto mahān ।
sāttviko rājasaścaiva tāmasaśca tridhoditaḥ ।।
tatastasmādahaṅkārastrividho vai vyajāyata ।
vaikārikastaijasaśca bhūtādiśca satāmasaḥ ।।
mahatā cāvṛtaḥ so api yathāvyaraktena vai mahān ।
bhūtādistu vikurvāṇaḥ śabdatanmātrakantataḥ ।।
sasarja śabdatanmātrādākāśaṃ śabdalakṣaṇam ।
ākāśaṃ śabdamātrantu bhūtādiścāvṛṇottataḥ ।।
sparśatanmātrameveha jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
balavān jāyate vāyustasya sparśaguṇo mataḥ ।।
vāyuścāpi vikurvāṇo rupamātraṃ sasarja ha ।
jyotirutpadyate vāyostadrūpaguṇamucyate ।।
sparśamātrastu vai vāyūrūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot ।
jyotiścāpi vikurvāṇaṃ rasamātraṃ sasarja ha ।।
sambhavanti tato hyāpaścāsan vai tā rasātmikāḥ ।
rasamātrantu tāhyāpo rūpamātraṃ samāvṛṇot ।।
āpaścāpi vikurvatyo gandhamātraṃ sasarjire ।
saṅghāto jāyate tasmāttasya gandho guṇo mataḥ ।।
tasmiṃstasmiṃstu tanmātraṃ tena tanmātratā smṛtā ।
aviśeṣavācakatvādaviśeṣāstataśca te ।।
na śāntā nāpi ghorāste na mūḍhāścāviśeṣataḥ ।
bhūtatanmātrasargo ayamahaṅkārāttu tāmasāt ।।
vaikārikādahaṅkārāt sattvodriktāttu sāttvikāt ।
vaikārikaḥ sa sargastu yugapat sampravartate ।।
buddhīndriyāṇi pañcaiva pañca karmendriyāṇi ca ।
taijasānīndriyāṇyāhurdevā vaikārikā daśa ।।
ekādaśaṃ manastatra devā vaikārikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
śrotaṃ tvakcakṣuṣī jihvā nāsikā caiva pañcamī ।।
śabdādīnāmavāptyarthaṃ buddhiyuktāni vakṣyate ।
pādau pāyurupasthaśca hastau vāk pañcamī bhavet ।।
gatirvisargo hyānandaḥ śilpaṃ vākyañca karma tat ।
ākāśaṃ śabdamātrantu sparśamātraṃ samāviśat ।।
dviguṇo jāyate vāyustasya sparśo guṇo mataḥ ।
rūpantathaivāviśataḥ śabdasparśaguṇāvubhau ।।
dviguṇastu tataścāgniḥ sa śabdasparśarūpavān ।
śabdaḥ sparśaśca rūpañca rasamātraṃ samāviśat ।।
tasmāccaturguṇā hyāpo vijñeyāstā rasātmikāḥ ।
śabdaḥ sparśaśca rūpañca raso gandhaṃ samāviśat ।।
saṃhatā gandhamātreṇa āvṛṇvaṃste mahīmimām ।
tasmāt pañcaguṇā bhūmiḥ sthūlā bhūteṣu dṛśyate ।।
śāntā ghorāśca mūḍhāśca viśeṣāstena te smṛtāḥ ।
parasparānupraveśāddhārayanti parasparam ।।
bhūmerantastvidaṃ sarvaṃ lokālokaṃ ghanāvṛtam ।
viśeṣāścendriyagrāhyā niyatatvācca te smṛtāḥ ।।
guṇaṃ pūrvasya pūrvasya prāpnuvantyuttarottaram ।
nānāvīryāḥ pṛthagbhūtāḥ saptaite saṃhatiṃ vinā ।।
nāśaknuvan prajāḥ straṣṭumasamāgamya kṛtsnaśaḥ ।
sametyānyonyasaṃyogamanyonyāśrayiṇaśca te ।।
ekasaṅghātacihnāśca saṃprāpyaikyamaśeṣataḥ ।
puruṣādhiṣṭhitatvācca avyaktānugraheṇa ca ।।
mahadādyā viśeṣāntā hyaṇḍamutpādayanti te ।
jalabudbudavattatra kramādvai vṛddhimāgatam ।।
bhūtebhyo aṇḍaṃ mahābuddhe ! vṛhattadudakeśayam ।
prākṛte aṇḍe vivṛddhaḥ san kṣetrajño brahmasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ sa vai puruṣa ucyate ।
ādikartā ca bhūtānāṃ brahmāgre samavartata ।।
tena sarvamidaṃ vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
merustasyānusambhūto jarāyuścāpi parvatāḥ ।।
samudā garbhasalilaṃ tasyāṇḍasya mahātmanaḥ ।
tasminnaṇḍe jagat sarvaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam ।।
dīpādyadrisamudrāśca rājyotirlokasaṃgrahaḥ ।
jalānilānalākāśaistato bhūtādinā bahiḥ ।।
vṛtamaṇḍaṃ daśaguṇairekekaikatvena taiḥ punaḥ ।
mahatā tatpramāṇena sahaivānena veṣṭitaḥ ।।
mahāṃstaiḥ sahitaḥ sarvairavyaktena samāvṛtaḥ ।
ebhirāvaraṇairaṇḍaṃ saptabhaiḥ prākṛtairvṛtam ।।
anyonyamāvṛtya ca tā aṣṭau prakṛtayaḥ sthitāḥ ।
eṣā sā prakṛtirnityā yadantaḥ puruṣaśca saḥ ।।
brahmākhyaḥ kathito yaste samāsāt śrū yatāṃ punaḥ ।
yathā magno jale kaścidunmajjan jalasambhavaḥ ।।
jalañca kṣipati brahmā sa tathā prakṛtirvibhu ।
avyaktaṃ kṣetramudiṣṭaṃ brahmā kṣetrajña ucyate ।।
etatsamastaṃ jānīyāt kṣetrakṣetrajñalakṣaṇam ।
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitastu saḥ ।
abuddhipūrvaḥ prathamaḥ prādurbhūtastaḍidyathā ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe brahmotpatirnāma pañcacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

śrīmanmaharṣivedavyāsapraṇītaṃ

śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam ।

ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

krauṣṭukiruvāca
bhagavaṃstvaṇḍasambhūtiryathāvat kathitā mama ।
brahmāṇḍe brahmaṇo janma tathā coktaṃ mahātmanaḥ ।।
etadicchāmyahaṃ śrotuṃ tvatto bhṛgukulodbhava ।
yadāna sṛṣṭirbhūtānāmasti kinnu na cāsti vā ।
kāle vai pralayasyānte sarvasminnupasaṃhṛte ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

yadā tu prakṛtau yāti layaṃ viśvamidaṃ jagat ।
tadocyate prākṛto ayaṃ vidvadbhiḥ pratisañcaraḥ ।।
svātmanyavasthitevyakte vikāre pratisaṃhṛte ।
prakṛtiḥ puruṣaścaiva sādharmyeṇāvatiṣṭhataḥ ।।
tadā tamaśca sattvañca samatvena vyavasthitau ।
anudriktāvanūnau ca tatprotau ca parasparam ।।
tileṣu vā yathā tailaṃ ghṛtaṃ payasi vā sthitam ।
tathā tamasi sattve ca rajo apyanusṛtaṃ sthitam ।।
utpattirbrahmaṇo yāvadāyuṣo dviparārdhikam ।
tāvaddinaṃ pareśasya tatsamā saṃyame niśā ।।
aharmukhe prabuddhastu jagadādiranādimān ।
sarvaheturacintyātmā paraḥ ko apyaparakriyaḥ ।।
prakṛtiṃ puruṣañcaiva prāviśyāśu jagatpatiḥ ।
kṣobhayāmāsa yogena pareṇa parameśvaraḥ ।।
yathā mado navastrīṇāṃ yathā vā mādhavānilaḥ ।
anupraviṣṭaḥ kṣobhāya tathāsau yogamūrtimān ।।
pradhāne kṣobhyamāne tu sa devo brahmasaṃjñitaḥ ।
samutpanno aṇḍakoṣastho yathā te kathitaṃ mayā ।।
sa eva kṣobhakaḥ pūrvaṃ sa kṣobhyaḥ prakṛteḥ patiḥ ।
sa saṅkocavikāśābhyāṃ pradhānatve api ca sthitaḥ ।।
atpannaḥ sa jagadyoniraguṇo api rajoguṇam ।
bhuñjan pravartate sarge brahmatvaṃ samupāśritaḥ ।।
brahmatve sa prajāḥ sṛṣṭvā tataḥ sattvātirekavān ।
viṣṇutvametya dharmeṇa kurute paripālanam ।।
tatastamoguṇodrikto rudratve cākhilaṃ jagat ।
upasaṃhṛtya vai śete trailokyaṃ triguṇo aguṇaḥ ।।
yathā prāgvyāpakaḥ kṣetrī pālako lāvakastathā ।
yathā sa saṃjñāmāyāti brahmaviṣṇvīśakāriṇīm ।।
brahmatve sṛjate lokān rudratve saṃharatyapi ।

viṣṇutve cāpyudāsīnastistro avasthāḥ svayambhuvaḥ ।।
rajo brahmā tamo rudro viṣṇuḥ sattvaṃ jagatpatiḥ ।
eta eva trayo devā eta eva trayo guṇāḥ ।।
anyonyamithunā hyete anyonyāśrayiṇastathā ।
kṣaṇaṃ viyogo nahyeṣāṃ na tyajanti parasparam ।।
evaṃ brahmā jagatpūrvo devadevaścaturmukhaḥ ।
rajoguṇaṃ samāśritya straṣṭṭatve sa vyavasthitaḥ ।।
hiraṇyagarbho devādiranādirupacārataḥ ।
bhūpadmakarṇikāsaṃstho brahmāgre samajāyata ।।
tasya varṣaśataṃ tvekaṃ paramāyurmahātmanaḥ ।
brahmyeṇaiva hi mānena tasya saṃkhyāṃ nibodha me ।।
nimeṣairdaśabhiḥ kāṣṭhā tathā pañcabhirucyate ।
kalāstriṃśacca vai kāṣṭhā muhūrtaṃ triṃśattāḥ kalāḥ ।।
ahorātraṃ muhūrtānāṃ nṛṇāṃ triṃśattu vai smṛtam ।
ahorātraiśca triṃśadbhiḥ pakṣau dvau māsa ucyate ।।
taiḥ ṣaḍbhirayanaṃ varṣaṃ dve ayane dakṣiṇottare ।
taddevānāmahorātraṃ dinaṃ tatrottarāyaṇam ।।
divyairvarṣasahasraistu kṛtatretādisaṃjñitam ।
caturyugaṃ dvādaśabhistadvibhāgaṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।।
catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ kṛtamucyate ।
śatāni sandhyā catvāri sandhyāṃśaśca tathāvidhaḥ ।।
tretā trīṇi sahasrāṇi divyābdānāṃ śatatrayam ।
tatsandhyā tatsamā caiva sandhyāṃśaśca tathāvidhaḥ ।।
dvāparaṃ dve sahasre tu varṣāṇāṃ dve śate tathā ।
tasya sandhyā samākhyātā dve śatābde tadaṃśakaḥ ।।
kaliḥ sahasraṃ divyānāmabdānāṃ dvijasattama ।
sandhyā sandhyāṃśakaścaiva śatakau samudāhṛtau ।।
eṣā dvādhaśasāhastrī yugākhyā kavibhiḥ kṛtā ।
etat sahasraguṇitamo brāhmyamudāhṛtam ।।
brahmaṇo divase brahman manavaḥ syuścaturdaśa ।
bhavanti bhāgaśasteṣāṃ sahasraṃ tadvibhajyate ।।
devāḥ saptarṣayaḥ sendrā manustatsūnavo nṛpāḥ ।
manunā saha sṛjyante saṃhriyante ca pūrvavat ।।
caturyugānāṃ saṃkhyātā sādhikā hye kasaptatiḥ ।
manvantaraṃ tasya saṃkhyāṃ mānuṣābdairnibodha me ।।
triṃśatkoṭyastu saṃpūrṇāḥ saṃkhyātāḥ saṃkhyayā dvija ।
satpaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutāni ca saṃkhyayā ।।
viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi kālo ayaṃ sādhikaṃ vinā ।
etanmanvantaraṃ proktaṃ divyairvarṣairnibodha me ।।
aṣṭau varṣasahasrāṇi divyayā saṃkhyayā yutam ।
dvipañcāśattathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni tu ।।
caturdaśaguṇo hyeṣa kālo brahmyamahaḥ smṛtam ।
tasyānte pralayaḥ prokto brahman naimittiko budhaiḥ ।।
bhūrloko atha bhuvarlokaḥ svarlokaśca vināśinaḥ ।
tathā vināśamāyānti maharlokaśca tiṣṭhati ।।
tadvāsino api tāpena janalokaṃ prayānti vai ।
ekārṇave ca trailokye brahmā svapiti vai niśi ।।
tatpramāṇaiva sā rātristadante sṛjyate punaḥ ।
evantu brahmaṇo varṣamekaṃ varṣaśatantu tat ।।
śataṃ hi tasya varṣāṇāṃ paramityabhidhīyate ।
pañcāśadbhistathā varṣaiḥ parārdhamiti kīrtyate ।।
evamasya parārdhantu vyatītaṃ dvijasattama ।
yasyānte abhūnmahākalpaḥ pādma ityabhiviśrutaḥ ।।
dvitīyasya parārdhasya vartamānasya vai dvija ।
vārāha iti kalpo ayaṃ prathamaḥ parikalpitaḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe brahmāyupramāṇo nāma ṣaṭṭatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

saptacatvāriśo adhyāyaḥ 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

yathā sasarja vai brahmā bhagavānādikṛt prajāḥ ।
prajāpatiḥ patirdevastanme vistarato vada ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

kathayāmyeṣa te brahman sasarja bhagavān yathā ।
lokakṛcchāśvataḥ kṛtsnaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam ।।
padmāvasāne pralaye niśāsutpotthitaḥ prabhuḥ ।
sattvodriktastadā brahmā śūnyaṃ lokamavaikṣata ।।
imañcodāharantyatra ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati ।
brahmasvarūpiṇaṃ devaṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam ।।
āpo nārā vai tanava ityapāṃ nāma śuśruma ।
tāsu śete sa yasmācca tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
vibuddhaḥ salile tasmin vijñāyāntargatāṃ mahīm ।
anumānāt samuddhāraṃ kartukāmastadā kṣite ।।
akarot sa tanūranyāḥ kalpādiṣu yathā purā ।
matsyakūrmādikāstadvadvārāhaṃ vapurāsthitaḥ ।।
vedayajñamayaṃ divyaṃ vedayajñamayo vibhuḥ ।
rūpaṃ kṛtvā viveśāpsu sarvagaḥ sarvasambhavaḥ ।।
samuddhṛkatya ca pātālānmumoca salile bhuvam ।
janalokasthitaiḥ siddhaiścintyamāno jagatpatiḥ ।।
tasyopari jalaughasya mahatī nairiva sthitā ।
vitatatvāttu dehasya na mahī yāti saṃplavam ।।
tataḥ kṣitiṃ samīkṛtya pṛthivyāṃ so asṛjad girīn ।
prāk sarge dahyamāne tu tadā saṃvartakāgninā ।।
tenāgninā viśīrṇāste parvatā bhuvi sarvaśaḥ ।
śailā ekārṇave magnā vāyunāpastu saṃhatāḥ ।।
niṣaktā yatra yatrāsaṃstatra tatrācalābhavan ।
bhūvibhāgantataḥ kṛtvā saptadvīpopaśobhitam ।।
bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokān pūrvaṃvat samakalpayat ।
sṛṣṭiñcintayatastasya kalpādiṣu yathā purā ।।
abuddhipūrvakastasmāt prādurbhūtastamomayaḥ ।
tamo moho mahāmohastāmistro hyandhasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ ।
pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyato apratibodhavān ।।
bahirantaścāprakāśaḥ saṃvṛtātmā nagātmakaḥ ।
mukhyā nagā yataścoktā mukhyasargastatastvayam ।।
taṃ dṛṣṭvāsādhakaṃ sargamamanyadaparaṃ punaḥ ।
tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ tiryakstroto hyavartata ।।
yasmāttiryakpravṛttiḥ sā tiryakstrotastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।
paśvādayaste vikhyātāstamaḥ prāyo hyavedinaḥ ।।
atpathagrāhinaścaiva te ajñāne jñānamāninaḥ ।

ahaṅkṛtā ahaṃmānā aṣṭāviśaśadvidhātmakāḥ ।।
antaḥ prakāśāste sarve āvṛtāstu parasparam ।
tamapyasādhakaṃ matvā dhyāyato anyastato abhavat ।।
ūrdhvastrotastṛtīyastu sāttvikaḥ samavartata ।
te sukhaprītibahulā bahirantastvanāvṛtāḥ ।।
prakāśā bahirantaśca ūrdhvastrotaḥ samudbhavāḥ ।
tuṣṭātmakastṛtīyastu devasargo hi sa smṛtaḥ ।।
tasmin sarge abhavat prītirniṣpanne brahmaṇastadā ।
tato anyaṃ sa tadā dadhyau sādhakaṃ sargamuttamam ।।
tathābhidhyāyatastasya satyābhidhyāyinastataḥ ।
prādurbabhau tadāvyaktādarvākstrotastu sādhakaḥ ।।
yasmādarvāg vyavartanta tator'vākstrotasastu te ।
te ca prakāśabahulāstamodriktā rajo adhikāḥ ।।
tasmāt te duḥ khabahulā bhūyobhūyaśca kāriṇaḥ ।
prakāśā bahirantaśca manuṣyāḥ sādhakāśca te ।।
pañcamo anugrahaḥ sargaḥ sa caturdhā vyavasthitaḥ ।
viparyayeṇa siddhyā ca śāntyā tuṣṭyā tathaiva ca ।।
nirvṛttaṃ vartamānañca ter'thaṃ jānanti vai punaḥ ।
bhūtādikānāṃ bhūtānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sarga sa ucyate ।।
te parigrāhiṇaḥ sarve saṃvibhāgaratāstathā ।
codanāścāpyaśīlāśca jñeyā bhūtādikāśca te ।।
prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇastu saḥ ।
tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūtasargaḥ sa ucyate ।।
vaikārikastṛtīyastu sargaścaindriyakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
ityeṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūto buddhaipūrvakaḥ ।।
mukhyaḥ sargaścaturthastu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
tiryakstrotastu yaḥ proktastiryagyonyaḥ sa pañcamaḥ ।।
tathordhvastrotasāṃ ṣaṣṭho devasargastu sa smṛtaḥ ।
tator'vākstrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ ।।
aṣṭamo anugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikastāmasaśca saḥ ।
pañcaite vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtāstu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
prākṛto vaikṛtaścaiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
ityete vai samākhyātā nava sargāḥ prajāpateḥ ।।

iti śrī mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe prākṛtavaikṛtasargo nāma saptacātvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

aṣṭacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

samāsāt kathitā sṛṣṭiḥ samyag bhagavatā mama ।
devādīnāṃ bhavaṃ brahman vistarāttu bravīhi me ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

kuśalākuśalairbrahman ! bhāvitā pūrvakamarmabhiḥ ।
khyātā tathā hyanirmuktāḥ pralaye hyu pasaṃhṛtāḥ ।।
devādyāḥ sthāvarāntāśca prajā brahmaṃścaturvidhāḥ ।
brahmaṇaḥ kurvataḥ sṛṣṭiṃ jajñire mānasāstadā ।।
tato devāsurān pitṝn mānuṣāṃśca catuṣṭayam ।
sisṛkṣurambhāṃsyetāni svamātmānamayūyujat ।।
yuktātmanastamomātrā udriktābhūt prajāpateḥ ।
sisṛkṣorjaghanāt pūrvamasurā jajñire tataḥ ।।
utsasarja tatastāntu tamomātrātmikāṃ tanum ।
sāpaviddhā tanustena sadyo rātrirajāyata ।।
anyāṃ tanumupādāya sisṛkṣuḥ prītimāpa saḥ ।
sattvodrekāstato devā mukhatastasya jajñire ।।
utsasarja ca bhūteśastanuṃ tāmapyasau vibhuḥ ।
sā cāpaviddhā divasaṃ sattvaprāyamajāyat ।।
sattvamātrātmikāmeva tato anyāṃ jagṛhe tanum ।
pitṛvanmanyamānasya pitarastasya jajñire ।।
sṛṣṭvā pitṝnutsasarja tanuṃ tāmapi sa prabhuḥ ।
sā cotsṛṣṭābhavat sandhyā divananaktāntarasthitā ।।
rajomātrātmikāmanyāṃ tanuṃ bheje atha sa prabhuḥ ।
tato manuṣyāḥ sambhūtā rajomātrāsamudbhavāḥ ।।
sṛṣṭvā manuṣyān sa vibhurutsasarja tanuṃ tataḥ ।
jyotsnā samabhavat sā ca naktānte aharmukhe ca yā ।।
ityetāstanavastasya devadevasya dhīmataḥ ।
khyātā rātryahanī caiva sandhyā jyotsnā ca vai dvija ।।
jyotstanā sandhyā tathaivāhasattvamātrātmakaṃ trayam ।
tamomātrātmikā rātriḥ sā vai tasmāt triyāmikā ।।
tasmād devā divā rātrāvasurāstu balānvitāḥ ।
jyotsnāgame ca manujāḥ sandhyāyāṃ pitarastathā ।।
bhavanti balino adhṛṣyā vipakṣāṇāṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।
tadviparyayamāsādya prayānti ca viparyayam ।।
jyotsno rātryahanī sandhyā catvāryetāni vai prabhoḥ ।
brahmaṇastu śarīrāṇi triguṇopaśritāni tu ।।
catvāryetānyathotpādya tanumanyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।
rajastamomayīṃ rātrau jagṛhe kṣuttṛḍanvitaḥ ।।
tadandhakāre kṣutkṣāmānasṛjad bhagavānajaḥ ।
virūpān śmaśrulānattumārabdhāste ca tāṃ tanum ।।
rakṣāma iti tebhyo anye ya ūcuste tu rākṣasāḥ ।
khādāma iti ye cocuste yakṣā yakṣaṇāt dvija ।।
tān dṛṣṭvā hyapriyeṇāsya keśāḥ śīryanta vedhasaḥ ।
samārohaṇahīnāśca śiraso brahmaṇastu te ।।
sarpaṇātte abhavan sarpā hīnatvādahayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
sarpān dṛṣṭvā tataḥ krodhāt krodhātmāno vinirmame ।।
varṇena kapilenogrāste bhūtāḥ piśitāśanāḥ ।
dhyāyato gāṃ tatastasya gandharvā jajñire sutāḥ ।।
jajñire pibato vācaṃ gandharvāstena te smṛtāḥ ।
aṣṭāsvetāsu sṛṣṭāsu devayoniṣu sa prabhuḥ ।।
tataḥ svadehato anyāni vayāṃsi paśavo asṛjat ।
mukhato ajāḥ sasarjātha vakṣasaścāvayo asṛjat ।।
gāvaścaivodarād brahmā pārśvābhyāñca vinirmame ।
padbhyāñcāśvān sa mātaṅgān rāsabān śaśakān mṛgān ।।
uṣṭrānaśvatarāṃścaiva nānārūpāśca jātayaḥ ।
oṣadhyaḥ phalamūlinyo romabhyastasya jajñire ।।
evaṃ paśvoṣadhīḥ sṛṣṭvā hyayajaccādhvare vibhuḥ ।
tasmādādau tu kalpasya tretāyugamukhe tadā ।।
gaurajaḥ puruṣo meṣo aśvāśvataragardabhāḥ ।
etān grāmyān paśūnāhurāraṇyāṃśca nibodha me ।।
śvāpadaṃ dvikhuraṃ hastī vānarāḥ pakṣipañcamāḥ ।
audakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamāstu sarīsṛpāḥ ।।
gāyatrīñca ṛcañcaiva trivṛt somaṃ rathantaram ।
agniṣṭomañca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamānmukhāt ।।
yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ dhandaḥ stomaṃ pañcadaśantathā ।
bṛhat sāma tathokathañca dakṣiṇādasṛjanmukhāt ।।
sāmāni jagatīcchandaḥ stomaṃ pañcadaśantathā ।
vairūpamatirātrañca nirmame paścimānmukhāt ।।
ekaviśamatharvāṇamāptoryāmāṇameva ca ।
anuṣṭubhaṃ savairājamuttarādasṛjanmukhāt ।।
vidyuto aśanimeghāśca rohitendradhanūṃṣi ca ।
vayāṃsi ca sasarjādau kalpasya bhagavān vibhuḥ ।।
uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastalasya jajñire ।
sṛṣṭvā catuṣṭayaṃ pūrvaṃ devāsurapitṝn prajāḥ ।।
tato asṛjat sa bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।
yakṣān piśācān gandharvāṃstathaivāpsarasāṅgaṇān ।।
narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥ paśumṛgoragān ।
avyayañca vyayañcaiva yadidaṃ sthāṇujaṅgamam ।।
teṣāṃ ye yāni karmāṇi prāk sṛṣṭeḥ pratipedire ।
tānyeva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।
hiṃstrāhiṃstre mṛdukrūre dharmādharmāvṛtānṛte ।
tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāttattasya rocate ।।
indriyārtheṣu bhūteṣu śarīreṣu ca sa prabhuḥ ।
nānātvaṃ viniyogañca dhātaiva vyadadhāt svayam ।।
nāma rūpañca bhūtānāṃ kṛtyānāñca prapañcanam ।
vedaśabdebhya evādau devādīnāñcakāra saḥ ।।
ṛṣīṇāṃ nāmadheyāni yāśca deveṣu sṛṣṭayaḥ ।
śarvaryante prasūtānāmanyeṣāñca dadāti saḥ ।।
yathartāvṛtuliṅgāni nānārūpāṇi paryaye ।
dṛśyante tāni tānyeva tathā bhāvā yugādiṣu ।।
evaṃvidhāḥ sṛṣṭayastu brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।
śarvaryante prabuddhasya kalpe kalpe bhavanti vai ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sṛṣṭiprakāraṇanāmāṣṭacatvāriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

ūnapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

arvākstrotastu kathito bhavatā yastu mānuṣaḥ ।
brahman ! vistarato brūhi brahmā samasṛjadyathā ।।
yathā ca varṇānasṛjadyad guṇāśca mahāmate ।
yacca yeṣāṃ smṛtaṃ karma viprādīnāṃ vadasva tat ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

brahmaṇaḥ sṛjataḥ pūrvaṃ satyābhidhyāyinastathā ।
mithunānāṃ sahasrantu mukhāt so athāsṛjanmune ।।
jātāste hyu papadyante sattvodriktāḥ svatejasaḥ ।
sahasramanyadvakṣasto mithunānāṃ sasarja ha ।।
te sarve rajasodriktāḥ śuṣmiṇaścāpyamarṣiṇaḥ ।
sasarjānyate sahasrantu dvandvānāmūrutaḥ punaḥ ।।
rajastamobhyāmudriktā īhāśīlāstu te smṛtāḥ ।
padbhyāṃ sahasramanyacca mithunānāṃ sasarja ha ।।
udriktāstamasā sarve niḥ śrīkā hyalpacetasaḥ ।
tataḥ saṃharṣamāṇāste dvandvotpannāstu prāṇinaḥ ।।
anyonyahṛrcchyāviṣṭā maithunāyopacakramuḥ ।
tataḥ prabhṛti kalpe asmin mithunānāṃ hi sambhavaḥ ।।
māsi māsyārtavaṃ yat tu na tadāsīttu yoṣitām ।
tasmāttadā na suṣuvuḥ sevitairapi maithunaiḥ ।।
āyuṣo ante prasūyante mithunānyeva tāḥ sakṛt ।
tataḥ prabhṛti kalpe asmin mithunānāṃ hi sambhavaḥ ।।
dhyānena manasā tāsāṃ prajānāṃ jāyate sakṛt ।
śabdādirviṣayaḥ śuddhaḥ pratyekaṃ pañcalakṣaṇaḥ ।।
ityeṣā mānuṣī sṛṣṭiryā pūrvaṃ vai prajāpateḥ ।
tasyānvavāyasambhūtā yairidaṃ pūritaṃ jagat ।।
saritsaraḥ samudrāṃśca sevante parvatānapi ।
tāstadā hyalpaśītoṣṇā yuge tasmiṃścaranti vai ।।
tṛptiṃ svābhāvikīṃ prāptā viṣayeṣu mahāmate ।
na tāsāṃ pratighāto asti na dveṣo nāpi matsaraḥ ।।
parvatodadhisevinyo hyaniketāstu sarvaśaḥ ।
tā vai niṣkāmacāriṇyo nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ ।।
piśācoragarakṣāṃsi tathā matsariṇo janāḥ ।
paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaścaiva nakrā matsyāḥ sarīsṛpāḥ ।।
avārakā hyaṇḍajā vā te hyadharmaprasūtayaḥ ।
na mūlaphalapuṣpāṇi nārtavā vatsarāṇi ca ।।
sarvakālasukhaḥ kālo nātyarthaṃ gharmaśītatā ।
kālena gacchatā teṣāṃ citrā siddhirajāyata ।।
tataśca teṣāṃ pūrvāhne madhyāhne ca vitṛptatā ।
punastathecchatāṃ tṛptiranāyāsena sābhavat ।।
icchatāñca tathāyāso manasaḥ samajāyata ।
apāṃ saukṣmyaṃ tatastāsāṃ siddhirnānārasollasā ।।
samajāyata caivānyā sarvakāmapradāyinī ।
asaṃskāryaiḥ śarīraiśca prajāstāḥ sthirayauvanāḥ ।।
tāsāṃ vinā tu saṃkalpaṃ jāyante mithunāḥ prajāḥ ।
samaṃ janma ca rūpañca mriyante caiva tāḥ samam ।।
anicchādveṣasaṃyuktā vartante tu parasparam ।
tulyarūpāyuṣaḥ sarvā adhamottamatāṃ vinā ।।
tatvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।
āyuḥ pramāṇaṃ jīvanti na ca kleśādvipattayaḥ ।।
kvacit kvacit punaḥ sābhūt kṣitirbhāgyena sarvaśaḥ ।
kālena gacchatā nāśamupayānti yathā prajāḥ ।।
tathā tāḥ kramaśo nāśaṃ jagmuḥ sarvatra siddhayaḥ ।
tāsu sarvāsu naṣṭāsu nabhasaḥ pracyutā narāḥ ।।
prāyaśaḥ kalpavṛkṣāste saṃbhūtā gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ ।
sarve pratyupabhogāśca tāsaṃ tebhyaḥ prajāyate ।।
vartayanti sma tebhyastāstretāyugamukhe tadā ।
tataḥ kālena vai rāgastāsāmākasmiko abhavat ।।
māsi māsyārtavotpattyā garbhotpattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
rāgotpattyā tatastāsāṃ vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ ।।
brahmannanvapareṣāntu petuḥ śākhā mahīruhām ।
vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣvābharaṇāni ca ।।
teṣveva jāyate teṣāṃ gandhavarṇarasānvitam ।
amākṣikaṃ māhavīryaṃ puṭake puṭake madhu ।।
tena vā vartayanti sma mukhe treyāyugasya vai ।
tataḥ kālāntareṇaiva punarlobhānvitāstu tāḥ ।।
vṛkṣāṃstāḥ paryagṛhṇanta mamatvāviṣṭacetasaḥ ।
neśustenāpacāreṇa te api tāsāṃ mahīruhāḥ ।।
tato dvandvānyajāyante śītoṣṇakṣunmukhāni vai ।
tāstaddvandvopaghātārthaṃ cakruḥ pūrvaṃ purāṇi tu ।।
marudhanvaṣu durgeṣu parvateṣu darīṣu ca ।
saṃśrayanti ca durgāṇi vārkṣaṃ pārvatamaudakam ।।
kṛtrimañca tathā durgaṃ mitvā mitvātmano।
mānārthāni pramāṇāni tāstu pūrvaṃ pracakrire ।।
paramāṇuḥ paraṃ sūkṣmaṃ traṣareṇurmahīrajaḥ ।
bālāgrañcaiva likṣāṃ ca yūkāṃ cātha yavodaram ।।
kramādaṣṭaguṇānyāhuryavānaṣṭau tathāṅgulam ।
ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ padaṃ tacca vitastirdviguṇaṃ smṛtam ।।
dve vitastī tathā hasto brāhmyatīrthādiveṣṭanaḥ ।
caturhastaṃ dhanurdaṇḍo nāḍikāryugameva ca ।।
dhanuṣāṃ dve sahasre tu gavyūtistaccaturguṇam ।
proktañca yojavanaṃ prājñaiḥ saṃkhyānārthamidaṃ param ।।
caturṇāmatha durgāṇāṃ svasamutthāni trīṇi tu ।
caturthaṃ kṛtrimaṃ durgaṃ te cakruryatnatastu vai ।।
purañca kheṭakañcaiva tadvad droṇīmukhaṃ dvija ।
śākhānagarakañcāpi tathā karvaṭakaṃ dramī ।।
grāmaṃ saghoṣavinyāsaṃ teṣu cāvasathān pṛthak ।
sotsedhavaprakārañca sarvataḥ parikhāvṛtam ।।
yojanārdhārdhaviṣkambhamaṣṭabhāgāyataṃ puram ।
prāgudakpravaṇaṃ śastaṃ śuddhavaṃśabahirgamam ।।
tadardhena tathā kheṭaṃ tatpādena ca karvaṭam ।
nyūnaṃ droṇīmukhaṃ tasmādantabhāgena cocyate ।।
prākāraparikhāhīnāṃ puraṃ kharvaṭamucyate ।
śākhānagarakañcānyanmantrisāmantabhuktimat ।।
tathā śūdrajanaprāyāḥ svasamṛddhikṛṣībalāḥ ।
kṣetropabhogyabhūmadhye vasatirgrāmasaṃjñitā ।।
anyasmānnagarāderyā kāryamuddiśya mānavaiḥ ।
kriyate vasatiḥ sā vai vijñeyā vasatirnaraiḥ ।।
duṣṭaprāyo vinā kṣetraiḥ parabhūmicaro balī ।
grāma eva dramīsaṃjño rājavallabhasaṃśrayaḥ ।।
śakaṭārūḍhabhāṇḍaiśca gopālairvipaṇaṃ vinā ।
gosamūhaistathā ghoṣo yatrecchābhūmiketanaḥ ।।
ta evaṃ nagarādīṃstu kṛtvā vāsārthamātmanaḥ ।
niketanāni dvandvānāṃ cakrurāvasathāya vai ।।
gṛhākārā yathā pūrvaṃ teṣāmāsannahīruhāḥ ।
tathā saṃsmṛtya tatsarvaṃ cakrurveśmāni tāḥ prajāḥ ।।
vṛkṣasyaivaṅgatāḥ śākhāstathaivañcāparī gatāḥ ।
natāścaivonnatāścaiva tadvacchākhāḥ pracakrire ।।
yāḥ śākhāḥ kalpavṛkṣāṇāṃ pūrvamāsan dvijottama ।
tā eva śākhā gehānāṃ śālātvaṃ tena tāsu tat ।।
kṛtvā dvandvopaghātante vārtopāyamacintayan ।
naṣṭeṣu madhunā sārdhaṃ kalpavṛkṣeṣvaśeṣataḥ ।।
viṣādavyākulāstā vai prajāstṛṣṇākṣudhārditāḥ ।
tataḥ prādurbabhau tāsāṃ siddhistretāmukhe tadā ।।
vārtāsvasādhitā hyanyā vṛṣṭistāsāṃ nikāmataḥ ।
tāsāṃ vṛṣṭyudakānīha yāni nimnagatāni vai ।।
vṛṣṭyāvaruddhairabhavat strotaḥ khātāni nimnagāḥ ।
ye purastādapāṃ stokā āpannāḥ pṛthivītale ।।
tato bhūmeśca saṃyogādoṣadhyastāstadā bhavan ।
aphālakṛṣṭāścānuptā grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa ।।
ṛtupuṣpaphalāścaiva vṛkṣā gulmāśca jajñire ।
prādurbhāvastu tretāyāmādyo ayamauṣadhasya tu ।।
tenauṣadhena vartante prajāstretāyuge mune ।
rāgalobhau samāsādya prajāścākasmikau tadā ।।
tatastāḥ paryagvahṇanta nadīkṣetrāṇi parvatān ।
vṛkṣagulmauṣadhīścaivamātmanyāyādyathābalam ।।
tena doṣeṇa tā neśurauṣadhyo miṣatāṃ dvija ।
agrasad bhūryugapattāstadauṣadhyo mahāmate ।।
punastāsu praṇaṣṭāsu vibhrāntāstāḥ punaḥ prajāḥ ।
brahmāṇaṃ śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ kṣudhārtāḥ parameṣṭhinam ।।
sa cāpi tattvato jñātvā tadā grastāṃ vasundharām ।
vatsaṃ kṛtvā sumeruntu dudoha bhagavān vibhuḥ ।।
dugdheyaṃ gaustadā tena śasyāni pṛthivītale ।
jajñire tāni bījāni grāmyāraṇyāstu tāḥ punaḥ ।।
oṣadhyaḥ phalapākāntā gaṇāḥ saptadaśā smṛtāḥ ।
vrīhayaśca yavāścaiva godhūmā aṇavastilāḥ ।।
priyaṅgavo hyudārāśca koradūṣāḥ sacīnakāḥ ।
māṣā mudgā masūrāśca niṣpāvāḥ sakulatthakāḥ ।।
āḍhakāścaṇakāścaiva gaṇāḥ saptadaśa smṛtāḥ ।
ityetā oṣadhīnāntu grāmyāṇāṃ jātayaḥ purā ।।
oṣadhyo jajñiyāścaiva grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa ।
vrīhayaśca yavāścaiva godhūmā aṇavastilāḥ ।।
priyaṅgusaptamā hyete aṣṭamāstu kulatthakāḥ ।
śyāmākāstvatha nīvārā yattilā sagavedhukāḥ ।।
kuruvindā markaṭakāstathā veṇuyavāśca ye ।
grāmyāraṇyāḥ smṛtā hyetā oṣadhyaśca caturdaśa ।।
yadā prasṛṣṭā oṣadhyo na prarohanti tāḥ punaḥ ।
tataḥ sa tāsāṃ vṛddhyarthaṃ vārtopāyañcakāra ha ।।
brahmā svayambhūrbhagavān hastasiddhiñca karmajām ।
tataḥ prabhṛtyathauṣadhyaḥ kṛṣṭapacyāstu jajñire ।।
saṃsiddhāyāntu vārtāyāṃ tatastāsāṃ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।
maryādāṃ sthāpayāmāsa yathānyāyaṃ yathāguṇam ।।
varṇānāmāśramāṇāñca dharmān dharmabhṛtāṃvara ।
lokānāṃ sarvavarṇānāṃ samyagdharmārthapālinām ।।
prājāpatyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ kriyāvatām ।
sthānamaindraṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ saṃgrāmeṣvapalāyinām ।।
vaiśyānāṃ mārutaṃ sthānaṃ svadharmamanuvartatām ।
gāndharvaṃ śūdrajātīnāṃ paricaryānuvartatām ।।
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇāmṛṣīṇāmūrdhvaretasām ।
smṛtaṃ teṣāntu yat sthānaṃ tadeva guruvāsinām ।।
saptarṣoṇāntu yat sthānaṃ smṛtaṃ tadvai vanaukasām ।
prājāpatyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ nyāsināṃ brahmaṇaḥ kṣayam ।
yogināmamṛtaṃ sthānamiti vai sthānakalpanā ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sṛṣṭiprakaraṇe ekonapañcāśadadhyāyaḥ

pañyāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tato abhidyāyatastasya jajñire mānasīḥ prajāḥ ।
taccharīrasamutpannaiḥ kāryaistaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ saha ।।
kṣetrajñāḥ samavartanta gātrebyastasya dhīmataḥ ।
te sarve samavartanta ye mayā pragudāhṛtāḥ ।।
devādyāḥ sthāvarāntāśca traiguṇyaviṣayāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
evaṃbhūtāni sṛṣṭāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।।
yadāsya tāḥ prajāḥ sarvā na vyavardhanta dhīmataḥ ।
athānyānmānasān putrānu sadṛśānātmano asṛjat ।।
bhṛguṃ pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratumaṅgirasantathā ।
marīciṃ dakṣamatriñca vasiṣṭañcaiva mānasam ।।
nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṅgatāḥ ।
tato asṛjat punarbrahmā rudraṃ krodhātmasambhavam ।।
saṅkalpañcaiva dharmañca pūrveṣāmapi pūrvajam ।
sanandanādayo ye ca pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।।
na te lokeṣu sajjanto nirapekṣāḥ samāhitāḥ ।
sarve te anāgatajñānā vītarāgā vimatsarāḥ ।।
teṣvevaṃ nirapekṣeṣu lokasṛṣṭau mahātmanaḥ ।
brahmaṇo abūnmahākrodhastatrotpannor'kasannibhaḥ ।।
ardhanārīnaravapuḥ puruṣo atiśarīravān ।
vibhajātmānamityuktvā sa tadāntardadhe tataḥ ।।
sa cokto vai pṛthak strītvaṃ puruṣatvaṃ tathākarot ।
bibheda puruṣatvañca daśadhā caikadhā tu saḥ ।।
saumyāsaumyaistathā śāntaiḥ puṃstvaṃ strītvañca sa prabhuḥ ।
bibheda bahudhā devaḥ puruṣairasitaiḥ sitaiḥ ।।
tato brahmātmasambhūtaṃ pūrvaṃ svāyambhuvaṃ prabhuḥ ।
ātmanaḥ sadṛśaṃ kṛtvā prajāpālo manuṃ dvija ।।
śatarūpāñca tāṃ nārīṃ taponirdhūtakalmaṣām ।
svāyambhuvo manurdevaḥ patnītve jagṛhe vibhuḥ ।।
tasmācca puruṣāt putrau śatarūpā vyajāyata ।
priyavratottānapādau prakhyātāvātmakarmabhiḥ ।।
kanye dve ca tathā ṛddhiṃ prasūtiñca tataḥ pitā ।
dadau pursūtiṃ dakṣāya tathā ṛddhiṃ ruceḥ purā ।।
prajāpatiḥ sa jagrāha tayoryajñaḥ sadakṣiṇaḥ ।
putro jajñe mahābhāga ! dampatīmithunaṃ tataḥ ।।
yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāntu putrā dvādaśa jajñire ।
yāmā iti samākhyātā devāḥ svāyambhuvo antare ।।
tasya putrāstu yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ sabhāsvarāḥ ।
prasūtyāñca tathā dakṣaścatastro viṃśatistathā ।।
sasarja kanyāstāsāñca samyaṅnāmāni me śṛṇu ।
śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtistuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirmedhā kriyā tathā ।।
buddhirlajjā vapuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrtistrayodaśī ।
patnyarthe pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ ।।
tābhyaḥ śiṣṭā yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ ।
khyātiḥ satyatha sambhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītistathā kṣamā ।।
santatiścānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā ।
bhṛgurbhavo marīciśca tathā caivāṅgirā muniḥ ।।
pulastyaḥ pulahaścaiva kratuśca ṛṣayastathā ।
vasiṣṭho atristathā vahniḥ pitaraśca yathākramam ।।
khyātyādyā jagṛhuḥ kanyā munayo munisattamāḥ ।
śraddhā kāmaṃ śrīśca darpaṃ niyamaṃ dhṛtirātmajam ।।
santoṣañca tathā tuṣṭirlobhaṃ puṣṭirajāyata ।
medhā śrutaṃ kriyā daṇḍaṃ nayaṃ vinayameva ca ।।
bodhaṃ buddhistathā lajjā vinayaṃ vapurātmajam ।
vyavasāyaṃ prajajñe vai kṣemaṃ śāntirasūyata ।।
sukhaṃ siddhiryaśaḥ kīrtirityete dharmayonayaḥ ।
kāmādatimudaṃ harṣaṃ dharmapautramasūyata ।।
hiṃsā bhāryā tvadharmasya tasyāṃ jajñe tathānṛtam ।
kanyā ca nirṛtistasyāṃ sutau dvau narakaṃ bhayam ।।
māyā ca vedanā caiva mithunaṃ dvayametayoḥ ।
tayorjajñe atha vai māyā mṛtyuṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam ।।
vedanātmasutañcāpi duḥkhaṃ jajñe atha rauravāt ।
mṛtyorvyādhi-jarā-śoka-tṛṣṇā-krodhāśca jajñire ।।
duḥ khodbhavāḥ smṛtā hyete sarve vādharmalakṣaṇāḥ ।
naiṣāṃ bhāryāsti putro vā sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ ।।
nirṛtiśca tathā cānyā mṛtyorbhāryābhavanmune ।
alakṣmīrnāma tasyāñca mṛtyoḥ putrāścaturdaśa ।।
alakṣmīputrakā hyete mṛtyorādeśakāriṇaḥ ।
vināśakāleṣu narān bhajantyete śṛṇuṣva tān ।।
indriyeṣu daśasvete tathā manasi ca sthitāḥ ।
sve sve naraṃ striyaṃ vāpi viṣaye yojayanti hi ।।
athendriyāṇi cākramya rāgakrodhādibhirnarān ।
yojayanti yathā hāniṃ yāntyadharmādibhirdvija ।।
ahaṅkāragataścānyastathānyo buddhisaṃsthitaḥ ।
vināśāya narāḥ strīṇāṃ yatante mahosaṃśritāḥ ।।
tathaivānyo gṛhe puṃsāṃ duḥ saho nāma viśrutaḥ ।
kṣutkṣāmo adhomukho nagraścīrī kākasamasvanaḥ ।।
sa sarvān khādituṃ sṛṣṭo brahmaṇā tamaso nidhiḥ ।
daṃṣṭrākarālamatyarthaṃ vivṛtāsyaṃ subhairavam ।।
tamattukāmamāhedaṃ brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
sarvabrahmamayaḥ śuddhaḥ kāraṇaṃ jagato avyayaḥ ।।

brahmovāca

nāttavyante jagadidaṃ jahi kopaṃ śamaṃ vraja ।
tyajaināntāmasī vṛttimapāsya rajasaḥ kalām ।।

duḥ saha uvāca

kṣutkṣāmo asmi jagannātha ! pipāsuścāpi durbalaḥ ।
kathaṃ tṛptimiyānnātha ! bhaveyaṃ balavān katham ।
kaścāśrayo mamākyāhi varteyaṃ yatra nirvṛtaḥ ।।

brahmovāca

tavāśrayo gṛhaṃ puṃsāṃ janaścādhārmiko balam ।
puṣṭiṃ nityakriyāhānyā bhavān vatsa ! gamiṣyati ।।
vṛthāsphoṭāśca te vastramāhārañca dadāmi te ।
kṣataṃ kīṭāvapannañca tathā śvabiravekṣitam ।।
bhagnabhāṇāgatantadvanmukhavātopaśāmitam ।
ucchiṣṭāpakvamāsvinnamavalīḍhamasaṃskṛtam ।।
bhagnāsanasthitairbhuktamāsannāgatameva ca ।
vidiṅmukhaṃ sandhyayośca nṛtyavādyasvanākulam ।।
udakyopahataṃ bhuktamudakyā dṛṣṭameva ca ।
yaccopaghātavat kiñcid bhakṣyaṃ peyamathāpi vā ।।
etāni tava puṣṭyarthamanyaccāpi dadāmi te ।
aśraddhayā hutaṃ dattamasnātairyadavajñayā ।।
yannāmbupūrvakaṃ kṣiptamanarthokṛtameva ca ।
tyaktumāviṣkṛtaṃ yat tu dattaṃ caivātivismayāt ।।
duṣṭaṃ kruddhārtadattañca yakṣa tadbhāgi tat phalam ।
yacca paunarbhavaḥ kiñcit karotyāmuṣmikaṃ kramam ।।
yacca paunarbhavā yoṣit tadyakṣa ! tava tṛptaye ।
kanyāśulkopadhānāya samupāste dhanakriyāḥ ।।
tathaiva yakṣa ! puṣṭyarthamasacchāstrakriyāśca yāḥ ।
yaccārthanirvṛtaṃ kiñcidadhītaṃ yanna satyataḥ ।।
tata sarvaṃ tava kālāṃśca dadāmi tava siddhaye ।
gurviṇyabhigame sandhyānityakāryavyatikrame ।।
asacchāstrakriyālāpadūṣiteṣu ca duḥ saha ।
tavābhibhavasāmarthyaṃ bhaviṣyati sadā nṛṣu ।।
paṅktibhede vṛthāpāke pākabhede tathā kriyā ।
nityañca gehakalahe bhavitā vasatistava ।।
apoṣyamāṇe ca tathā bhṛtye govāhanādike ।
asandhyābhyukṣitāgāre kāle tvatto bhayaṃ nṛṇām ।।
nakṣatragrahapīḍāsu trividhotpātadarśane ।
aśāntikaparān yakṣa ! narānabhibhaviṣyasi ।।
vṛthopavāsino martyā dyūtastrīṣu sadā ratāḥ ।
tvadbhāṣaṇopakartāro vaiḍālavratikāśca ye ।।
abrahmacāriṇādhītamijyā cāviduṣā kṛtā ।
tapovane grāmyabhujāṃ tathaivānirvajitātmanām ।।
brāhmaṇa-kṣatriya-viśāṃ śūdrāṇāñca svakarmataḥ ।
paricyutānāṃ yā ceṣṭā paralokārthamīpsatām ।।
tasyāśca yat phalaṃ sarvaṃ tat te yakṣa ! bhaviṣyati ।
anyacca te prayacchāmi puṣṭyarthaṃ sannibodha tat ।।
bhavato vaiśvadevānte nāmoccāraṇapūrvakam ।
etat taveti dāsyanti bhavato balimūrjitam ।।
yaḥ saṃskṛtāśī vidhivacchucirantastathā bahiḥ ।
alolupo jitastrīkastadgehamapavarjaya ।।
pūjyante havyakavyābhyāṃ devatāḥ pitarastathā ।
yāmayo atithayaścāpi tadgehaṃ yakṣa ! varjaya ।।
yatra maitrī gṛhe bālavṛddhayoṣinnareṣu ca ।
tathā svajanavargeṣu gṛhaṃ taccāpi varjaya ।।
yoṣito abiratā yatra na vahirgamanotsukāḥ ।
lajjānvitāḥ sadā gehaṃ yakṣa ! tat parivarjaya ।।
vayaḥ sambandhayogyāni śayanānyaśanāni ca ।
yatra gehe tvayā yakṣa ! tadvarjyaṃ vacanānmama ।।
yatra kāruṇikā nityaṃ sādhukarmaṇyavasthitāḥ ।
sāmānyopaskarairyuktāstyajethā yakṣa ! tadgṛham ।।
yatrāsanasthāstiṣṭhatsu guru-vṛddha-dvijātiṣu ।
na tiṣṭhanti gṛhaṃ tacca varjyaṃ yakṣa ! tvayā sadā ।।
tarugulmādibhirdhāraṃ na viddhaṃ yasya veśmanaḥ ।
marmabhedo athavā puṃsastacchreyo bhavanaṃ na te ।।
devatāpitṛbhṛttyānāmatithīnāñca vartanam ।
ysāyavaśiṣṭenānnena puṃsastasya gṛhaṃ tyaja ।।
satyavākyān kṣamāśīlānahiṃstrānnānutāpinaḥ ।
puruṣānīdṛśān yakṣa ! tyajethāścānasūyakān ।।
bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇe yuktāmasatstrīsaṅgavarjitām ।
kuṭumbabhartṛśeṣānnapuṣṭāñca tyaja yoṣitam ।।
yajanādhyayanābhyāsadānāsaktamatiṃ sadā ।
yājanādhyāpanādānakṛtavṛttiṃ dvijaṃ tyaja ।।
dānādhyayanayajñeṣu sadodyuktañca duḥ saha ।
kṣatriyaṃ tyaja sacchulkaśastrājīvāttavetanam ।।
tribhiḥ pūrvaguṇairyuktaṃ pāśupālya-vaṇijyayoḥ ।
kṛṣeścāvāptavṛttiñca tyaja vaiśyamakalmaṣam ।।
dānejhyā-dvijaśuśrūṣā-tatparaṃ yakṣa ! santyaja ।
śūdrañca brāhmaṇādīnāṃśuśrūṣāvṛttipoṣakam ।।
śrutismṛtyavirodhena kṛtavṛttirgṛhe gṛhī ।
yatra tatra ca tatpatni tasyaivānugatātmikā ।।
yatra putro guroḥ pūjāṃ devānāñca tathā pituḥ ।
patnī ca bhartuḥ kurute tatrālakṣmībhayaṃ kutaḥ ।।
sadānuliptaṃ sandhyāsu gṛhamambusamukṣitam ।
kṛtapuṣpabaliṃ yakṣa ! na tvaṃ śaknoṣi vīkṣitum ।।
bhāskarādṛṣṭaśayyāni nityāgnisalilāni ca ।
sūryāvalokadīpāni lakṣmyā gehāni bhājanam ।।
yatrokṣā candanaṃ vīṇā ādarśo madhusarpiṣī ।
viṣājyatāmrapātrāṇi tadgṛhaṃ na tavāśrayaḥ ।।
yatra kaṣṭakino vṛkṣā yatra niṣpāvavallarī ।
bhāryā punarbhūrvalmīkastadyakṣa ! tava mandiram ।।
yasmin gṛhe narāḥ pañca strītrayaṃ tāvatīśca gāḥ ।
andhakārendhanāgniśca tadgṛhaṃ vasatistava ।।
ekacchāgaṃ dvivāleyaṃ trigavaṃ pañcamāhiṣam ।
ṣaḍaśvaṃ saptamātaṅgaṃ gṛhaṃ yakṣāśu śoṣaya ।।
kuddāladātrapiṭakaṃ tadvat sthālyādibhājanam ।
yatra tatraiva kṣiptāni tava dadyuḥ pratiśrayam ।।
musalolūkhale strīṇāmāsyā tadvadudumbare ।
avaskare mantraṇañca yakṣaitadupakṛt tava ।।
laṅghyante yatra dhānyāni pakvāpakvāni veśmani ।
tadvacchāstrāṇi tatra tvaṃ yatheṣṭaṃ cara duḥ saha ।।
sthālīpidhāne yatrāgnirdatto darvophalena vā ।
gṛhe tatra duriṣṭānāmaśeṣāṇāṃ samāśrayaḥ ।।
mānuṣāsthi gṛhe yatra divārātraṃ mṛtasthitiḥ ।
tatra yakṣa ! tavāvāsastathānyeṣāñca rakṣasām ।।
adattvā bhuñjate ye vai bandhoḥ piṇḍaṃ tathodakam ।
sapiṇḍān sodakāṃścaiva tatkāle tān narān bhaja ।।
yatra padmapahāpadmau surabhirmokāśinī ।
vṛṣabhairāvatau yatra kalpyante tadgṛhaṃ tyaja ।।
aśastrā devatā yatra saśastrāścāhavaṃ vinā ।
kalpyante manujairarcyāstat parityaja mandiram ।।
paurajānapadairyatra prākprasiddhamahotsavāḥ ।
kriyante pūrvavad gehe na tvaṃ tatra gṛhe cara ।।
śūrpavātaghaṭāmbhobhiḥ strānaṃ vastrāmbuvipruṣaiḥ ।
nakhāgrasalilaiścaiva tān yāhi hatalakṣaṇān ।।
deśācārān samayān jñātidharmaṃ
japaṃ hopaṃ maṅgalaṃ devateṣṭim ।
samyakśaucaṃ vidhivallokavādān
puṃsastvayā kurvato māstu saṅgaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ityuktvā duḥ sahaṃ brahmā tatraivāntaradhīyata ।
cakāra śāsanaṃ so api tathā paṅkajajanmanaḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe yakṣānuśāsano nāma pañcāśo adhyāyaḥ

ekapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

duḥ sahasyābhavadbhāryā nirmāṣṭirnāma nāmataḥ ।
jātā kalestu bhāryāyāmṛtau cāṇḍāladarśanāt ।।
tayorapatyānyabhavane jagadvyāpīni ṣoḍaśa ।
aṣṭau kumārāḥ kanyāśca tathāṣṭāvatibhīṣaṇāḥ ।।
tantākṛṣṭistathoktiśca parivartastathāparaḥ ।
aṅgadhruk śakuniścaiva gaṇḍaprāntaratistathā ।।
garbhahā sasyahā cānyaḥ kumārāstanayāstayoḥ ।
kanyāścānyāstathaivāṣṭau tāsāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।।
niyojikā vai prathamā tathaivānyā virodhinī ।
svayaṃhārakarī caiva bhrāmaṇī ṛtuhārikā ।।
smṛtibījahare cānye tayoḥ kanye atidāruṇe ।
vidveṣaṇyaṣṭamī nāma kanyā lokabhayāvahā ।।
etāsāṃ karma vakṣyāmi doṣapraśamanañca yat ।
aṣṭānāñca kumārāṇāṃ śruyatāṃ dvijasattama ।।
dantākṛṣṭiḥ prasuptānāṃ bālānāṃ daśanasthitaḥ ।
karoti dantasaṃgharṣaṃ cikīrṣurduḥ sahāgamam ।।
tasyopaśamanaṃ kāryaṃ suptasya sitasarṣapaiḥ ।
śayanasyopari kṣiptairmānuṣairdaśanopari ।।
suvārccalauṣadhīsnānāttathā sacchāstrakīrtanāt ।
uṣṭrakaṇṭakakhaḍgāsthi-kṣaumavastravidhāraṇāt ।।
tiṣṭhatyanyakumārastu tathāsttvityasakṛd bruvan ।
śubhāśubhe nṛṇāṃ yuṅkte tathoktistacca nānyathā ।।
tasmādaduṣṭaṃ maṅgalyaṃ vaktavyaṃ paṇḍitaiḥ sadā ।
duṣṭe śrute tathaivokte kīrtanīyo janārdanaḥ ।।
carācaragururbrahmā yā yasya kuladevatā ।
anyagarbhe parān garbhān sadaiva parivartayan ।।
ratimāpnoti vākyañca vivakṣoranyadeva yat ।
parivartakasaṃjño ayaṃ tasyāpi sitasarṣapaiḥ ।।
rakṣoghnamantrajapyaiśca rakṣāṃ kurvota tattvavit ।
anyaścānilavannṛṇāmaṅgeṣu sphuraṇoditam ।।
śubhāśubhaṃ samācaṣṭe kuśaistasyāṅgatāḍanam ।
kākādipakṣisaṃstho anyaḥ śvāderaṅgagato api vā ।।
śubhāśubhañca śakuniḥ kumāro anyo bravīti vai ।
tatrāpi duṣṭe vyākṣepaḥ prārambhatyāga eva ca ।।
śubhe drutataraṃ kāryamiti prāha prajāpatiḥ ।
gaṇḍānteṣu sthitaścānyo muhūrtārdhaṃ dvijottama ।।
sarvārambhān kumāro atti śastātāñcānasūyatām ।
viproktyā devatāstutyā mūlotkhātena ca dvija ।।
gomūtrasarṣapastrānaistadṛkṣagrahapūjanaiḥ ।
punaśca dharmopaniṣatkaraṇaiḥ śāstradarśanaiḥ ।।
anajñayā janmanaśca praśamaṃ yāti gaṇḍavān ।
garbhe strīṇāṃ tathānyastu phalanāśī sudāruṇaḥ ।।
tasya rakṣā sadā kāryā nityaṃ śaucaniṣevaṇāt ।
prasiddhamantralikhanācchastamālyādidhāraṇāt ।।
viśuddhagehāvasathādanāyāsācca vai dvija ।
tathaiva sasyahā cānyaḥ sasyardhimupahanti yaḥ ।।
tasyāpi rakṣāṃ kurvota jīrṇopānadvidhāraṇāt ।
tathāpasavyagamanācchāṇḍālasya praveśanāt ।।
bahirbalipradānācca somāmbuparikīrtanāt ।
paradārapahadravyaharaṇādiṣu mānavān ।।
niyojayati caivānyān kanyā sā ca niyojikā ।
tasyāḥ pavitrapaṭhanāt krodhalobhādivarjanāt ।।
niyojayati māmiṣṭavirodhācca vivarjanam ।
ākruṣṭo anyena manyeta tāḍito vā niyojikā ।।
niyojayatyenamiti na gacchettadvaśaṃ budhaḥ ।
paradārādisaṃsarge cittamātmānameva ca ।।
niyojayatyatra sā māmiti prājño vicintayet ।
virodhaṃ kurute cānyā dampatyoḥ prīyamāṇayoḥ ।।
bandhūnāṃ suhṛdāṃ pitroḥ putraiḥ sāvarṇikaiśca yā ।
virodhinī sā tadrakṣāṃ kurvota balikarmaṇā ।।
tathātivādasahanācchāstrācāraniṣevaṇāt ।
dhānyaṃ khalād gṛhād gobhyaḥ payaḥ sarpistathāparā ।।
samṛddhimṛddhimaddravyādapahinti ca kanyakā ।
sā svayaṃhāriketyuktā sadāntardhānatatparā ।।
mahānasādardhasiddhamannāgārasthitaṃ tathā ।
pariviśyamāṇañca sadā sārdhaṃ bhuṅkte ca bhuñjatā ।।
uccheṣaṇaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ haratyannañca durharā ।
karmāntāgāraśālābhyaḥ siddhardhi harati dvija ।।
gostrīstanebhyaśca payaḥ kṣīrahārī sadaiva sā ।
dadhno ghṛtaṃ tilāttailaṃ surāgārāttathā surām ।।
rāgaṃ kusumbhakādīnāṃ kārpāsāt sūtrameva ca ।
sā svayaṃhārikā nāma haratyavirataṃ dvija ।।
kuryācchikhaṇḍinordvandvaṃ rakṣārthaṃ kutrimāṃ striyam ।
rakṣāścaiva gṛhe lekhyā varjyāco cchiṣṭatā tathā ।।
homāgnidevatādhūpabhasmanā ca pariṣkriyā ।
kāryā kṣīrādibhāṇḍānāmevaṃ tadrakṣaṇaṃ smṛtam ।।
udvegaṃ janayatyanyā ekasthānanivāsinaḥ ।
puruṣasya tu yā proktā bhrāmaṇī sā tu kanyakā ।।
tasyātha rakṣāṃ kurvota vikṣiptaiḥ sitasarṣapaiḥ ।
āsane śayane corvyāṃ yatrāste sa tu mānavaḥ ।।
cintayecca naraḥ pāpā māmeṣā duṣṭacetanā ।
bhrāmayatyasakṛjjapyaṃ bhuvaḥ sūktaṃ samādhinā ।।
strīṇāṃ puṣpaṃ haratyanyā pravṛttaṃ sā tu kanyakā ।
tathāpravṛttaṃ sā jñeyā dauḥ sahā ṛtahārikā ।।
kurvota tīrthadevaukaścaityaparvatasānuṣu ।
nadīsaṅgamakhāteṣu strapanaṃ tatpraśānyate ।।
mantravit kṛtatattvajñaḥ parvasūṣasi ca dvija ।
cikitsājñaśca vai vaidyaḥ saṃprayuktairvarauṣadhaiḥ ।।
smṛtiñcāpaharatyanyā strīṇāṃ sā smṛtihārikā ।
viviktadeśasevitvāttasyāścopaśamo bhavet ।।
bījāpahāriṇī cānyā strīpuṃsoratibhīṣaṇā ।
medhyānnabhojanaiḥ snānaistasyāścopaśamo bhaveta ।।
aṣṭamī dveṣaṇī nāma kanyā lokabhayāvahā ।
yā karoti janadviṣṭaṃ naraṃ nārīmathāpi vā ।।
madhukṣīraghṛtāktāṃstu śāntyarthaṃ homayettilān ।
kurvota mitravindāñca tatheṣṭintat praśānyate ।।
eteṣāntu kumārāṇāṃ kanyānāṃ dvijasattama ।
aṣṭatriṃśadapatyāni teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।।
dantākṛṣṭerabhūt kanyā vijalpā kalahā tathā ।
avajñānṛtaduṣṭoktirvijalpā tatpraśāntaye ।।
tāmeva cintayet prājñaḥ prayataśca gṛhī bhavet ।
kalahā kalahaṃ gehe karotyavirataṃ nṛṇām ।।
kuṭumbanāśahetuḥ sā tatpraśāntiṃ niśāmaya ।
dūrvāṅkurānmadhughṛtakṣīrāktān balikarmaṇi ।।
vikṣipejjuhuyāccaivānalaṃ mitrañca kīrtayet ।
bhūtānāṃ mātṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ bālakānāntu śāntaye ।।
vidyānāṃ tapasāñcaiva saṃyamasya yamasya ca ।
kṛṣyāṃ vāṇijyalābhe ca śāntiṃ kurvantu me sadā ।।
pūjitāśca yathānyāyaṃ tuṣṭiṃ gacchantu sarvaśaḥ ।
kuṣmāṇḍā yātudhānāśca ye cānye gaṇasaṃjñitāḥ ।।
mahādevaprasādena maheśvaramatena ca ।
sarva ete nṛṇāṃ nityaṃ tuṣṭimāśu vrajantu te ।।
tuṣṭāḥ sarvaṃ nirasyantu duṣkṛtaṃ duranuṣṭhitam ।
mahāpatākajaṃ sarvaṃ yaccānyadvighnakāraṇam ।।
teṣāmeva prasādena vighnā naśyantu sarvaśaḥ ।
udvāheṣu ca sarveṣu vṛddhikarmaṃsu caiva hi ।।
puṇyānuṣṭhānayogeṣu gurudevārcaneṣu ca ।
japayajñavidhāneṣu yātrāsu ca caturdaśa ।।
śarīrārogyabhogyeṣu sukhadānadhaneṣu ca ।
vṛddhabālātureṣveva śāntiṃ kurvantu me sadā ।।
somāmbupau tathāmbhodhiḥ savitā cānilānalau ।
tathokteḥ kālajihvo abhūt putrastālaniketanaḥ ।।
sa yeṣāṃ rasanāsaṃsthāstānasādhūn vibādhate ।
parivartasutau dvau tu virūpavikṛtau dvija ।।
tau tu vṛkṣāgraparikhāprākārāmbhodhisaṃśrayau ।
gurviṇyāḥ parivartantau kurutaḥ pādapāṇiṣu ।।
krauṣṭuke parivartaḥsyāt garbhasyānyodarāttataḥ ।
na vṛkṣaṃ caiva naivādriṃ na prākāraṃ mahodadhim ।।
parikhāṃ vā samākrāmedabalā garbhadhāriṇī ।
aṅgadhruk tanayaṃ lebhe piśunaṃ nāma nāmataḥ ।।
so asthimajjāgataḥ puṃsāṃ balamattyajitātmanām ।
śyena-kāka-kapotāṃśca gṛdhrolūkaiśca vai sutān ।।
avāpa śakuniḥ pañca jagṛhustān surāsurāḥ ।
śyenaṃ jagrāha mṛtyuśca kākaṃ kālo gṛhītavān ।।
ulūkaṃ nirṛtiścaiva jagrāhātibhayāvaham ।
gṛdhraṃ vyādhistadīśo atha kapotaṃ ca svayaṃ yamaḥ ।।
eteṣāmeva caivoktā bhūtāḥ pāpopapādane ।
tasmācchyenādayo yasya nilīyeyuḥ śirasyatha ।।
tenātmarakṣaṇāyālaṃ śāntiṃ kuryādvijottama ।
gehe prasūtireteṣāṃ tadvannīḍaniveśanam ।।
narastaṃ varjayed gehaṃ kapotākrāntamastakam ।
śyenaḥ kapoto gṛdhraśca kākolūkau gṛhe dvija ।।
praviṣṭaḥ kathayedantaṃ vasatāṃ tatra veśmani ।
īdṛk parityajed gehaṃ śāntiṃ kuryācca paṇḍitaḥ ।।
svapne api hi kapotasya darśanaṃ na praśasyate ।
ṣaḍapatyāni kathyante gaṇḍaprāntaratestathā ।।
strīṇāṃ rajasyavasthānaṃ teṣāṃ kālāṃśca me śṛṇu ।
catvāryahāni pūrvāṇi tathaivānyat trayodaśa ।।
ekādaśa tathaivānyadapatyaṃ tasya vai dine ।
anyaddinābhigamane śrāddhadāne tathāpare ।।
parvasvathānyat tasmāttu varjyānyetāni paṇḍitaiḥ ।
garbhahantuḥ suto nighno mohanī cāpi kanyakā ।।
praviśya garbhamattyeko bhuktvā mohayate aparā ।
jāyante mohanāttasyāḥ sarpamaṇḍūkakacchapāḥ ।।
sarīsṛpāṇi cānyāni purīṣamathavā punaḥ ।
ṣaṇmāsān gurviṇīṃ māṃsamaśnuvānāmasaṃyatām ।।
vṛkṣacchāyāśrayāṃ rātrāvathavā tricatuṣpathe ।
śmaśānakaṭabhūmiṣṭhāmuttarīyavivarjitām ।।
rudamānāṃ niśīthe atha āviśettāmasau striyam ।
śasyahantustathaivaikaḥ kṣudrako nāma nāmataḥ ।।
śasyardhiṃ sa sadā hanti labdhvā randhraṃ śṛṇuṣva tat ।
amaṅgalyadinārambhe atṛpto vapate ca yaḥ ।।
kṣetreṣvanupraveśaṃ vai karotyantopasaṅgiṣu ।
tasmāt kalpaḥ supraśaste dine abhyarcya niśākaram ।।
kuryādārambhamuptiñca hṛṣṭastuṣṭaḥ sahāyavān ।
niyojiketi yā kanyā duḥ sahasya mayoditā ।।
jātaṃ pracodikāsaṃjñaṃ tasyāḥ kanyācatuṣṭayam ।
mattonmattapramattāstu narān nārīstu tāḥ sadā ।।
samāviśanti nāśāya codayantīha dāruṇam ।
adharmaṃ dharmarūpeṇa kāmañcākāmarūpiṇam ।।
anarthañcārtharūpeṇa mokṣañcāmokṣarūpiṇam ।
durvinītā vinā śaucaṃ darśayanti pṛthaṅnarān ।।
bhraśyantyābhiḥ praviṣṭābhiḥ puruṣārthāt pṛthaṅnarāḥ ।
tāsāṃ praveśaśca gṛhe saṃdhyārakte hyathāmbare ।।
dhātāvidhātrośca baliryatra kāle na dīyate ।
bhuñjatāṃ pibatāṃ vāpi saṅgibhirjalavipruṣaiḥ ।।
navanārīṣu saṃkrāntistāsāmāśvabhijāyate ।
virodhinyāstrayaḥ putrāścodako grāhakastathā ।।
tamaḥ pracchādakaścānyastatsvarūpaṃ śṛṇuṣva me ।
pradīpadailasaṃsargadūṣite laṅghite khale ।।
muṣalolūkhale yatra pāduke vāsane striyaḥ ।
śūrpadātrādikaṃ yatra padākṛṣya tathāsanam ।।
yatropaliptañcānarcya vihāraḥ kriyate gṛhe।
darvomukhena yatrāgnirāhṛto anyatra nīyate ।।
virodhinīsutāstatra vijṛmbhante pracoditāḥ ।
eko jihvāgataḥ puṃsāṃ strīṇāñcālīkasatyavān ।।
codako nāma sa proktaḥ paiśunyaṃ kurute gṛhe ।
avadhānagataścānyaḥ śravaṇastho atidurmatiḥ ।।
karoti grahaṇanteṣāṃ vacasāṃ grāhakastu saḥ ।
ākramyānyo mano nṝṇāṃ tamasācchādya durmatiḥ ।।
krodhaṃ janayate yastu tamaḥ pracchādakastu saḥ ।
svayaṃhāryāstu cauryeṇa janitantanayatrayam ।।
sarvahāryardhahārī ca vīryahārī tathaiva ca ।
anācāntagṛheṣvete mandācāragṛheṣu ca ।।
aprakṣālitapādeṣu praviśatsu mahānasam ।
khaleṣu goṣṭheṣu ca vai droho yeṣu gṛheṣu vai ।।
teṣu sarve yathānyāyaṃ viharanti ramanti ca ।
bhrāmaṇyāstanayastvekaḥ kākajaṅgha iti smṛtaḥ ।।
tenāviṣṭo ratiṃ sarvo naiva prāpnoti vai pure ।
bhuñjan yo gāyate maitre gāyate hasate ca yaḥ ।।
sandhyāmaithuninañcaiva naramāviśati dvija ।
kanyātrayaṃ prasūtā sā yā kanyā ṛtuhāriṇī ।।
ekā kucaharā kanyā anyā vyañjanahārikā ।
tṛtīyā tu samākhyātā kanyakā jātahāriṇī ।।
yasyā na kriyate sarvaḥ samyag vaivāhiko vidhiḥ ।
kālātīto athavā tasyā haratyekā kucadvayam ।।
samyak śrāddhamadattvā ca tathānarcya ca mātaram ।
vivāhitāyāḥ kanyāyā harati vyañjanaṃ tathā ।।
agnyambuśūnye ca tathā vidhūpe sūtikāgṛhe ।
adīpaśastramusale bhūtisarṣapavarjite ।।
anupraviśya sā jātamapahṛtyātmasambhavam ।
kṣaṇaprasavinī bālaṃ tatraivotsṛjate dvija ।।
sā jātahāriṇī nāma sughorā piśitāśanā ।
tasmāt saṃrakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yatnataḥ sūtikāgṛhe ।।
smṛtiñcāprayatānāñca śūnyāgāraniṣevaṇāt ।
apahanti sutastasyāḥ pracaṇḍo nāma nāmataḥ ।।
pautrebhyastasya saṃbhūtā līkāḥ śatasahasraśaḥ ।
caṇḍālayonayaścāṣṭau daṇḍapāśātibhīṣaṇāḥ ।।
kṣudhāviṣṭāstato līkāstāśca caṇḍālayonayaḥ ।
abhyadhāvanta cānyonyamattukāmāḥ parasparam ।।
pracaṇḍo vāriyitvā tu tāstāścaṇḍālayonayaḥ ।
samaye sthāpayāmāsa yādṛśe tādṛśaṃ śṛṇu ।।
adyaprabhṛti līkānāmāvāsaṃ yo hi dāsyati ।
daṇḍaṃ tasyāhamatulaṃ pātayiṣye na saṃśayaḥ ।।
caṇḍālayonyo avasathe līkā yā prasaviṣyati ।
tasyāśca santiḥ pūrvā sā ca sadyo naśiṣyati ।।
prasūte kanyake dve tu strīpuṃsorbojahāriṇī ।
vātarūpāmarūpāñca tasyāḥ praharaṇantu te ।।
vātarūpā niṣekānte sā yasmai kṣipate sutam ।
sa pumān vātaśukratvaṃ prayāti vanitāpi vā ।।
tathaiva gacchataḥ sadyo nirbojatvamarūpayā ।
asnātāśī naro yo vai tathaiva piśitāśanaḥ ।।
vidveṣiṇī tu yā kanyā bhṛkuṭīkuṭilānanā ।
tasyā dvau tanayau puṃsāmapakāraprakāśakau ।।
nirbojatvaṃ naro yāti nārī vā śaucavarjitā ।
paiśunyābhirataṃ lolamasajjananiṣevaṇam ।।
puruṣadveṣiṇañcaitau nāramākramya tiṣṭhataḥ ।
mātrā bhrātrā tathā mitrairabhīṣṭaiḥ svajanaiḥ paraiḥ ।।
vidviṣṭo nāśamāyāti puruṣo dharmator'thataḥ ।
ekastu svaguṇāṃlloke prakāśayati pāpakṛt ।।
dvitīyastu guṇān maitrīṃ lokasthāmapakarṣati ।
ityete dauḥ sahāḥ sarve yakṣmaṇaḥ santatāvatha ।
pāpācārāḥ samākhyātā yairvyāptamakhilaṃ jagat ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe duḥ sahotpatisamāpanaṃ nāmaikapañcāśau'dhyāyaḥ

dvipañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityeṣa tāmasaḥ sargo brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।
rudrasargaṃ pravakṣyāmi tanme nigadataḥ śṛṇu ।।
tanayāśca tathaivāṣṭau patnyaḥ putrāśca te tathā ।
kalpādāvātmanastulyaṃ sutaṃ pradhyāyataḥ prabhoḥ ।।
prādurāsīdathāṅke asya kumāro nīlalohitaḥ ।
ruroda susvaraṃ so atha dravaṃśca dvijasattama ।।
kiṃ rodiṣīti taṃ brahmā rudantaṃ pratyuvāca ha ।
nāma dehīti taṃ so atha pratyuvāca jagatpatim ।।
rudrastvaṃ deva ! nāmnāsi mā rodīrdhairyamāvaha ।
evamuktastataḥ so atha saptakṛtvo ruroda ha ।।
tato anyāni dadau tasmai sapta nāmāni vai prabhuḥ ।
sthānāni caiṣāmaṣṭānāṃ patnīḥ putrāṃśca vai dvija ।।
bhavaṃ śarvaṃ tatheśānaṃ tathā paśupatiṃ prabhuḥ ।
bhīmamugraṃ mahādevamuvāca sa pitāmahaḥ ।।
cakre nāmānyathaitāni sthānānyeṣāñcakāra ha ।
sūryo jalaṃ mahī vahnirvāyurākāśameva ca ।।
dīkṣito brāhmaṇaḥ soma ityetāstanavaḥ kramāt ।
suvarcalā tathaivomā vikeśī cāparā svadhā ।।
svāhā diśastathā dīkṣā rohiṇī ca yathākramam ।
sūryādīnāṃ dvijaśreṣṭha ! rudrādyairnāmabhiḥ saha ।।
śanaiścarastathā śukro lohitāṅgo manojavaḥ ।
skandaḥ sargo atha santāno budhaścānukramāt sutaḥ ।।
evamprakāro rudro asau satīṃ bhāryāmavindata ।
dakṣakopācca tatyāja sā satī svaṃ kalevaram ।।
himavadduhitā sābhūnmenāyāṃ dvijasattama ।
tasyā bhrātā tu mainākaḥ sakhāmbhodheranuttamaḥ ।।
upayeme punaścaināmananyāṃ bhagavān bhavaḥ ।
devau dhātāvidhātārau bhṛgoḥ khyātirasūyata ।।
śriyañca devadevasya patnī nārāyaṇāsya yā ।
āyātirniyatiścaiva meroḥ kanye mahātmanaḥ ।।
dhātāvidhātroste bhārye tayorjātau sutāvubhau ।
prāṇaścaiva mṛkaṇḍuśca pitā mama mahāyaśāḥ ।।
manasvinyāmahaṃ tasmāt putro vedaśirā mama ।
dhūmravatyāṃ samabhavat prāṇasyāpi nibodha me ।।
prāṇasya dyutimān putra utpannastasya cātmajaḥ ।
ajarāśca tayoḥ putrāḥ pautrāśca bahavo abhavan ।।
patnī marīceḥ sambhūtiḥ paurṇamāsamasūyata ।
virajāḥ parvataścaiva tasya putrau mahātmanaḥ ।।
tayoḥ putrāṃstu vakṣye ahaṃ vaṃśasaṃkīrtane dvija ।
smṛtiścāṅgirasaḥ patnī prasūtā kanyakāstathā ।।
sinīvālī kuhūścaiva rākā bhānumatī tathā ।
anasūyā tathaivātrerjajñe putrānakalpaṣān ।।
somaṃ durvāsasañcaiva dattātreyañca yoginam ।
prītyāṃ pulastyabhāryāyāṃ datto anyastatsuto abhavat ।।
pūrvajanmani so agastyaḥ smṛtaḥ svāyambhuve antare ।
kardamaścārvavīraśca sahiṣṇuśca sutatrayam ।।
kṣamā tu suṣuve bhāryā pulahasya prajāpateḥ ।
kratostu sannatirbhāryā bālakhilyānasūyata ।।
ṣaṣṭiryāni sahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇāmūrdhvaretasām ।
ūrjāyāntu vasiṣṭhasya saptājāyanta vai sutāḥ ।।
rajogātrordhvabāhuśca sabalaścānaghastathā ।
sutapāḥ śukla ityete sarve saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
yo asāvagnirabhīmānī brahmaṇastanayo agrajaḥ ।
tasmāt svāhā sutān lebhe trīnudāraujaso dvija ।।
pāvakaṃ pavamānañca śuciñcāpi jalāśinam ।
teṣāntu santātāvanye catvāriṃśacca pañca ca ।।
kathyante bahuśaścaite pitā putratrayañca yat ।
evamekonapañcāśad durjayāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।
pitaro brahmaṇā sṛṣṭā ye vyākhyātā mayā tava ।
agniṣvāttā barhiṣado anagnayaḥ sāgnayaśca ye ।।
tebhyaḥ svadhā sute jajñe menāṃ vai dhāriṇīṃ tathā ।
te ubhe brahmavādinyau yoginyau cāpyubhe dvija ।।
uttamajñānasaṃpanne sarvaiḥ samudite guṇaiḥ ।
ityeṣā dakṣakanyānāṃ kathitāpatyasaṃtatiḥ ।
śraddhāvān saṃsmarannityaṃ prajāvānabhijāyate ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe rudrasargābhidhāno nāma dvipañcāśo adhyāyaḥ

tripañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

svāyambhuvaṃ tvayākhyātametanmanvantarañca yat ।
tadahaṃ bhagavan ! samyak śrotumicchāmi kathyatām ।।
manvantarapramāṇañca devā devarṣayastathā ।
ye ca kṣitīśā bhagavan ! devendraścaiva yastathā ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

manvantarāṇāṃ saṃkhyātā sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ ।
mānuṣeṇa pramāṇena śṛṇu manvantarañca me ।।
triṃśatkoṭyastu saṃkhyātāḥ sahasrāṇi ca viṃśatiḥ ।
saptaṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutāni ca saṃkhyayā ।।
manvantarapramāṇañca ityetat sādhikaṃ vinā ।
aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi divyayā saṃkhyayā smṛtam ।।
dvipañcāśattathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni ca ।
svāyambhuvo manuḥ pūrvaṃ manuḥ svārociṣastathā ।।
auttamastāmasaścaiva raivataścākṣuṣastathā ।
ṣaḍete manavo atītāstathā vaivasvato adhunā ।।
sāvarṇiḥ pañca raucyāśca bhautyāścāgāminastvamī ।
eteṣāṃ vistaraṃ bhūyo manvantaraparigrahe ।।
vakṣye devānṛṣīṃścaiva yakṣendrāḥ pitaraśca ye ।
utpattiṃ saṃgrahaṃ brahman ! śrūyatāmasya santatiḥ ।।
yacca teṣāmabhūt kṣetraṃ tatputrāṇāṃ mahātmanām ।
manoḥ svāyambhuvasyāsan daśa putrāstu tatsamāḥ ।।
yairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā saparvatā ।
sasamudrākaravatī prativarṣaṃ niveśitā ।।
sasamudrākaravatī prativarṣaṃ tretāyuge tathā ।
priyavratasya putraistaiḥ pautraiḥ svāyambhuvasya ca ।।
priyavratāt prajāvatyāṃ vīrāt kanyā vyajāyata ।
kanyā sā tu mahābhāgā kardamasya prajāpate ।।
kanye dve daśa putrāṃśca samrāṭkukṣī ca te ubhe ।
tayorvai bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ prajāpatisamā daśa ।।
āgnīdhro medhātithiśca vapuṣmāṃśca tathāparaḥ ।
jyotiṣmāndyutimān bhavyaḥ savanaḥ sapta eva te ।।
priyavrato abhyaṣiñcattān sapta saptasu pārthivān ।
dvīpeṣu tena dharmeṇa dvīpāṃścaiva nibodha me ।।
jambudvīpe tathāgnīdhraṃ rājānaṃ kṛtavān pitā ।
plakṣadvīpeśvaraścāpi tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ ।।
śālmalestu vapuṣmantaṃ jyotiṣmantaṃ kuśāhvaye ।
krauñcadvīpe dyutimantaṃ bhavyaṃ śākāhvayeśvaram ।।
puṣkarādhipatiñcāpi savanaṃ kṛtavān sutam ।
mahāvīto dhātakiśca puṣkarādhipateḥ sutau ।।
dvidhā kṛtvā tayorvarṣaṃ puṣkare saṃnyaveśayat ।
bhavyasya putrāḥ saptāsannāmatastānnibodha me ।।
jaladaśca kumāraśca sukumāro manīvakaḥ ।
kuśottaro atha medhāvī saptamastu mahādrumaḥ ।।
tannāmakāni varṣāṇi śākadvīpe cakāra saḥ ।
tathā dyutimataḥ sapta putrāstāṃśca nibodha me ।।
kuśalo manugaścoṣṇaḥ prākaraścārthakārakaḥ ।
muniśca dundubhiścaiva saptamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।
teṣāṃ svanāmadheyāni krauñcadvīpe tathābhavan ।
jyotiṣmataḥ kuśadvīpe putranāmāṅkitāni vai ।।
tatrāpi sapta varṣāpi teṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।
udbhidaṃ vaiṣṇavañcaiva surathaṃ lambanaṃ tathā ।।
dhṛtimat prākarañcaiva kāpilaṃ cāpi saptamam ।
vapuṣmataḥ sutāḥ sapta śālmaleśasya cābhavan ।।
śvetaśca haritaścaiva jīmūto rohitastathā ।
vaidyuto mānasaścaiva ketumān saptamastathā ।।
tathaiva śālmalesteṣāṃ samanāmāni sapta vai ।
sapta medhātitheḥ putrāḥ plakṣadvīpeśvarasya vai ।।
yeṣāṃ nāmāṅgitairvarṣaiḥ plakṣadvīpastu saptadhā ।
pūrvaṃ śākabhavaṃ varṣaṃ śiśirantu sukhodayam ।।
ānandañca śivañcaiva kṣemakañca dhruvantathā ।
plakṣadvīpādibhūteṣu śākadvīpāntimeṣu vai ।।
jñeyaḥ pañcasu dharmaśca varṇāśramavibhāgajaḥ ।
nityaḥ svābhāvikaścaiva ahiṃsāvidhivardhitaḥ ।।
pañcasveteṣu varṣeṣu sarvasādhāraṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
agnīdhrāya pitā pūrvaṃ jambudvīpaṃ dadau dvija ।।
tasya putrā babhūvurhi prajāpatisamā nava ।
jyeṣṭho nābiriti khyātastasya kiṃpuruṣo anujaḥ ।।
harivarṣastṛtīyastu caturtho abhūdilāvṛtaḥ ।
vaśyaśca pañcamaḥ putro hiraṇyaḥ ṣaṣṭha ucyate ।।
kurustu saptamasteṣāṃ bhadrāśvaścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
navamaḥ ketumālaśca tannāmnā varṣasaṃsthitiḥ ।।
yāni kipuruṣādyāni varjayitvā himāhvayam ।
teṣāṃ svabāvataḥ siddhiḥ sukhaprāyā hyatnataḥ ।।
viparyayo na teṣvasti jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ na ca ।
dharmādharmau na teṣvāstāṃ nottamādhamamadhyamāḥ ।।
na vai caturyugāvasthā nārtavā ṛtavo na ca ।
āgnīdhrasūnornābhestu ṛṣabho abhūt suto dvija ।।
ṛṣabhādbharato jajñe vīraḥ putraśatādvaraḥ ।
so abhiṣicyarṣabhaḥ putraṃ mahāpravrājyamāsthitaḥ ।।
tapastepe mahābhāgaḥ pulahāśramasaṃśrayaḥ ।
himāhviṃ dakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ bharatāya pitā dadau ।।
tasmāt tu bhārataṃ varṣaṃ tasya nānmā mahātmanaḥ ।
bhatasyāpyabhūt putraḥ sumatirnāma dhārmikaḥ ।।
tasmin rājyaṃ samāveśya bharato api vanaṃ yayau ।
eteṣāṃ putrapautraistu saptadvīpā vasundharā ।।
priyavratasya putraistu bhuktvā svāyambhuve antare ।
eṣa svāyambhuvaḥ sargaḥ kathitaste dvijottama ।।
pūrvamanvantare samyak kimanyat kathayāmi te ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhamanvantarakathanaṃ' nāma tripañcāśo adhyāyaḥ

catuḥpañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

katidvīpāḥ samudrā vā parvatā vā kati dvija ।
kiyanti caiva varṣāṇi teṣāṃ nadyaśca kā mune ।।
mahābhūtapramāṇañca lokālokantathaiva ca ।
paryāsaṃ parimāṇañca gatiñcandrārkayorapi ।।
etat prabrūhi me sarvaṃ vistareṇa mahāmune ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

śatārdhakoṭivistārā pṛthivī kṛtstraśo dvija ।
tasyā hi sthānamakhilaṃ kathayāmi śṛṇuṣva tat ।।
ye te dvīpā mayā proktā jambudvīpādayo dvija ।
puṣkarāntā mahābhāga ! śṛṇveṣāṃ vistaraṃ punaḥ ।।
dvīpāt tu dviguṇo dvīpo jambuḥ plakṣo atha śālmalaḥ ।
kuśaḥ krauñcastathā śākaḥ puṣkaradvīpa eva ca ।।
lavaṇekṣu-surā-sarpirdadhi-dugdhaḥjalābdhibhiḥ ।
dviguṇairdviguṇairvṛddhyā sarvataḥ pariveṣṭitāḥ ।।
jambudvīpasya saṃsthānaṃ pravakṣye ahaṃ nibodha me ।
lakṣamekaṃ yojanānāṃ vṛttau vistāradairghyataḥ ।।
himavān hemakūṭaśca ṛṣabho merureva ca ।
nīlaḥ śvetastathā śṛṅgī saptāsmin varṣaparvatāḥ ।।
dvau lakṣayojanāyāmau madhye tatra mahācalau ।
tayordakṣiṇato yau tu yau tathottarato girī ।।
daśabhirdaśabhirnyūnaiḥ sahasraistaiḥ parasparam ।
dvisāhastrocchrayāḥ sarve tāvadvistāriṇaśca te ।।
samudrāntaḥ praviṣṭāśca ṣaḍasmin varṣaparvatāḥ ।
dakṣiṇottarato nimnā madhye tuṅgāyatā kṣitiḥ ।।
vedyardhe dakṣime trīṇi trīṇi varṣāṇi cottare ।
ilāvṛtaṃ tayormadhye candrārdhākāravat sthitam ।।
tataḥ pūrveṇa bhadrāśvaṃ ketumālañca paścime ।
ilāvṛtasya madhye tu meruḥ kanakaparvataḥ ।।
caturaśītisāhastrastasyocchrāyo mahāgireḥ ।
praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastādvistīrṇaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu ।।
śarāvasaṃsthitatvācca dvātriṃśanmūrdhni vistṛtaḥ ।
śuklaḥ pīto asito raktaḥ prācyādiṣu yathākramam ।।
vipro vaiśyastathā śūdraḥ kṣatriyaśca svavarṇataḥ ।
tasyopari tathaivāṣṭau puryo dikṣu yathākramam ।।
indrādilokapālānāṃ tanmadhye brahmaṇaḥ sabhā ।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa samucchritā ।।
ayutocchrāyāstasyādhastathā viṣakambhavarvatāḥ ।
prācyādiṣu krameṇaiva mandaro gandhamādanaḥ ।।
vipulaśca supārśvaśca ketupādapaśobhitāḥ ।
kadambo mandare keturjambuva gandhamādane ।।
vipule ca tathāśvatthaḥ supārśve ca vaṭo mahān ।
ekādaśaśatāyāmā yojanānāmime nagāḥ ।।
jaṭharo devakūṭaśca pūrvasyāṃ diśi parvatau ।
ānīlaniṣadhau prāptau parasparanirantarau ।।
niṣadhaḥ pāriyātraśca meroḥ pārśve tu paścime ।
yathā pūrvau tathā caitāvānīlaniṣadhāyatau ।।
kailāso himavāṃścaiva dakṣiṇena mahācalau ।
pūrvapaścāyatāvetāvarṇavāntarvyavasthitau ।।
śṛṅgavān jārudhiścaiva tathaivottaraparvatau ।
yataiva dakṣiṇe tadvadarṇapvāntarvyavasthitau ।।
maryādāparvatā hyete kathyante aṣṭau dvijottama ।
himavaddhemakūṭādiparvatānāṃ parasparam ।।
navayojanasāhastraṃ prāgudagdakṣiṇottaram ।
merorilāvṛte tadvadantare vai caturdiśam ।।
phalāni yāni vai jambvāḥ gandhamādanaparvate ।
gajadehapramāṇāni patanti girimūrdhani ।।
teṣāṃ strāvāt prabhavati khyātā jambūnadīti vai ।
yatra jāmbūnadaṃ nāma kanakaṃ samprajāyate ।।
sā parikramya vai meruṃ jambūmūlaṃ punarnadī ।
viśati dvijaśārdūla ! pīyamānā janaiśca taiḥ ।।
bhadrāśve aśvaśirā viṣṇurbhārate kūrmasaṃsthitiḥ ।
varāhaḥ ketumāle ca matsyarūpastathottare ।।
teṣu nakṣatravinyāsādviṣayāḥ samavasthitāḥ ।
caturṣvapi dvijaśreṣṭha ! grahābhibhavapāṭhakāḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe bhuvanakośaṭhajambūdvīpavarṇanaṃ' nāma catuḥ pañcāśo adhyāya

pañcapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

śaileṣu mandārādyeṣu caturṣvapi dvijottama ।
vānani yāni catvāri sarāṃsi ca nibodha me ।।
pūrvaṃ caitrarathaṃ nāma dakṣiṇe nandanaṃ vanam ।
vaibhrājaṃ paścime śaile sāvitraṃ cottarācale ।।
aruṇodaṃ saraḥ pūrvaṃ mānasaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā ।
śītodaṃ paścime merormahābhadraṃ tathottare ।।
śītārtaścakramuñjaśca kulīro atha sukaṅkavān ।
maṇiśailo atha vṛṣavān mahānīlo bhavācalaḥ ।।
sūbindurmandaro veṇustāmaso niṣadhastathā ।
devaśailaśca pūrveṇa mandarasya mahācalaḥ ।।
trikaṭaśikharādriśca kaliṅgo atha pataṅgakaḥ ।
rucakaḥ sānumāṃścādristāmrako atha viśākhavān ।।
śvetodaraḥ samūlaśca vasudhāraśca ratnavān ।
ekaśṛṅgo mahāśailo rājaśālaḥ pipāṭhakaḥ ।।
pañcaśailo atha kailāso himavāṃścācalottamaḥ ।
ityete dakṣiṇe pārśve meroḥ proktā mahācalāḥ ।।
surakṣaḥ śiśirākṣaśca vaiduryaḥ kapilastathā ।
piñjaro atha mahābhadraḥ surasaḥ piṅgalo madhuḥ ।।
añjanaḥ kukkuṭaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ pāṇḍaraścālottamaḥ ।
sahasraśikharaścādriḥ pāriyātraḥ saśṛṅgavān ।।
paścimena tathā merorviskambhāt paścimādvahiḥ ।
ete acalāḥ samākhyātāḥ śṛṇuṣvanyāṃstathottarān ।।
śaṅkhakūṭo atha vṛṣabho haṃsanābhastathācalaḥ ।
kapilendrastathā śailaḥ sānumān nīla eva ca ।।
svarṇaśṛṅgī śātaśṛṅgī puṣpako meghaparvataḥ ।
virajākṣo varāhādrirmayūro jārudhistathā ।।
ityete kathitā brahman ! meroruttarato nagāḥ ।
eteṣāṃ parvatānāntu drauṇyo atīva manoharāḥ ।।
vanairamalapānīyaiḥ sarobhirupaśobhitāḥ ।
tāsu puṇyakṛtāṃ janma manuṣyāṇāṃ dvijottama ।।
ete bhaumā dvijaśreṣṭha ! svargāḥ svargaguṇādhikāḥ ।
na tāsu puṇyapāpānāmapūrvāṇāmupārjanam ।।
puṇyopabhogā evoktā devānāmapi tāsvapi ।
śītāntādyeṣu caitaṣu śaileṣu dvijasattama ।।
vidyādharāṇāṃ yakṣāṇāṃ kinnaroragarakṣasām ।
devānāñca mahāvāsā gandharvāṇāṃ ca śobhanāḥ ।।
mahāpuṇyā manojñaiśca sadaivopavanairyutāḥ ।
sarāṃsi ca manojñāni sarvartusukhado anilaḥ ।।
na caiteṣu manuṣyāṇāṃ vaimanasyāni kutracit ।
tadevaṃ pārthivaṃ padmaṃ catuṣpatraṃ mayoditam ।।
bhadrāścabhāratādyāni patrāṇyasya caturdiśam ।
bhārataṃ nāma yadvarṣaṃ dakṣiṇena mayoditam ।।
tat karmabhūmirnānyatra saṃprāptiḥ puṇyapāpayoḥ ।
etat pradhānaṃ vijñeyaṃ yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।
tasmāt svargāpavargau ca mānuṣyanārakāvapi ।
tiryaktvamathavāpyanyat naraḥ prāpnoti vai dvija ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe bhuvanakośe pañcapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ

ṣaṭpañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

dharādharāṃ jagadyoneḥ padaṃ nārāyaṇasya ca ।
tataḥ pravṛttā yā devī gaṅgā tripathagāminī ।।
sā praviśya sudhāyoniṃ somamādhāramambhasām ।
tataḥ sambadhyamānārkaraśmisaṅgatipāvanī ।।
papāta merupṛṣṭhe ca sā caturdhā tato yayau ।
merukūṭataṭāntebhyo nipatantī vavartitā ।।
vikīryamāṇasalilā nirālambā papāta sā ।
mandarādyeṣu pādeṣu pravibhaktodakā samam ।।
caturṣvapi papātāmbuvibhinnāṅghriśiloccayā ।
pūrvā sīte ati vikhyātā yayau caitrarathaṃ vanam ।।
tat plāvayitvā ca yayau varuṇodaṃ sarovanam ।
śītāntañca giriṃ tasmāttataścānyān girīn kramāt ।।
gatvā bhuvaṃ samāsādya bhadrāśvājjaladhiṃ gatā ।
tathaivālakanandākhyā dakṣiṇe gandhamādane ।।
merupādavanaṃ gatvā nandanaṃ devanandanam ।
mānasañca mahāvegāt plāpayitvā sarovaram ।।
āsādya śailarājānaṃ ramyaṃ hi śikharantathā ।
tasmācca parvatān sarvān dakṣiṇopakramoditān ।।
tān plāvayitvā saṃprāptā himavantaṃ mahāgirim ।
dadhāra tatra tāṃ śambhurna mumoca vṛṣadhvajaḥ ।।
bhaghīrathenopavāsaiḥ stutyā cārādhito vibhuḥ ।
tatra muktā ca śarveṇa saptadhā dakṣiṇodadhim ।।
praviveśa tridhā prācyāṃ plāvayantī mahānadī ।
bhagīratharathasyānu strotasaikena dakṣiṇām ।।
tathaiva paścime pāde vipule sā mahānadī ।
sucakṣuriti vikhyātā vaibhrājaṃ sācalaṃ yayau ।
śītodañca sarastasmāt plāvayantī mahānadī ।
sucakṣuḥ parvataṃ prāptā tataśca triśikhaṃ gatā ।।
tasmāt krameṇa cādrīṇāṃ śikhareṣu nipatya sā ।
ketumālaṃ samāsādya praviṣṭā lavaṇodadhim ।।
supārśvantu tathaivādriṃ merupādaṃ hi sā gatā ।
tatra someti vikhyātā sā yayau saviturvanam ।।
tatpāvayantī saṃprāptā mahābhadraṃ sarovaram ।
tataśca śaṅkhakūṭaṃ sā prayātā vai mahānadī ।।
tasmācca vṛṣabhādīn sā kramāt prāpya śiloccayān ।
mahārṇavamanuprāptā plāvayitvottarān kurūn ।।
evameṣā mayā gaṅgāṃ kathitā te dvijarṣabha ।
jambudvīpaniveśaśca varṣāṇi ca yathātatham ।।
vasanti teṣu sarveṣu prajāḥ kiṃpuruṣādiṣu ।
sukhaprāyā nirātaṅkā nyūnatotkarṣavarjitāḥ ।।
navasvapi ca varṣeṣu sapta sapta kulācalāḥ ।
ekaikasmiṃstathā deśe nadyaścādriviniḥ sṛtāḥ ।।
yāni kiṃpuruṣādyāni varṣāṇyaṣṭau dvijottama ।
teṣūdbhijjāni toyāni meghavāryatra bhārate ।।
vārkṣo svābhāvikī deśyā toyotthā mānasī tathā ।
karmajā ca nṛṇāṃ siddharvarṣeṣveteṣu cāṣṭasu ।।
kāmapradebhyo vṛkṣebhyo vārkṣo siddhiḥ svabhāvajā ।
svābhāvikī samākhyātā tṛptirdeśyā ca daiśikī ।।
apāṃ śaukṣmyācca toyotthā dhyānopetā ca mānasī ।
upāsanādikāryāttu dharmajā sāpyudāhṛtā ।।
na caiteṣu yugāvasthā nādhyo vyādhayo na ca ।
puṇyāpuṇyasamārambho naiva teṣu dvijottama ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe gaṅgāvatāro nāma ṣaṭpañcāśo adhyāyaḥ

saptapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

bhagavan ! kathitantvetajjambūdvīpaṃ samāsataḥ ।
yadetadbhavatā proktaṃ karma nānyatra puṇyadam ।।
pāpāya vā mahābhāga ! varjayitvā tu bhāratam ।
itaḥ svargaśca mokṣaśca madhyañcāntañca gamyate ।।
na khalvanyatra martyānāṃ bhūmau karma vidhīyate ।
tasmādvistaraśo brahman ! mamaitadbhārataṃ vada ।।
ye cāsya bhedā yāvanto yathāvat sthitireva ca ।
varṣo ayaṃ dvijaśārdūla ! ye cāsmin deśaparvatāḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

bhāratasyāsya varṣasya nava bhedānnibodha me ।
samudrāntaritā jñeyāste tvagamyāḥ parasparam ।।
indradvīpaḥ kaśerumāṃstāmravarṇo gabhastimān ।
nāgadvīpastathā saumyo gāndharvo vāruṇastathā ।।
ayantu navamasteṣāṃ dvīpaḥ sāgarasaṃvṛtaḥ ।
yojanānāṃ hasastraṃ vai dvīpo ayaṃ dakṣiṇottarāt ।।
pūrve kirātā yasyānte paścime yavanāstathā ।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścāntaḥ sthitā dvija ।।
ijyādhyāyavaṇijyādyaiḥ karmabhiḥ kṛtapāvanāḥ ।
teṣāṃ saṃvyavahāraśca ebhiḥ karmabhiriṣyate ।।
svargāpavargaprāptiśca puṇyaṃ pāpañca vai tadā ।
mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimānṛkṣaparvataḥ ।।
vindhyaśca pāriyātraśca saptaivātra kulācalāḥ ।
teṣāṃ sahasraśaścānye bhūdharā ye samīpagāḥ ।।
vistārocchrayiṇo ramyā vipulāścātra sānavaḥ ।
kolāhalaḥ savaibhrājo mandaro dardurācalaḥ ।।
vātasvano vaidyutaśca mainākaḥ svarasastathā ।
tuṅgaprastho nāgagirī rocanaḥ pāṇḍarācalaḥ ।।
puṣpo girirdurjayanto raivator'buda eva ca ।
ṛṣyamūkaḥ sagomantaḥ kūṭaśailaḥ kṛtasmaraḥ ।।
śrīparvataścakoraśca śataśo anye ca parvatāḥ ।
tairvimiśrā janapadā mlecchāścāryāśca bhāgaśaḥ ।।
taiḥ pīyante saritśreṣṭhā yāstāḥ samyaṅnibodha me ।
gaṅgā sarasvatī sindhuścandrabhāgā tathāparā ।।
yamunā ca śatadruśca vitasterāvatī kuhuḥ ।
gomatī dhūtapāpā ca bāhudā sadṛśadvatī ।।
vipāśā devikā raṅkṣurniścīrā gaṇḍakī tathā ।
kauśikī cāpagā vipra ! himavatpādaniḥ sṛtāḥ ।।
vedasmṛtirvedavatī vṛtraghrī sindhureva ca ।
veṇvā sānandanī caiva sadānīrā mahī tathā ।।
pārā carmaṇvatī nūpī vidiśā vetravatyapi ।
śiprā hyavarṇo ca tathā pāriyātrāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
śoṇo mahānadaścaiva narmadā surathādrijā ।
mandākinī daśārṇā ca citrakūṭā tathāparā ।।
citrotpalā satamasā karamodā piśācikā ।
tathānyā pippaliśroṇirvipāśā vañjulā nadī ।।
sumerujā śuktimatī śakulī tridivākramuḥ ।
pādaprasūtā vai tathānyā vegavāhinī ।।
śiprā payoṣṇī nirvindhyā tāpī saniṣadhāvatī ।
veṇyā vaitaraṇī caiva sinīvālī kumudvatī ।।
karatoyā mahāgaurī durgā cāntaḥ śirā tathā ।
pādaprasūtāstā nadyaḥ puṇyajalāḥ śubhāḥ ।।
godāvarī bhīmarathā kṛṣṇā veṇyā tathāparā ।
tuṅgabhadrā suprayogā vāhyā kāveryathāpagā ।।
pādaviniṣkrāntā ityetāḥ sariduttamāḥ ।
kṛtamālā tāmraparṇo puṣpajā sūtpalāvatī ।।
malayādrisamudbhūtā nadyaḥ śītajalāstvimāḥ ।
pitṛsomarṣikulyā ca ikṣukā tridivā ca yā ।।
lāṅgūlinī vaṃśakarā mahendraprabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
ṛṣikulyā kumārī ca mandagā mandavāhinī ।।
kṛpā palāśinī caiva śuktimatprabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
sarvāḥ puṇyāḥ sarasvatyaḥ sarvā gaṅgāḥ samudragāḥ ।।
viśvasya mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarvapāpaharāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
anyāḥ sahasraśaścoktāḥ kṣudranadyo dvijottama ।।
prāvṛṭkālavahāḥ santi sadākālavahāśca yāḥ ।
matsyāśvakūṭāḥ kulyāśca kuntalāḥ kāśikośalāḥ ।।
atharvāścārkaliṅgāśca malakāśca vṛkaiḥ saha ।
madhyadeśyā janapadāḥ prāyaśo amī prakīrtitāḥ ।।
sahyasya cottare yā tu yatra godāvarī nadī ।
pṛthivyāmapi kṛtastrāyāṃ sa pradeśo manoramaḥ ।।
govardhanaṃ puraṃ ramyaṃ bhārgavasya mahātmanaḥ ।
vāhlīkā vāṭadhānāśca ābhīrāḥ kālatoyakāḥ ।।
aparāntāśca śūdrāśca pallavāścarmakhaṇḍikāḥ ।
gāndhārā gabalāścaiva sindhusauvīramadrakāḥ ।।
śatadrujāḥ kaliṅgāśca pāradā hālamūṣikāḥ ।
māṭharā bahubhadrāśca kaikeyā daśamālikāḥ ।।
kṣatriyopaniveśāśca vaiśyaśūdrakulāni ca ।
kāmbojā daradāścaiva varvarā harṣavardhanāḥ ।।
cīnāścaiva tukhārāśca bahulā bāhyatonarāḥ ।
ātreyāśca bharadvājāḥ puṣkalāśca kaśerukāḥ ।।
lampākāḥ śūlakārāśca cūlikā jāguḍaiḥ saha ।
auṣadhāścānimadrāśca kirātānāñca jātayaḥ ।।
tāmasā haṃsamārgāśca kāśmīrāstuṅganāstathā ।
śūlikāḥ kuhakāścaiva ūrṇā darvāstathaiva ca ।।
ete deśā hyudīcyāstu prācyāndeśānnibodha me ।
adhrārakā mudakarā antargiryā bahirgirāḥ ।।
yathā pravaṅgā raṅgeyā mānadā mānavartikāḥ ।
brāhmottarāḥ pravijayā bhārgavā jñeyamallakāḥ ।।
prāgjyotiṣāśca madrāśca videhāstāmraliptakāḥ ।
mallā magadhagomantāḥ prācyā janapadāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
athāpare janapadā dakṣiṇāpathavāsinaḥ ।
puṇḍrāśca kevalāścaiva golāṅgūlāstathaiva ca ।।
śailūṣā mūṣikāścaiva kusumā nāmavāsakāḥ ।
mahārāṣṭrā māhiṣakā kaliṅgāścaiva sarvaśaḥ ।।
ābhīrāḥ saha vaiśikyā āḍhakyāḥ śabarāśca ye ।
pulindā vindhyamauleyā vaidarbhā daṇḍakaiḥ saha ।।
paurikā maulikāścaiva aśmakā bhogavardhanāḥ ।
naiṣikāḥ kuntalā andhā udibhadā vanadārakāḥ ।।
dākṣiṇātyāstvamī deśā aparāntān nibodha me ।
sūrpārakāḥ kālibalā durgāścānīkaṭaiḥ saha ।।
pulindāśca sumīnāśca rūpapāḥ svāpadaiḥ saha ।
tathā kuruminaścaiva sarve caiva kaṭhākṣarāḥ ।।
nāsikyāvāśca ye cānye ye caivottaranarmadāḥ ।
bhīrukacchāḥ samāheyāḥ saha sārasvatairapi ।।
kāśmīrāśca surāṣṭrāśca avantyāścārbudaiḥ saha ।
ityete hyaparāntāśca śṛṇu vindhyanivāsinaḥ ।।
sarajāśca karūṣāśca keralāścotkalaiḥ saha ।
uttamarṇā daśārṇāśca bhojyāḥ kiṣkindhakaiḥ saha ।।
tośalāḥ kośalāścaiva traipurā vaidiśāstathā ।
tumburāstumbulāścaiva paṭavo naiṣadheḥ saha ।।
annajāstuṣṭikārāśca vīrahotrā hyavantayaḥ ।
ete janapadāḥ sarve vindhyapṛṣṭhanivāsinaḥ ।।
ato deśān pravakṣyāmi parvatāśrayiṇaśca ye ।
nīhārā haṃsamārgāśca kuravo gurgaṇāḥ khasāḥ ।।
kuntaprāvaraṇāścaiva ūrṇā dārvāḥ sakṛtrakāḥ ।
trigartā gālavāścaiva kirātāstāmasaiḥ saha ।।
kṛtatretādikaścātra caturyugakṛto vidhiḥ ।
etattu bhārataṃ varṣaṃ catuḥ saṃsthānasaṃsthitam ।।
dakṣiṇāparato hyasya pūrveṇa ca mahodadhiḥ ।
himavānuttareṇāsya kārmukasya yathā guṇaḥ ।।
tadetad bhārataṃ varṣaṃ sarvabījaṃ dvijottama ।
brahmatvamamareśatvaṃ devatvaṃ marutastathā ।।
mṛgapaśvapsaroyonistadvat sarve sarīsṛpāḥ ।
sthāvarāṇāñca sarveṣāmito brahman ! śubhāśubhaiḥ ।।
prayāti karmabhūrbrahman ! nānyā lokeṣu vidyate ।
devānāmapi viprarṣe ! sadā eṣa manorathaḥ ।।
api mānuṣyamāpsyāmo devatvāt pracyutāḥ kṣitau ।
manuṣyaḥ kurute tattu yanna śakyaṃ surāsuraiḥ ।।
tatkarmanigaḍagrastaiḥ svakarmakhyāpanotsukaḥ ।
na kiñcit kriyate karma sukhaleśopabṛṃhitaiḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhanadyādivarṇana' nāma saptapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ

aṣṭapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

bhagavan ! kathitaṃ samyak bhavatā bhārataṃ mama ।
saritaḥ parvatā deśā ye ca tatra vasanti vai ।।
kintu kūrmastvayā pūrvaṃ bhārate bhagavān hariḥ ।
kathitastasya saṃsthānaṃ śrotumicchāmyaśeṣataḥ ।।
kathaṃ sa saṃsthito devaḥ kūrmarūpī janārdanaḥ ।
śubhāśubhaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ vyajyate ca tataḥ katham ।
yathāmukhaṃ yathāpādantasya tad brūhyaśeṣataḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

prāṅmukho bhagavān ! devaḥ kūrmarūpī vyavasthitaḥ ।
ākramya bhārataṃ varṣaṃ navabhedamidaṃ dvija ।।
navadhā saṃsthitānyasya nakṣatrāṇi samantataḥ ।
viṣayāśca dvijaśreṣṭha ! ye samyak tānnibodha me ।।
vedamantrā vimāṇḍavyāḥ śālvanīpāstathā śakāḥ ।
ujjihānāstathā vatsa ! ghoṣasaṃkhyāstathā khasāḥ ।।
madhye sārasvatā matsyāḥ śūrasenāḥ samāthurāḥ ।
dharmāraṇyā jyotiṣikā gauragrīvā guḍāśmakāḥ ।।
kālakoṭisapāṣaṇḍāḥ pāriyātranivāsinaḥ ।
kāpiṅgalāḥ kururbāhyastathaivoḍumbarā janāḥ ।।
vaidehakāḥ sapāñcālāḥ saṃketāḥ kaṅkamārutāḥ ।
gajāhvayāśca kūrmasya jalamadhyanivāsinaḥ ।।
kṛttikā rohiṇī saumyā eteṣāṃ madhyavāsinām ।
nakṣatratritayaṃ vipra ! śubhāśubhavipākadam ।।
vṛṣadhvajo añjanaścaiva jambvākhyo mānavācalaḥ ।
śūrpakarṇo vyāghramukhaḥ kharmakaḥ karvaṭāśanaḥ ।।
tathā candreśvarāścaiva khaśāśca magadhāstathā ।
girayo maithilāḥ śubhrāstathā vadanadanturāḥ ।।
prāgjyotiṣāḥ salauhityāḥ sāmudrāḥ puruṣādakāḥ ।
purṇotkaṭo bhadragaurastathodayagirirdvija ! ।।
kaśāyā mekhalāmuṣṭāstāmraliptaikapādapāḥ ।
vardhamānā kośalāśca mukhe kūrmasya saṃśthitāḥ ।।
raudraḥ punarvasuḥ puṣyo nakṣatratritayaṃ mukhe ।
pāde tu dakṣiṇe deśāḥ krauṣṭuke vadataḥ śṛṇu ।।
kaliṅgavaṅgajaṭharāḥ kośalā mūṣikāstathā ।
cedayaścordhvakarṇāśca matsyādyā vindhyavāsinaḥ ।।
vidarbhā nārikelāśca dharmadvīpāstathailikāḥ ।
vyāghragrīvā mahāgrīvāstraipurāḥ śmaśrudhāriṇaḥ ।।
kaiṣkindhyā haimakūṭāśca niṣadhāḥ kaṭakasthalāḥ ।
daśārṇāhārikā nagnā niṣādāḥ kākulālakāḥ ।।
tathaiva parṇaśabarāḥ pāde vai pūrvadakṣiṇe ।
āśleṣarkṣaṃ tathā paitryaṃ phālguṇyaḥ prathadamāstathā ।।
nakṣatratritayaṃ pādamāśritaṃ pūrvadakṣiṇam ।
laṅkā kālājināścaiva śailikā nikaṭāstathā ।।
mahendramalayādrau ca durdure ca vasanti ye ।
karkoṭakavane ye ca bhṛgukacchāḥ sakoṅkaṇā ।।
sarvāścaiva tathābhīrā veṇyāstīranivāsinaḥ ।
avantayo dāsapurāstathaivākaṇino janāḥ ।।
mahārāṣṭrāḥ sakarṇāṭā gonardāścitrakūṭakāḥ ।
colāḥ kolagirāścaiva krauñcadvīpajaṭādharāḥ ।।
kāverī ṛṣyamūkasthā nāsikyāścaiva ye janāḥ ।
śaṅkhaśuktyādivaidūryaśailaprāntacarāśca ye ।।
tathā vāricarāḥ kolāḥ carmapaṭṭanivāsinaḥ ।
gaṇabāhyāḥ parāḥ kṛṣṇā dvīpavāsanivāsinaḥ ।।
sūryādrau kumudādrau ca te vasanti tathā janāḥ ।
aukhāvanāḥ sapiśikāstathā ye karmanāyakāḥ ।।
takṣiṇāḥ kauruṣā ye ca ṛṣikāstāpasāśramāḥ ।
ṛṣabhāḥ sihalāścaiva tathā kāñcīnivāsinaḥ ।।
tilaṅgā kuñjāradarīkacchavāsāśca ye janāḥ ।
tāmraparṇo tathā kukṣiriti kūrmasya dakṣiṇaḥ ।।
phālgunyaścottarā hastā citrā carkṣatrayaṃ dvija ।
kūrmasya dakṣiṇe kukṣau bāhyapādastathāparam ।।
kāmbojāḥ pahlavāścaiva tathaiva vahavāmukhāḥ ।
tathā ca sindusauvīrāḥ sānartā vanitāmukhāḥ ।।
drāvaṇāḥ mārgikāḥ śūdrā karṇaprādheyavarvarāḥ ।
kirātāḥ pāradāḥ pāṇḍyāstathā pāraśavāḥ kalāḥ ।।
dhūrtakā haimagirikāḥ sindhukālakavairatāḥ ।
saurāṣṭrā daradāścaiva drāviḍāśca mahārṇavāḥ ।।
ete janapadāḥ pāde sthitā vai dakṣiṇe apare ।
svātyo viśākhā maitrañca nakṣatratrayameva ca ।।
maṇimeghaḥ kṣurādriśca khañjano astagiristathā ।
aparāntikā haihayāśca śāntikā vipraśastakāḥ ।।
kauṅkaṇāḥ pañcanadakā vāmanā hyavarāstathā ।
tārakṣurā hyaṅgatakāḥ karkarāḥ śālmaveśmakāḥ ।।
gurusvirāḥ phalguṇakā veṇumatyāñca ye janāḥ ।
tathā phalgulukā ghorā guruhāśca kalāstathā ।।
ekekṣaṇā vājikeśā dīrghagrīvāḥ sacūlikāḥ ।
aśvakeśāstathā pucche janāḥ kūrmasya saṃsthitāḥ ।।
aindraṃ mūlantathāṣāga nakṣatratrayameva ca ।
māṇḍavyāścaṇḍakhārāśca aśvakālanatāstathā ।।
kunyatālaḍahāścaiva strībāhyā bālikrāstathā ।
nṛsiṃhā veṇumatyāñca balāvasthāstathāpare ।।
dharmabaddhāstathālūkā urukarmasthitā janāḥ ।
vāmapāde janāḥ pārśve sthitāḥ kūrmasya bhāgure ।।
āṣāḍhāśravaṇe caiva dhaniṣṭhā yatra saṃsthitā ।
kailāso himavāṃścaiva dhanuṣmān vasumāṃstathā ।।
krauñcāḥ kuruvakāścaiva kṣudravīṇāśca ye janāḥ ।
rasālayā sakaikeyā bhogaprasthāḥ sayāmunāḥ ।।
antardvopāstrigartāśca agnījyāḥ sārdanā janāḥ ।
tathaivāśvamukhāḥ prāptāściviḍāḥ keśadhāriṇaḥ ।।
dāserakā vāṭadhānāḥ śavadhānāstathaiva ca ।
puṣkalādhamakairātāstathā takṣaśilāśrayāḥ ।।
ambālā mālavā madrā veṇukāḥ savadantikāḥ ।
piṅgalā mānakalahā hūṇāḥ kohalakāstathā ।।
māṇḍavyā bhūtiyuvakāḥ śātakā hematārakāḥ ।
yaśomatyāḥ sagāndhārāḥ kharasāgararāśayaḥ ।।
yaudheyā dāsameyāśca rājanyāḥ śyāmakāstathā ।
kṣemadhūrtāśca kūrmasya vāmakukṣimupāśritāḥ ।।
vāruṇañcātra nakṣatraṃ tatra prauṣṭhapadādvayam ।
yena kinnararājyañca puśupālaṃ sakīcakam ।।
kāśmīrakaṃ tathā rāṣṭramabhisārajanastathā ।
davadāstvaṅganāścaiva kulaṭā vanarāṣṭrakāḥ ।।
sairiṣṭhā brahmapurakāstathaiva vanavāhyakāḥ ।
kirātakauśikā nandā janāḥ pahṇavalolanāḥ ।।
dārvādā marakāścaiva kuraṭāścānnadārakāḥ ।
ekapādā khaśā ghoṣāḥ svargabhaumānavadyakāḥ ।।
tathā sayavanā hiṅgāścīraprāvaraṇāśca ye ।
trinetrāḥ pauravāścaiva gandharvāśca dvijāttama ।।
pūrvottarantu kūrmasya padāmete samāśritāḥ ।
revatyaścāśvidaivatyaṃ yāmyañcarkṣamiti trayam ।।
tatra pāde samākhyātaṃ pākāya munisattama ।
deśeṣveteṣu caitāni nakṣatrāṇyapi vai dvija ।।
etatpīḍā amī deśāḥ pīḍyante ye kramoditāḥ ।
yānti cābhyudayaṃ vipra ! grahaiḥ samyagavasthitaiḥ ।।
yasyarkṣasya patiryo vai grahastadbhāvito bhayam ।
taddeśasya muniśreṣṭha ! tadutkarṣe śubhāgamaḥ ।।
pratyekaṃ deśasāmānyaṃ nakṣatragrahasambhavam ।
bhayaṃ lokasya bhavati śobhanaṃ vā dvijottama ।।
svarkṣairaśobhanairjantoḥ sāmānyamiti bhītidam ।
grahairbhavati pīḍotthamalpāyāsamaśobhanam ।।
tathaiva śobhanaḥ pāko duḥ sthitaiśca tathā grahaiḥ ।
alpopakārāya nṛṇāṃ deśajñaiścātmano budhaiḥ ।।
dravye goṣṭhe atha bhṛtyeṣu suhṛtsu tanayeṣu vā ।
bhāryāyāñca grahe dusthe bhayaṃ puṇyavatāṃ nṛṇām ।।
ātmanyathālpapuṇyānāṃ sarvatraivātipāpinām ।
naikatrāpi hyapāpānāṃ bhayamasti kadācana ।।
digdeśajanasāmānyaṃ nṛpasāmānyamātmajam ।
nakṣatragrahasāmānyaṃ naro bhuṅkte śubhāśubham ।।
parasparābhirakṣā ca grahādausthyena jāyate ।
etebhya eva viprendra ! śubhahānistathāśubhaiḥ ।।
yadetat kūrmasaṃsthānaṃ nakṣatreṣu mayoditam ।
etat tu deśasāmānyamaśubhaṃ śubhameva ca ।।
tasmādvijñāya deśarkṣaṃ grahapīḍāntathātmanaḥ ।
kurvota śāntiṃ medhāvī lokavādāṃśca sattama ।।
ākāśāddevatānāñca daityādīnāñca daurhṛdāḥ ।
pṛthvyāṃ patanti te loke lokavādā iti śrutāḥ ।।
tāṃ tathaiva budhaḥ kuryāt lokavādānna hāpayet ।
teṣāntatkaraṇānnṝṇāṃ yukto duṣṭāgamakṣayaḥ ।।
śubhodayaṃ prahāniñca pāpānāṃ dvijasattama ।
prajñāhāniṃ prakuryuste dravyādīnāñca kurvate ।।
tasmācchāntiparaḥ prājño lokavādaratastathā ।
lokavādāṃśca śāntīśca grahapīḍāsu kārayet ।।
adrohānupavāsāṃśca śastaṃ caityādivandanam ।
japaṃ homaṃ tathā dānaṃ strānaṃ krodhādivarjanam ।।
adrohaḥ sarvabhūteṣu maitrīṃ kuryācca paṇḍitaḥ ।
varjayedasatīṃ vācamativādāṃstathaiva ca ।।
