grahapūjāñca kurvota sarvapīḍāsu mānavaḥ ।
evaṃ śāmyantyaśeṣāṇi ghorāṇi dvijasattama ।।
prayatānāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ graharkṣotthānyaśeṣataḥ ।
eṣa kūrmo mayā khyāto bhārate bhagavān vibhuḥ ।।
nārāyaṇo hyacintyātmā yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
tatra devāḥ sthitāḥ sarve pratinakṣatrasaṃśrayāḥ ।।
tathā madhye hutavahaḥ pṛthvī somaśca vai dvija ।
meṣādayastrayo madhye mukhe dvau mithunādikau ।।
prāgdakṣiṇe tathā pāde karkasiṃhau vyavasthitau ।
siṃhakanyātulāścaiva kukṣau rāśaitrayaṃ sthitam ।।
tulātha vṛścikāścobhau pāde dakṣiṇapaścime ।
pṛṣṭhe ca vṛścikenaiva saha dhanvī vyavasthitaḥ ।।
vāyavye cāsya vai pāde dhanurgrāhādikaṃ trayam ।
kumbhamīnau tathaivāsya uttarāṃ kukṣimāśritau ।।
mīnameṣau dvijaśreṣṭha ! pāde pūrvottare sthitau ।
kūrme deśāstatharkṣāṇi deśeṣveteṣu vai dvija ।।
rāśayaśca tatharkṣeṣu graharāśiṣvavasthitāḥ ।
tasmād graharkṣapīḍāsu deśapīḍāṃ vinirdiśet ।।
tatra strātvā prakurvota dānahomādikaṃ vidhim ।
sa eṣa vaiṣṇavaḥ pādo brahmā madhye grahasya yaḥ ।
nārāyaṇākhyo acintyātmā kāraṇaṃ jagataḥ prabhuḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe kūrmaniveśo nāmāṣṭapañcāśo adhyāyaḥ

ūnaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evantu bhārataṃ varṣaṃ yathāvat kathitaṃ mune ।
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparañca tathāthiṣyaṃ catuṣṭayam ।।
atraivaitadyugānāntu cāturvarṇyo atra vai dvija ।
catvāri trīṇi dve caiva tathaikañca śaracchatam ।।
jīvantyatra narā brahman ! kṛtatretādike kramāt ।
devakūṭasya pūrvasya śailendrasya mahātmanaḥ ।।
pūrveṇa yat sthitaṃ varṣaṃ bhadrāśvaṃ tannibodha me ।
śvetaparṇaśca nīlaśca śaivālaścācalottamaḥ ।।
kaurañjaḥ parṇaśālāgraḥ pañcaite tu kulācalāḥ ।
teṣāṃ prasūtiranye ye bahavaḥ kṣudraparvatāḥ ।।
tairviśiṣṭā janapadā nānārūpāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।
tataḥ kumudasaṃkāśāḥ śuddhasānusumaṅgalāḥ ।।
ityevamādayo anye api śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।
sītā śaṅkhāvatī bhadrā cakrāvartādikāstathā ।।
nadyo atha bahvyo vistīrṇāḥ śītatoyaughavāhikāḥ ।
atra varṣe narāḥ śaṅkhaśuddhahemasamaprabhāḥ ।।
divyasaṅgaminaḥ puṇyā daśavarṣaśatāyuṣaḥ ।
mandottamau na teṣu staḥ sarve te samadarśanāḥ ।।
titikṣādibhiraṣṭābhaiḥ prakṛtyā te guṇairyutāḥ ।
tatrāpyaśvaśirā devaścaturbāhurjanārdanaḥ ।।
śirohṛdayomeḍhrāṅghrihastaiścākṣitrayānvitaḥ ।
tasyāpyathaivaṃ viṣayā vijñeyā jagataḥ prabhoḥ ।।
ketumālamato varṣaṃ nibodha mama paścimam ।
viśālaḥ kambalaḥ kṛṣṇo jayanto hariparvataḥ ।।
viśoko vardhamānaśca saptaite kulaparvatāḥ ।
anye sahasraśaḥ śailā yeṣu lokagaṇaḥ sthitaḥ ।।
maulayaste mahākāyāḥ śākapotakambhakāḥ ।
aṅgulapramukhāścāpi vasanti śataśo janāḥ ।।
ye pibanti mahānadyo vaṅkṣuṃ śyāmāṃ sakambalām ।
amoghāṃ kāminīṃ śyāmāṃ tathaivānyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।।
atrāpyāyuḥ samaṃ pūrvairatrāpi bhagavān hariḥ ।
varāharūpī pādāsyahṛtpṛṣṭhapārśvatastathā ।।
trinakṣatrayute deśe nakṣatrāṇi śubhāni ca ।
ityetat ketumālante kathitaṃ munisattama ।।
ataḥ paraṃ kurūn vakṣye nibodheha mamottarān ।
tatra vṛkṣā madhuphalā nityapuṣpaphalopagāḥ ।।
vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣvābharaṇāni ca ।
sarvakāmapradāste hi sarvakāmaphalapradāḥ ।।
bhūmirmaṇimayī vāyuḥ sugandhaḥ sarvadā sukhaḥ ।
jāyante mānavāstatra devalokaparicyutāḥ ।।
mithunāni prasūyante samakālasthitāni vai ।
anyonyamanuraktāni cakravākopamāni ca ।।
caturdaśasahasrāṇi teṣāṃ sārdhāni vai sthitiḥ ।
candrakāntaśca śailendraḥ sūryakāntastathāparaḥ ।।
tasmin kulācalau varṣe tanmadhye ca mahānadī ।
bhadrasomā prayātyurvyāṃ puṇyāmalajalaughinī ।।
sahasraśastathaivānyā nadyo varṣe api cottare ।
tathānyāḥ kṣīravāhinyo ghṛtavāhinya eva ca ।।
dadhno hradāstathā tatra tathānye cānuparvatāḥ ।
amṛtāsvādakalpāni phalāni vividhāni ca ।।
vaneṣu teṣu varṣeṣu śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।
tatrāpi bhagavān viṣṇuḥ prākśirā matsyarūpavān ।।
vibhakto navadhā vipra ! nakṣatrāṇāṃ trayaṃ trayam ।
diśastathāpi navadhā vibhaktā munisattama ।।
candradvīpaḥ samudre ca bhadradvīpastathāparaḥ ।
tatrāpi puṇyo vikhyātaḥ samudrāntarmahāmune ।।
ityetat kathitaṃ brahman ! kuruvarṣaṃ mayottaram ।
śṛṇu kiṃpuruṣādīni varṣāṇi gadato mama ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhauttarakurukathanaṃ' nāmaikonaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ

ṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

yattu kimpuruṣaṃ varṣaṃ tat pravakṣyāmyahaṃ dvija ।
yatrāyurdaśasāhastraṃ puruṣāṇāṃ vapuṣmatām ।।
anāmayā hyaśokāśca narā yatra tathā striyaḥ ।
plakṣaḥ ṣaṇḍaśca tatroktaḥ sumahānnandanopamaḥ ।।
tasya te vai phalarasaṃ pibantaḥ puruṣāḥ sadā ।
sthirayauvananiṣpannāḥ striyaścotpalagandhikāḥ ।।
ataḥ paraṃ kiṃpuruṣāddharivarṣaṃ pracakṣyate ।
mahārajatasaṅkāśā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।।
devalokacyutāḥ sarve devarūpāśca sarvaśaḥ ।
harivarṣe narāḥ sarve pibantīkṣurasaṃ śubham ।।
na jarā bādhate tatra na jīryante ca karhicit ।
tāvantameva te kālaṃ jīvantyatha nirāmayāḥ ।।
meruvarṣaṃ mayā proktaṃ madhyamaṃ yadilāvṛtam ।
na tatra sūryastapati na te jīryanti mānavāḥ ।।
labhante nātmalābhañca raśmayaścandrasūryayoḥ ।
nakṣatrāṇāṃ grahāṇāñca merostatra parā dyutiḥ ।।
padmaprabhāḥ padmagandhā jambūphalarasāśinaḥ ।
padmapatrāyatākṣāstu jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।।
varṣāṇāntu sahasrāṇi tatrāpyāyustrayodaśa ।
sarāvākārasaṃstāro merumadhye ilāvṛte ।।
merustatra mahāśailastadākhyātamilāvṛtam ।
ramyakaṃ varṣamasmācca kathayiṣye nibodha tat ।।
vṛkṣastatrāpi cottuṅgo nyagrodho haritacchadaḥ ।
tasyāpi te phalarasaṃ pibanto vartayanti vai ।।
varṣāyutāyuṣastatra narāstatphalabhoginaḥ ।
ratipradhānavimalā jarādaurgandhyavarjitāḥ ।।
tasmādathottaraṃ varṣaṃ nāmnā khyātaṃ hiraṇmayam ।
hiraṇvatī nadī yatra prabhūtakamalojjvalā ।।
mahābalāḥ satejaskā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।
mahākāyā mahāsattvā dhaninaḥ priyadarśanāḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhakiṃpuruṣādivarṣavarṇanam a nāma ṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ

ekaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

kathitaṃ bhavatā samyag yat pṛṣṭo asi mahāmune ।
bhūsamudrādisaṃsthānaṃ pramāṇāni tathā grahāḥ ।।
teṣāñcaiva pramāṇañca nakṣatrāṇāñca saṃsthitiḥ ।
bhūrādayastathā lokāḥ pātālānyakhilānyapi ।।
svāyambhuvaṃ tathā khyātaṃ mune ! manvantaraṃ mama ।
tadantarāṇyahaṃ śrotumicche manvantarāṇi vai ।
manvantarādhipān devānṛṣīṃstattanayānnṛpān ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

manvantaraṃ mayākhyātaṃ tava svāyambhuvaṃ ca yat ।
svārociṣākhyamanyat tu śṛṇu tasmādanantaram ।।
kaścid dvijātipravaraḥ pure abhūdaruṇāspade ।
varuṇāyāstaṭe vipro rūpeṇātyaśvināvapi ।।
mṛdusvabhāvaḥ sadvṛtto vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।
sadātithipriyo rātrāvāgatānāṃ samāśrayaḥ ।।
tasya buddhiriyaṃ tvāsīdahaṃ paśye vasundharām ।
atiramyavanodyānāṃ nānānagaraśobhitām ।।
athāgato।ñatithiḥ kaścit kadācittasya veśmani ।
nānauṣadhiprabhāvajño mantravidyāviśāradaḥ ।।
abhyarthitastu tenāsau śraddhāpūtena cetasā ।
tasyācakhyau sa deśāṃśca ramyāṇi nagarāṇi ca ।।
vanāni nadyaḥ śailāṃśca puṇyānyāyatanāni ca ।
sa tato vismayāviṣṭaḥ prāha taṃ dvijasattamam ।।
anekadeśadarśitvenātiśramasamanvitaḥ ।
tvaṃ nātivṛddho vayasā nātivṛttaśca yauvanāt ।
kathamalpena kālena pṛthivīmaṭasi dvija ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

mantrauṣadhiprabhāveṇa viprāpratihatā gatiḥ ।
yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ hi dinārdhena vrajāmyam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ sa viprastaṃ bhūyaḥ pratyuvācedamādarāt ।
śraddhadhāno vacastasya brāhmaṇasya vipaścitaḥ ।।
mama prasādaṃ bhagavan ! kuru mantraprabhāvajam ।
draṣṭumetāṃ mama mahīmatīvecchā pravartate ।।
prādāt sa brāhmaṇaścāsmai pādalepamudāradhīḥ ।
abhimantrayāmāsa diśaṃ tenākhyātāñca yatnataḥ ।।
tenānuliptapādo atha sa dvijo dvijasattama ।
himavantamagād draṣṭuṃ nānāprastravaṇānvitam ।।
sahasraṃ yojanānāṃ hi dinārdhena vrajāmi yat ।
āyāsyāmīti sañcintya tadardhenāpareṇa hi ।।
samprāpto himavatpṛṣṭhaṃ nātiśrāntatanurdvija ।
vicacāra tatastatra tuhinācalabhūtale ।।
pādākrāntena tasyātha tuhinena vilīyatā ।
prakṣālitaḥ pādalepaḥ paramauṣadhisambhaḥ ।।
tato jaḍagatiḥ so atha itaścetaśca paryaṭan ।
dadarśātimanojñāni sānūni himabhūbhṛtaḥ ।।
siddhagandharvajuṣṭāni kinnarābhiratāni ca ।
krīḍāvihāraramyāṇi devādīnāmitastataḥ ।।
divyāpsarogaṇaśatairākīrṇānyavalokayan ।
nātṛpyata dvijaśreṣṭhaḥ prodbhūtapulako mune ।।
kvacit prastravaṇād bhraṣṭajalapātamanoramam ।
pranṛtyacchikhikekābhiranyataśca nināditam ।।
dātyūhakoyaṣṭikādyaiḥ kvaciccātimanoharaiḥ ।
puṃskokilakalālāpaiḥ śrutihāribhiranvitam ।।
praphullatarugandhena vāsitānilavījitam ।
mudā yuktaḥ sa dadṛśe himavantaṃ mahāgirim ।।
dṛṣṭvā caitaṃ dvijasuto himavantaṃ mahācalam ।
śvo drakṣyāmīti saṃcintya matiñcakre gṛhaṃ prati ।।
vibhraṣṭapādalepo atha cireṇa jaḍitakramaḥ ।
cintayāmāsa kimidaṃ mayājñānādanuṣṭhitam ।।
yadi pralepo naṣṭo me vilīno himavāriṇā ।
śailo atidurgamaścāyaṃ dūrañcāhamihāgataḥ ।।
prayāsyāmi kriyāhānimagniśuśrūṣaṇādikam ।
kathamatra kariṣyāmi saṅkaṭaṃ mahadāgatam ।।
idaṃ ramyamidaṃ ramyamityasmin varaparvate ।
śaktadṛṣṭirahaṃ tṛptiṃ na yāsye abdaśatairapi ।।
kinnarāṇāṃ kalālāpāḥ samantācchrotrahāriṇaḥ ।
praphullatarugandhāṃśca ghrāṇamatyantamṛcchati ।।
sukhasparśastathā vāyuḥ phalāni rasavanti ca ।
haranti prasabhaṃ ceto manojñāni sarāṃsi ca ।।
evaṃ gate tu paśyeyaṃ yadi kañcit taponidhim ।
sa mamopadiśenmārgaṃ gamanāya gṛhaṃ prati ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

sa evaṃ cintayan vipro babhrāma ca himācale ।
bhraṣṭapādauṣadhibalo vaiklavaṃ paramaṃ gataḥ ।।
taṃ dadarśa bhramantañca muniśreṣṭhaṃ varūthinī ।
varāpsarā mahābhāgā mauleyā rūpaśālinī ।।
tasmin dṛṣṭe tataḥ sābhūd dvijavarye varūthinī ।
madanākṛṣṭahṛdayā sānurāgā hi tatkṣaṇāt ।।
cintayāmāsa ko nveṣa ramaṇīyatamākṛtiḥ ।
saphalaṃ me bhavejjanma yadi māṃ nāvamanyate ।।
aho asya rūpamādhuryamaho asya lalitā gatiḥ ।
aho gambhīratā dṛṣṭeḥ kuto asya sadṛśo bhuvi ।।
dṛṣṭā devāstathā daityāḥ siddhagandharvapannagāḥ ।
kathameko api nāstyasya tulyarūpo mahātmanaḥ ।।
yathāhamasminmayyeṣa sānurāgastathā yadi ।
bhavedatra mayā kāryastatkṛtaḥ puṇyasañcayaḥ ।।
yadyeṣa mayi sustrigdhāṃ dṛṣṭimadya nipātayet ।
kṛtapuṇyā na matto anyā trailokye vanitā tataḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evaṃ sañcintayantī sā divyayoṣit smarāturā ।
ātmānaṃ darśayāmāsa kamanīyatarākṛtim ।।
tāntu dṛṣṭvā dvijasutaścārurūpāṃ varūthinīm ।
sopacāraṃ samāgamya vākyametaduvāca ha ।।
kā tvaṃ kamalagarbhābhe kasya kiṃ vānutiṣṭhasi ।
brāhmaṇo ahamihāyāto nagarādaruṇāspadāt ।।
pādalepo atra me dhvasto vilīno himavāriṇā ।
yasyānubhāvādatrāhamāgato madirekṣaṇe ।।

varūthinyuvāca

mauleyāhaṃ mahābhāgā nāmnā khyātā varūthinī ।
vicarāmi sadaivātra ramaṇīye mahācale ।।
sāhaṃ tvaddarśanādvipra ! kāmavaktavyatāṅgatā ।
praśādhi yanmayā kāryaṃ tvadadhīnāsmi sāmpratam ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

yenopāyena gaccheyaṃ nijagehaṃ śucismite ।
tanmamācakṣva kalyāṇi hānirno akhilakarmaṇām ।।
nityanaimittikānāntu mahāhānirdvijanmanaḥ ।
bhavatyatastvaṃ he bhadre ! māmuddhara himālayāt ।।
praśasyate na pravāso brāhmaṇānāṃ kadācama ।
aparāddhaṃ na me bhīru deśadarśanakautukam ।।
sato gṛhe dvijāgryasya niṣpattiḥ sarvakarmaṇām ।
nityanaimittikānāñca hānirevaṃ pravāsinaḥ ।।
sā tvaṃ kiṃ bahunoktena tathā kuru yaśasvini ।
yathā nāstaṃ geta sūrye paśyāmi nijamālayam ।।

varūthinyuvāca

maivaṃ brūhi mahābhāga ! mā bhūtsa divaso mama ।
māṃ parityajya yatra tvaṃ nijagehamupaiṣyasi ।।
aho ramyataraḥ svargo na yato dvijanandana ।
ato vayaṃ parityajya tiṣṭhāmo atra surālayam ।।
sa tvaṃ saha mayā kānta ! kānte atra tuhinācale ।
ramamāṇo na martyānāṃ bāndhavānāṃ smariṣyasi ।।
strajo vastrāṇyalaṅkārān bhogabhojyānulepanam ।
dāsyāmyatra tathāhante smareṇa vaśagā hṛtā ।।
vīṇāveṇusvanaṃ gītaṃ kinnarāṇāṃ manoramam ।
aṅgāhlādakaro vāyuruṣṇānnamudakaṃ śuci ।।
manobhilaṣitā śayyā sugandhamanulepanam ।
ihāsato mahābhāga gṛhe kinte nije adhikam ।।
ihāsato naiva jarā kadācitte bhaviṣyati ।
tridaśānāmiyaṃ bhūmiryauvanopacayapradā ।।
ityuktvā sānurāgā sā sahasā kamalekṣaṇā ।
āliliṅga prasīdeti vadantī kalamunmanāḥ ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

mā māṃ sprākṣīrvrajānyatra duṣṭe yaḥ sadṛśastava ।
mayānyathā yācitā tvamanyathaivāpyupaiṣi mām ।।
sāyaṃ prātarhutaṃ havyaṃ lokān yacchati śāśvatān ।
trailokyametadakhilaṃ mūḍhe ivye pratiṣṭhitam ।।

varūthinyuvāca

kiṃ te nāhaṃ priyā vipra ! ramaṇīyo na kiṃ giriḥ ।
gandharvān kinnarādīṃśca tyaktvābhīṣṭo hi kastava ।।
nijamālayamapyasmādbhavān yāsyatyasaṃśayam ।
svalpakālaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ bhuṅkṣava bhogān sudurlabhān ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

aṣṭāvātmaguṇā ye hi teṣāmādau dayā dvija ।
tāṃ karoṣi kathaṃ na tvaṃ mayi saddharmapālaka ।।
tvadvimuktā na jīvāmi tathā prītimatī tvayi ।
naitadvadāmyahaṃ mithyā prasīda kulanandana ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

yadi prītimatī satyaṃ nopacārādbravīṣi mām ।
tadupāyaṃ samācakṣva yena yāmi svamālayam ।।

varūthinyuvāca

nijamālayamapyasmādbhavān yāsyatyasaṃśayam ।
svalpakālaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ bhuṅkṣva bhogān sudurlabhān ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

na bhogārthāya viprāṇāṃ śasyate hi varūthinī ।
iha kleśāya viprāṇāṃ ceṣṭā pretyāphalapradā ।।

varūthinyuvāca

santrāṇaṃ mriyamāṇāyā mama kṛtvā paratra te ।
puṇyasyaiva phalaṃ bhāvi bhogāścānyatra janmani ।।
evaṃ ca dvayamapyatra tavopacayakāraṇam ।
pratyākhyānādahaṃ mṛtyuṃ tvañca pāpamavāpsyasi ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

parastriyaṃ nābhilaṣedityucurguravo mama ।
tena tvāṃ nābhivāñchāmi kāmaṃ vilapa śuṣya vā ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityuktvā sa mahābhāgaḥ spṛṣṭvāpaḥ prayataḥ śuciḥ ।
prāhedaṃ praṇipatyāgniṃ gārhapatyamupāṃśunā ।।
bhagavan ! gārhapatyāgne yonistvaṃ sarvakarmaṇām ।
tvatta āhavanīyo agnirdakṣiṇāgniśca nānyataḥ ।।
yuṣmadāpyāyanād devā vṛṣṭiśasyādihetavaḥ ।
bhavanti śasyādakhilaṃ jagadbhavati nānyataḥ ।।
evaṃ tvatto bhavatyetadyena satyena vai jagat ।
tathāhamadya svaṃ gehaṃ paśyeyaṃ sati bhāskare ।।
yathā vai vaidikaṃ karma svakāle nojjhitaṃ mayā ।
tena satyena paśyeyaṃ gṛhastho adya divākaram ।।
yathā ca na paradravye paradāre ca me matiḥ ।
kadācit sābhilāṣābhūttathaitat siddhimetu me ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhabrāhmaṇavākyam' nāmaikaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ

dviṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evantu vadatastasya dvijaputrasya pāvakaḥ ।
gārhapatyaḥ śarīre tu sannidhānamathākarot ।।
tena cādhiṣṭhitaḥ so atha prabhāmaṇḍalamadhyagaḥ ।
vyadīpayata taṃ deśaṃ mūrtimāniva havyavāṭ ।।
tasyāstu sutarāṃ tatra tādṛgrūpe dvijanmani ।
anurāgo abhavadvipraṃ paśyantyā devayoṣitaḥ ।।
tataḥ so adhiṣṭhitastena havyavāhena tatkṣaṇāt ।
yathāpūrvaṃ tathā gantuṃ pravṛtto dvijanandanaḥ ।।
jagāma ca tvarāyuktastayā devyā nirīkṣitaḥ ।
ādṛṣṭipātāttanvaṅgyā niśvāsotkampikandharam ।।
tataḥ kṣaṇenaiva tadā nijagehamavāpya saḥ ।
yathāproktaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhaścakāra sakalāḥ kriyāḥ ।।
atha sā cārusarvāṅgī tatrāsaktātmamānasā ।
niśvāsaparamā ninye dinaśeṣaṃ tathā niśām ।।
niśvasantyanavadyāṅgī hāheti rudatī muhuḥ ।
mandabhāgyeti cātmānaṃ nininda madirekṣaṇā ।।
na vihāre na cāhāre ramaṇīye na vā vane ।
na kandareṣu ramyeṣu sā babandha tadā ratim ।।
cakāra ramamāṇe ca cakravākayuge spṛhām ।
muktā tena varārohā nininda nijayauvanam ।।
kvāgatāhamimaṃ śailaṃ duṣṭadaivabalātkṛtā ।
kva ca prāptaḥ sa me dṛṣṭergocaraṃ tādṛśo naraḥ ।।
yadyadya sa mahābhāgo na me saṅgamupaiṣyati ।
tatkāmāgniravaśyaṃ māṃ kṣapayiṣyati duḥ sahaḥ ।।
ramaṇīyamabhūdyattatpuṃskokilanināditam ।
tena hīnantadevaitaddahatīvādya māmalam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

itthaṃ sā madanāviṣṭā jagāma munisattama ।
vavṛdhe ca tadā rāgastasyāstasmin pratikṣaṇam ।।
kalirnāmnā tu gandharvaḥ sānurāgo nirākṛtaḥ ।
tayā pūrvamabhūtso atha tadavasthāṃ dadarśa tām ।।
sa cintayāmāsa tadā kiṃ nveṣā gajagāminī ।
niśvāsapavanamlānā girāvatra varūthinī ।।
muniśāpakṣatā kiṃnu kenacit kiṃ vimānitā ।
vāṣpavāripariklinnamiyandhatte yato mukham ।।
tataḥ sa dadhyau suciraṃ tamarthaṃ kautukāt kaliḥ ।
jñātavāṃśca prabhāveṇa samādheḥ sa yathātatham ।।
punaḥ sa cintayāmāsa tadvijñāya muneḥ kaliḥ ।
mamopapāditaṃ sādhu bhāgyairetatpurākṛtaiḥ ।।
mayaiṣā sānurāgeṇa bahuśaḥ prārthitā satī ।
nirākṛtavatī seyamadya prāpyā bhaviṣyati ।।
mānuṣe sānurāgeyaṃ tatra tadrūpadhāriṇi ।
raṃsyate mayyasandigdhaṃ kiṃ kālena karomi tat ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ātmaprabhāveṇa tatastasya rūpaṃ dvijanmanaḥ ।
kṛtvā cacāra yatrāste niṣaṇṇā sā varūthinī ।।
sā taṃ dṛṣṭvā varārohā kiñcidutphullalocanā ।
sametya prāha tanvaṅgī prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ ।।
tvayā tyaktā na sandehaḥ parityakṣyāmi jīvitam ।
tatrādharmaḥ kaṣṭataraḥ kriyālopo bhaviṣyati ।।
mayā sametya ramye asmin mahākandarakandare ।
matparitrāṇajaṃ dharmamavaśyaṃ pratipatsyase ।।
āyuṣaḥ sāvaśeṣaṃ me nṛnamasti mahāmate ।
nivṛttastena nūnaṃ tvaṃ hṛdayāhlādakārakaḥ ।।

kaliruvāca
kiṃ karomi kriyāhānirbhavatyatra sato mama ।
tvamapyevaṃvidhaṃ vākyaṃ bravīṣi tanumadhyame ।।
tadahaṃ saṅkaṭaṃ prāpto yadbravīmi karoṣi tat ।
yadi syāt saṅgamo me adya bhavatyā saha nānyathā ।।

varūthinī uvāca

prasīda yadbravīṣi tvaṃ tatkaromi na te mṛṣā ।
bravīmyetadanāśaṅkaṃ yatte kāryaṃ mayādhunā ।।

kaliruvāca

nādya saṃbhogasamaye draṣṭavyo ahaṃ tvayā vane ।
nimīlitākṣyāḥ saṃsargastava subhru mayā saha ।।

varūthinyuvāca

evaṃ bhavatu bhadrante yathecchasi tathāstu tat ।
mayā sarvaprakāraṃ hi vaśe stheyaṃ tavādhunā ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe svārociṣe manvantare dviṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ ।

triṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ saha tathā so atha rarāma girisānuṣu ।
phullakānanahṛdyeṣu manojñeṣu saraḥ su ca ।।
kandareṣu ca ramyeṣu nimnagāpulineṣu ca ।
manojñeṣu tathānyeṣu deśeṣu mudito dvija ।।
vahninādhiṣṭhitasyāsīd yadrūpantasya tejasā ।
acintayadbhogakāle nimīlitavilocanā ।।
tataḥ kālena sā garbhamavāpa munisattama ।
gandharvavīryato rūpacintanācca dvijanmanaḥ ।।
tāṃ garbhadhāriṇīṃ so atha sāntvayitvā varūthinīm ।
viprarūpadharo yātastayā prītyā visarjitaḥ ।।
jajñe sa bālo dyutimāna jvalanniva vibhāvasuḥ ।
svarocibhairyathā sūryo bhāsayan sakalā diśaḥ ।।
svarocibhiryato bhāti bhāsvāniva sa bālakaḥ ।
tataḥ svarocirityevaṃ nāmnā khyāto babhūta saḥ ।।
vavṛdhe ca mahābhāgo vayasānudinantathā ।
guṇaughaiśca yathā bālaḥ kalābhiḥ śaśalāñchanaḥ ।।
sa jagrāha dhanurvedaṃ vedāṃścaiva yathākramam ।
vidyāścaiva mahābhāgastadā yauvanagocaraḥ ।।
mandarādrau kadācit sa vicaraṃścāruceṣṭitaḥ ।
dadarśaikāṃ tadā kanyāṃ giriprasthe bhayāturām ।।
trāyasveti nirīkṣyainaṃ sā tadā vākyamabravīt ।
mā bhaiṣīriti sa prāha bhayaviplutalocanām ।।
kimetaditi tenokte vīravākye mahātmanā ।
tataḥ sā kathayāmāsa śvāsākṣepaplutākṣaram ।।

kanyovāca

ahamindīvarākhyasya sutā vidyādharasya vai ।
nāmnā manoramā jātā sutāyāṃ marudhanvanaḥ ।।
mandāravidyādharajā sakhī mama vibhāvarī ।
kalāvatī cāpyaparā sutā pārasya vai muneḥ ।।
tābhyāṃ saha mayā yātaṃ kailāsataṭamuttamam ।
tatra dṛṣṭo muniḥ kaścittapasātikṛśākṛtiḥ ।।
kṣutkṣāmakaṇṭho nistejā dūrapātākṣitārakaḥ ।
mayāvahasitaḥ kruddhaḥ sa tadā māṃ śaśāpa ha ।।
kṣāmakṣāmasvaraḥ kiñcitkalpitādharapallavaḥ ।
tvayāvahasito yasmādanārye duṣṭatāpasi ।।
tasmāt tvāmacireṇaiva rākṣaso abhibhaviṣyasi ।
datte śāpe matsakhībhyāṃ sa tu nirbhatsito muniḥ ।।
dhik te brāhmaṇyamakṣāntyā hṛtante nikhilantapaḥ ।
amarṣaṇairdharṣito asi tapasā nātikarṣitaḥ ।।
kṣāntyāspadaṃ vai brāhmaṇyaṃ krodhasaṃyamanantapaḥ ।
etacchrutvā dadau śāpaṃ tayorapyamitadyutiḥ ।।
ekasyāḥ kuṣṭhamaṅgeṣu bhāvyanyasyāstathā kṣayaḥ ।
tayostathaiva tajjātaṃ yathoktaṃ tena tatkṣaṇāt ।।
mamāpyevaṃ mahadrakṣaḥ samupaiti padānugam ।
na śṛṇoṣi mahānādaṃ tasyādūre api garjataḥ ।।
tṛtīyamadya divasaṃ yanme pṛṣṭhanna muñcati ।
astragrāmasya sarvasya hṛdajñāhamadya te ।।
te prayacchāmi māṃ rakṣa rakṣaso asmānmahāmate ।
prādāt svāyambhuvasyādau svayaṃ rudraḥ pinākadhṛk ।।
svāyambhuvo vasiṣṭhāya siddhavaryāya dattavān ।
tenāpi dattaṃ manmātuḥ pitre citrāyudhāya vai ।।
prādādaudvāhikaṃ so api matpitre śvaśuraḥ svayam ।
mayāpi śikṣitaṃ vīra ! sakāśād bālayā pituḥ ।।
hṛdayaṃ sakalāstrāṇāmaśeṣaripunāśanam ।
tadidaṃ gṛhyatāṃ śīghramaśeṣāstraparāyaṇam ।।
tato jahi durātmānamenaṃ rākṣasamāgatam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tathaityukte tatastena vāryupaspṛśya tasya tat ।
astrāṇāṃ hṛdayaṃ prādāt sarahasyanivartanam ।।
etasminnantare rakṣastattadā bhīṣaṇākṛti ।
nardamānaṃ mahānādamājagāma tvarānvitam ।।
mayābhibhūtā kiṃ trāṇamupaiṣi drutamehi me ।
bhakṣāmi kiñcireṇeti bruvāṇaṃ taṃ dadarśa saḥ ।।
svarociścintayāmāsa dṛṣṭvā taṃ samupāgatam ।
gṛhṇātveṣa vacaḥ satyaṃ tasyāstviti mahāmuneḥ ।।
jagrāha samupetyaināṃ tvarayā so api rākṣasaḥ ।
trāhi trāhīti karuṇaṃ vilapantīṃ sumadhyamām ।।
tataḥ svarociḥ saṃkruddhaścaṇḍāstramatibhairavam ।
dṛṣṭyāṃ niveśya tadrakṣo dadarśānimiṣekṣaṇaḥ ।।
tadābhibhūtaḥ sa tadā tāmutsṛjya niśācaraḥ ।
prasīda śāmyatāmastraṃ śrūyatāñcetyabhāṣata ।।
mokṣitoṣa'haṃ tvayā śāpādatighorānmahādyute ।
pradattādatitīvreṇa brahmamitreṇa dhīmatā ।।
upakārī na me tvatto mahābhāgādhiko aparaḥ ।
yenāhaṃ sumahākaṣṭānmahāśāpādvimokṣitaḥ ।।

svarociruvāca
brahmamitreṇa muninā kinnimittaṃ mahātmanā ।
śaptastvaṃ kīdṛśaścaiva śāpo datto abhavat purā ।।

rākṣasā uvāca

brahmamitro aṣṭadhā bhinnamāyurvedamadhītavān ।
trayodaśādhikārañca pragṛhyātharvaṇo dvijaḥ ।।
ahañcendīvarākhyeti khyāto asyā janako abhavam ।
vidyādharapateḥ putro nalanābhasya khaṅginaḥ ।।
mayā ca yācitaḥ purvaṃ brahmamitro abhavanmuniḥ ।
āyurvedamaśeṣaṃ me bhagavan ! dātumarhasi ।।
yadā tu bahuśo vīra ! praśrayāvanatasya me ।
na prādādyācito vidyāmāyurvedātmikāṃ mama ।।
śiṣyebhyo dadatastasya mayāntardhānagena hi ।
āyurvedātmikā vidyā gṛhītābhūttadānagha ।।
gṛhītāyāntu vidyāyāṃ māsairaṣṭābhirantarāt ।
mamātiharṣādabhavaddhāso atīva punaḥ punaḥ ।।
pratyabhijñāya māṃ hāsānmuniḥ kopasamanvitaḥ ।
vikampikandharaḥ prāha māmidaṃ paruṣākṣaram ।।
rākṣasenaiva yasmānme tvayādṛśyena durmate ।
hṛtā vidyāvahāsaśca māmavajñāya vai kṛtaḥ ।।
tasmāttvaṃ rākṣasaḥ pāpa ! macchāpena nirākṛtaḥ ।
bhaviṣyasi na sandehaḥ saptarātreṇa dāruṇaḥ ।।
ityukte praṇipātādyairupacāraiḥ prasāditaḥ ।
sa māmāha punarviprastatkṣaṇānmṛdumānasaḥ ।।
yanmayoktamavaśyantadbhāvi gandharva ! nānyathā ।
kintu tvaṃ rākṣaso bhūtvā punaḥ svaṃ prāpsyase vapuḥ ।।
naṣṭasmṛtiryadā kruddhaḥ svamapatyañcikhādiṣuḥ ।
niśācaratvaṃ gantāsi tadastrānalatāpitaḥ ।।
punaḥ saṃjñāmavāpya svāmavāpsyasi nijaṃ vapuḥ ।
tathaiva svamadhiṣṭhānaṃ loke gandharvasaṃjñite ।।
so ahaṃ tvayā mahābhāga ! mokṣito asmānmahābhayāt ।
niśācaratvād yadvīra ! tena me prārthanāṃ kuru ।।
imānte tanayāṃ bhāryāṃ prayacchāmi pratīccha tām ।
āyurvedaśca sakalastvaṣṭāṅgo yo mayā tataḥ ।
muneḥ sakāśāt saṃprāptastaṃ gṛhṇīṣva mahāmate ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ityuktvā pradadau vidyāṃ sa ca divyāmbarojjavalaḥ ।
stragbhūṣaṇadharo divyaṃ purāṇaṃ vapurāsthitaḥ ।।
dattvā vidyāṃ tataḥ kanyāṃ sa dātumupacakrame ।
tamāha sā tadā kanyā janitāraṃ svarūpiṇam ।।
anurāgo mamāpyatra tātātīva mahātmani ।
darśanādeva saṃjāto viśeṣeṇopakāriṇi ।।
kintveṣā me sakhī sā ca matkṛte duḥ khapīḍite ।
ato nābhilaṣe bhogān bhoktumetena vai samam ।।
puruṣairapi no śakyā kartumitthaṃ nṛśaṃsatā ।
svabhāvarucirairmādṛk kathaṃ yoṣit kariṣyati ।।
sāhaṃ yathā te duḥ khārte matkṛte kanyake pitaḥ ।
tathā sthāsyāmi tadduḥ khe tacchokānalatāpitā ।।

svarociruvāca

āyurvedaprasādena te kariṣye punarnave ।
sakhyau tava mahāśokaṃ samutsṛja sumadhyame ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ pitrā svayaṃ dattāṃ tāṃ kanyāṃ sa vidhānataḥ ।
upayeme girau tasmin svarociścārulocavanām ।।
dattāntu tāṃ tadā kanyāmabhiśāntya ca bhāminīm ।
jagāma divyayā gatyāgandharvaḥ svapurantataḥ ।।
sa cāpi sahitastanvyā sadudyānantadā yayau ।
kanyakāyugalaṃ yatra tacchāpotthagadāturam ।।
tatastayoḥ sa tattvajño rogaghnairauṣadhai rasaiḥ ।
cakāra nīrujau dehau svarociraparājitaḥ ।।
tato atiśobhane kanye vimukte vyādhitaḥ śubhe ।
svakāntyodyoti digbhāgaṃ cakrāte tanmahīdharam ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe svārociṣe manvantare triṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ

catuḥ ṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evaṃ vimuktarogā tu kanyakā taṃ mudānvitā ।
svarociṣamuvācedaṃ śṛṇuṣva vacanaṃ prabho ।।
mandāravidyādharajā nāmnā khyātā vibhāvarī ।
upakārin ! svamātmānaṃ prayacchāmi pratīccha mām ।।
vidyāñca tubhyaṃ dāsyāmi sarvabūtarutāni te ।
yayābhivyaktimeṣyanti prasādapurago bhava ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evamastviti tenokte dharmajñena svarociṣā ।
dvitīyā tu tadā kanyā idaṃ vacanamabravīt ।।
kumārabrahmacāryāsīt pāro nāma pitā mama ।
brahmarṣiḥ sumahābhāgo vedavedāṅgapāragaḥ ।।
tasya puṃskokilālāparamaṇīye madhau purā ।
ājagāmāpsarābhyāsaṃ prakhyātā puñjikāstanā ।।
kāmavaktavyatāṃ nītaḥ sa tadā munipuṅgavaḥ ।
tatsaṃyoge ahamutpannā tasyāmatra mahācale ।।
vihāya māṃ gatā sā ca mātāsminnirjane vane ।
bālāmekāṃ mahīpṛṣṭhe vyālaśvāpadasaṃkule ।।
tataḥ kalābhiḥ somasya vardhantībhirahaḥ kṣaye ।
āpyāyyamānāharaho vṛddhiṃ yātāsmi sattama ।।
tataḥ kalāvatītyetanmama nāma mahātmanā ।
gṛhītāyaḥ kṛtaṃ pitrā gandharveṇa śubhānanā ।।
na dattāhaṃ tadā tena yācitena mahātmanā ।
devāriṇālinā suptastato me ghātitaḥ pitā ।।
tato ahamatinirvedādātmavyāpādanodyatā ।
nivāritā śambhupatnyā satyā satyapratiśravā ।।
mā śucaḥ subhru ! bhartā te mahābhāgo bhaviṣyati ।
svarocirnāma putraśca manustasya bhaviṣyati ।।
ājñāñca nidhayaḥ sarve kariṣyanti tavādṛtāḥ ।
yathābhilaṣitaṃ vittaṃ pradāsyanti ca te śubhe ।।
yasyā vatse prabhāveṇa vidyāyāstāṃ gṛhāṇa me ।
padminī nāma vidyeyaṃ mahāpadmābhipūjitā ।।
ityāha māṃ dakṣasutā satī satyaparāyaṇā ।
svarocistvaṃ dhruvaṃ devī nānyathā sā vadiṣyati ।।
sāhaṃ prāṇapradāyādya tāṃ vidyāṃ svaṃ tathā vapuḥ ।
prayacchāmi pratīccha tvaṃ prasādasumukho mama ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evamastviti tāmāha sa tu kanyāṃ kalāvatīm ।
vibhāvaryāḥ kalāvatyāḥ snigdhadṛṣṭyānumoditaḥ ।।
jagrāha ca tataḥ pāṇī sa tayoramaradyutiḥ ।
nadatsu devatūryeṣu nṛtyantīṣvapsaraḥ su ca ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇjaḍeyapurāṇeṭhasvārociṣe manvantare' catuḥ ṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ

pañcaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ sa tābhiḥ sahitaḥ patnībhiramaradyutiḥ ।
rarāma tasmin śailendre ramyakānananirjhare ।।
sarvopabhogaratnāni madhūni madhurāṇi ca ।
nidhayaḥ samupājahruḥ padminyā vaśavartinaḥ ।।
strajo vastrāṇyalaṅkārān gandhāḍhyamanulepanam ।
āsanānyatiśubhrāṇi kāñcanāni yathecchayā ।।
sauvarṇāni mahābhāga ! karakān bhājanāni ca ।
tathā śayyāśca vividhā divyairāstaraṇairyutāḥ ।।
evaṃ sa tābhiḥ sahito divyagandhādhivāsite ।
rarāma svarucirbhābhirbhāsite varaparvate ।।
tāścāpi saha teneti lebhire mudamuttamām ।
ramamāṇā yathā svarge tathā tatra śiloccaye ।।
kalahaṃsī jagādaikāṃ cakravākīṃ jale satīm ।
tasya tāsāñca lalite sambandhe ca spṛhāvatī ।।
dhanyo ayamatipuṇyo ayaṃ yo aya yauvanagocaraḥ ।
dayitābhiḥ sahaitābhirbhuṅkte bhogānabhīpsitān ।।
santi yauvaninaḥ ślāghyāstatpatnyo nātiśobhanāḥ ।
jagatyāmalpakāḥ patnyaḥ patayaścātiśobhanāḥ ।।
abhīṣṭā kasyacit kāntā kāntaḥ kasyāścidīpsitaḥ ।
parasparānurāgāḍhyaṃ dāmpatyamatidurlabham ।।
dhanyo ayaṃ dayitābhīṣṭo hyetāścāsyātivallabhāḥ ।
parasparānurāgo hi dhanyānāmeva jāyate ।।
etanniśamyavacanaṃ kalahaṃsīsamīritam ।
uvāca cakravākī tāṃ nātivismitamānasā ।।
nāyaṃ dhanyo yato lajjā nānyastrīsannikarṣataḥ ।
anyāṃ striyamayaṃ bhuṅkte na sarvāsvasya mānasam ।।
cittānurāga ekasminnadhiṣṭhāne yataḥ sakhi ।
tato hi prītimāneṣa bhāryāsu bhavitā katham ।।
etā na dayitāḥ patyurnaitāsāṃ dayitaḥ patiḥ ।
vinodamātramevaitā yathā parijano aparaḥ ।।
etāsāñca yadiṣṭo ayaṃ tat kiṃ prāṇānna muñcati ।
āliṅgatyaparāṃ kāntāṃ dhyāto vai kāntayānyayā ।।
vidyāpradānamūlyena vikrīto hyeṣa bhṛtyavat ।
pravartate na hi prema samaṃ bahvīṣu tiṣṭhati ।।
kalahaṃsi ! patirdhanyo mama dhanyāhameva ca ।
yasyaikasyāñciraṃ cittaṃ yasyāścaikatra saṃsthitam ।।
sarvasattvarutajño asau svarociraparājitaḥ ।
niśamya lajjito dadhyau satyameva hi nānṛtam ।।
tato varṣaśate yāte ramamāṇo mahāgirau ।
ramamāṇaḥ samaṃ tābhirdadarśa purato mṛgam ।।
susnigdhapīnāvayavaṃ mṛgayūthavihāriṇam ।
vāsitābhiḥ surūpābhirmṛgībhiḥ parivāritam ।।
ākṛṣṭaghrāṇapuṭakā jighrantīstāstato mṛgīḥ ।
uvāca sa mṛgo rāmā lajjātyāgena gamyatām ।।
nāhaṃ svarocistacchīlo na caivāhaṃ sulocanāḥ ।
nirlajjā bahavaḥ santi tādṛśāstatra gacchataḥ ।।
ekā tvanekānugatā yathā hāsāspadaṃ jane ।
anekābhistathaivaiko bogadṛṣṭyā nirīkṣitaḥ ।।
tasya dharmakriyāhānirahanyahani jāyate ।
sakto anyabhāryayā cānyakāmāsaktaḥ sadaiva saḥ ।।
yastādṛśo anyastacchīlaḥ paralokaparāṅmukhaḥ ।
taṃ kāmayata bhadraṃ vo nāhaṃ tulyaḥ svarociṣā ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe svārociṣe manvantare pañcaṣaṣṭitamo adhyāyaḥ

ÆÑḥâå>üúåßÑādādanāgatam ।
yathāhaṃ samatītañca vartamānañca sarvataḥ ।।
ālocyājñāpayetyukte tato jñātaṃ mayāpi tat ।
tato na dattavānarghamahaṃ tubhyaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।
satyaṃ rājan ! tvamarghārhaḥ kule svāyambhuvasya ca ।
tathāpi nārghayogyaṃ tvāṃ manyāmo vayamuttamam ।।

rājovāca

kiṃ kṛtaṃ hi mayā brahman ! jñānādajñānato api vā ।
yena tvattor'ghamarhāmi nāhamabhyāgataścirāt ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

kiṃ vismṛtante yatpatnī tvayā tyaktā ca kānane ।
parityaktastayā sārdhaṃ tvayā dharmo nṛpākhilaḥ ।।
pakṣeṇa karmaṇo hānyā prayātyasparśatāṃ naraḥ ।
viṇmūtrairvārṣikī yasya hāniste nityakarmaṇaḥ ।।
patnyānukūlayā bhāvyaṃ yathāśīle api bhartari ।
duḥ śīlāpi tathā bhāryā poṣaṇīyā nareśvara ।।
pratikūlā hi sā patnī tasya viprasya yā hṛtā ।
tathāpi dharmakāmo asau tvāmudyotitavān nṛpa ।।
calataḥ sthāpayasyanyān svadharmeṣu mahīpate ।
tvāṃ svadharmādvicalitaṃ ko aparaḥ sthāpayiṣyati ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

vilakṣyaḥ sa mahīpāla ityuktastena dhīmatā ।
tathetyuktvā ca papraccha hṛtāṃ patnīṃ dvijanmanaḥ ।।
bhagavan ! kena nītā sā patnī viprasya kutra vā ।
atītānāgataṃ vetti jagatyavitathaṃ bhavān ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

tāṃ jahārādritanayo balāko nāma rākṣasaḥ ।
drakṣyase cādya tāṃ bhūpa ! utpalāvatake vane ।।
gaccha saṃyojayāśu tvaṃ bhāryayā hi dvijāttamam ।
mā pāpāspadatāṃ yātu tvamivāsau dine dine ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe auttamamanvantare ekonasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

saptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

athāruroha svarathaṃ praṇipatya mahāmunim ।
tenākhyātaṃ vanantacca prayayāvutpalāvatam ।।
yathākhyātasvarūpāñca bhāryāṃ bhartrā dvijasya tām ।
bhakṣayantīṃ dadārśātha śrīphalāni nareśvaraḥ ।।
papraccha ca kathaṃ bhadre ! tvametadvanamāgatā ।
sphuṭaṃ bravīhi vaiśālerapi bhāryā suśarmaṇaḥ ।।

brāhmaṇyuvāca

sutāhamatirātrasya dvijasya vanavāsinaḥ ।
patnī viśālaputrasya yasya nāma tvayoditam ।।
sāhaṃ hṛtā balākena rākṣasena durātmanā ।
prasuptā bhavanasyānte bhrātṛmātṛviyojitā ।।
bhasmībhavatu tadrakṣo yenāsmyevaṃ viyojitā ।
mātrā bhrātṛbhiranyaiśca tiṣṭāmyatra suduḥ khitā ।।
asmin vane atigahane tenānīyāhamujjhitā ।
na vedmi kāraṇaṃ ki tannopabhuṅkte na khādati ।।

rājovāca
api tajjñāyate rakṣastvāmutsṛjya kva vai gatam ।
ahaṃ bhartrā tavaivātra preṣito dvijanandini ।।

brāhmaṇyuvāca

asyaiva kānanasyānte sa tiṣṭhati niśācaraḥ ।
praviśya paśyatu bhavān na bibheti tato yadi ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

praviveśa tataḥ so atha tayā vartmani darśite ।
dadṛśe parivāreṇa samavetañca rākṣasam ।।
dṛṣṭamātre tatastasmin tvaramāṇaḥ sa rākṣasaḥ ।
dūrādeva mahīṃ mūrdhnā spṛśan pādāntikaṃ yayau ।।

rākṣasa uvāca

mamātrāgacchatā gehaṃ prasādaste mahān kṛtaḥ ।
praśādhi kiṃ karomyeṣa vasāmi viṣaye tava ।।
arghañcemaṃ pratīccha tvaṃ sthīyatāñcedamāsanam ।
vayaṃ bhṛtyā bhavān svāmī dṛḍhamājñāpayasva mām ।।

rājovāca

kṛtameva tvayā sarvaṃ sarvāmevātithikriyām ।
kimarthaṃ brāhmaṇavadhūstvayānītā niśācara ।।
neyaṃ surūpā santyanyā bhāryārthañced hṛtā tvayā ।
bhakṣyārthaṃ cetkathaṃ nāttā tvayaitatkathyatāṃ mama ।।

rākṣasa uvāca

na vayaṃ mānuṣāhārā anye te nṛpa ! rākṣasāḥ ।
sukṛtasya phalaṃ yattu tadaśnīmo vayaṃ nṛpa ।।
svabhāvañca manuṣyāṇāṃ yoṣitāñca vimānitāḥ ।
mānitāśca samaśnīmo na vayaṃ jantukhādakāḥ ।।
yadasmābhirnṛṇāṃ kṣāntirbhuktā krudhyanti te tadā ।
bhukte duṣṭe svabhāve ca guṇavanto bhavanti ca ।।
santi naḥ pramadā bhūpa ! rūpeṇāpsarasāṃ samāḥ ।
rākṣasyastāsu tiṣṭhatsu mānuṣīṣu ratiḥ katham ।।

rājovāca

yadyeṣā nopabhogāya nāhārāya niśācara ।
gṛhaṃ praviśya viprasya tatkimeṣā hṛtā tvayā ।।

rākṣasa uvāca

mantravit sa dvijaśreṣṭho yajñe yajñe gatasya me ।
rakṣoghnamantrapaṭhanāt karotyuccāṭanaṃ nṛpa ।।
vayaṃ bubhukṣitāstasya mantroccāṭanakarmaṇā ।
kva yāmaḥ sarvayajñeṣu sa ṛtvig bhavati dvijaḥ ।।
tato asmābhiridantasya vaikalyamupapāditam ।
patnyā vinā pumānijyākarmayogyo na jāyate ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

vaikalyoccāraṇāttasya brāhmaṇasya mahāmateḥ ।
tataḥ sa rājātibhṛśaṃ viṣaṇṇaḥ samajāyata ।।
vaikalyamevaṃ viprasya vadanmāmeva nindati ।
anarhamarghasya ca māṃ so apyāha munisattamaḥ ।।
vaikalyaṃ tasya viprasya rākṣaso apyāha me yathā ।
apatnīkatayā so ahaṃ saṅkaṭaṃ mahadāsthitaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evaṃ cintayatastasya punarapyāha rākṣasaḥ ।
praṇāmanamro rājānaṃ baddhāñjalipuṭo mune ।।
narendrājñāpradānena prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ mama ।
bhṛtyasya praṇatasya tvaṃ yuṣmadviṣayavāsinaḥ ।।

rājovāca

svabhāvaṃ vayamaśnīmastvayoktaṃ yanniśācara ।
tadarthino vayaṃ yena kāryeṇa śṛṇu tanmama ।।
asyāstvayādya brāhmaṇyā dauḥ śīlyamupabhujyatām ।
yena tvayāttadauḥ śīlyā tadvinītā bhavediyam ।।
nīyatāṃ yasya bhāryeyaṃ tasya veśma niśācara ।
asmin kṛte kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ gṛhamabhyāgatasya me ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ sa rākṣasastasyāḥ praviśyāntaḥ svamāyayā ।
bhakṣayāmāsa dauḥ śīlyaṃ nijaśaktyā nṛpājñayā ।।
dauḥ śīlyenātiraudreṇa patnī tasya dvijanmanaḥ ।
tena sā saṃparityaktā tamāha jagatīpatim ।।
svakarmaphalapākena bhartustasya mahātmanaḥ ।
viyojitāhaṃ taddheturayamāsīnniśācaraḥ ।।
nāsya doṣo na vā tasya mama bharturmahātmanaḥ ।
mamaiva doṣo nānyasya sukṛtaṃ hyupabhujyate ।।
anyajanmani kasyāpi viprayogaḥ kṛto mayā ।
so ayaṃ mamāpyupagataḥ ko doṣo asya mahātmanaḥ ।।

rākṣasa uvāca

prāpayāmi tavādeśādimāṃ bhartṛgṛhaṃ prabho ।
yadanyatkaraṇīyante tadājñāpaya pārthiva ।।

rājovāca

asmin kṛte kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ tvayā me rajanīcara ।
āgantavyañca te vīra ! kāryakāle smṛtena me ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

nathetyuktvā tu tadrakṣastāmādāya dvijāṅganām ।
ninye bhartṛgṛhaṃ śuddhāṃ dauḥ śolyāpagamāttadā ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe auttamamanvantare saptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

ekasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tāṃ preṣayitvā rājāpi svabhartṛgṛhamaṅganām ।
cintayāmāsa niḥ śvasya kimatra sukataṃ bhavet ।।
anarghayogyatā kaṣṭaṃ sa māmāha mahāmanāḥ ।
vaikalyaṃ vipramuddiśya tathāhāyaṃ niśācaraḥ ।।
so ahaṃ kathaṃ kariṣyāmi tyaktā patnī mayā hi sā ।
athavā jñānadṛṣṭiṃ taṃ pṛcchāmi munisattamam ।।
sañcintyetthaṃ sa bhūpālaḥ samāruhya ca taṃ ratham ।
yayau yatra sa dharmātmā trikālajño mahāminiḥ ।।
avaruhya rathāt so atha taṃ sametya praṇamya ca ।
yathāvṛttaṃ samācakhyau rākṣasena samāgamam ।।
brāhmaṇyā darśanañcaiva dauḥ śīlyāpagamaṃ tathā ।
preṣaṇaṃ bhartṛgehe ca kāryamāgamane ca yat ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

jñātametanmayā pūrvaṃ yat kṛtante narādhipa ।
kāryamāgamane caiva matsamīpe tavākhilam ।।
pṛccha māmiha kiṃ kāryaṃ mayetyudvignamānasaḥ ।
tvayyāgate mahīpāla ! śṛṇu kāryañca yattvayā ।।
patnī dharmārthakāmānāṃ kāraṇaṃ prabalaṃ nṛṇām ।
viśeṣataśca dharmasya santyaktastyajatā hi tām ।।
apatnīko naro bhūpa ! na yogyo nijakarmaṇām ।
brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vaiśyaḥ śūdro api vā nṛpa ।।
tyajatā bhavatā patnīṃ na śobhanamanuṣṭhitam ।
atyājyo hi yathā bhartā strīṇāṃ bharyā tathā nṛṇām ।।

rājovāca

bhagavan ! kiṃ karomyeṣa vipāko mama karmaṇām ।
nānukūlānukūlasya yasmāttyaktā tato mayā ।।
yadyatkaroti tat kṣāntaṃ dahyamānena cetasā ।
bhagavaṃstadviyogārtibibhītenāntarātmanā ।।
sāmprataṃ tu vane tyaktā na vedmi kva nu sā gatā ।
bhakṣitā vāpi vipine siṃhavyāghraniśācaraiḥ ।।
ṛṣīruvāca

na bhakṣitā sā bhūpāla ! sihavyāghraniśācaraiḥ ।
sā tvaviplutacāritrā sāmpratantu rasātale ।।

rājovāca

sā nītā kena pātālamāste sādūṣitā katham ।
atyadbhutamidaṃ brahman ! yathāvadvaktumarhasi ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

pātāle nāgarājo asti prakhyātaśca kapotakaḥ ।
tena dṛṣṭā tvayā tyaktā bhramamāṇā mahāvane ।।
sā rūpaśālinī tena sānurāgeṇa pārthiva ।
veditārthena pātālaṃ nītā sā yuvatī tadā ।।
tatastasya sutā subhrūrnandā nāma mahīpate ।
bhāryā manoramā cāsya nāgarājasya dhīmataḥ ।।
tayā mātuḥ sapatnīyaṃ sā bhavitrīti śobhanā ।
dṛṣṭā svagehaṃ sā nītā guptā cāntaḥ pure śubhā ।।
yadā tu yācitā nandā na dadāti nṛpottaram ।
mūkā bhaviṣyasītyāha tadā tāṃ tanayāṃ pitā ।।
evaṃ śaptā sutā tena sā cāste tatra bhūpate ।
nītā tenoragendreṇa dhṛtā tatsutayā satī ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tato rājā paraṃ harṣamavāpya tamapṛcchata ।
dvijavaryaṃ svadaurbhāgyakāraṇaṃ dayitāṃ prati ।।

rājovāca

bhagavan ! sarvalokasya mayi prītiranuttamā ।
kinnu tatkāraṇaṃ yena svapatnī nātivatsalā ।।
mama cāsāvatīveṣṭā prāṇebhyo api mahāmune ।
sā ca māṃ prati duḥ śīlā brūhi yatkāraṇaṃ dvija ।।

ṛṣīruvāca
pāṇigrahaṇakāle tvaṃ sūryabhaumaśanaiścaraiḥ ।
śukravācaspatibhyāñca tava bhāryāvalokitā ।।
tanmuhūrte abhavaccandrastasyāḥ somasutastathā ।
parasparavipakṣau tau tataḥ pārthiva ! te bhṛśam ।।
tadgaccha tvaṃ svadharmeṇa paripālaya medinīm ।
patnīsahāyaḥ sarvāśca kuru dharmavatīḥ kriyāḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityukte praṇipatyainamāruhya syandanaṃ tataḥ ।
uttamaḥ pṛthivīpāla ājagāma nijaṃ puram ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe auttamamanvantare ekasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

dvisaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ svanagaraṃ prāpya taṃ dadarśa dvijaṃ nṛpaḥ ।
sametaṃ bhāryayā caiva śīlavatyā mudānvitam ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

rājavarya ! kṛtārtho asmi yato dharmo hi rakṣitaḥ ।
dharmajñaneha bhavatā bhāryāmānayatā mama ।।

rājovāca

kṛtārthastvaṃ dvijaśreṣṭha ! nijadharmānupālanāt ।
vayaṃ saṅkaṭino vipra ! yeṣāṃ patnī na veśmani ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

narendra ! sā hi vipine bhakṣitā śvanāpadairyadi ।
alantayā kimanyasyā na pāṇirgṛhyate tvayā ।
krodhasya vaśamāgamya dharmo na rakṣitastvayā ।।

rājovāca

na bhakṣitā me dayitā śvāpadaiḥ sā hi jīvati ।
avidūṣitacāritrā kathametatkaromyaham ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

yadi jīvati te bhāryā na caiva vyabhicāriṇī ।
tadapatnīkatājanma kiṃ pāpaṃ kriyate tvayā ।।

rājovāca

ānītāpi hi sā vipra ! pratikūlā sadaiva me ।
duḥ khāya na sukhāyālaṃ tasyā maitrī na vai mayi ।
tathā tvaṃ kuru yatnaṃ me yathā sā vaśagāminī ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca

tava saṃprītaye tasyā vareṣṭirupakāriṇī ।
kriyate mitrakāmairyā mitravindāṃ karomi tām ।।
aprītayoḥ prītikaro sā hi saṃjananī param ।
bhāryāpatyormanuṣyendra ! tāntaveṣṭiṃ karomyaham ।।
yatra tiṣṭhati sā subhrūstava bhāryā mahīpate ।
tasmādānoyatāṃ sā te parāṃ prītimupaiṣyati ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityuktaḥ sa tu sambhārānaśeṣānavanīpatiḥ ।
ānināya cakāreṣṭiṃ sa ca tāṃ dvijasattamaḥ ।।
saptakṛtvaḥ sa tu tadā cakāreṣṭiṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।
tasya rājño dvijaśreṣṭho bhāryāsampādanāya vai ।।
yadāropitamaitrīntāmamanyata mahāmuniḥ ।
svabhartari tadā viprastamuvāca narādhipam ।।
ānīyatāṃ naraśreṣṭha ! yā taveṣṭātmano antikam ।
bhuṅkṣva bhogāṃstayā sārdhaṃ yaja yajñāṃstathādṛtaḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityuktastena vipreṇa bhūpālo vismitastadā ।
sasmāra taṃ mahāvīryaṃ satyasandhaṃ niśācaram ।।
smṛtastena tadā sadyaḥ samupetya narādhipam ।
kiṃ karomīti so apyāha praṇipatya mahāmune ।।
tatastena narendreṇa vistareṇa nivedite ।
gatvā pātālamādāya rājapatnīmupāyayau ।।
ānītā cātihārdena sā dadarśa tadā patim ।
uvāca ca prasīdeti bhūyobhūyo mudānvitā ।।
tataḥ sa rājā rabhasā pariṣvajyāha māninīm ।
priye ! prasanna evāhaṃ bhūyo apyevaṃ bravīṣi kim ।।

patnyuvāca

yadi prisādapravaṇaṃ narendra ! mayi te manaḥ ।
tadetadabhiyāce tvāṃ tat kuruṣva mamārhaṇam ।।

rājovāca

niḥ śaṅkaṃ brūhi matto yadbhavātyā kiñcidīpsitam ।
tadalabhyaṃ na te bhīru ! tavāyatto asmi nānyathā ।।

patnyuvāca

madarthaṃ tena nāgena sutā śaptā sakhī mama ।
mūkā bhaviṣyasītyāha sā ca mūkatvamāgatā ।।
tasyāḥ pratikriyāṃ prītyā mama śaknoti cedbhavān ।
vāgvighātapraśāntyarthaṃ tataḥ kiṃ na kṛtaṃ mama ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ sa rājā taṃ vipramāhāsmin kīdṛśī kriyā ।
tanmūkatāpanodāya sa ca taṃ prāha pārthivam ।।

brāhmaṇa uvāca
bhūpa ! sārasvatīmiṣṭiṃ karomi vacanāttava ।
patnī taveyamānṛṇyaṃ yātu tadvākpravartanāt ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

iṣṭiṃ sārasvatīṃ cakre tadarthaṃ sa dvijottamaḥ ।
sārasvatāni sūktāni jajāpa ca samāhitaḥ ।।
tataḥ pravṛttavākyāntāṃ gargaḥ prāha rasātale ।
upakāraḥ sakhībhartrā kṛto ayamatiduṣkaraḥ ।।
itthaṃ jñānaṃ samāsādya nandā śīghragatiḥ puram ।
tato rājñīṃ pariṣvajya svasakhīmuragātmajā ।।
tañca saṃstūya bhūpālaṃ kalyāṇoktyā punaḥ punaḥ ।
uvāca madhuraṃ nāgī kṛtāsanaparigrahā ।।
upakāraḥ kṛto vīra ! bhavatā yo mamādhunā ।
tenāsmyākṛṣṭahṛdayā yadbravīmi śṛṇuṣva tat ।।
tava putro mahāvīryo bhaviṣyati narādhipa ।
tasmāpratihataṃ cakramasyāṃ bhuvi bhaviṣyati ।।
sarvārthaśāstratattvajño dharmānuṣṭhānatatparaḥ ।
manvantareśvaro dhīmān ! bhaviṣyati sa vai manuḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

iti datvā varaṃ tasmai nāgarājasutā tataḥ ।
sakhīṃ tāṃ saṃpariṣvajya pātālamagamanmune ।।
tatra tasya tayā sārdhaṃ ramataḥ pṛthivīpateḥ ।
jagāma kālaḥ sumahān prajāḥ pālayatastathā ।।
tataḥ sa tasyāntanayo jajñe rājño mahātmanaḥ ।
paurṇamāsyāṃ yathā kāntaścandraḥ saṃpūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।।
tasmin jāte mudaṃ prāpuḥ prajāḥ sarvā mahātmani ।
devadundubhayo neduḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiḥ papāta ca ।।
tasya dṛṣṭvā vapuḥ kāntaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ śīlameva ca ।
auttamaśceti munayo nāma cakruḥ samāgatāḥ ।।
jāto ayamuttame vaṃśe tatra kāle tathottame ।
uttamāvayavastena auttamo ayaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

uttamasya sutaḥ so atha nāmnā khyātastathauttamaḥ ।
manurāsīttatprabhāvo bhāgure śrūyatāṃ mama ।।
uttamākhyānamakhilaṃ janma caivottamasya ca ।
nityaṃ śṛṇoti vidveṣaṃ sa kadācinna gacchati ।।
iṣṭairdāraistathā putrairbandhubhirvā kadācana ।
viyogo nāsya bhavitā śṛṇvataḥ paṭhato api vā ।।
tasya manvantaraṃ brahman ! vadato me niśāmaya ।
śrūyatāṃ tatra yaścendro ye ca devāstatharṣayaḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe auttamamanvantare dvisaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

trisaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

manvantare tṛtīye asmin auttamasya prajāpateḥ ।
devānindramṛṣīn bhūpān nibodha gadato mama ।।
svadhāmānastathā devā yathānāmānukāriṇaḥ ।
satyākhyaśca dvitīyo anyastridaśānāṃ tathā gaṇaḥ ।।
tṛtīye tu gaṇe devāḥ śivākhyā munisattama ।
śivāḥ svarūpataste tu śrutāḥ pāpapraṇāśanāḥ ।।
pratardanākhyaśca gaṇo devānāṃ munisattama ।
caturthastatra kathita auttamasyāntare manoḥ ।।
vaśavartinaḥ pañcame api devāstatra gaṇe dvija ।
yathākhyātasvarūpāstu sarva eva mahāmune ।।
ete devagaṇāḥ pañca smṛtā yajñabhujastathā ।
manvantare manuśreṣṭhe sarve dvādaśakā gaṇāḥ ।।
teṣāmindro mahābhāgastrailokye sa gururbhavet ।
śataṃ kratūnāmāhṛtya suśāntirnāma nāmataḥ ।।
yasyopasarganāśāya nāmākṣaravibhūṣitā ।
adyāpi mānavairgāthā gīyate tu mahītale ।।
śuśāntirdevarāṭ kāntaḥ śuśāntiṃ sa prayacchati ।
sahitaḥ śivasatyādyaistathaiva vaśavartibhiḥ ।।
ajaḥ paraśucirdivyo mahābalaparākramaḥ ।
putrastasya manorāsan vikhyātāstridaśopamāḥ ।।
tatsūtisambhavairbhūmiḥ pālitābhūnnareśvaraiḥ ।
yāvanmanvantara tasya manoruttamatejasaḥ ।।
caturyugānāṃ saṃkhyātā sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ ।
kṛtatretādisaṃjñānāṃ yānyuktāni yuge mayā ।।
svatejasā hi tapaso variṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ ।
tanayāścāntare tasmin sapta saptarṣayo abhavan ।।
tṛtīyametatkathitaṃ tava manvantaraṃ mayā ।
tāmasasya caturthantu manorantaramucyate ।।
viyonijanmano yasya yaśasā dyotitaṃ jagat ।
janma tasya manorbrahman ! śruyatāṃ gadato mama ।।
atīndriyamaśeṣāṇāṃ manūnāñcaritantathā ।
tathā janmāpi vijñeyaṃ prabhāvaśca mahātmanām ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe auttamamanvantare trisaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

catuḥ saptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

rājābhūd vikhyātaḥ svarāṣṭro nāma vīryavān ।
anekayajñakṛt prājñaḥ saṃgrāmeṣvaparājitaḥ ।।
tasyāyuḥ sumahatprādāt mantriṇārādhito raviḥ ।
patnīnāñca śatantasya dhanyānāmabhavad dvija ।।
tasya dīrghāyuṣaḥ patnyo nātidīrghāyuṣo mune ।
kālena jagmurnidhanaṃ bhṛtyamantrijanāstathā ।।
sa bhāryābhistathāyukto bhṛtyaiśca sahajanmabhiḥ ।
udvignacetāḥ saṃprāpa vīryahānimaharniśam ।।
taṃ vīryahīnaṃ nibhṛtairbhṛtyaistyaktaṃ suduḥ khitam ।
anantaro vimardākhyo rājyāccyāvitavāṃstadā ।।
rājyāccyutaḥ so api vanaṃ gatvā nirviṇṇamānasaḥ ।
tapastepe mahābhāge vitastāpuline sthitaḥ ।।
grīṣme pañcatamā bhūtvā varṣāsvabhrāvakāśikaḥ ।
jalaśāyī ca śiśire nirāhāro yatavrataḥ ।।
tatastapasyatastasya prāvṛṭkāle mahāplavaḥ ।
babhūvānudinaṃ meghairvarṣadbhiranusantatam ।।
na digvijñāyate pūrvā dakṣiṇā vā na paścimā ।
nottarā tamasā sarvamanuliptamivābhavat ।।
tato atipūreṇa nṛpaḥ sa nadyāḥ preritastaṭam ।
prārthayannāpi nāvāpa hriyamāṇo mahīpatiḥ ।।
atha dūre jalaughena hriyamāṇo mahīpatiḥ ।
āsasāda jale rauhīṃ sa pucche jagṛhe ca tām ।।
tena plavena sa yayāvūhyamāno mahītale ।
itaścetaścāndhakāre āsasāda taṭantataḥ ।।
vistāri paṅkamatyarthaṃ dustaraṃ sa nṛpastaran ।
tathaiva kṛṣyamāṇo anyadramyaṃ vanamavāpa saḥ ।।
tatrāndhakāre sā rauhī cakarṣa vasudhādhipam ।
pucche lagnaṃ mahābhāgaṃ kṛśaṃ dhamanisantatau ।।
tasyāśca sparśasaṃbhūtāmavāpamudamuttamām ।
so andhakāre bhraman bhūyo madanākṛṣṭamānasaḥ ।।
vijñāya sānurāgaṃ taṃ pṛṣṭhasparśanatatparam ।
narendraṃ tadvanasyāntaḥ sā mṛgī tamuvāca ha ।।
kiṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ vepathumatā kareṇa spṛśase mama ।
anyathaivāsya kāryasya sañjātā nṛpate gatiḥ ।।
nāsthāne vo mano yātaṃ nāgamyāhaṃ taveśvara ।
kintu tvatsaṅgame vighnameṣa lolaḥ karoti me ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

iti śrutvā vacastasyā mṛgyāśca jagatīpatiḥ ।
jātakautūhalo rauhīmidaṃ vacanamabravīt ।।
kā tvaṃ brūhi mṛgī vākyaṃ kathaṃ mānuṣavadvadet ।
kaścaiva lolo yo vighnaṃ tvatsaṅge kurute mama ।।

mṛgyuvāca

ahante dayitā bhūpa ! prāgāsamutpalāvatī ।
bharyā śatāgramahiṣī duhitā dṛḍhadhanvanaḥ ।।

rājovāca

kintu yāvat kṛtaṃ karma yenemāṃ yonimāgatā ।
pativratā dharmaparā sā cetthaṃ sathamīdṛśī ।।

mṛgyuvāca

ahaṃ pitṛgṛhe bālā sakhībhiḥ sahitā vanam ।
rantuṃ gatā dadarśaikaṃ mṛgaṃ mṛgyā samāgatam ।।
tataḥ samīpavartinyā mayā sā tāḍitā mṛgī ।
mayā trastā gatānyatra kruddhaḥ prāha tato mṛgaḥ ।।
mūḍhe kimevaṃ mattāsi dhikte dauḥ śīlyamīdṛśam ।
ādhānakālo yenāyaṃ tvayā me viphalīkṛtaḥ ।।
vācaṃ śrutvā tatastasya mānuṣasyeva bhāṣataḥ ।
bhītā tamabruvaṃ ko asītyetāṃ yonimupāgataḥ ।।
tataḥ sa prāha putro ahamṛṣernirvṛticakṣuṣaḥ ।
sutapā nāma mṛgyāntu sābhilāṣo mṛgo abhavam ।।
imāñcānugataḥ premṇā vāñchitaścānayā vane ।
tvayā viyojitā duṣṭe tasmācchāpaṃ dadāmi te ।।
mayā coktaṃ tavājñānādaparādhaḥ kṛto mune ।
prasādaṃ kuru śāpaṃ me na bhavān dātumarhati ।।
ityuktaḥ prāha māṃ so api muniritthaṃ mahīpate ।
na prayacchāmi śāpaṃ te yadyātmānaṃ dadāsi me ।।
mayā coktaṃ mṛgī nāhaṃ mṛgarūpadharā vane ।
lapsyase anyāṃ mṛgīntāvanmayi bhāvo nivartyatām ।।
ityuktaḥ koparaktākṣaḥ sa prāha sphuritādharaḥ ।
nāhaṃ mṛgī tvayetyuktaṃ mṛgī mūḍhe bhaviṣyasi ।।
tato bhṛśaṃ pravyathitā praṇamya munimabruvam ।
svarūpasthamatikruddhaṃ prasīdeti punaḥ punaḥ ।।
bālānabhaijñā vākyānāṃ tataḥ proktamidaṃ mayā ।
pitaryasati nārībhirvriyate hi patiḥ svayam ।।
sati tāte kathañcāhaṃ vṛṇomi munisattama ।
sāparādhāthavā pādau prasīdeśa namāmyaham ।।
prasīdeti prasīdeti praṇatāyā mahāmate ।
itthaṃ lālapyamānāyāḥ sa prāha munipuṅgavaḥ ।।
na bhavatyanyathā proktaṃ mama vākyaṃ kadācana ।
mṛgī bhaviṣyasi mṛtā vane asminneva janmani ।।
mṛgatve ca mahābāhustava garbhamupaiṣyati ।
lolo nāma muneḥ putraḥ siddhavīryasya bhāmini ।।
jītismarā bhavitrī tvaṃ tasmin garbhamupāgate ।
smṛtiṃ prāpya tathā vācaṃ mānuṣīmīrayiṣyasi ।।
tsamin jāte mṛgītvāt tvaṃ vimuktā patinārcitā ।
lokānavāpsyasi prāpyā ye na duṣkṛtakarmabhiḥ ।।
so api lolo mahāvīryaḥ pitṛśatrūn nipātya vai ।
jitvā vasundarāṃ kṛtstrāṃ bhaviṣyati tato manuḥ ।।
evaṃ śāpamahaṃ labdhvā mṛtā tiryaktvamāgatā ।
tvatsaṃsparśācca garbho asau saṃbhūto jaṭhare mama ।।
ato bravīmi nāsthāne tava yātaṃ mano mayi ।
na cāpyagamyā garbhastho lolo vighnaṃ karotyasau ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evamuktastataḥ so api rājā prāpya parāṃ mudam ।
putro mamārīñjitveti pṛthivyāṃ bhavitā manuḥ ।।
tatastaṃ suṣuve putraṃ sā mṛgī lakṣaṇānvitam ।
tasmin jāte ca bhūtāni sarvāṇi prayayurmudam ।।
viśeṣataśca rājāsau putre jāte mahābale ।
sā vimuktā mṛgī śāpāt prāpa lokānanuttamān ।।
tatastasyarṣayaḥ sarve sametya munisattama ।
avekṣya bhāvinīmṛddhiṃ nāma cakrurmahātmanaḥ ।।
tāmasīṃ bhajamānāyāṃ yoniṃ mātaryajāyata ।
tamasā cāvṛte loke tāmaso ayaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।
tataḥ sa tāmasastena pitrā saṃvardhito vane ।
jātabuddhiruvācedaṃ pitaraṃ munisattama ।।
kastvaṃ tāta kathaṃ vāhaṃ putro mātā ca kā mama ।
kimarthamāgataśca tvametat satyaṃ bravīhi me ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ pitā yathāvṛttaṃ svarājyacyāvanādikam ।
tasyācaṣṭe mahābahuḥ putrasya jagatīpatiḥ ।।
śrutvā tat sakalaṃ so api samārādhya ca bhāraskaram ।
avāca divyānyastrāṇi sasaṃhārāṇyaśeṣataḥ ।।
kṛtāstrastānarīn jitvā piturānīya cāntikam ।
anujñātān munocātha tena svaṃ dharmamāsthitaḥ ।।
pitāpi tasya svān lokāṃstapoyajñasamārjitān ।
visṛṣṭadehaḥ saṃprāpto dṛṣṭvā putramukhaṃ sukham ।।
jitvā samastāṃ pṛthivīṃ tāmasākhyaḥ sa pārthivaḥ ।
tāmasākhyo manurabhuttasya manvantaraṃ śṛṇu ।।
ye devā yatpatiryaśca devendro ye tatharṣayaḥ ।
ye putrāśca manostasya pṛthivīparipālakāḥ ।।
satyāstathānye sudhiyaḥ surūpā harayastathā ।
ete devagaṇāstatra saptaviṃśatikā mune ।।
mahābalo mahāvīryaḥ śatayajñopalakṣitaḥ ।
śikhirindrastathā teṣāṃ devānāmabhavadvibhuḥ ।।
jyotirdharmā pṛthuḥ kāvyaścaitro agnirvalakastathā ।
pīvaraśca tathā brahman ! sapta gaptarṣayo abhavan ।।
naraḥ kṣāntiḥ śāntadāntajānujaṅghādayastathā ।
putrāstu tāmasasyāsan rājānaḥ sumahābalāḥ ।।
ityetattāmasaṃ vipra manvantaramudāhṛtam ।
yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyādvāpi tamasā sana bādhyate ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇeṭhatāmasamanvantare' catuḥ saptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

pañcasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

pañcamo api manurbrahman raivato nāma viśrutaḥ ।
tasyotpattiṃ vistaraśaḥ śṛṇuṣva kathayāmi te ।।
ṛṣirāsīnmahābhāga ṛtavāgiti viśrutaḥ ।
tasyāputrasya putro abhūdrevatyante mahātmanaḥ ।।
sa tasya vidhivaccakre jātakarmādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।
tathopanayanādīṃśca sa cāśīlo abhavanmune ।।
yataḥ prabhṛti jāto asau tataḥ prabhṛti so apyṛṣiḥ ।
dīrgharogaparāmarśamavāpa munipuṅgavaḥ ।।
mātā tasya parāmārti kuṣṭharogādipīḍitā ।
jagāma sa pitā cāsya cintayāmāsa duḥ khitaḥ ।।
kimetaditi so apyasya putro apyatyantadurmatiḥ ।
jagrāha bhāryāmanyasya muniputrasya saṃmukhīm ।।
tato viṣaṇṇamanasā ṛtavāgidamuktavān ।
aputratā manuṣyāṇāṃ śreyase na kuputratā ।।
kuputro hṛdayāyāsaṃ sarvadā kurute pituḥ ।
mātuśca svargasaṃsthāṃśca svapitṝn pātayatyadhaḥ ।।
suhṛdāṃ nopakārāya pitṝṇāñca na tṛptaye ।
pitrorduḥ khāya dhig janma tasya duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ ।।
dhanyāste tanayā yeṣāṃ sarvalokābhisaṃmatāḥ ।
paropakāriṇaḥ śāntāḥ sādhukarmaṇyanuvratāḥ ।।
anirvṛtaṃ tathā mandaṃ paralokaparāṅmukham ।
narakāya na sadgatyai kuputrālambi janmanaḥ ।।
karoti suhṛdāṃ dainyamahitānāṃ tathā mudam ।
akāle ca jarāṃ pitroḥ kuputraḥ kurute dhruvam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evaṃ so atyantaduṣṭasya putrasya caritairmuniḥ ।
dahyamānamanovṛttirvṛttaṃ gargamapṛcchata ।।

ṛtavāguvāca

suvratena purā vedā gṛhītā vidhivanmayā ।
samapya vedān vidhivat kṛto dāraparigrahaḥ ।।
sadāreṇa kriyāḥ kāryāḥ śrautāḥ smārtā vaṣaṭkriyāḥ ।
na me nyūnāḥ kṛtāḥ kāścidyāvadadya mahāmune ।।
garbhādhānavidhānena na kāmamanurudhyatā ।
putrārthaṃ janitaścāyaṃ punnāmno bibhyatā mune ।।
so ayaṃ kimātmadoṣeṇa mama doṣaṇa vā mune ।
asmadduḥ khavaho jāto dauḥ śīlyād bandhuśokadaḥ ।।
revatyante muniśreṣṭha ! jāto ayaṃ tanayastava ।
tena duḥ khāya te duṣṭe kāle yasmādajāyata ।।
na te apacāro naivāsya māturnāyaṃ kulasya te ।
tasya dauḥ śīlyahetustu revatyantamupāgatam ।।

ṛtavāguvāca

yasmānmamaikaputrasya revatyantasamudbhavam ।
dauḥ śīlyametat sā tasmāt patatāmāśu revatī ।।
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tenaivaṃ vyāhṛte śāpe revatyṛkṣaṃ papāta ha ।
paśyataḥ sarvalokasya vismayāviṣṭacetasaḥ ।।
revatyṛkṣañca patitaṃ kumudādrau samantataḥ ।
bhāvayāmāsa sahasā vanakandaranirjharam ।।
kumudādriśca tatpātāt khyāto raivatako abhavat ।
atīva ramyaḥ sarvasyāṃ pṛthivyāṃ pṛthivīdharaḥ ।।
tasyarkṣasya tu yā kāntirjātā paṅkajinī saraḥ ।
tato jajñe tadā kanyā rūpeṇātīva śobhanā ।।
revatīkāntisambhūtāṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā pramuco muniḥ ।
tasyā nāma cakāretthaṃ revatī nāma bhāgure ।।
poṣayāmāsa caivaitāṃ svāśramābhyāsasambhavām ।
pramucaḥ sa mahābhāgastasminneva mahācale ।।
tāntu yauvaninīṃ dṛṣṭvā kānyakāṃ rūpaśālinīm ।
sa muniścintamāmāsa ko asyā bhartā bhavediti ।।
evaṃ cintayatastasya yayau kālo mahān mune ।
na cāsasāda sadṛśaṃ varaṃ tasyā mahāmuniḥ ।।
tatastasyā varaṃ praṣṭumagniṃ sa pramuco muniḥ ।
viveśa vahniśālāṃ vai praṣṭāraṃ prāha havyabhuk ।।
mahābalo mahāvīryaḥ priyavāg dharmavatsalaḥ ।
durgamo nāma bhavitā bhartā hyasya mahīpatiḥ ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

anantarañca mṛgayāprasaṅgenāgato mune ।
tasyāśramapadaṃ dhīmān durgamaḥ sa narādhipaḥ ।।
priyavratānvayabhavo mahābalaparākramaḥ ।
putro vikramaśīlasya kālindījaṭharodbhavaḥ ।।
sa praviśyāśramapadaṃ tāṃ tanvīṃ jagatīpatiḥ ।
apaśyamānastamṛṣiṃ priyetyāmantrya pṛṣṭavān ।।

rājovāca

kva gato bhagavānasmādāśramānmunipuṅgavaḥ ।
taṃ praṇetumihecchāmi tat tvaṃ prabrūhi śobhane ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
agnisālāṃ gato viprastacchrutvā tasya bhāṣitam ।
priyetyāmantraṇañcaiva niścakrāma tvarānvitaḥ ।।
sa dadarśa mahātmānaṃ rājānaṃ durgamaṃ muniḥ ।
narendracihnasahitaṃ praśrayāvanataṃ puraḥ ।।
tasmin dṛṣṭe tataḥ śiṣyamuvāca sa tu gautamam ।
gautamānīyatāṃ śīghramargho asya jagatīpateḥ ।।
ekastāvadayaṃ bhūpaścirakālādupāgataḥ
jāmātā ca viśeṣeṇa yogyor'ghasya mato mama ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ sa cintayāmāsa rājā jāmātṛkāraṇam ।
viveda ca na tanmaunī jagṛher'ghañca taṃ nṛpaḥ ।।
tamāsanagataṃ vipro gṛhītārghaṃ mahāmuniḥ ।
svāgataṃ prāha rājendramapi te kuśalaṃ gṛhe ।।
koṣe bale atha mitreṣu bhṛtyāmātye nareśvara ।
tathātmani mahābāho yatra sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।
patnī ca te kuśalinī yata evānutiṣṭhati ।
pṛcchāmyasyāstato nāhaṃ kuśalinyo aparāstava ।।

rājovāca

tvatprasādādakuśalaṃ na kvacinmama suvrata ।
jātakautūhalaścāsmi mama bhāryātra kā mune ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

revatī sumahābhāgā trailokyasyāpi sundarī ।
tava bharyā varārohā tāṃ tvaṃ rājanna vetsi kim ।।

rājovāca

subhadrāṃ śāntatanayāṃ kāverītanayāṃ vibho ।
surāṣṭrajāṃ sujātāñca kadambāñca varūthajām ।।
vipāṭhāṃ nandinīñcaiva vedmi bhāryāṃ gṛhe dvija ।
tiṣṭhanti me na bhagavan revatīṃ vedmi kānviyam ।।

ṛṣiruvāca
priyeti sāmprataṃ yeyaṃ tvayoktā varavarṇinī ।
kiṃ vismṛtante bhūpāla ! ślāghyeyaṃ gṛhiṇī tava ।।

rājovāca

satyamuktaṃ mayā kintu bhāvo duṣṭo na me mune ।
nātra kopaṃ bhavān kartumarhatyasmāsu yācitaḥ ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

tattvaṃ bravīṣi bhūpāla ! na bhāvastava dūṣitaḥ ।
vyājahāra bhavānetadvahninā nṛpa coditaḥ ।।
mayā pṛṣṭo hutavahaḥ ko asyā bharteti pārthiva ।
bhavitā tena cāpyukto bhavānevādya vai varaḥ ।।
tadgṛhyatāṃ mayā dattā tubhyaṃ kanyā narādhipa ।
priyetyāmantritā ceyaṃ vicāraṃ kuruṣe katham ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tato asāvabhavanmaunī tenoktaḥ pṛthivīpatiḥ ।
ṛṣistathodyataḥ kartuṃ tasyā vaivāhikaṃ vidhim ।।
tamudyataṃ sā pitaraṃ vivāhāya mahāmune ।
uvāca kanyā yatkiñcit praśrayāvanatānanā ।।
yadi me prītimāṃstāta prisādaṃ kartumarhasi ।
revatyṛkṣe vivāhaṃ me tatkarotu prasāditaḥ ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

revatyṛkṣaṃ na vai bhadre candrayogi vyavasthitam ।
anyāni santi ṛkṣāṇi subhru vaivāhikāni te ।।

kanyovāca

tāta tena vinā kālo viphalaḥ pratibhāti me ।
vivāho viphale kāle madvidhāyāḥ kathaṃ bhavet ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

ṛtavāgiti vikhyātastapasvī revatīṃ prati ।
cakāra kopaṃ kruddhena tenarkṣaṃ vinipātitam ।।
mayā cāsmai pratijñātā bharyeti madirekṣaṇā ।
na cecchasi vivāhaṃ tvaṃ saṅkaṭaṃ naḥ samāgatam ।।

kanyovāca

ṛtavāk sa munistāta kimevaṃ taptavāṃstapaḥ ।
na tvayā mama tātena brahmabandhoḥ sutāsmi kim ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

brahmabandhoḥ sutā na tvaṃ bāle naiva tapasvinaḥ ।
sutā tvaṃ mama yo devān kartumanyān samutsahe ।।

kanyovāca

tapasvī yadi me tātastatkimṛkṣamidaṃ divi ।
samāropya vivāho me tadṛkṣe kriyate na tu ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

evaṃ bhavatu bhadrante bhadre prītimatī bhava ।
āropayāmīndumārge revatyṛkṣaṃ kṛte tava ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tatastapaḥ prabhāveṇa revatyṛkṣaṃ mahāmuniḥ ।
yathāpūrvantathā cakre somayogi dvijottama ।।
vivāhañcaiva duhiturvidhivad mantrayoginam ।
niṣpādya prītimān bhūyo jāmātāramathābravīt ।।
audvāhikante bhūpāla kathyatāṃ kiṃ dadāmyaham ।
durlabhyamapi dāsyāmi mamāpratihatantapaḥ ।।

rājovāca

manoḥ svayambhuvasyāhamutpannaḥ santatau mune ।
manvantarādhipaṃ putraṃ tvatprasādād vṛṇomyaham ।।
ṛṣiruvāca

bhaviṣyatyeṣa te kāmo manustvattanayo mahīm ।
sakalāṃ bhokṣyate bhūpa dharmavicca bhaviṣyati ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tāmādāya tato bhūpaḥ svameva nagaraṃ yayau ।
tasmādajāyata suto revatyā raivato manuḥ ।।
sametaḥ sakalairdharmairmānavairaparājitaḥ ।
vijñātākhilaśāstrārtho vedavidyārthaśāstravit ।।
tasya manvantare devān munidevendrapārthivān ।
kathyamānān mayā brahman nibodha susamāhitaḥ ।।
sumedhasastatra devāstathā bhūpatayo dvija ।
vaikuṇṭhaścāmitābhaśca caturdaśa caturdaśa ।।
teṣāṃ devagaṇānāntu caturṇāmapi ceścaraḥ ।
nāmnā vibhurabhūdindraḥ śatayajñopalakṣakaḥ ।।
hiraṇyalomā vedaśrīrūrdhvabāhustathāparaḥ ।
vedabāhuḥ sudhāmā ca parjanyaśca mahāmuniḥ ।।
vasiṣṭhaśca mahābhāgo vedavedāntapāragaḥ ।
ete saptarṣayaścāsan raivatasyāntare manoḥ ।।
balabandhurmahāvīryaḥ suyaṣṭavyastathāparaḥ ।
satyakādyāstathaivāsan raivatasya manoḥ sutāḥ ।।
raivatāntāstu manavaḥ kathitā ye mayā tava ।
svāyambhuvāśrayā hyete svārociṣamṛte manum ।।
(ya eṣāṃ śṛṇuyānnityaṃ paṭhedākhyānamuttamam ।
vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo lokaṃ prāpnotyabhīpsitam ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe raivatamanvantare pañcasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

ṣaṭsaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityetat kathitaṃ tubhyaṃ pañca manvantaraṃ tava ।
cākṣuṣasya manoḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ śrūyatāmidamantaram ।।
anyajanmani jāto asau cakṣuṣaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ ।
cākṣuṣatvamatastasya janmanyasminnapi dvija ।।
jātaṃ mātā nijotsaṅge sthitamullāpya taṃ punaḥ ।
pariṣvajati hārdena punarullāpayatyatha ।।
jātismaraḥ sa jāto vai māturutsaṅgamāsthitaḥ ।
jahāsa taṃ tadā mātā saṃkruddhā vākyamabravīt ।।
bhītāsmi kimidaṃ vatsa ! hāso yadvadane tava ।
akālabodhaḥ sañjātaḥ kaccit paśyasi śobhanam ।।

putra uvāca

māmattumicchati puro mārjārī kima na paśyasi ।
antardhānagatā ceyaṃ dvitīyā jātahāriṇī ।।
putraprītyā ca bhavatī sahārdā māmavekṣatī ।
ullāpyollāpya bahuśaḥ pariṣvajati māṃ yataḥ ।।
udbhūtapulakā snehasambhavāstrāvilekṣaṇā ।
tato mamāgato hāsaḥ śṛṇu cāpyatra kāraṇam ।।
svārthe prasaktā mārjārī prasaktaṃ māmavekṣate ।
tathāntardhānagā caiva dvitīyā jātahāriṇī ।।
svārthāya snigdhahṛdayā yathaivaite mamopari ।
pravṛtte svārthamāsthāya tathaiva pratibhāsi me ।।
kintu madupabhogāya mārjārī jātahāriṇī ।
tvantu krameṇopabhogyaṃ mattaḥ phalamabhīpsasi ।।
na māṃ jānāsi ko apyeṣa na caivāpakṛtaṃ mayā ।
saṅgataṃ nātikālīnaṃ pañcasaptadinātmakam ।।
tathāpi strihyase sāstrā pariṣvajasi cāpyati ।
tāteti vatsa ! bhadreti nirvyalīkaṃ bravīṣi mām ।।

mātovāca
na tvāhamupakārārthaṃ vatsa ! prītyā pariṣvaje ।
na cedetadbhavatprītyai parityaktāsmyahaṃ tvayā ।।
svārtho mayā parityakto yastvatto me bhaviṣyati ।
ityuktvā sā tamutsṛjya niṣkrāntā sūtikāgṛhāt ।।
jaḍāṅgabāhyakaraṇaṃ śuddhāntaḥ karaṇātmakam ।
jahāra taṃ parityaktaṃ sā tadā jātahāriṇī ।।
sā hṛtvā taṃ tadā bālaṃ vikrāntasya mahībhṛtaḥ ।
prasūtapatnīśayane nyasya tasyādade sutam ।।
tamapyanyagṛhe nītvā gṛhītvā tasya cātmajam ।
tṛtīyaṃ bhakṣayāmāsa sā kramājjātahāriṇī ।।
hṛtvā hṛtvā tṛtīyantu bhakṣayatyatinirghṛṇā ।
karotyanudinaṃ sā nu parivartantathānyayoḥ ।।
vikrānto api tatastasya sutasyaiva mahīpatiḥ ।
kārayāmāsa saṃskārān rājanyasya bhavanti ye ।।
ānandeti ca nāmāsya pitā cakre vidhānataḥ ।
mudā paramayā yukto vikrāntaḥ sa narādhipaḥ ।।
kṛtopanayanaṃ tantu gururāha kumārakam ।
jananyāḥ prāgupasthānaṃ kriyatāñcābhivādanam ।।
sa gurostadvacaḥ śrutvā vihasyaivamathābravīt ।
vandyā me katamā mātā jananī pālanī nu kim ।।

gururuvāca

na tviyaṃ te mahābhāga ! janayitrī ruthātmajā ।
vikrāntasyāgramahiṣī haiminī nāma nāmataḥ ।।

ānanda uvāca

iyaṃ janitrī caitrasya viśālagramavāsinaḥ ।
viprāgryabodhaputrasya yo asyāṃ jāto anyato vacam ।।

gururuvāca

kutastvaṃ kathayānanda ! caitraḥ ko vā tvayocyate ।
saṅkaṭaṃ mahadābhāti kva jāto atra bravīṣi kim ।।

ānanda uvāca

jāto ahamavanīndrasya kṣatriyasya gṛhe dvija ।
tatpatnyāṃ giribhadrāyāmādade jātahāriṇī ।।
tayātra mukto haiminyā gṛhītvā ca sutañca sā ।
bodhasya dvijamukhyasya gṛhe nītavatī punaḥ ।।
bhakṣayāmāsa ca sutaṃ tasya bodhadvijanmanaḥ ।
sa tatra dvijasaṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛto haiminīsutaḥ ।।
vayamatra mahābhāga ! saṃskṛtā guruṇā tvayā ।
mayā tava vacaḥ kāryamupaimi katamāṃ guro ।।

gururuvāca

atīva gahanaṃ vatsa ! saṅkaṭaṃ mahadāgatam ।
na vedmi kiñcinmohena bhramantīva hi buddhayaḥ ।।

ānanda uvāca

mohasyāvasaraḥ ko atra jagatyevaṃ vyavasthite ।
kaḥ kasya putro viprarṣe ! ko vā kasya nu bāndhavaḥ ।।
ārabhya janmano nṝṇāṃ sambandhitvamupaiti yaḥ ।
anye sambandhino vipra ! mṛtyunā sannivartitāḥ ।।
atrāpi jātasya sataḥ sambandhoyo asya bāndhavaiḥ ।
so apyastaṅgate dehe prayātyeṣo akhilakramaḥ ।।
ato bravīmi saṃsāre vasataḥ ko na bāndhavaḥ ।
ko vāpi satataṃ bandhuḥ kiṃ vo vibhrāmyate matiḥ ।।
pitṛdvayaṃ mayā prāptamasminneva hi janmani ।
mātṛdvayañca kiñcitraṃ yadanyad dehasambhave ।।
so ahaṃ tapaḥ kariṣyāmi tvayā yo hyasya bhūpateḥ ।
viśālagrāmataḥ putraścaitra ānīyatāmiha ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ sa vismito rājā sabhāryaḥ saha bandhubhiḥ ।
tasmānnivartya mamatāmanumene vanāya tam ।।
caitramānīya tanayaṃ rājyayogyaṃ cakāra saḥ ।
saṃmānya brāhmaṇaṃ yena putrabuddhyā sa pālitaḥ ।।
so apyānandastapastepe bāla eva mahāvane ।
karmaṇāṃ kṣupaṇārthāya vimukteḥ paripanthinām ।।
tapasyantaṃ tatastañca prāha devaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
kimarthaṃ tapyase vatsa ! tapastīvraṃ vadasva tat ।।

ānanda uvāca

ātmanaḥ śuddhikāmo ahaṃ karomi bhagavaṃstapaḥ ।
bandhāya mama karmāṇi yāni tatkṣapaṇonmukhaḥ ।।

brahmovāca

kṣīṇādhikāro bhavati muktiyogyo na karmavān ।
sattvādhikāravān muktimavāpsyati tato bhavān ।।
bhavatā manunā bhāvyaṃ ṣaṣṭhena vraja tat kuru ।
alante tapasā tasmin kṛte muktimavāpsyasi ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityukto brahmaṇā so api tathetyuktvā mahāmatiḥ ।
tatkarmābhimukho yātastapaso virarāma ha ।।
cākṣuṣetyāha taṃ brahmā tapaso vinivartayan ।
pūrvanāmnā babhūvātha prakhyātaścākṣuṣo manuḥ ।।
upayeme vidarbhāṃ sa sutāmugrasya bhūbhṛtaḥ ।
tasyāñcotpādayāmāsa putrān prakhyātavikramān ।।
tasya manvantareśasya ye antare tridaśā dvija ।
ye carṣayastathaivendro ye sutāścāsya tān śṛṇu ।।
āpyā nāma surāstatra teṣāmeko aṣṭako gaṇaḥ ।
prakhyātakarmaṇāṃ vipra ! yajñe havyabhujāmayam ।।
prakhyātabalavīryāṇāṃ prabhāmaṇḍaladurdṛśām ।
dvitīyaśca prasūtākhyo devānāmaṣṭako gaṇaḥ ।।
tathaivāṣṭaka evānyo bhavyākhyo devatāgaṇaḥ ।
caturthaśca gaṇastatra yūthagākhyastathāṣṭakaḥ ।।
lekhasaṃjñāstathaivānye tatra manvantare dvija ।
pañcame ca gaṇe devāstatsaṃjñā hyamṛtāśinaḥ ।।
śataṃ kratūnāmāhṛtya yasteṣāmadhipo abhavat ।
manojavastathaivendraḥ saṃkhyāto yajñabhāgabhuk ।।
sumedhā virajāścaiva haviṣmānunnato madhuḥ ।
atināmā sahiṣṇuśca saptāsanniti carṣayaḥ ।।
ūru-puru-śatadyumnapramukhāḥ sumahābalāḥ ।
cākṣuṣasya manoḥ putrāḥ pṛthivīpatayo abhavan ।।
etatte kathitaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ mayā manvantaraṃ dvija ।
cākṣuṣasya tathā janma caritañca mahātmanaḥ ।।
sāmprataṃ vartate yo ayaṃ nāmnā vaivasvato manuḥ ।
saptamīye antare tasya devādyāstān śṛṇuṣva me ।।
ya idaṃ kīrtayed dhīmān cākṣuṣasyāntaraṃ bhuvi ।
śṛṇute ca labhet putrānārogyasukhasampadam ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe ṣaṣṭhaṃ manvantaraṃ samāptam,adhyāyaḥ ṣaṭsaptatitamaḥ

saptasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

mārtaṇḍa rasyaverbhāryā tanayā viśvakarmaṇaḥ ।
saṃjñā nāma mahābhāga tasyāṃ bhānurajījanat ।।
manuṃ prakhyātayaśasamanekajñānapāragam ।
vivasvataḥ suto yasmāttasmādvaivasvatastu saḥ ।।
saṃjñā ca raviṇā dṛṣṭā nimīlayati locane ।
yatastataḥ saroṣor'kaḥ saṃjñāṃ niṣṭhuramabravīt ।।
mayi dṛṣṭe sadā yasmāt kuruṣe netrasaṃyamam ।
tasmājjaniṣyase mūḍhe prajāsaṃyamanaṃ yamam ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tataḥ sā capalāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ devī cakre bhayākulā ।
vilolitadṛśaṃ dṛṣṭvā punarāha ca tāṃ raviḥ ।।
yasmādvilolitā dṛṣṭirmayi dṛṣṭe tvayādhunā ।
tasmādvilolāṃ tanayāṃ nadīṃ tvaṃ prasaviṣyasi ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tatastasyāntu saṃjajñe bhartṛśāpena tena vai ।
yamaśca yamunā ceyaṃ prakhyātā sumahānadī ।।
sāpi saṃjñā ravestejaḥ sehe duḥ khena bhāminī ।
asahantī ca sā tejaścintayāmāsa vai tadā ।।
kiṅkaromi kva gacchāmi kva gatāyāśca nirvṛtiḥ ।
bhavenmama kathaṃ bhartā kopamarkaśca naiṣyati ।।
iti saṃcintya bahudhā prajāpatisutā tadā ।
bahu mene mahābhāgā pitṛsaṃśrayameva sā ।।
tataḥ pitṛgṛhe gantuṃ kṛtabuddhiryaśasvinī ।
chāyāmayīmātmatanuṃ nirmame dayitāṃ raveḥ ।।
tāñcovāca tvayā veśmanyatra bhānoryathā mayā ।
tathā samyagapatyeṣu vartitavyaṃ yathā ravau ।।
pṛṣṭayāpi na vācyante tathaitadgamanaṃ mama ।
saivāsmi nāma saṃjñeti vācyametatsadā vacaḥ ।।

chāyasaṃjñovāca

ākeśagrahaṇād devi ! āśāpācca vacastava ।
kariṣye kathayiṣyāmi vṛttantu śāpakarṣaṇāt ।।
ityuktā sā tadā devī jagāma bhavanaṃ pituḥ ।
dadarśa tatra tvaṣṭāraṃ tapasā dhūtakalmaṣam ।।
bahumānācca tenāpi pūjitā viśvakarmaṇā ।
tasthau pitṛgṛhe sā tu kañcitkālamaninditā ।।
tatastāṃ prāha cārvaṅgī pitā nāticiroṣitām ।
stutvā ca tanayāṃ premabahumānapuraḥ saram ।।
tvāntu me paśyato vatse dināni subahūnyapi ।
muhūrtārdhasamāni syuḥ kintu dharmo vilupyate ।।
bāndhaveṣu ciraṃ vāso nārīṇāṃ na yaśaskaraḥ ।
manoratho bāndhavānāṃ nāryā bhartṛgṛhe sthitiḥ ।।
sā tvaṃ trailokyanāthena bhartrā sūryeṇa saṅgatā ।
pitṛgehe ciraṃ kālaṃ vastuṃ nārhasi putrike ।।
sā tvaṃ bhartṛgṛhaṃ gaccha tuṣṭo ahaṃ pūjitāsi me ।
punarāgamanaṃ kāryaṃ darśanāya śubhe mama ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityuktā sā tadā pitrā tathetyuktvā ca sā mune ।
saṃpūjayitvā pitaraṃ jagāmāthottarān kurūn ।।
sūryatāpamanicchantī tejasastasya bibhyatī ।
tapaścacāra tatrāpi vaḍavārūpadhāriṇī ।।
saṃjñeyamiti manvāno dvitīyāyāmahaspatiḥ ।
janayāmāsa tanayau kanyāñcaikāṃ manoramām ।।
chāyāsaṃjñā tvapatyeṣu yathā sveṣvativatsalā ।
tathā na saṃjñākanyāyāṃ putrayoścānvavartata ।।
lālanādyupabhogeṣu viśeṣamanuvāsaram ।
manustat kṣāntavānasya yamastasyā na cakṣame ।।
tāḍanāya ca vai kopāt pādastena samudyataḥ ।
tasyāḥ punaḥ kṣāntimatā na tu dehe nipātitaḥ ।।
tataḥ śaśāpa taṃ kopācchāyāsaṃjñā yamaṃ dvija ।
kiñcit prasphuramāṇauṣṭhī vicalatpāṇipallavā ।।
pituḥ patnīmamaryādaṃ yanmāṃ tarjayase padā ।
bhuvi tasmādayaṃ padāstavādyaiva patiṣyati ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ityākarṇya yamaḥ śāpaṃ mātrā dattaṃ bhayāturaḥ ।
abhyetya pitaraṃ prāha praṇipātapuraḥ saram ।।

yama uvāca

tātaitanmahadāścaryaṃ na dṛṣṭamiti kenacit ।
mātā vātsalyamutsṛjya śāpaṃ putre prayacchati ।।
yathā manurmamācaṣṭe neyaṃ matā tathā mama ।
viguṇeṣvapi putreṣu na mātā viguṇā bhavet ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

yamasyaitadvacaḥ śrutvā bhagavāṃstimirāpahaḥ ।
chāyāsaṃjñāṃ samāhūya papraccha kva gateti sā ।।
sā cāha tanayā tvaṣṭurahaṃ saṃjñā vibhāvaso ।
patnī tava tvayāpatyānyetāni janitāni me ।।
itthaṃ vivasvataḥ sā tu bahuśaḥ pṛcchato yadā ।
nācacakṣe tataḥ kruddho bhāsvāṃstāṃ śaptumudyataḥ ।।
tataḥ sā kathayāmāsa yathāvṛttaṃ vivasvataḥ ।
viditārthaśca bhagavān jagāma tvaṣṭurālayam ।।
tataḥ sa pūjayāmāsa tadā trailokyapūjitam ।
bhāsvantaṃ parayā bhaktyā nijagehamupāgatam ।।
saṃjñāṃ pṛṣṭastadā tasmai kathayāmāsa viśvakṛt ।
āgataiveha me veśma bhavataḥ preṣiteti vai ।।
divākaraḥ samādhistho vaḍavārūpadhāriṇīm ।
tapaścarantīṃ dadṛśe uttareṣu kuruṣvatha ।।
saumyamūrtiḥ śubhākāro mama bhartā bhavediti ।
abhisandhiñca tapaso bubudhe asyā divākaraḥ ।।
śātanaṃ tejaso me adya kriyatāmiti bhāskaraḥ ।
tañcāha viśvakarmāṇaṃ saṃjñāyāḥ pitaraṃ dvija ।।
saṃvatsarabhramestasya viśvakarmā karavestataḥ ।
tejasaḥ śātanañcakre stūyamānaśca daivataiḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe vaivasvatamanvantare saptasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

aṣṭasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tatastaṃ tuṣṭuvurdevāstathā devarṣayo ravim ।
vāgbhiroḍyamaśeṣasya trailokyasya samāgatāḥ ।।

devā ūcuḥ

namaste ṛksvarūpāya sāmarūpāya te namaḥ ।
yajuḥ svarūparūpāya sāmnāndhāmavate namaḥ ।।
jñānaikadhāmabhūtāya nirdhūtatamase namaḥ ।
śuddhajyotiḥ svarūpāya viśuddhāyāmalātmane ।।
variṣṭhāya vareṇyāya parasmai paramātmane ।
namo akhilajagadvyāpisvarūpāyātmamūrtaye ।।
idaṃ stotravaraṃ ramyaṃ śrotavyaṃ śraddhayā naraiḥ ।
śiṣyo bhūtvā samādhistho dattvā deyaṃ gurorapi ।।
na śūnyabhūtaiḥ śrotavyametattu saphalaṃ bhavet ।
sarvakāraṇabhūtāya niṣṭhāyai jñānacetasām ।।
namaḥ sūryasvarūpāya prakāśātmasvarūpiṇe ।
bhāskarāya namastubhyaṃ tathā dinakṛte namaḥ ।।
śarvarīhetave caiva sandhyājyotsnākṛte namaḥ ।
tvaṃ sarvametad bhagavan jagadudbhramatā tvayā ।।
bhramatyāviddhamakhilaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ sacarācaram ।
tvadaṃśubhiridaṃ spṛṣṭaṃ sarvaṃ sañjāyate śuci ।।
kriyate tvatkaraiḥ sparśājjalādīnāṃ pavitratā ।
homadānādiko dharmo nopakārāya jāyate ।।
tāvadyāvanna saṃyogi jagadetat tvadaṃśubhiḥ ।
ṛcaste sakalā hyetā yajūṃṣyetāni cānyataḥ ।।
sakalāni ca sāmāni nipatanti tvadaḍgataḥ ।
ṛṅmayastvaṃ jagannātha ! tvameva ca yajurmayaḥ ।।
yataḥ sāmamayaścaiva tato nātha ! trayīmayaḥ ।
tvameva brahmaṇo rūpaṃ parañcāparameva ca ।।
mūrtāmūrtastathā sūkṣmaḥ sthūlarūpastathā sthitaḥ ।
nimeṣakāṣṭhādimayaḥ kālarūpaḥ kṣayātmakaḥ ।
prasīda svecchayā rūpaṃ svatejaḥ śamanaṃ kuru ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

evaṃ saṃstūyamānastu devairdevarṣibhistathā ।
mumoca svaṃ tadā tejastejasāṃ rāśiravyayaḥ ।।
yattasya ṛṅmayaṃ tejo bhavitā tena medinī ।
yajurmayenāpi divaṃ svargaḥ sāmamayaṃ raveḥ ।।
śātitāstejaso bhāgā ye tvaṣṭrā daśa pañca ca ।
tvaṣṭraiva tena śarvasya kṛtaṃ śūlaṃ mahātmanā ।।
cakraṃ viṣṇorvasūnāñca śaṅkavo atha sudāruṇāḥ ।
pāvakasya tathā śaktiḥ śibikā dhanadasya ca ।।
anyeṣāmasurārīṇāmastrāṇyugrāṇi yāni vai ।
yakṣavidyādharāṇāñca tāni cakre sa viśvakṛt ।।
tataśca ṣoḍaśaṃ bhāgaṃ bibharti bhagavān vibhuḥ ।
tattejaḥ pañcadaśadhā śātitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā ।।
tato aśvarūpadhṛgbhānuruttarānagamat kurūn ।
tadṛśe tatra saṃjñāñca vaḍavārūpadhāriṇīm ।।
sā ca dṛṣṭvā tamāyāntaṃ parapuṃso viśaṅkayā ।
jagāma saṃmukhaṃ tasya pṛṣṭharakṣaṇatatparā ।।
tataśca nāsikāyogaṃ tayostatra sametayoḥ ।
nāsatyadastrau tanayāvaśvīvaktravinirgatau ।।
retaso ante ca revantaḥ khaḍgī carmo tanutradhṛk ।
aśvārūḍhaḥ samudbhūto bāṇatūṇasamanvitaḥ ।।
tataḥ svarūpamatulaṃ darśayāmāsa bhānumān ।
tasyaiṣā ca samālokya svarūpaṃ mudamādade ।।
svarūpadhāriṇīñcaimāmānināya nijāśrayam ।
saṃjñāṃ bhāryāṃ prītimatīṃ bhāskaro vāritaskaraḥ ।।
tataḥ pūrvasuto yo asyāḥ so abhūdvaivasvato manuḥ ।
dvitīyaśca yamaḥ śāpāddharmadṛṣṭirabhūt sutaḥ ।।
kṛmayo māṃsamādāya pādato asya mahītale ।
patiṣyantīti śāpāntaṃ tasya cakre pitā svayam ।।
dharmadṛṣṭiryataścāsau samo mitre tathāhite ।
tato niyogaṃ taṃ yāmye cakāra timirāpahaḥ ।।
yamunā ca nadī jajñe kalindāntaravāhinī ।
aśvinau devabhiṣajau kṛtau pitrā mahātmanā ।।
guhyakādhipatitve ca revanto api niyojitaḥ ।
cchāyāsaṃjñāsutānāñca niyogaḥ śruyatāṃ mama ।।
pūrvajasya manostulyaśchāyāsaṃjñāsuto agrajaḥ ।
tataḥ sāvarṇikīṃ saṃjñāmavāpa tanayo raveḥ ।।
bhaviṣyati manuḥ so api balirindro yadā tadā ।
śanaiścaro grahāṇāñca madhye pitrā niyojitaḥ ।।
tayostṛtīyā yā kanyā tapatī nāma sā kurum ।
nṛpāt saṃvaraṇāt putramavāpa manujeśvaram ।।
tasya vaivasvatasyāhaṃ manoḥ saptamamantaram ।
kathayāmi sutān bhūpānṛṣīn devān surādhipam ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare vaivasvatotpattirnāmāṣṭasaptatitamo adhyāyaḥ

ūnāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

ādityā vasavo rudrāḥ sādhyā viśve marudgaṇāḥ ।
bhṛgavo aṅgirasaścāṣṭau yatra devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
ādityā vasavo rudrā vijñeyāḥ kaśyapātmajāḥ ।
sādhyāśca maruto viśve dharmaputragaṇāstrayaḥ ।।
bhṛgostu bhṛgavo devāḥ putrā hyaṅgirasaḥ sutāḥ ।
eṣa sargaśca mārīco vijñeyaḥ sāmpratādhipaḥ ।।
ūrjasvī nāma caivendro mahātmā yajñabhāgabhuk ।
atītānāgatā ye ca vartante sāmpratañca ye ।।
sarve te tridaśendrāstu vijñeyāstulyalakṣaṇāḥ ।
sahasrākṣāḥ kuliśinaḥ sarva eva purandarāḥ ।।
maghavanto vṛṣāḥ sarve śṛṅgiṇo gajagāminaḥ ।
te śatakratavaḥ sarve bhūtābhibhavatejasaḥ ।।
dharmādyaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ suddhairādhipatyaguṇānvitāḥ ।
bhūtabhavyabhavannāthāḥ śṛṇu caitat trayaṃ dvija ।।
bhūrloko ayaṃ smṛtā bhūmirantarikṣaṃ divaḥ smṛtam ।
divyākhyāśca tathā svargastrailokyamiti gadyate ।।
atriścaiva vasiṣṭhaśca kāśyapaśca mahānṛṣiḥ ।
gautamaśca bharadvājau viśvāmitro atha kauśikaḥ ।।
tathaiva putro bhagavānṛcīkasya mahātmanaḥ ।
jamadagnistu saptaite munayo atra nathāntare ।।
ikṣvākurnābhagaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireva ca ।
nariṣyantaśca vikhyāto nābhāgāriṣṭa eva ca ।।
karūṣaśca pṛṣadhraśca vasumān lokaviśrutaḥ ।
manorvaivasvatasyaite nava putrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।
vaivasvatamidaṃ brahman ! kathitante mayāntaram ।
asmin śrute naraḥ sadyaḥ paṭhite caiva sattama ।
mucyate pātakaiḥ sarvaiḥ puṇyañca mahadaśnate ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare vaivasvatakīrtanaṃ nāmaikonāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

aśītitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

krauṣṭukiruvāca

svāyambhuvādyāḥ kathitāḥ saptaite manavo mama ।
tadantareṣu ye devā rājāno munayastathā ।।
asmin kalpe sapta ye anye bhaviṣyanti mahāmune ।
manavastān samācakṣva ye ca devādayaśca ye ।।
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

kathitastava sāvarṇiśchāyāsaṃjñāsutaśca yaḥ ।
pūrvajasya manostulyaḥ sa manurbhavitāṣṭamaḥ ।।
rāmo vyāso gālavaśca dīptimān kṛpa eva ca ।
ṛṣyaśṛṅgastathā droṇastatra saptarṣayo abhavan ।।
sutapāścāmitābhāśca mukhyāścaiva tridhā surāḥ ।
viṃśakaḥ kathitāścaiṣāṃ trayāṇāṃ triguṇo gaṇaḥ ।।
tapastaptaśca śakraśca dyutirjyotiḥ prabhākaraḥ ।
prabhāso dayito dharmastejoraśmiścirakratuḥ ।।
ityādikastu sutapā devānāṃ viṃśako gaṇaḥ ।
prabhurvibhurvibhāsādyastathānyo viṃśako gaṇaḥ ।।
surāṇāmamitābhānāṃ tṛtīyamapi me śṛṇu ।
damo dānto ṛtaḥ somo vittādyāścaiva viṃśatiḥ ।।
mukhyā hyete samākhyātā devā manvantarādhipāḥ ।
mārīcasyaiva te putrāḥ kaśyapasya prajāpateḥ ।।
bhaviṣyāśca bhaviṣyanti sāvarṇasyāntare manoḥ ।
teṣāmindro bhaviṣyastu balirvairocanirmune ।।
pātāla āste yo adyāpi daityaḥ samayabandhanaḥ ।
virajāścārvavīraśca nirmohaḥ satyavāk kṛtiḥ ।
viṣṇvādyāścaiva tanayāḥ sāvarṇasya manornṛpāḥ ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe aśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

ekāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ- ।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

sāvarṇiḥ sūryatanayo yo manuḥ kathyate aṣṭamaḥ ।
niśāmaya tadutpattiṃ vistarād gadato mama ।।
mahāmāyānubhāvena yathā manvantarādhipaḥ ।
sa babhūva mahābhāgaḥ sāvarṇistanayo raveḥ ।।
svārociṣe antare pūrvaṃ caitravaṃśasamudbhavaḥ ।
suratho nāma rājābhūt samaste kṣitimaṇḍale ।।
tasya pālayataḥ samyak prajāḥ putrānivaurasān ।
babhūvuḥ śatravo bhūpāḥ kolāvidhvaṃsinastathā ।।
tasya tairabhavad yuddhamatiprabaladaṇḍinaḥ ।
nyūnairapi sa tairyuddhe kolāvidhvaṃsibhirjitaḥ ।।
tataḥ svapuramāyāto nijadeśādhipo abhavat ।
ākrāntaḥ sa mahābhāgastaistadā prabalāribhiḥ ।।
amātyairbalibhirduṣṭairdurbalasya durātmabhiḥ ।
koṣo balañcāpahṛtaṃ tatrāpi svapure tataḥ ।।
tato mṛgayāvyājena hṛtasvāmyaḥ sa bhupatiḥ ।
ekākī hayamāruhya jagāma gahanaṃ vanam ।।
sa tatrāśramamadrākṣīd dvijavaryasya medhasaḥ ।
praśāntaśvāpadākīrṇaṃ muniśṣyopaśobhitam ।।
tasthau kañcit sa kālañca muninā tena satkṛtaḥ ।
itaścaitaśca vicaraṃstasmin munivarāśrame ।।
so acintayat tadā tatra mamatvākṛṣṭacetanaḥ ।
matpūrvaiḥ pālitaṃ pūrvaṃ mayā hīnaṃ puraṃ hi tat ।
madbhṛtyaistairasadvṛttairdharmataḥ pālyate na vā ।।
na jāne sa pradhāno me śūrahastī sadāmadaḥ ।
mama vairivaśaṃ yātaḥ kān bhogānupalapsyate ।।
ye mamānugatā nityaṃ prasādadhanabhojanaiḥ ।
anuvṛttiṃ dhruvaṃ te adya kurvantyanyamahībhṛtām ।।
asamyagvyayaśīlaistaiḥ kurvadbhiḥ satataṃ vyayam ।
saṃcitaḥ so atiduḥ khena kṣayaṃ kośo gamiṣyati ।।
etaccānyacca satataṃ cintayāmāsa pārthivaḥ ।
tatra viprāśramābhyāse vaiśyamekaṃ dadarśa saḥ ।।
sa pṛṣṭastena kastvaṃ bhoḥ hetuścāgamane atra kaḥ ।
saśoka iva kasmāttvaṃ durmanā iva lakṣyase ।।
ityākarṇya vacastasya bhūpateḥ praṇayoditam ।
pratyuvāca sa taṃ vaiśyaḥ praśrayāvanato nṛpam ।।

vaiśya uvāca

samādhirnāma vaiśyo ahamutpanno dhanināṃ kule ।
putradārairnirastaśca dhanalobhādasādhubhiḥ ।।
vihīnaśca dhanairdāraiḥ putrairādāya me dhanam ।
vanamabhyāgato duḥ khī nirastaścāptabandhubhaiḥ ।।
so ahaṃ na vedmi putrāṇāṃ kuśalākuśalātmikām ।
pravṛttiṃ svajanānāñca dārāṇāñcātra saṃsthitaḥ ।।
kiṃ nu teṣāṃ gṛhe kṣemamakṣemaṃ kiṃ nu sāmpratam ।
kathaṃ te kiṃ nu sadvṛttāḥ durvṛttāḥ kiṃ nu me sutāḥ ।।

rājovāca

yairnirasto bhavāṃllubdhaiḥ putradārādibhirdhanaiḥ ।
teṣu kiṃ bhavataḥ snehamanubadhnāti mānasam ।।

vaiśca uvāca

evametadyathā prāha bhavānasmadgataṃ vacaḥ ।
kiṃ karomi na badhnāti mama niṣṭhuratāṃ manaḥ ।।
yaiḥ santyajya pitṛsnehaṃ dhanalubdhairnirākṛtaḥ ।
patisvajanahārdaṃ ca hārdi teṣveva me manaḥ ।।
kimetannābhijānāmi jānannapi mahāmate ।
yatpremapravaṇaṃ cittaṃ viguṇeṣvapi bandhuṣu ।।
teṣāṃ kṛte me niḥ śvāso daurmanasyaṃ ca jāyate ।
karomi kiṃ yanna manasteṣvaprītiṣu niṣṭhuram ।।

mārkaṇḍeya uvāca

tatastau sahitau vipra taṃ muniṃ samupasthitau ।
samādhirnāma vaiśyo asau sa ca pārthivasattamaḥ ।।
kṛtvā tu tau yathānyāyaṃ yathārhaṃ tena saṃvidam ।
upaviṣṭau kathāḥ kāściccakraturvaiśya-pārthivau ।।

rājauvāca

bhagavaṃstvāmahaṃ praṣṭumiccāmyekaṃ vadasva tat ।
duḥ khāya yanme manasaḥ svacittāyattatāṃ vinā ।।
mamatvaṃ gatarājyasya rājyāṅgeṣvakhileṣvapi ।
jānato api yathājñasya kimetanmunisattama ।।
ayaṃ ca nikṛtaḥ putrairdārairbhṛtyaistathojjhitaḥ ।
svajanena ca santyaktasteṣu hārde tathāpyati ।।
evameṣa tathāhaṃ ca dvāvapyatyantaduḥ khitau ।
dṛṣṭadoṣe api viṣaye mamatvākṛṣṭamānasau ।।
tatkimetanmahābhāga yanmoho jñāninorapi ।
mamāsya ca bhavatyeṣā vivekāndhasya mūḍhatā ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

jñānamasti samastasya jantorviṣayagocare ।
viṣayaśca mahābhāga yāti caivaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।
divāndhāḥ prāṇinaḥ kecidrātrāvandhāstathāpare ।
kecid divā tathā rātrau prāṇinastulyadṛṣṭayaḥ ।।
jñānino manujāḥ satyaṃ kintu te na hi kevalam ।
yato hi jñāninaḥ sarve paśu-pakṣi-mṛgādayaḥ ।।
jñānaṃ ca tanmanuṣyāṇāṃ yatteṣāṃ mṛgṛpakṣiṇām ।
manuṣyāṇāṃ ca yatteṣāṃ tulyamanyattathobhayoḥ ।।
jñāne api sati paśyaitān pataṅgāñchāvacañcuṣu ।
kaṇamokṣādṛtān mohātpīḍyamānānapi kṣudhā ।।
mānuṣā manujavyāghra sābhilāṣāḥ sutān prati ।
lobhātpratyupakārāya nanvetān kiṃ na paśyasi ।।
tathāpi mamatāvarte mohagarte nipātitāḥ ।
mahāmāyāprabhāveṇa saṃsārasthitikāriṇā ।।
tannātra vismayaḥ kāryo yoganidrā jagatpateḥ ।
mahāmāyā hareścaitattathā saṃmohyate jagat ।।
jñānināmapi cetāṃsi devī bhagavatī hi sā ।
balādākṛṣya mohāya mahāmāyā prayacchati ।।
tayā visṛjyate viśvaṃ jagadetaccarācaram ।
saiṣā prasannā varadā nṛṇāṃ bhavati muktaye ।।
sā vidyā paramā mukterhetubhūtā sanātanī ।
saṃsārabandhahetuśca saiva sarveśvareśvarī ।।

rojovāca

bhagavan ! kā hi sā devī mahāmāyeti yāṃ bhavān ।
bravīti kathamutpannā sā karmāsyāśca kiṃ dvija ।।
yatsvabhāvā ca sā devī yatsvarūpā yadudbhavā ।
tat sarvaṃ śrotumicchāmi tvatto brahmavidāṃ vara ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

nityaiva sā jaganmūrtistayā sarvamidaṃ tatam ।
tathāpi tatsamutpattirbahudhā śruyatāṃ mama ।।
devānāṃ kāryasiddhyarthamāvirbhavati sā yadā ।
utpanneti tadā loke sā nityāpyabhidhīyate ।।
yoganidrāṃ yadā viṣṇurjagatyekārṇavīkṛte ।
āstīrya śeṣamabhajat kalpānte bhagavān prabhuḥ ।।
tadā dvāvasurau ghorau vikhyātau madhukaiṭabhau ।
viṣṇukarṇamalodbhūtau hantuṃ brahmāṇamudyatau ।।
sa nābhikamale viṣṇoḥ sthito brahmā prajāpatiḥ ।
dṛṣṭvā tāvasurau cograu prasuptaṃ ca janārdanam ।।
tuṣṭāva yoganidrāṃ tāmekāgrahṛdayasthitaḥ ।
vibodhanārthāya harerharinetrakṛtālayām ।।

brahmovāca

viśveśvarīṃ jagaddhātrīṃ sthiti-saṃhārakāriṇīm ।
nidrāṃ bhagavatīṃ viṣṇoratulāṃ tejasaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
tvaṃ svāhā tvaṃ svadhā tvaṃ hi vaṣaṭkāraḥ svarātmikā ।
sudhā tvamakṣare nitye tridhā mātrātmikā sthitā ।।
ardhamātrā sthitā nityā yānuccāryā viśeṣataḥ ।
tvameva sandhyā sāvitrī tvaṃ devi jananī parā ।।
tvayaiva dhāryate sarvaṃ tvayaitatsṛjyate jagat ।
tvayaitatpālyate devi tvamatsyante ca sarvadā ।।
visṛṣṭau sṛṣṭirūpā tvaṃ sthitirūpā ca pālane ।
tathā saṃhṛtirūpānte jagato asya jaganmaye ।।
mahāvidyā mahāmāyā mahāmedhā mahāsmṛtiḥ ।
mahāmohā ca bhavatī mahādevī maheśvarī ।।
prakṛtistvañca sarvasya guṇatrayavibhāvinī ।
kālarātrirmahārātrirmoharātriśca dāruṇā ।।
tvaṃ śrīstvamīśvarī tvaṃ hrīstvaṃ buddhirbodhalakṣaṇā ।
lajjā puṣṭistathā tuṣṭistvaṃ śāntiḥ kṣāntireva ca ।।
khaḍiganī śūlinī ghorā gadinī cakriṇī tathā ।
śaṅkhinī cāpinī bāṇa-bhuśuṇḍī parighāyudhā ।।
saumyā saumyatarāśeṣa-saumyebhyastvatisundarī ।
parāparāṇāṃ paramā tvameva parameśvarī ।।
yacca kiñcit kvacidvastu sadasadvākhilātmike ।
tasya sarvasya yā śiktiḥ sā tvaṃ kiṃ stūyate tadā ।।
yayā tvayā jagatstraṣṭā jagatpātyatti yo jagat ।
so api nidrāvaśaṃ nītaḥ kastvāṃ stotumiheśvaraḥ ।।
viṣṇuḥ śarīragrahaṇamahāmīśāna eva ca ।
kāritāste yato atastvāṃ kaḥ stotuṃ śaktimān bhavet ।।
sā tvamitthaṃ prabhāvaiḥ svairudārairdevi saṃstutā ।
mohayaitau durādharṣāvasuro madhukaiṭabhau ।।
prabodhañca jagatsvāmī nīyatāmacyuto laghu ।
bodhaśca kriyatāmasya hantumetau mahāsurau ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

evaṃ stutā tadā devī tāmasī tatra vedhasā ।
viṣṇoḥ prabodhanārthāya nihantuṃ madhukaiṭabhau ।।
netrāsyanāsikā-bāhu-hṛdayebhyastathorasaḥ ।
nirgamya darśane tasthau brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।।
uttasthau ca jagannāthastayā mukto janārdanaḥ ।
ekārṇave ahiśayanāttataḥ sa dadṛśe ca tau ।।
madhukaiṭabhau durātmānāvativīryaparākramau ।
krodharaktekṣaṇāvattuṃ brahmāṇaṃ janitodyamau ।।
samutthāya tatastābhyāṃ yuyudhe bhagavān hariḥ ।
pañcavarṣasahasrāṇi bāhupraharaṇo vibhuḥ ।।
tāvapyatibalonmattau mahāmāyāvimohitau ।
uktavantau varo asmatto vriyatāmiti keśavam ।।

bhagavānuvāca

bhavanetāmadya me tuṣṭau mama vadhyāvubhāvapi ।
kimanyena vareṇātra etāvaddhi vṛtaṃ mama ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

vañcitābhyāmiti tadā sarvamāpomayaṃ jagat ।
vilokya tābhyāṃ gadito bhagavān kamalekṣaṇaḥ ।।
āvāṃ jahi na yatrorvo salilena pariplutā ।
prītau svastava yuddhena ślāghyastvaṃ mṛtyurāvayoḥ ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

tathetyuktvā bhagavatā śaṅkha-cakra-gadābhṛtā ।
kṛtvā cakreṇa vai cchinne jaghane śirasī tayoḥ ।।
evameṣā samutpannā brahmaṇā saṃstutā svayam ।
prabhāvamasyā devyāstu bhūyaḥ śṛṇu vadāmi te ।।

iti śrīmārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe sāvarṇike manvantare devīmāhātmye madhukaiṭabhavadho nāma ekāśītitamo adhyāyaḥ

dvyaśītitamo adhyāyaḥ- 

ṛṣiruvāca

devāsuramabhūd yuddhaṃ pūrṇamabdaśataṃ purā ।
mahiṣe asurāṇāmadhipe devānāṃ ca purandare ।।
tatrāsurairmahāvīryairdevasainyaṃ parājitam ।
jitvā ca sakalān devānindro abūnmahiṣāsuraḥ ।।
tataḥ parājitā devāḥ padmayoniṃ prajāpatim ।
puraskṛtya gatāstatra yatreśa-garuḍadhvajau ।।
yathāvṛttaṃ tayostadvanmahiṣāsuraceṣṭitam ।
tridaśāḥ kathayāmāsurdevābhibhavavistaram ।।
sūryendragnyanilendūnāṃ yamasya varuṇasya ca ।
anyeṣāṃ cādhikārān sa svayamevādhitiṣṭhiti ।।
svargānnirākṛtāḥ sarve tena devagaṇā bhuvi ।
vicaranti yathā martyā mahiṣeṇa durātmanā ।।
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvamamarāriviceṣṭitam ।
śaraṇaṃ vaḥ prapannāḥ smo vadhastasya vicintyatām ।।

ṛṣiruvāca

itthaṃ niśamya devānāṃ vacāṃsi madhusūdanaḥ ।
cakāra kopaṃ śambhuśca bhrukuṭīkuṭilānanau ।।
tato atikopapūrṇasya cakriṇo vadanāttataḥ ।
niścakrāma mahattejo brahmaṇaḥ śaṅkarasya ca ।।
anyeṣāñcaiva devānāṃ śakrādīnāṃ śarīrataḥ ।
nirgataṃ sumahattejastaccaikyaṃ samagacchata ।।
atīva tejasaḥ kūṭaṃ jvalantamiva parvatam ।
dadṛśuste surāstatra jvālāvyāptadigantaram ।।
atulaṃ tatra tattejaḥ sarvadevaśarīrajam ।
